### [1] [Dissecting the Scalar Cosmological Collider with the Cosmic Microwave Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18369)
*Oliver H. E. Philcox*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过联合分析多场暴胀拉格朗日量（multi-field inflationary Lagrangian），利用宇宙学 bootstrap 和宇宙学流（cosmological flow）等现代理论工具，构建了原始三点关联函数（primordial bispectra）库，并结合 Planck 数据对八参数多场似然函数（multi-field likelihood）进行贝叶斯探索。研究发现，弱混合假设（weak mixing assumption）与当前数据不兼容，而强混合暴胀子的 Planck 约束远强于理论界限；在全参数空间中未发现新物理的证据，最大 χ² 改进仅为 5.3。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学对撞机（cosmological collider）计划通过暴胀期间粒子交换产生的振荡信号探测超高能物理，但由于暴胀的非线性对称性，这些信号不会孤立出现，且其振幅受微扰性（perturbativity）和幺正性（unitarity）约束。已有研究多假设弱混合，但该假设的有效性尚未被系统检验。因此，有必要对完整的多场暴胀拉格朗日量进行联合分析，以全面探测宇宙学对撞机物理。

Method: 作者利用宇宙学 bootstrap 和宇宙学流（CosmoFlow）等现代理论工具，构建了涵盖单场、双场和三场标量场交换及自相互作用的原始三点关联函数库。结合 Planck 对暴胀形状函数（inflationary shape function）的最新测量与现代采样技术，对包含八个参数的多场似然函数进行贝叶斯探索。针对强混合情形，通过 CosmoFlow 数值求解暴胀三点关联函数，首次实现强混合暴胀子的数据分析。

Result: 伴生研究表明，弱混合假设与当前数据集不兼容（最小质量情形除外）。强混合暴胀子的 Planck 约束远紧于理论界限，尽管振荡贡献被显著压低。在整个多场参数景观中，未发现新物理的证据，最大 χ² 改进仅为 5.3。

Conclusion: 当前 Planck 数据对多场暴胀参数空间施加了比理论界限更严格的约束；弱混合假设被排除；宇宙学对撞机信号在多场框架下受到强烈抑制，尚未探测到新物理信号。

Abstract: The cosmological collider program probes ultra-high-energy physics by searching for subtle oscillatory signatures induced by inflationary particle exchange. Due to the non-linear symmetries usually assumed in inflation, these signals do not appear in isolation; moreover, their amplitudes are bounded by perturbativity and unitarity. To comprehensively probe cosmological collider physics, we must jointly analyze the full multi-field inflationary Lagrangian: in this work, we conduct such a study, probing single, double, and triple scalar field exchange and self-interactions across a wide range of masses (in both the complementary and principal series), mixings, and sound-speeds. Using modern theoretical tools (including the cosmological bootstrap and the cosmological flow), we construct a vast library of tree-level primordial bispectra: combining these with recent measurements of the inflationary shape function from Planck and modern sampling techniques, we perform Bayesian exploration of the eight-parameter multi-field likelihood. Most previous studies of cosmological collider physics assume weak mixing, such that the coupling between the scalar field and the Goldstone mode can be treated perturbatively: in our companion study, we demonstrate that this assumption is incompatible with current datasets except at the smallest masses. By solving for the inflationary bispectra numerically using CosmoFlow, we perform the first analysis of the strongly-mixed collider, demonstrating that the Planck constraints are much tighter than the theoretical bounds, though the oscillatory contributions are heavily suppressed. Across the full multi-field landscape, we find no evidence for new physics with a maximal $χ^2$ improvement of $5.3$.

</details>


### [2] [Probing large mass-splitting inelastic Dark Matter with RES-NOVA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18378)
*D. Alloni,G. Benato,P. Carniti,M. Cataldo,L. Chen,M. Clemenza,M. Consonni,G. Croci,I. Dafinei,F. A. Danevich,C. de Vecchi,D. Di Martino,R. Elleboro,N. Ferreiro Iachellini,F. Ferroni,F. Filippini,S. Ghislandi,A. Giachero,L. Gironi,P. Gorla,C. Gotti,D. L. Helis,D. V. Kasperovych,V. V. Kobychev,G. Marcucci,A. Melchiorre,A. Menegolli,S. Nisi,M. Musa,L. Pagnanini,L. Pattavina,G. Pessina,S. Pirro,S. Pozzi,M. C. Prata,A. Puiu,S. Quitadamo,M. P. Riccardi,M. Rossella,R. Rossini,E. Sala,F. Saliu,A. Salvini,V. I. Tretyak,L. Trombetta,D. Trotta,H. Yuan,J. Luengas,H. Ramani*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本工作利用考古铅制成的PbWO4低温量热器（cryogenic calorimeter）RES-NOVA原型探测器，在意大利Gran Sasso地下实验室采集的32.4克·天暴露数据（2.5 keV–1 MeV能区）下，对非弹性暗物质（inelastic dark matter）在大质量劈裂（large mass splittings）参数空间给出了超越现有Xe基时间投影室（TPC）技术的直接探测约束，在标准晕模型（SHM）和大麦哲伦云（LMC）速度分布下分别将劈裂上限拓展至510 keV和780 keV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测大质量劈裂区间的非弹性暗物质需要重靶核、宽反冲能范围以及暗物质分布的高速度尾端，现有技术（如Xe基TPC）仅能覆盖至约330 keV的劈裂能区，不足以探索更大参数空间。

Method: 采用RES-NOVA原型探测器——由考古铅（archaeological Pb）制成的PbWO4低温量热器，运行于意大利Gran Sasso国家实验室的深地环境；分析了32.4克·天的暴露数据，反冲能窗口为2.5 keV至1 MeV；分别基于标准晕模型（SHM）和大麦哲伦云（LMC）驱动的速度分布设定暗物质晕基准。

Result: 在SHM（LMC）基准下，将非弹性暗物质的直接探测约束劈裂上限从约330 keV延伸至510 keV（780 keV）；未来更长的暴露数据将进一步探测新的参数空间区域。

Conclusion: 基于考古铅PbWO4低温量热器的RES-NOVA原型能够有效拓展非弹性暗物质在大质量劈裂区间的探测能力，为后续更大暴露量的实验提供了有前景的路径。

Abstract: Probing inelastic dark matter at large mass splittings requires heavy target nuclei, an extended recoil-energy range, and the high-velocity tail of the dark-matter distribution. We exploit these features with the RES-NOVA prototype detector, featuring a PbWO4 cryogenic calorimeter, produced from archaeological Pb and operated at the deep-underground laboratory of Gran Sasso of INFN (Italy), analyzing a 32.4 g day exposure over 2.5 keV - 1 MeV under both the Standard Halo Model (SHM) and a Large Magellanic Cloud (LMC)-motivated velocity distribution. We extend direct-detection constraints beyond the 330 keV reach of established technologies (e.g. Xe-based TPCs), probing splittings up to 510 (780) keV in the SHM (LMC) benchmark, while future exposures will probe new regions of the parameter space.

</details>


### [3] [GUEST: Gravitational Universe Exploration with Satellite Tracking. A passive satellite laser-ranging mission for the dark gravitational Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18390)
*Diego Blas,Aurélien Hees,F. Javier Atapuerca,Giada Bargiacchi,Massimo Bassan,Joshua N. Benabou,Bruno Bertrand,Adrien Bourgoin,Clare Burrage,Nicolò Burzillà,Alfonso Caldiero,Roberto Campagnola,Andrea Caputo,Ana Caramete,Laurentiu Caramete,Joan Manel Casalta Escuer,Julien Chabé,Gabriel Chiritoi,Marco Cinelli,Florin-Ioan Constantin,Neil J. Cornish,Clément Courde,Simone Dell'Agnello,Alessandro Di Marco,Sebastian Ellis,Malcolm Fairbairn,Ariadna Farrés,Joshua W. Foster,Silvia Gasparotto,Marta Goli,Yann Gouttenoire,Michael Häfner,Antonio J. Iovino,Maria-Catalina Isfan,Justin Janquart,Alexander C. Jenkins,Jean-Paul Kneib,Sébastien Le Maistre,David Lucchesi,Marco Lucente,Angus Macdonald,Jorge Martín Camalich,Rosa Martínez Rubiella,Josep J. Masdemont,Ilia Musco,Toshimichi Otsubo,Cristóbal Padilla,Fco. Rogelio Palomo Pinto,Alice Paun,Alice Perego,Roberto Peron,Florentina-Crenguta Pislan,Florin Adrian Popescu,Luca Porcelli,Nanda Rea,Rafael Rebolo,Marco Reyes,Ignasi Ribas,José C. Rodríguez,Pascal Rosenblatt,Albert Roura,Soumen Roy,Mariano Sánchez Nogales,Francesco Santoli,Feliciana Sapio,Anja Schlicht,Ulrich Schreiber,Angela Serrano,Daniel Serrano Lombillo,Alberto Sesana,Carlos F. Sopuerta,Krzysztof Sośnica,Nicola Tamanini,Elisa Todarello,Sokratis Trifinopoulos,Miguel Vanvlasselaer,Dario Vetrano,Massimo Visco,Hanxi Wang,Xiao Xue,Miguel Zumalacárregui*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: GUEST是一项空间任务概念，旨在通过部署在高度椭圆地球轨道（偏心率e≥0.7，周期P≥33小时）上的两个无源球体，利用全球卫星激光测距（satellite laser ranging）网络连续跟踪至少10年（预期总时长30年），探测微赫兹（microhertz）频段的引力波（gravitational waves, GWs），同时涵盖粒子物理、引力波天文学、宇宙学、天体物理和大地测量学等多学科科学目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有及计划中的探测器均无法在微赫兹频段实现显著水平的引力波探测，而该频段包含丰富的物理信息。GUEST旨在填补这一频率窗口的空白，开启超长周期引力波信号的全新探测途径。

Method: 将两个覆盖角隅棱镜（cube-corner retroreflectors）的密集无源球体部署于高度椭圆地球轨道，由全球卫星激光测距站网络连续跟踪，轨道自身作为振荡引力微扰的谐振探测器（resonant detectors），通过选定的轨道参数实现微赫兹灵敏度。

Result: 在微赫兹频段首次实现对超大质量黑洞双星（supermassive black-hole binaries）的相干引力波搜索；探索脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar-timing arrays）与LISA之间未探索能隙中的原初引力波背景；在现有实验未触及的参数区域探测超轻暗物质（ultra-light dark matter）；寻找超轻玻色子（ultra-light bosons）；在天文尺度上对新引力相互作用进行数量级改进的检验；实现对GM⊕的绝对测定阶跃性提升，支撑全球大地测量观测系统（Global Geodetic Observing System）及未来导航与对地观测任务。

Conclusion: GUEST以一个相对简单的任务概念，在微赫兹引力波探测这一无法被其他探测器覆盖的频段上，实现了涵盖基础物理、引力波天文学、宇宙学、天体物理和大地测量学等多个领域的广泛科学产出，具有跨学科的科学影响力。

Abstract: GUEST is a space mission concept whose central objective is the detection of gravitational waves (GWs) in the microhertz band -- a physics-rich frequency window that no other present or planned detector can reach at a significant level. The concept is simple: two dense, passive spheres, covered with cube-corner retroreflectors, deployed in {highly eccentric} Earth orbits ($e \gtrsim 0.7$, period $P \gtrsim 33$ h), tracked continuously by the global network of satellite laser-ranging stations over a minimum observation time of 10 years, with an expected total duration of 30 years. The orbits themselves act as resonant detectors of the oscillating gravitational perturbations, with the microhertz sensitivity emerging from the selected orbital parameters. From the same data stream, GUEST delivers a programme of fundamental and applied science that cuts across particle physics, gravitational-wave astronomy, cosmology, astrophysics, and geodesy: the first coherent search for GWs from supermassive black-hole binaries in the $μ$Hz band, the exploration of primordial GW backgrounds in the unexplored energy-scale gap between pulsar-timing arrays and LISA, a dedicated probe of ultra-light dark matter in a parameter region untouched by any other experiment, a new way to search for ultra-light bosons, order-of-magnitude-improved tests of new gravitational interactions at astronomical ranges, and a step change in the absolute determination of $GM_\oplus$ that underpins the Global Geodetic Observing System and future navigation and Earth-observation missions. This white paper presents the motivation, scientific reach, and mission concept of GUEST.

</details>


### [4] [Detection of cosmic strings by gravitational wave lensing. Predictions for Einstein Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18441)
*Jakub Szyndler,Tomasz Bulik*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究探讨宇宙弦（cosmic strings）能否通过爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope, ET）以引力波透镜（gravitational lensing）效应被探测。采用波光学（wave optics）方法分析放大因子、信噪比（Signal-to-Noise Ratio, SNR）和波形，并基于八次并合模拟数据利用贝叶斯推断（Bayesian Inference）估计弦张力。结果表明宇宙弦可被ET探测，估计的对数弦张力值为$\bar{\log{Gμ}}=-9.78^{+0.44}_{-0.49}$，与注入值$-10$一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙弦是早期宇宙中形成的拓扑缺陷（topological defects），尚未被实验确认。它们可以弯曲光线或引力波，产生类似引力透镜（gravitational lensing）的效应。研究旨在检验宇宙弦能否被爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）作为引力波透镜探测到。

Method: 采用波光学（wave optics）框架进行分析。首先研究放大因子（amplification factor）的强度与行为；随后针对不同的源倾角（inclination），考察波形、信噪比（SNR）中的波效应（wave effects）；最后基于StarTrack模拟中的八次并合事件，利用贝叶斯推断（Bayesian Inference）方法估计弦张力（string tension）。

Result: 波效应在波形、SNR及特征应变（characteristic strains）中清晰可见；大部分事件根据SNR值可被探测；几乎全部特征应变位于ET的探测范围内。对弦张力的对数估计值为$\bar{\log{Gμ}}=-9.78^{+0.44}_{-0.49}$，与注入值$-10$一致。

Conclusion: 宇宙弦（CS）可通过爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）被探测到。

Abstract: Cosmic strings are not yet confirmed, topological defects formed in the early Universe. They can bend light or gravitational waves, which causes an effect similar to the gravitational lensing. Our goal is to check whether cosmic string could be detected as a lenses of gravitational waves by the Einstein Telescope (ET). To do that the apparatus of wave optics had been applied. Firstly we explored the amplification factor strength and behaviour. Next the wave effects in SNRs and waveforms was examined for different inclinations of the source. Lastly we estimated the string tensions based on eight mergers from the \textsc{StarTrack} simulation, using the Bayesian Inference methods. The wave effects were easily to see in waveforms, SNR and characteristic strains. Also most of the events could be detected, based on their Signal to Noise Ratio values. Almost whole characteristic strain lies in the range of the ET. When it comes to mock observations, we had got estimated vale of a logarithm of the CS tension equal to $\bar{\log{Gμ}}=-9.78^{+0.44}_{-0.49} $, which were consistent with injected value equal to $-10$. At the end we conclude that CSs could be detected by the ET.

</details>

### [5] [Nonlinear collective flow reveals the breakdown of quadrupole--hexadecapole scaling in heavy ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18752)
*Hadi Mehrabpour,Zahra Sheibani,Li Yan,Chunjian Zhang,Abolfazl Mirjalili*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文通过超中心铀-铀碰撞的粘性流体动力学模拟，证明高阶集体流能够分离内禀十六极形变（β₄）的贡献，并揭示非线性QGP动力学如何将高阶几何信息编码到末态观测量中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 内禀十六极形变（β₄）在原子核结构中的作用长期未能确定，需要新的方法将其贡献从核结构观测中分离出来。

Method: 采用事件逐事件（event-by-event）粘性流体动力学模拟，对超中心（ultra-central）238U+238U碰撞（质心系能量√sNN=193 GeV）进行建模，分析高阶集体流对β₄的敏感性。

Result: β₄的符号信息在夸克-胶子等离子体演化后得以保留，并通过非线性流体动力学响应被增强；第四阶流谐波主要依赖线性响应获得拓扑敏感性，而第六阶谐波的敏感性几乎完全源于非线性模式耦合；非线性响应系数ξ6,222能够清晰地分离(β₂,β₄)内禀原子核拓扑。

Conclusion: β₄的符号可作为偏离四极-十六极关联的实验可观测信号，高阶集体流直接探测原子核多极结构，同时揭示了非线性QGP动力学如何将细微的高阶几何信息编码到末态观测量中。

Abstract: Determining the role of intrinsic hexadecapole deformation ($β_4$) in nuclear structure remains a long-standing challenge. Relativistic heavy-ion collisions provide a unique opportunity to address this problem by converting the initial nuclear geometry into the collective motion of the quark--gluon plasma (QGP). Using event-by-event viscous hydrodynamic simulations of ultra-central $^{238}$U+$^{238}$U collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}=193$ GeV, we investigate whether higher-order collective flow can isolate the contribution of $β_4$ and test the $β_2-β_4$ correlation. We demonstrate that information carried by the sign of $β_4$ survives the QGP evolution and is enhanced through nonlinear hydrodynamic response: the fourth-order flow harmonic acquires its topology dependence predominantly from the linear response, whereas the sensitivity of the sixth-order harmonic originates almost entirely from nonlinear mode coupling. As a consequence, the nonlinear response coefficient $ξ_{6,222}$ cleanly separates the $(β_2,β_4)$ intrinsic nuclear topologies. These results establish the sign of $β_4$ as an experimentally accessible signature of deviations from the quadrupole--hexadecapole correlation, demonstrating that higher-order collective flow provides a direct probe of nuclear multipole structure while revealing how nonlinear QGP dynamics encode subtle higher-order geometric information into final-state observables.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mtrl-sci'></div>

# cond-mat.mtrl-sci [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Towards a universal model for spin-orbit coupled Wannier Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18403)
*Alexander C. Tyner*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出G(Wa)NN，首个能够在正交Wannier基（orthogonal Wannier basis）下生成固态体系电子哈密顿量（electronic Hamiltonian）的深度学习模型，并配套推出后处理工具包Tailwater，将预测结果高效转化为宏观量子输运模拟所需的物理可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习模型几乎仅能处理非正交基哈密顿量（non-orthogonal basis Hamiltonians），严重限制了大规模输运模拟的效率；同时缺少将预测结果自动化转化为物理观测量的标准化工具链。

Method: G(Wa)NN模型在包含超过111K个Wannier哈密顿量（超过1.5亿个跳跃矩阵）的多样化数据集上训练，数据集覆盖69种元素；采用优化推理（optimized inference）结合正交哈密顿量的线性标度方法（linear-scaling methods）；支持局部微调（local finetuning）以适应自定义数据集。配套的Tailwater包提供API接口、自动低能子空间投影（类似于Wannier90工作流）以及核多项式方法（Kernel Polynomial Method, KPM）函数，利用正交基实现光谱观测量的严格线性标度计算。

Result: 模型实现了对固态正交Wannier基电子哈密顿量的生成，并解锁了超过10,000个原子的大规模输运模拟。Tailwater工具包提供了从预测哈密顿量到光谱可观测量（spectral observables）的完整自动化转换流程。

Conclusion: G(Wa)NN与Tailwater共同构成的生态系统，旨在弥合深度学习与宏观量子输运模拟之间的差距，为大规模材料模拟提供端到端的深度学习解决方案。

Abstract: While machine learning interatomic potentials (MLiPs) have matured to revolutionize material science, deep learning models for electronic structure are just beginning to emerge and restricted, almost exclusively, to non-orthogonal basis Hamiltonians. We introduce G(Wa)NN, the first deep-learning model capable of generating the electronic Hamiltonian of solid-state systems in an orthogonal Wannier basis. G(Wa)NN is trained on an unprecedented, diverse dataset of more than 111K Wannier Hamiltonians (150M+ hopping matrices) spanning 69 elements. The combination of optimized inference and linear-scaling methods for orthogonal Hamiltonians unlock transport simulations at massive scales (10K+ atoms). Crucially, the framework supports local finetuning, allowing users to adapt the base model to custom Wannier Hamiltonian datasets. To seamlessly translate these predictions into physical observables, we introduce Tailwater, a Python package providing an API interface to G(Wa)NN alongside a high performance post-processing library. Tailwater enables automated projection of the predicted Hamiltonian into an arbitrary low-energy subspace-directly mirroring familiar Wannier90 workflows-and includes a suite of Kernel Polynomial Method (KPM) functions that exploit the orthogonal basis to achieve strict linear scaling for spectral observables. The Tailwater ecosystem, with the G(Wa)NN model at its core, aims to help bridge the gap between deep learning and macro-scale quantum transport simulations.

</details>

Abstract: The characterization of electron transfer through the emitting surface is of crucial importance for optimizing existing and developing new photocathodes. Here we propose and develop a method for the direct determination of the electron escape probability in high-efficiency semiconductor photocathodes. The proposed method is based on the variations in the surface photovoltage upon the injection of emitted photoelectrons back into a photocathode (``reverse injection"), which is induced by the polarity reversal of the external electric field. We demonstrate the method on \textit{p}-GaN(Cs,O) photocathodes with negative effective electron affinity by measuring the evolution of photoemission quantum efficiency upon the reverse injection of emitted electrons.

Abstract: We investigate the recombination dynamics of localized defect emission in monolayer WSe$_2$ using time-resolved photoluminescence over the temperature range from 4 to 120 K. The defect emission comprises a dominant sub-nanosecond exponential component and two weak, long-lived power-law channels extending from a few nanoseconds to several hundred nanoseconds. The power-law relaxation admits an interpretation in terms of continuous distributions of recombination lifetimes associated with an inhomogeneous ensemble of localized states. Temperature-dependent measurements were performed to examine the thermal detrapping mechanisms governing these long-lived channels. Spin-resolved electronic-structure and optical-transition calculations provide microscopic insight into the localized states and the available recombination pathways. ### [9] [Vacancy Diffusion Across FeCrAl Alloy Composition Space for Accident-Tolerant Fuel Cladding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18472)
*Mihai Pitigoi,Peter Hatton*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文采用物种分辨的动力学蒙特卡罗（KMC）模型，结合基于Hop-Decorate工作流生成的迁移势垒数据库训练的线性替代模型，系统研究了FeCrAl合金中空位扩散的微观机制。研究发现，合金中Cr含量的增加会逐步降低空位的整体扩散率，尽管活化能保持相对稳定；而富Cr的α'相则表现出显著升高的活化能和缓慢的扩散速度，揭示了成分对辐照条件下微观结构演化的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FeCrAl合金是轻水反应堆事故容错燃料包壳的领先候选材料，其高温抗氧化性能优异，但在反应堆内服役寿命受辐照诱导微观结构演化（radiation-induced microstructural evolution）控制，其中点缺陷输运（point defect transport）是主导机制，然而目前对此认识不足。

Method: 采用物种分辨的动力学蒙特卡罗（kinetic Monte Carlo, KMC）模型模拟FeCrAl中的空位扩散，模型参数化基于线性替代模型（linear surrogate models），替代模型在通过Hop-Decorate工作流生成的迁移势垒（migration barriers）数据库上训练得到。通过采样覆盖Fe-Cr-Al体系中富Fe到富Cr范围的成分，绘制局部化学环境如何控制空位跳跃及宏观扩散率。

Result: 增加Cr含量会逐步降低空位的全局扩散率，即便活化能保持相对恒定；富Fe成分中空位扩散更快，增加了与快速移动间隙原子的湮灭事件，可能减少辐照诱导缺陷并提高辐照耐受性；富Cr的α'相则表现出明显升高的活化能和显著降低的扩散速度，在事故相关温度下扩散率低至数个数量级。

Conclusion: 合金成分强烈调控空位扩散行为：富Fe成分有利于空位快速扩散和缺陷湮灭，从而提升辐照耐受性；而富Cr的α'相中空位迁移率受抑制，这一机制可能与辐照条件下该相的形成有关，对理解FeCrAl合金在堆内服役行为具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: Iron-chromium-aluminium (FeCrAl) alloys are leading candidates for accident-tolerant fuel cladding in light-water reactors, where their superior high-temperature oxidation resistance promises to extend coping times during loss-of-coolant accidents. The in-reactor lifetime of cladding is ultimately governed by radiation-induced microstructural evolution of which point defect transport is the dominant mechanism, however, this remains poorly understood. Here, we use a species-resolved kinetic Monte Carlo (KMC) model for vacancy diffusion in FeCrAl, parameterised by linear surrogate models trained on a database of migration barriers generated through the Hop-Decorate workflow. By sampling compositions spanning the Fe-rich to Cr-rich range of the Fe-Cr-Al system, we map how the local chemical environment controls vacancy hopping and hence macroscopic diffusivity. We find that increasing the Cr content in the alloy progressively decreases global diffusivity of vacancies even though activation energies stay relatively constant. This implies that the higher the Fe content in the alloy, the faster vacancies diffuse, thereby increasing annihilation events with fast-moving interstitials, potentially reducing irradiation induced defects and increasing radiation tolerance. Conversely, we find that Cr-rich alloy compositions stand out with a markedly elevated activation energy and significantly slower diffusion, orders of magnitude lower at accident-relevant temperatures. This indicates suppressed vacancy mobility in Cr-rich $α'$ phases which are known to form under irradiation.

### [10] [Data-Efficient Training of Linear ACE Potentials through Leverage-Guided Subset Selection of ASSYST Structure Pools](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18524)
*Aynour Khosravi,Marvin Poul,Jörg Neugebauer,Chad Sinclair*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习原子间势函数（MLIPs）的构建常受限于生成大规模DFT训练数据集的高昂成本。对于像ASSYST这类系统生成的结构池，一个核心实际问题是最少需要标注多少构型才能达到可靠的精度。

Method: 采用统计杠杆分数（statistical leverage scores）和CUR型采样（CUR-type sampling）进行基于几何的无标签子集选择，并将其与随机、基于能量和基于力的基线方法在受控迭代协议下进行比较。以元素Al作为主要基准，Cu和Al-Cu合金用于迁移验证。

Conclusion: 描述符空间引导的无标签子采样（descriptor-space-guided, label-free subsampling）能够显著降低基于ASSYST结构池训练的线性ACE模型的DFT计算负担，同时不损害缺陷水平的保真度。

Abstract: The construction of machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs) is often limited by the cost of generating large density-functional-theory (DFT) training datasets. For systematically generated structure pools such as ASSYST, a central practical question is how many configurations must be labeled to achieve reliable accuracy. Here we assess geometry-based, label-free subset selection for training linear Atomic Cluster Expansion (ACE) potentials. Using statistical leverage scores and CUR-type sampling, we compare leverage-guided selection against random, energy-based, and force-based baselines under controlled iterative protocols. Elemental Al provides the primary benchmark, with Cu and Al-Cu alloys used for transfer validation. Leverage-guided subsets recover plateau-level energy and force accuracy using substantially smaller labeled fractions (approximately 30-40%) than random sampling, corresponding to an effective 2-3x reduction in DFT labeling for the systems studied. In alloy tests, defect energetics remain comparable across strategies once sufficient chemical diversity is included, while leverage selection maintains competitive accuracy at reduced training size.
  These results demonstrate that descriptor-space-guided, label-free subsampling can significantly reduce DFT workload for linear ACE models trained on ASSYST structure pools without degrading defect-level fidelity.

### [11] [Battery Material Comparisons Should Refocus on Diffusivity with Best Practices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18590)
*CJ Sturgill,Roya Rajabi,Md Abdullah Al Muhit,Hans-Conrad zur Loye,Morgan Stefik*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文呼吁电池材料研究中重新关注扩散率（diffusivity）的比较，指出当前半数相关论文虽使用扩散率值支撑结构-性能输运关系，但仅少数明确说明了研磨后测量长度尺度的做法。通过分析303篇开放获取论文、比较多种测量方法及TiNb2O7和Ti2Nb10O29的实例，作者强调遵循“研磨后测量”的最佳实践对建立有意义的构效关系至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 改进电池性能需要发现具有更优输运性质的材料，而离子扩散率（ionic diffusivity）作为关键材料属性，其测量高度依赖活性材料长度尺度的准确评估（通常依据质量比表面积）。然而，当前文献中扩散率的比较和测量方法存在不一致性，可能误导结构-性能关系的推断。

Method: 作者对303篇近期关于电池材料开发的开放获取（open-access）出版物进行了程序性综述，统计了其中使用扩散率值支持结构-性能输运主张的比例，以及明确说明长度尺度测量步骤的比例。同时，比较了扫描电子显微镜（SEM）、比表面积分析（BET）和小角X射线散射（SAXS）等多种测量方法及其导致的表观扩散率差异，并以溶胶-凝胶（sol-gel, SOL）和固态（solid state, SS）法制备的TiNb2O7（TNO1）和Ti2Nb10O29（TNO2）为实例进行定量对比。

Result: 综述发现：49%的出版物使用扩散率值支持输运主张；其中仅15%明确说明了长度尺度是在研磨后测量或声明未使用研磨。在实例中，SOL样品的长度尺度更小且扩散系数更低，但恒电流（galvanostatic）测试显示其较短的长度尺度足以补偿较低的扩散率，从而获得更好的高倍率容量保持率。

Conclusion: 电池材料开发需要重新聚焦于扩散率等属性测量，遵循“研磨后测量”（grind-measure）的最佳实践而非相反顺序，才能从测量中得出有意义的构效关系（structure-property relationships）见解。

Abstract: The continuous demand for improved batteries motivates the discovery and advancement of materials with improved transport. Ionic diffusivity is the relevant material property where its measurement depends on accurate assessment of the active material length-scale, generally from the mass-specific surface area. In this perspective, we argue for renewed focus on diffusivity comparisons. A procedural review of 303 recent open-access publications about battery material development revealed two aspects: (1) 49% of publications support structure-property transport claims using diffusivity values and (2) of those reporting diffusivity values, 15% clearly stated that the length scale was measured after grinding-alone or stated that grinding was not used at all. Diffusivity assessment rationally requires length scale measurement after grinding (grind-measure), rather than the reverse. A range of measurement methods are compared, including SEM, BET, and SAXS as well as the resulting apparent diffusivities. Common errors and pitfalls of each of these approaches are described. As an example, datasets are presented for TiNb2O7 (TNO1) and Ti2Nb10O29 (TNO2) made from sol-gel (SOL) and solid state (SS) techniques using rigorous quantitative measurements to separately compare material diffusivities and galvanostatic performance. Here, the SOL samples had shorter length-scales and lower diffusion coefficients. Galvanostatic cell measurements, however, revealed that the shorter length-scales more than compensated for the lower diffusivities with better overall high-rate capacity retention. This example shows how cell level metrics often differ from underlying diffusivities. We argue that materials development needs renewed focus on property measurements like diffusivity where best-practices are important to derive meaningful insights towards structure-property relationships.

</details>

### [13] [Data-driven Design of Metal-Organic Frameworks with Tunable Negative Thermal Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18594)
*Prathami Divakar Kamath,Francesco Tavani,Alin Marin Elena,Théo Jaffrelot Inizan,Yen-hsu Lin,Jian Yin,Wenqian Xu,Omar M. Yaghi,Kristin A. Persson*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 负热膨胀（negative thermal expansion, NTE）材料在需要精确控制热膨胀的应用中至关重要。金属有机框架（metal-organic frameworks, MOFs）因其优异的化学可调性、灵活的结构和低能晶格振动，成为探索NTE的丰富平台。然而，在庞大的MOF设计空间中识别控制NTE的结构基序（structural motifs）在实验上极具挑战，而大规模的第一性原理（first-principles）声子计算在计算上不可行。

Method: 采用基于MACE-MP-MOF0（一种针对MOF微调、具有近第一性原理精度的机器学习原子间势能）的高通量工作流，构建了PhononMOFdb数据库，该数据库包含超过12,000种MOF的声子（phonons）、非弹性中子散射光谱、体模量（bulk moduli）和热容（heat capacities）。随后通过高通量筛选分析影响NTE的因素，并利用高分辨率温度依赖性同步辐射粉末X射线衍射对Ce-UiO-66及其溴化变体进行实验验证。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种数据驱动的MOF中NTE工程策略，展示了机器学习加速发现与针对性实验验证相结合如何解锁预测性材料设计（predictive materials design）。

Abstract: Materials with negative thermal expansion (NTE) are essential for applications requiring precise control of thermal expansion. Owing to their exceptional chemical tunability, flexible architectures, and low-energy lattice vibrations, metal-organic frameworks (MOFs) represent a rich platform for exploring NTE. However, uncovering the structural motifs that govern NTE across the enormous MOF design space remains experimentally challenging, and large-scale first-principles phonon calculations are computationally prohibitive. Here, we comprehensively evaluate the factors influencing NTE in MOFs by utilizing a high-throughput workflow based on MACE-MP-MOF0, a machine learning interatomic potential fine-tuned for MOFs with near-ab initio accuracy, to construct PhononMOFdb, a database of phonons, inelastic neutron scattering spectra, bulk moduli, and heat capacities for over 12,000 MOFs. High-throughput screening of this database reveals that highly porous cubic topology frameworks with heavier, lower-valent metal nodes favor strong NTE, while linker functionalization provides a practical handle for tuning NTE magnitude and sign without compromising mechanical stability. Experimental validation via high-resolution temperature-dependent synchrotron powder X-ray diffraction on the Ce-UiO-66 MOF and its brominated variants confirms the design recipe and yields volumetric NTE coefficients surpassing current records. ### [14] [Alchemical thermodynamic integration for ab initio free-energy calculations in solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18750)
*Liangrui Wei,Feng Zhang,Renata M. Wentzcovitch,Kai-Ming Ho,Yang Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种炼金术热力学积分（alchemical thermodynamic integration）方案，在蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）和分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟中动态耦合从头算（ab initio）力计算器。该方案在高压Fe-Ni和常温Li-Na液体溶液中得到了验证，能够高效计算第一性原理（first-principles）自由能，并复现了Li-Na实验观察到的混溶间隙（miscibility gap），其计算效率与标准从头算分子动力学相当。

Method: 提出了一种炼金术热力学积分方案，在蒙特卡罗和分子动力学模拟过程中动态（on the fly）耦合从头算力计算器，实现第一性原理自由能的直接计算。

Result: 在高压Fe-Ni和常温Li-Na液体溶液体系中对方案进行了验证，结果与先前计算吻合，并成功复现了Li-Na体系实验观察到的混溶间隙。代码效率与标准从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics）相当。

Conclusion: 该方案被确立为一种实用的炼金术积分（alchemical-integration）框架，可用于溶液体系的第一性原理自由能计算。

Abstract: We develop an alchemical thermodynamic integration scheme that couples ab initio force calculators on the fly during Monte Carlo and molecular dynamics simulations. The implementation is validated against existing hybrid-Hamiltonian approaches. The scheme yields ab initio free energies of high-pressure Fe-Ni and ambient Li-Na liquid solutions that agree with previous calculations and reproduce the experimentally observed Li-Na miscibility gap. The code has an efficiency comparable to standard ab initio molecular dynamics. These results establish this scheme as a practical alchemical-integration framework for first-principles free-energy calculations in solutions.

### [15] [Phase equilibria in MnSb2Te4-GeSb2Te4 system and magnetic properties of Mn1-xGexSb2Te4 solid solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18925)
*Fuad Safarov,Dunya Babanly,Jerome Robert,Elnur Orujlu,Elvin Ahmadov,Martin Bowen,Bohdan Kundys*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了反铁磁拓扑绝缘体（antiferromagnetic topological insulator）MnSb₂Te₄中Mn位被Ge替代形成的Mn₁₋ₓGeₓSb₂Te₄固溶体，发现全组分范围内均可形成均匀单相样品，Ge替代增强了顺磁性但降低了有效磁矩和饱和磁化强度，并揭示了两种不同的磁转变以及负磁化与自旋翻转（spin-flop）转变等复杂磁行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MnSb₂Te₄作为反铁磁拓扑绝缘体MnBi₂Te₄的姊妹化合物，是探索磁性拓扑相（magnetic topological phases）的候选材料；而结构类似的非磁性相变材料GeSb₂Te₄也表现出非平庸的能带拓扑（nontrivial band topology）。基于两者相同的晶体结构、Mn²⁺与Ge²⁺相近的离子半径，以及探究磁性与拓扑之间相互作用的动机，本文研究了Ge替代MnSb₂Te₄中Mn位的影响。

Method: 采用高温固相反应（high-temperature solid-state reaction）合成Mn₁₋ₓGeₓSb₂Te₄固溶体，并利用SEM-EDS、PXRD、DTA和SQUID等手段对样品的组成、结构、相行为和磁性进行表征。

Result: Ge在MnSb₂Te₄的全组分范围内均可实现成功替代，形成均匀单相样品，且熔点表现为包晶反应（peritectic reaction）。Ge替代增强了样品的顺磁性，但直到x=0.75仍保持亚铁磁有序（ferrimagnetic ordering），有效磁矩和饱和磁化强度随Ge含量增加而降低。观察到两种不同的磁转变——高温顺磁到亚铁磁转变和低温亚铁磁到铁磁转变——其中低温磁转变对Ge替代呈现穹顶状（dome-like）依赖关系。纯MnSb₂Te₄和x=0.12样品出现负磁化现象（negative magnetization），而x=0.32和x=0.55样品中出现两个明显的自旋翻转（spin-flop）转变，归因于竞争性磁有序。

Conclusion: 这些发现有助于未来选择性生长均匀磁性相的单晶，为磁输运（magneto-transport）和拓扑表面态（topological surface states）研究铺平道路。

Abstract: As a sister compound of the antiferromagnetic topological insulator MnBi2Te4, MnSb2Te4 is also a candidate for exotic magnetic topological phases. On the other hand, the structurally analogous but nonmagnetic phase-change material GeSb2Te4 is also known to exhibit nontrivial band topology. Motivated by their shared crystal structure, the similar ionic radii of Mn2+ and Ge2+, and the opportunity to explore the interplay between magnetism and topology, here we investigate the effects of Ge substitution at Mn sites in MnSb2Te4. The Mn1-xGexSb2Te4 solid solutions were synthesized via high-temperature solid-state reaction and characterized for composition, structure, phase behavior, and magnetism using SEM-EDS, PXRD, DTA, and SQUID. Ge substitution was successful across the full composition range, producing homogeneous, single-phase samples that melt via peritectic reactions, as confirmed by the MnSb2Te4GeS-b2Te4 phase diagram. Ge substitution strengthens the sample's paramagnetism, but with ferrimagnetic ordering up to x = 0.75, with both effective moment and saturation magnetization decreasing with increasing Ge content. Two distinct magnetic transitions - high-temperature paramagnetic to ferrimagnetic and low-temperature ferrimagnetic to ferromagnetic - were identified, with a dome-like shape dependence of the low-temperature magnetic transition on Ge substitution. A negative magnetization was observed in the pristine MnSb2Te4 and x = 0.12 substituted samples, while two distinct spin-flop transitions appeared in the samples with x = 0.32 and x = 0.55 Ge substitutions as a result of competing magnetic orderings. These findings facilitate future selective single-crystal growth of homogeneous, magnetic phases, paving the way for magneto-transport and topological surface states investigations.

### [16] [Stereochemical Vacuum Gap Explains Out-of-Plane Thermal Insulation in MXenes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18963)
*O. Mateos-Lopez,J. G. Vilhena,Isaac Armstrong,Hendrik Heinz,Miguel Muñoz Rojo,Juan Carlos Cuevas*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示MXene材料中异质表面终止基团（heterogeneous surface terminations）是导致其面外热导率实验与模拟结果巨大差异的根本原因。通过非平衡分子动力学模拟，发现不同尺寸的表面终止基团共存时会产生立体化学诱导的真空间隙，显著抑制面外热传导，使模拟值与实验定量吻合，并提出基于化学调控热传输的工程路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维MXene材料在热管理和光谱隐身（spectral camouflage）领域具有巨大潜力，但实验测量的面外热导率（0.14–0.8 W/mK）存在近一个数量级的波动，且模拟结果系统性地高估了热导率。这一差距表明当前对MXene中热传输机制的理解存在根本性空白。

Method: 采用非平衡分子动力学模拟（Non-Equilibrium Molecular Dynamics, NEMD），以Ti₃C₂Tₓ为模型体系，系统研究了不同表面终止基团组合对面外热导率的影响。

Result: 表面终止基团的异质性会导致相邻层间形成立体化学诱导的真空间隙（stereochemically induced vacuum gap），即使轻微偏离均一终止也会大幅抑制面外热导率，使模拟值与实验值定量一致。热导率与原子密度强相关，引入大体积表面终止基团（包括残余水分子）可将热导率降至0.3 W/mK，比均一终止情况低一个数量级，并低于无序固体（disordered solids）预测的最小热导率极限。

Conclusion: 异质表面终止基团是MXene面外热导率异常行为的关键因素，为通过化学手段（chemistry-driven route）定向调控MXene中的热传输性能提供了理论基础和工程路径。

Abstract: Two-dimensional MXenes are promising materials for thermal management and spectral camouflage, combining low out-of-plane thermal conductivity with low infrared emissivity and mechanical robustness. Yet the near-order-of-magnitude spread in experimental out-of-plane thermal conductivity measurements (0.14-0.8 W/mK) and the systematic overestimation by simulations point to a fundamental gap in our understanding of heat transport in these materials. Here, we argue these differences originate in the overlooked role of heterogeneous surface terminations. Using Non-Equilibrium Molecular Dynamics simulations of Ti3C2Tx, we show that this discrepancy arises from a stereochemically induced vacuum gap between adjacent layers, formed when surface terminations of different sizes coexist. Even minor deviations from homogeneous terminations drastically suppress out-of-plane thermal conductivity, bringing simulated values into quantitative agreement with experiment. We also show that thermal conductivity scales strongly with the atomic density, and that introducing bulky surface terminations, including residual water, reduces the thermal conductivity to 0.3 W/mK, an order of magnitude below homogeneous termination values and below the minimum thermal conductivity limit predicted for disordered solids. Thus, we propose a chemistry-driven route to engineer thermal transport in MXenes.

### [17] [Sixteen-State Energy Mapping for First-Principles Four-Spin Ring Exchange: Validation on $La_2CuO_4$ and $SrFeO_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18986)
*Xavier Rocquefelte,Peter Blaha*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过将四态方法推广至十六态方案，首次实现了对自旋环型交换耦合（$J_{ring}$）的直接第一性原理提取，并揭示了双线性交换（$J$）本身受环交换重整化的机制，在T-La$_2$CuO$_4$和SrFeO$_2$中验证了该方法的有效性与局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环型交换（ring exchange）$J_{ring}$是铜酸盐及其他正方晶格磁体海森堡自旋哈密顿量中的关键组分，但一直缺乏类似于四态方法（four-state method）对双线性交换（bilinear exchange）$J$ 那样的直接局域第一性原理提取方案。

Method: 将四态方法推广至十六态方案（sixteen-state scheme, $2^4$）；利用对称性将16个组态约化为6或8个不等价能量以降低计算成本；引入参考态（reference bath）分析环交换对四态耦合的重整化效应。

Result: 对T-La$_2$CuO$_4$，三条独立路径得出的$J_{ring}$一致至0.2%，$J_{ring}/J_1 = 0.25$；未指明参考态的四态$J_1$在此材料中误差达12%。十六态提取本身依赖于参考态，Néel态和铁磁（ferromagnetic）参考态给出的值分别框定了映射值（mapping value）的上下界。对SrFeO$_2$（$S=2$），$J_{ring}/J = 0.006$，证实plaquette结构对环交换是必要但远非充分的条件。

Conclusion: 四态磁耦合$J$本身受到环交换的$\pm 2 J_{ring} S^2$重整化，符号取决于参考态；十六态方案可直接提取$J_{ring}$；超出对加环模型（pair-plus-ring model）的四阶特征表明存在更高阶自旋环耦合（six- and eight-spin loop couplings）；完整工作流已集成于开源Mag4软件包中。

Abstract: Four-spin ring (cyclic) exchange $J_{ring}$ is an essential ingredient of the Heisenberg spin Hamiltonian of cuprates and other square-lattice magnets, yet it has lacked the kind of direct, local first-principles extraction that the four-state method provides for bilinear exchange, $J$. We supply it by generalizing that method to a sixteen-state ($2^4$) scheme. Symmetry reduces the sixteen configurations to six or eight inequivalent energies, so the cost is modest. The derivation also shows that the conventional four-state magnetic coupling, $J$, is itself ring-renormalized, by $\pm 2 J_{ring} S^2$ with the sign set by the reference state. T-La$_2$CuO$_4$ confirms this quantitatively: three independent routes agree on $J_{ring}$ to $0.2\%$, giving $J_{ring}/J_1 = 0.25$, and a four-state $J_1$ quoted without naming its reference is wrong by $12\%$ in this material. The direct sixteen-state extraction itself proves reference-dependent, the Néel and ferromagnetic baths bracketing the mapping value: a fourth-order fingerprint of interactions beyond the pair-plus-ring model, which additional reference baths resolve into a bare $J_{ring}$ and a converging tower of six- and eight-spin loop couplings. SrFeO$_2$ ($S = 2$), with the same plaquette yet $J_{ring}/J = 0.006$, provides the negative control: a plaquette is necessary for ring exchange, far from sufficient. The complete workflow, including the band-gap and local-moment diagnostics that certify any such extraction, is implemented in the openly available Mag4 package, so that $J_{ring}$ costs no more effort to obtain than $J$.

Result: 识别出两种不同的发射驱动机制：压电贡献（piezoelectric contribution）以及第二种显然具有普适性的机制——应力诱导点缺陷位点的结构重组（stress-induced structural reorganization）。晶体维度、应力类型和点缺陷三者共同决定了材料的发光行为。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个力致发光材料的设计框架，其核心原则是刻意匹配晶体维度、应力类型与应力敏感的点缺陷，以调控发射行为并优化整体性能。

Abstract: Mechanoluminescent materials exhibit a broad spectrum of controllable light-emission responses to mechanical stimuli of varying types and magnitudes. Yet progress toward high-performance systems remains constrained by an incomplete and often contradictory mechanistic understanding. Here, density functional theory (DFT) calculations optimized for the quantitative treatment of point defects are used to systematically investigate the interplay between stress type (hydrostatic vs. shear) and active-phase dimensionality (1D vs. 3D), using $SrAl_2O_4:Eu^{2+}, Dy^{3+}$ and $Ba_4Si_6O_{16}:Eu^{2+}, Ho^{3+}$ as representative model systems. Two distinct emission-driving mechanisms are identified: a piezoelectric contribution, and a second, apparently universal, mechanism arising from stress-induced structural reorganization at point defects sites. These results establish a design framework for mechanoluminescent materials in which crystal dimensionality, stress type and stress-sensitive point defects are deliberately matched to tune emission behavior and overall performance.

Abstract: The ability to tune charge density waves (CDWs) through external control knobs, such as doping, pressure or strain is crucial for exploring the phase diagram of two dimensional (2D) or quasi-2D materials. ### [20] [Thermal and electrical conductivity of a refractory high-entropy alloy after high-pressure torsion: Electron versus phonon contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19123)
*Jacqueline Hidalgo-Jimenez,Payam Edalati,Md Amirul Islam,Makoto Arita,Bidyut Baran Saha,Kaveh Edalati*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过高压扭转（high-pressure torsion, HPT）对等原子比难熔高熵合金TiZrHfNbTa进行纳米结构化和缺陷工程处理，研究了其对热导率和电导率的影响。结果表明，热导率和电导率随应变呈现不同的演化趋势，电子贡献主导热输运，而声子贡献仅占11–23%。热导率与电导率的对比演化归因于低应变下位错主导振动向高应变下晶界主导振动的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究纳米结构化（nanostructuring）和缺陷工程（defect engineering）对等原子比难熔高熵合金TiZrHfNbTa的热输运和电输运性质的影响机制。

Method: 采用高压扭转（high-pressure torsion, HPT）对TiZrHfNbTa进行严重塑性变形（severe plastic deformation, SPD），诱导位错累积、晶粒细化至纳米级（平均40 nm）以及BCC相向omega相的部分转变。利用Wiedemann-Franz定律分析电子与声子对热输运的贡献。

Result: 硬度随加工达到稳态；比热容呈现非单调行为，低应变下因位错抑制低频振动模式而下降，高应变下因新形成的大角晶界处的非谐振动而部分恢复；热导率低应变下降后高应变略有恢复，而电导率单调下降至稳态无恢复。电子贡献主导热输运，声子贡献仅占11–23%。

Conclusion: 热导率与电导率的对比演化归因于低应变下位错主导振动向高应变下晶界主导振动的转变，这一转变对声子和电子的散射效率不同，导致二者的输运行为出现差异。

Abstract: The equiatomic refractory high-entropy alloy TiZrHfNbTa was processed by high-pressure torsion (HPT) to investigate the effect of nanostructuring and defect engineering on thermal and electrical transport properties. Severe plastic deformation (SPD) via the HPT treatment induces substantial accumulation of dislocations, grain refinement to the nanometer level (average: 40 nm), and partial transformation from the BCC phase to the omega phase. While hardness increases to a steady state with processing, the specific heat capacity exhibits a non-monotonic behavior: it decreases at low strains due to the suppression of low-frequency vibrational modes by dislocations, then partially recovers at high strains due to anharmonic vibrations at newly formed high-angle grain boundaries. Thermal conductivity decreases at low strains but shows a slight recovery at high strains, whereas electrical conductivity decreases monotonically to a steady state without recovery. Analysis using the Wiedemann-Franz law reveals that the electronic contribution dominates thermal transport, while the phononic contribution (limited by the scattering of phonons on defects) is only 11 to 23%, depending on the degree of straining. The contrasting evolution of thermal and electrical conductivity is ascribed to the transition from dislocation-dominated vibrations at low strains to grain boundary-dominated vibrations at high strains, which affects phonons and electrons with different efficiencies.

### [21] [ATLAS: A Foundation Neural Sampler for Amorphous Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19198)
*Mouyang Cheng,Denis Blessing,Botao Yu,Gerhard Neumann,Mingda Li,Carles Domingo-Enrich,Yuanqi Du*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出ATLAS，一种基于扩散过程（diffusion process）的生成模型，利用等变图神经网络（equivariant graph neural network）直接从目标能量函数生成服从玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）的非晶结构。ATLAS能跨系统尺寸、温度和组分泛化，在Kob-Andersen系统、Cu-Zr和Cr-Co-Ni金属玻璃中，以极低的能量评估次数实现了高精度结构分布、自由能和熵的估计，并通过大型语言模型（LLM）代理高效探索多元素高熵金属玻璃的设计优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶材料（amorphous materials）具有优异的力学和功能特性，但其崎岖的能量景观（energy landscape）极难采样。在玻璃化转变温度（glass-transition temperature）以下，传统分子动力学（molecular dynamics）和蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）方法因依赖稀有势垒穿越事件而效率低下，而数据驱动的生成模型又受限于稀缺且有偏差的参考系综。因此，需要一种能够高效、准确采样非晶结构的新方法。

Method: ATLAS学习一个扩散过程（diffusion process），直接从目标能量函数生成玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）的非晶结构；模型通过等变图神经网络（equivariant graph neural network, EGNN）参数化，能够跨系统尺寸、温度和组分泛化；利用扩散过程的时间反转（time reversal）进行热力学量的高效估计并引导结构朝向目标可观测量（observable）生成。

Result: 在二维Kob-Andersen系统中，ATLAS复现了并行回火马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（parallel tempering Markov chain Monte Carlo）的结构分布、自由能和熵，在低温玻璃区域自由能误差低于0.2%，且能量评估次数减少超过500倍。在Cu-Zr和Cr-Co-Ni金属玻璃中，ATLAS恢复了实验观测到的短程有序（short-range-order）趋势，并引导结构朝向指定序参数（order parameter）和优化体模量（bulk modulus）。组分分摊预训练（composition-amortized pretraining）相比从头训练的组分特定模型，效率提升数百倍，并支持使用昂贵的通用机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potential）进行采样。结合大语言模型（large language model, LLM）代理，ATLAS在8元空间中搜索高熵金属玻璃（high-entropy metallic glass），在480次评价内收敛到Pareto前沿。

Conclusion: ATLAS被确立为非晶材料采样、引导和设计的基座模型（foundation model），在采样效率、精度和泛化能力上显著优于传统方法，并能有效整合外部设计工具实现多目标优化。

Abstract: Amorphous materials exhibit exceptional mechanical and functional properties, yet their rugged energy landscapes are notoriously difficult to sample. Below the glass-transition temperature, conventional molecular dynamics and Monte Carlo become inefficient because equilibration relies on rare barrier-crossing events, while data-driven generative models are constrained by scarce and biased reference ensembles. Here, we introduce ATLAS, an efficient sampler that learns a diffusion process to generate Boltzmann-distributed amorphous structures directly from a target energy function. Parameterized by an equivariant graph neural network, ATLAS generalizes across system size, temperature, and composition. By exploiting the time reversal of the diffusion process, it enables efficient estimation of thermodynamic quantities and steering toward target observables. In two-dimensional Kob-Andersen systems, ATLAS reproduces parallel tempering Markov chain Monte Carlo structural distributions, free energies and entropies, achieving below 0.2% free energy error in the low-temperature glass regime with over 500-fold fewer energy evaluations. In Cu-Zr and Cr-Co-Ni metallic glasses, ATLAS recovers experimentally observed short-range-order trends and steers structures toward prescribed order parameters and optimized bulk moduli. Moreover, composition-amortized pretraining outperforms composition-specific training from scratch, reduces inverse-design costs by several hundred-fold, and enables sampling with expensive universal machine learning interatomic potentials. Coupled to a large language model agent, ATLAS searches an eight-element space for high-entropy metallic glasses balancing stiffness and ductility, identifying a converged Pareto frontier within 480 oracle evaluations. Together, these results establish ATLAS as a foundation model for sampling, steering and designing amorphous materials.

</details>


### [22] [Spatially resolved in-situ characterisation of competing martensitic transformation pathways during nanoscratch in 316H Stainless Steel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19239)
*A. Kareer,R. W. Kerr,D. Craven,A. V. Davydok,C. Krywka,D. M. Collins*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文结合原位同步辐射X射线纳米衍射（in-situ synchrotron X-ray nanodiffractometry）与纳米划痕实验（nanoscratch testing），解析了316H不锈钢在单滑移接触下摩擦层（tribolayer）中马氏体相变（martensitic transformation）的压力驱动路径选择机制，揭示了从γ→ε→α'的序列相变路径，并为理解不同硬面合金的耐磨损性能差异提供了微观机制解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 摩擦接触（frictional contact）会在表面下方形成微观结构与性质异于基体的摩擦层（tribolayer）。在奥氏体不锈钢中，该摩擦层通过两种竞争性马氏体相变路径形成，但这两条路径的微观机制尚不明确，特别是压力对相变路径选择的调控作用缺乏直接实验证据。

Method: 采用原位同步辐射X射线纳米衍射（in-situ synchrotron X-ray nanodiffractometry）与纳米划痕测试（nanoscratch testing）相结合的方法，获取单个滑移接触下（single sliding asperity）的应变场空间分布图。同时，利用有限元建模（finite element modelling）解释马氏体相的分布结果。

Result: 发现压力驱动的路径选择机制：接触前方的静水压缩（hydrostatic compression）抑制α'形成，促进γ→ε转变；侧向滑移解除约束后引入剪切应变（shear strain），驱动ε→α'转变，形成序列路径γ→ε→α'。在持续静水约束的区域中ε-马氏体被保留；在材料堆积且无约束的表面上方，相变直接进行至α'。α'-马氏体相邻的γ-奥氏体中位错密度升高，表明α'形成由周围基体的塑性变形（plastic deformation）所容纳。

Conclusion: 该路径选择机制可解释铁基与钴基硬面合金（hardfacing alloys）的抗磨损性能差异：形成ε-马氏体的钴基合金具有更优的耐磨损性。所提出的方法能够解析宏观、多接触（multiple asperity contacts）静态测量无法获得的瞬态微观结构状态，为更广泛的摩擦学现象提供了通往机制性洞察的途径。

Abstract: Localised surface deformation beneath frictional contacts generates a tribolayer whose microstructure and properties differ from the bulk. In austenitic stainless steels, this tribolayer forms through two competing martensitic transformation pathways. Here, these pathways are isolated in 316H stainless steel using in-situ synchrotron X-ray nanodiffractometry combined with nanoscratch testing, which together yield spatial maps of the evolving strain field beneath a single sliding asperity. Finite element modelling interprets the resulting distribution of martensitic phases, revealing a pressure driven pathway selection where hydrostatic compression ahead of the contact suppresses $α'$ formation and favours the $γ\rightarrow \varepsilon$ transformation, while lateral sliding relieves this constraint and introduces a shear strain driving $\varepsilon \rightarrow α'$ , producing an overall sequential $γ\rightarrow \varepsilon \rightarrow α'$ pathway in the tribolayer. Where hydrostatic constraint persists, $\varepsilon$-martensite is retained; where material piles up and is unconstrained above the surface, the transformation proceeds directly to $α'$. The $γ$-austenite adjacent to $α'$- martensite shows elevated dislocation density, indicating that $α'$ formation is accommodated by plastic deformation in the surrounding matrix. This distinction could explain differences in galling performance among iron-based and cobalt-based hardfacing alloys, where the $\varepsilon$-martensite forming cobalt alloys offer superior galling resistance. The methodology presented resolves transient microstructural states inaccessible to static measurements of macroscale, multiple asperity contacts, establishing a route to mechanistic insight across tribological phenomena more broadly.

</details>


### [23] [Time-resolved ARPES in pumped excitonic systems: Floquet physics induced by excitonic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19242)
*Amir Eskandari-asl,Adolfo Avella*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于动力学投影算子方法（DPOA）构建理论框架，研究泵浦激子体系的时间分辨角分辨光电子能谱（TR-ARPES），在哈特里-福克（HF）层次包含库仑电子-电子相互作用，捕捉了泵浦脉冲下激子束缚态的形成，并识别出激子场诱导的Floquet边带与能带共振诱导的边带两种非平衡特征。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展一套能够描述泵浦激子系统非平衡动力学的理论框架，用于解释和预测时间分辨角分辨光电子能谱（TR-ARPES）中的Floquet边带现象，并验证动力学投影算子方法（DPOA）在处理强关联电子系统超快过程方面的有效性。

Method: 基于动力学投影算子方法（DPOA）建立理论框架，在哈特里-福克（HF）层次处理库仑电子-电子相互作用，以二维两带半导体为原型体系，分别分析平衡相图和非平衡条件下的TR-ARPES信号特征。

Result: 平衡态下观察到从半导体相到激子绝缘体相的转变；非平衡态下，当泵浦频率与激子模式共振时，激子序参量持续相干振荡并在TR-ARPES谱中产生清晰的Floquet边带，该边带与泵浦激光场引起的边带不同；还识别出能带共振诱导的边带，源于带隙与泵浦频率共振处的残余相干性。

Conclusion: 研究结果证实了近期实验中观测到的激子场诱导Floquet类边带现象，并表明DPOA是一种高效且精确的模拟相互作用电子系统中超快过程的方法。

Abstract: We develop a theoretical framework based on the Dynamical Projective Operatorial Approach (DPOA) to study the time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (TR-ARPES) of pumped excitonic systems. Including Coulomb electron-electron interactions at the Hartree-Fock (HF) level, our formalism captures the formation of excitonic bound states under the application of pump pulses. Considering a prototypical two-dimensional two-band semiconductor, we analyze the equilibrium phase diagram, which shows the expected transition from a semiconducting to an excitonic-insulator phase as the Coulomb interaction strength or its range increase. Out of equilibrium, we find that when the pump frequency is resonant with an excitonic mode, coherent oscillations of the excitonic order parameter persist after the pump pulse subsides and give rise to clear Floquet sidebands in the TR-ARPES spectrum. These exciton-field-induced sidebands are distinct from those originating from the pump laser field. We also identify band-resonance-induced sidebands arising from residual coherences at momenta where the band gap is resonant with the pump frequency. Finally, we analyze the local Coulomb interaction limit. Our results corroborate recent experimental observations of exciton-field-induced Floquet-like sidebands and establish DPOA as an efficient and accurate method for simulating ultrafast phenomena in interacting electron systems.

### [24] [Complete Hierarchy of Nonrelativistic Odd-Parity Spin Splitting in Collinear Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19303)
*Yichen Liu,Junxi Yu,Pu Zhang,Cheng-Cheng Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过群论（group theory）建立了共线磁体中奇宇称自旋劈裂（odd-parity spin splitting）的完整分类，发现了 $h$-波（$\ell=5$）、$k$-波（$\ell=7$）和 $m$-波（$\ell=9$）等高阶分波类型，并揭示了其与反常霍尔响应（anomalous Hall response）之间的对称性判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 偶宇称自旋劈裂（如 $s$、$d$、$g$、$i$ 波）已被广泛研究，但奇宇称自旋劈裂除 $p$ 波和 $f$ 波外尚未被系统探索。现有分类缺少对高阶奇宇称分波的完整理解，限制了对其物理效应的认识。

Method: 利用群论对共线磁体中的奇宇称自旋劈裂进行完整分类；推导晶体学点群不可约表示（irreducible representations）到最低阶奇宇称基函数的完整映射；建立对称性破缺轴向场（axial field）与母Néel序之间的耦合规则；构建最小晶格模型；基于MAGNDATA数据库筛选候选材料。

Result: 奇宇称自旋劈裂存在 $p$、$f$ 波之外允许的 $h$-波（$\ell=5$）和 $k$-波（$\ell=7$）形式，而 $m$-波（$\ell=9$）构成上限。圆偏振光可将 $\mathcal{PT}$ 对称反铁磁体 Fe$_2$TeO$_6$ 和 MgFe$_6$Ge$_6$ 分别驱动至 $h$-波和 $k$-波相。$h$-波和 $k$-波类允许反常霍尔响应（anomalous Hall response），而 $m$-波类则禁止。

Conclusion: 该工作完成了共线磁体中奇宇称自旋劈裂的完整分波层次（partial-wave hierarchy），为高阶分波类中的反常输运建立了对称性判据。

Abstract: Momentum-dependent nonrelativistic spin splitting provides a symmetry fingerprint of collinear magnets and can govern unconventional electronic, magnonic, and transport phenomena. Whereas even-parity $s$-, $d$-, $g$-, and $i$-wave splittings in collinear magnets have been extensively studied, odd-parity counterparts remain unexplored beyond the $p$-wave and $f$-wave classes. Here, using group theory, we establish the complete classification of odd-parity spin splitting in collinear magnets. We show that, in addition to the $p$-wave and $f$-wave forms, $h$- and $k$-wave splittings with $\ell=5$ and $7$ are allowed, while $m$-wave splitting with $\ell=9$ constitutes the upper bound. We derive a complete mapping from crystallographic point-group irreducible representations to the lowest-order odd-parity basis functions and formulate the coupling rule between a symmetry-breaking axial field and the parent Néel order that selects the induced odd-parity class. We further construct minimal lattice models that realize $h$-, $k$-, and $m$-wave splitting. Guided by this classification, we screen the MAGNDATA database and show that circularly polarized light can drive the $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric antiferromagnets Fe$_2$TeO$_6$ and MgFe$_6$Ge$_6$ into $h$-wave and $k$-wave phases, respectively, exhibiting the hallmark spin splittings in both electronic bands and magnon spectra. Symmetry analysis and Berry-curvature calculations show that collinear odd-parity magnets of both $h$- and $k$-wave allow an anomalous Hall response, whereas the $m$-wave class forbids it. Together, these results complete the partial-wave hierarchy of odd-parity spin splitting in collinear magnets and establish symmetry criteria for anomalous transport in the high-partial-wave classes.

### [25] [Long-time asymptotic behavior for the defocusing Hirota equation on a finite-genus algebro-geometric background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19119)
*Taohua Luo,Zhenya Yan,Guoqiang Zhang*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究散焦Hirota方程在有限亏格代数几何背景下的柯西问题在整个时空半平面上的长时间渐近行为，将时空平面划分为四个区域并给出各区域的主项与次主项渐近形式，包括Painlevé-XXXIV模型转换区域和Zakharov–Manakov区域等。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在可积系统（integrable systems）的长时间渐近分析中，对于有限的背景解（如有限亏格代数几何解）上的扰动演化的理解仍有待深入，本文旨在推广已有的零背景或单孤子背景结果到更一般的代数几何背景上。

Method: 方法基于Riemann-Hilbert（RH）问题表述以及Deift-Zhou非线性最速下降法（nonlinear steepest descent method），对相位函数的临界值进行分析以划分时空平面区域，并在各区域中分别进行渐近展开。

Result: 相位函数的临界值将时空平面划分为四个区域。主项为相位偏移的有限亏格代数几何解；次主项行为因区域而异：转换区域中修正项为$t^{-1/3}$阶并由Painlevé-XXXIV模型RH问题描述，Zakharov–Manakov区域中主要辐射为$t^{-1/2}$阶，快速衰减区域中误差为$O(t^{-1})$。

Conclusion: 本文结果可推广至AKNS层次（AKNS hierarchy）的其他高阶成员，为更一般的可积系统在代数几何背景上的长时间渐近分析提供了框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the long-time asymptotics for the solution of the Cauchy problem of the defocusing Hirota equation on a finite-genus algebro-geometric background in the whole $(x,t)$-half-plane, whose method is mainly based on a Riemann-Hilbert (RH) formulation and Deift-Zhou nonlinear steepest descent method. The critical values of the phase function in the associated RH problem divide the space-time plane into four regions, in which the leading-order term is given by a phase-shifted finite-genus algebro-geometric solution. The subleading behavior depends on the region: the correction is of order $t^{-1/3}$ and is governed by a Painlevé-XXXIV model RH problem in the transition regions; the leading radiation is of order $t^{-1/2}$ in the Zakharov--Manakov region; and the error is $O(t^{-1})$ in the fast-decay region. These results can also be extended to other higher-order members of the AKNS hierarchy.

### [26] [Quantum logistic map considered as discrete-time Heisenberg equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19159)
*Maciej Janowicz,Arkadiusz Orłowski*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文将标量逻辑斯蒂迭代表示为 $L^2([0,1])$ 上的乘法算子，在归一化移位勒让德基（normalized shifted-Legendre basis）下研究其固定矩阵元。在 $r=5/2$、$r=16/5$ 和 $r=4$ 三个参数区域实现了解析控制，揭示了矩阵元随迭代步数收敛到 Kronecker delta 形式的明确极限。此外还对 $r=37/10$ 进行了受限数值研究，并考察了有限维矩阵递归及其他诊断量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索逻辑斯蒂映射（logistic map）在算子表示下的固定矩阵元（fixed matrix elements）行为，试图在少数特参数区域实现精确解析控制，并补充有限数值诊断手段，以理解非线性动力系统在算子层面的结构。

Method: 将标量逻辑斯蒂迭代视为 $L^2([0,1])$ 上的乘法算子（multiplication operators），在归一化移位勒让德基（normalized shifted-Legendre basis）下展开。对 $r=5/2$、$16/5$ 和 $4$ 进行解析控制；对 $r=37/10$ 采用有限数值精化研究。还引入了有限维矩阵递归 $X_{k+1}=R X_k(I-X_k)R^\dagger$，并计算了多种诊断量，包括矩阵元时间依赖、分岔图、时间平均强度、归一化二阶强度矩及归一化标量 OTOC 型对易子关联矩阵（normalized scalar OTOC-type commutator correlation matrices）。

Result: 在 $r=5/2$ 时，所有固定矩阵元收敛到 $3\delta_{kl}/5$；在 $r=16/5$ 时，吸引二周期轨道（attracting period-two orbit）给出偶数和奇数子序列的相位分辨极限；在 $r=4$ 时，精确切比雪夫矩表示（exact Chebyshev-moment representation）给出固定矩阵元以 $O(4^{-n})$ 速度趋近 $\delta_{kl}/2$。$r=37/10$ 仅通过数值研究获得初步观测。明确指出这些解析结论仅针对指定基索引的固定矩阵元，不蕴含算子范数收敛（operator-norm convergence）。

Conclusion: 在三个特定参数点实现了对逻辑斯蒂映射算子表示中固定矩阵元的解析描述，而更一般的参数和有限维递归仅能通过有限时间数值方法探索。该工作为非线性动力系统的算子理论分析提供了一个受控的案例研究，并引入了相空间提升（phase-space lift）作为可视化工具。

Abstract: We represent scalar logistic iterates as multiplication operators on $L^2([0,1])$ and study their fixed matrix elements in the normalized shifted-Legendre basis. Three parameter regimes permit analytical control. At $r=5/2$, every fixed matrix element converges to $3δ_{kl}/5$, where $δ_{kl}$ is the Kronecker delta. At $r=16/5$, the attracting period-two orbit yields phase-resolved limits for the even and odd subsequences. At $r=4$, an exact Chebyshev-moment representation gives an $O(4^{-n})$ approach of every fixed matrix element at iteration $n$ to $δ_{kl}/2$. The case $r=37/10$ is treated only by a controlled finite numerical refinement study. Complementary finite diagnostics comprise matrix-element time dependence, a bifurcation-style plot, a time-averaged mean intensity, a normalized second-order intensity moment, and normalized scalar OTOC-type commutator correlation matrices. We also examine the separate finite-dimensional recursion $X_{k+1}=R X_k(I-X_k)R^\dagger$, with fixed matrix $R$, using diagonal and tridiagonal amplitude profiles. These operator-valued calculations are exploratory finite-time numerics. The analytical statements concern fixed matrix elements for the specified basis indices; they are distinct from the finite-resolution observations and do not imply operator-norm convergence. A regularized phase-space lift is included as a controlled visualization.

### [28] [Programmable Spin Conversion in Gradient Quantum Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19105)
*Mamoru Matsuo,Yuta Sekino,Hiroyuki Tajima*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出超冷气体（ultracold gases）中的可编程自旋转换（programmable spin conversion）作为梯度量子物质（gradient quantum matter），其自旋依赖的自能（spin-dependent self-energy）在空间中变化。量子动理学理论（Quantum kinetic theory）表明，耗散自能曲率（dissipative self-energy curvature）将力驱动的标量各向异性（force-driven scalar anisotropy）转化为具有混合纵-横动量宇称（mixed longitudinal-transverse momentum parity）的自旋源。自旋分辨的飞行时间成像（Spin-resolved time-of-flight imaging）可以揭示横向自旋织构（transverse spin texture），该织构在驱动或可编程曲率反转时改变符号。因此，超冷气体为梯度量子物质提供了一个可控的自旋源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超冷气体中可编程自旋转换机制，以实现对梯度量子物质中自旋源的控制和观测。

Method: 采用量子动理学理论进行分析，提出利用自旋分辨的飞行时间成像来探测自旋织构。

Result: 耗散自能曲率可将力驱动的标量各向异性转化为具有混合纵-横动量宇称的自旋源；该自旋源产生的横向自旋织构在驱动方向或可编程曲率反转时改变符号。

Conclusion: 超冷气体可作为梯度量子物质的可控自旋源，为相关研究提供了新的实验平台。

Abstract: We propose programmable spin conversion in ultracold gases as gradient quantum matter, whose spin-dependent self-energy varies in space. Quantum kinetic theory shows that a dissipative self-energy curvature turns a force-driven scalar anisotropy into a spin source with mixed longitudinal-transverse momentum parity. Spin-resolved time-of-flight imaging can reveal a transverse spin texture that changes sign when either the drive or programmed curvature is reversed. Ultracold gases thereby offer a controllable spin source for gradient quantum matter.

</details>

# astro-ph.HE [[Back]](#toc)

### [29] [Gravitational-Wave Sky Mapping with Pulsar Timing Arrays: The Full Earth-Pulsar Response and Fundamental Resolution Limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19329)
*S. A. Andrianov,S. M. Kopeikin*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于完整地球-脉冲星响应和张量球谐分解（tensor spherical harmonic decomposition）的引力波天空制图框架，将脉冲星计时阵（PTA）的巡天重建转化为线性逆问题。研究表明PTA行为类似衍射极限引力波天文台，其角分辨率由参数ωL决定，存在四个响应区域；尽管脉冲星项在数学上存在过渡区域，但实际PTA需要约10¹¹颗精密计时脉冲星才能利用相干脉冲星项信息，因此为当前观测中采用的地球项近似（Earth-term approximation）提供了定量依据。最后将形式化方法扩展到随机引力波背景（stochastic GW backgrounds），建立了统一的数学框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵（PTA）是观测纳赫兹引力波（nanohertz gravitational waves）的唯一手段，现有分析主要利用地球项（Earth term），而完整探测器响应（full detector response）中的脉冲星项（pulsar terms）编码了额外的方向信息。本文旨在开发一种基于完整地球-脉冲星响应和张量球谐分解的引力波天空制图框架，以揭示PTA的角分辨率极限，并量化脉冲星项信息的实际可用性。

Method: 基于完整地球-脉冲星响应和张量球谐分解（tensor spherical harmonic decomposition）构建引力波天空制图框架，推导出基本基线（elementary baseline）的闭式响应函数（closed-form response functions），将PTA巡天重建形式化为线性逆问题（linear inverse problem）。采用Fisher信息（Fisher-information）和奇异值分析（singular-value analysis），研究角分辨率的约束因素。

Result: PTA的行为类似于衍射极限引力波天文台（diffraction-limited GW observatory），其角灵敏度由无量纲参数ωL（ω为引力波角频率，L为脉冲星距离）支配。探测器响应存在四个不同区域：地球项主导区、过渡区、脉冲星项主导区以及指数灵敏度截止区（截止点l_cut≈ωL），后者定义了PTA天空制图的基本角分辨率极限。相干脉冲星项信息只有在PTA包含约10¹¹颗精密计时脉冲星时才能改善全天空引力波制图，这一数量远高于现实PTA的规模，从而定量证明了地球项近似的合理性。

Conclusion: 尽管脉冲星项过渡区域在数学上存在，但对于现实PTA而言不可达，因此为当代观测中采用的地球项近似提供了定量依据。此外，将形式化方法扩展至随机引力波背景，建立了用于PTA天空制图和各向异性研究的统一数学框架。

Abstract: Pulsar timing arrays (PTAs) are the only means to observe nanohertz gravitational waves (GWs). While current analyses primarily exploit the Earth term, the full detector response encodes additional directional information in the pulsar terms. We develop a GW sky-mapping framework based on the complete Earth--pulsar response and a tensor spherical harmonic decomposition of the GW field. This yields closed-form response functions for an elementary baseline and casts PTA sky reconstruction as a linear inverse problem.
  We show that a PTA behaves as a diffraction-limited GW observatory whose angular sensitivity is governed by the dimensionless parameter $ωL$, where $ω$ is the GW angular frequency and $L$ is the pulsar distance. The detector response exhibits four distinct regimes: an Earth-term dominated regime, a transition regime, a pulsar-term-dominated regime, and an exponential sensitivity cutoff at $l_{cut}\simeqωL$. This cutoff defines the fundamental angular resolution limit of PTA sky maps.
  Using Fisher-information and singular-value analyses, we show that the achievable angular resolution is constrained not only by the intrinsic detector response but also by the finite number of pulsars, their sky distribution, and timing noise. In particular, we find that coherent pulsar-term information can improve full-sky gravitational-wave mapping only for PTAs containing of order $N_{trans}\sim10^{11}$ precisely timed pulsars. This result demonstrates that, although the transition to a pulsar-term-sensitive regime exists mathematically, it is inaccessible for realistic PTAs and therefore provides a quantitative justification for the Earth-term approximation adopted in contemporary observations.
  Finally, we extend the formalism to stochastic GW backgrounds, establishing a unified mathematical framework for PTA sky mapping and anisotropy studies.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [30] [Hawking emission of massive vector fields by Kerr black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18395)
*Marco Calzà,Miguel Faria,Yuber F. Perez-Gonzalez,João G. Rosa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文首次计算了旋转克尔（Kerr）黑洞对质向量场（Proca场）的霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）谱，确定了灰体因子（greybody factor）以及质量和自旋损失函数。研究发现，质向量场的标量（纵向）极化模式在无质量极限下趋近于自由标量场的谱，而两个矢量（横向）极化模式在无质量极限下与麦克斯韦（Maxwell）场结果一致。黑洞蒸发率在慢旋时由标量模主导，在近极端（extremal）时由矢量模主导。霍金温度 $T_H\lesssim |\mu-\Omega_H|$ 时辐射受玻尔兹曼抑制（Boltzmann-suppressed），但高自旋黑洞可在远低于场质量的温度下有效发射质向量场。此外，质向量场的超辐射（superradiance）放大因子可达约7%，高于无质量光子的约4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前霍金辐射的研究多集中于标量场和（无质量）电磁场，而自然界中可能存在有质量的自旋1粒子（如暗光子等），其辐射特性尚未被探索。该工作旨在填补这一空白，首次系统计算旋转黑洞对质向量场的蒸发谱和超辐射效应。

Method: 基于克尔黑洞背景，对质量向量（Proca）场的三种极化模式（一个标量/纵向模式与两个矢量/横向模式）分别求解其灰体因子，进而导出霍金辐射谱以及黑洞质量和自旋的损失函数。通过对比无质量极限与已知的标量场和麦克斯韦场结果来验证计算，并分析有限质量下的差异。

Result: 标量（纵向）极化模式在无质量极限下趋近自由标量场的辐射谱，但在有限质量下显示出显著差异；两个矢量（横向）极化模式在无质量极限下与Page关于麦克斯韦场的结果一致。黑洞蒸发率在慢旋时由标量模主导，近极端时由矢量模主导。霍金温度满足 $T_H\lesssim |\mu-\Omega_H|$ 时辐射被玻尔兹曼抑制，但高自旋黑洞仍可在 $T_H$ 远低于场质量时有效发射。质向量场的超辐射放大因子最大约7%，高于无质量光子的约4%。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解有质量自旋1场在旋转黑洞背景下的霍金辐射和超辐射提供了首个完整计算，揭示了不同极化模式在不同自旋参数下的主导行为，并表明超辐射效应对质向量场更为显著。这对于黑洞蒸发、暗物质候选者以及早期宇宙物理均有潜在意义。

Abstract: We compute, for the first time, the Hawking emission spectrum of massive vector (Proca) fields by spinning Kerr black holes, determining the associated greybody factors and the resulting mass and spin loss functions. We show, in particular, that the scalar (longitudinal) polarization of the Proca field has a spectrum approaching that of a free scalar field in the massless limit (in which it becomes a pure gauge mode), although we find substantial differences for finite mass. The contribution of the two vector (transverse) polarization modes coincides, as expected, with the one obtained by Page for the Maxwell field in the massless limit. The black hole's evaporation rate is dominated by the scalar mode for slowly spinning black holes and by the two vector modes as the black hole approaches extremality. As for other fields, we find that Proca Hawking emission is Boltzmann-suppressed for Hawking temperatures $T_H\lesssim |μ-Ω_H|$, where $μ$ is the field mass and $Ω_H$ is the angular velocity of the black hole's horizon. This implies that highly spinning black holes can efficiently emit massive vector fields at temperatures parametrically below the field's mass. Finally, we also find that superradiant emission is more pronounced for massive vector fields, with a maximum amplification factor of $\simeq 7\%$ (compared to $\simeq 4\%$ for massless photons).

</details>


### [31] [Nonradial perturbations of static charged wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18399)
*Jose Luis Blázquez-Salcedo,Luis Manuel González-Romero,Fech Scen Khoo,Jutta Kunz,Pablo Navarro Moreno*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中与幻标量场最小耦合的静态带电Ellis–Bronnikov虫洞的非径向准正则模谱。通过推导轴极和极向扰动方程并采用切比雪夫谱方法计算能谱，发现电荷可显著降低阻尼率，并在大质量虫洞中揭示了一种非径向极向不稳定性，该不稳定性对带电虫洞的动力学可行性施加了额外约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究关注静态Ellis–Bronnikov虫洞的径向扰动，但对其非径向（nonradial）准正则模谱（quasinormal-mode spectrum）及其在带电情形下的行为尚缺乏系统分析。本文旨在填补这一空白，考察电荷对虫洞阻尼时间和振荡频率的影响，并探索非径向扰动是否引入新的不稳定性。

Method: 在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中引入最小耦合的幻标量场（phantom scalar field），导出背景解（分为次临界、临界和超临界三类）。推导轴向（axial）和极向（polar）扇区的线性扰动方程，涵盖引力、电磁和幻标量自由度，并采用切比雪夫谱方法（Chebyshev spectral method）计算相应的准正则模谱。

Result: 不带电极限复现了已知的Ellis–Bronnikov谱，并呈现出预期的电磁等谱性（electromagnetic isospectrality）。带电情形下，随着接近极端Reissner–Nordström极限，电荷可显著降低阻尼率（damping rates）。此外，在大质量虫洞的基本l=2分支中，发现了一种非径向极向不稳定性（nonradial polar instability），该不稳定性不同于已知的径向Ellis–Bronnikov不稳定性。

Conclusion: 电荷效应对虫洞的准正则模谱有显著影响，尤其在接近极端Reissner–Nordström构型时能大幅降低阻尼。新发现的非径向极向不稳定性表明，非径向扇区对带电虫洞的动力学稳定性施加了额外约束，虫洞的动力学可行性不仅取决于径向扰动，还需考虑非径向扰动带来的限制。

Abstract: We investigate the nonradial quasinormal-mode spectrum of static charged Ellis--Bronnikov wormholes in Einstein--Maxwell theory minimally coupled to a phantom scalar field. The background solutions are known in closed form and comprise three classes: subcritical, critical and supercritical, which all approach the extremal Reissner--Nordström geometry at the boundary of their domain of existence. We derive the linear perturbation equations for axial and polar sectors, including the coupled gravitational, electromagnetic and phantom-scalar degrees of freedom, and compute the corresponding spectra by means of a Chebyshev spectral method. The uncharged limit reproduces the known Ellis--Bronnikov spectrum and exhibits the expected electromagnetic isospectrality. For charged configurations we track the axial and polar branches across the three families of solutions and identify the effect of the charge on the damping times and oscillation frequencies. In particular, we find that charge can substantially reduce damping rates as the extremal Reissner--Nordström limit is approached. We also uncover a nonradial polar instability, most clearly visible in the fundamental $l=2$ branch for sufficiently large wormhole masses. This instability is distinct from the familiar radial Ellis--Bronnikov instability and shows that the nonradial sector imposes additional constraints on the dynamical viability of charged wormholes.

</details>


### [32] [Extreme mass-ratio inspirals into Newtonian Proca stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18405)
*João Bernardo Silva,Richard Brito*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在牛顿极限下研究了Proca星（Proca stars）对内部小质量绕行物体的响应，计算了轨道能量损失，并与标量场玻色子星进行对比，发现两者在基态下的能量损失相似（差异≤20%），但存在中心黑洞时基态构型的轨道能量损失率可比球对称情形高1-2个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超轻玻色场可形成自引力孤子结构，有望描述星系中心超大质量黑洞周围的暗物质（dark matter）晕核心，且未来引力波探测器可能探测暗物质结构性质。然而，现有超轻暗物质的分析大多集中于标量场（scalar field），对矢量场（vector field）——即Proca星——在绕行扰动下的响应研究不足。

Method: 在牛顿极限（Newtonian limit）下，分别考虑牛顿球对称Proca星和非球对称基态解（ground-state solutions），分析一个小质量物体从内部绕行时对Proca星的扰动，计算其总能量损失，并与标量场玻色子星情形进行对比。

Result: 在牛顿极限下，Proca星基态中绕行物体的能量损失与对应的标量场玻色子星相似，相对差异最多约20%；而在存在中心寄生黑洞（parasitic black hole）时，基态构型的最大轨道能量损失率可比球对称Proca星高1-2个数量级。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持采用完全相对论（fully relativistic）框架进一步研究Proca星中的极端质量比旋进（extreme mass-ratio inspirals, EMRIs），因为在该框架下Proca星与标量玻色子星基态的差异预计将更为显著。

Abstract: Massive bosonic fields can form self-gravitating solitonic structures, which for vector fields are known as Proca stars. For ultralight fields, these structures can describe the cores of dark matter haloes surrounding the supermassive black holes at the center of galaxies. It has been argued that future gravitational-wave detectors might be able to probe the properties of dark matter structures. However, most of the analyses considering ultralight dark matter have focused on massive scalar fields. In this work, we study how Proca stars respond to a perturbing small object inspiralling in their interior, in the Newtonian limit. We consider both Newtonian spherically symmetric Proca stars and the non-spherically symmetric ground-state solutions. We compute the total energy lost by the orbiting object and compare it to the case where the bosonic star is composed of a scalar field. Our results show that, at the Newtonian level, the energy lost by the object in a Proca star ground-state is similar to that in its scalar field counterpart, with relative differences of at most $\sim 20\%$, while the maximum orbital energy loss rate in the ground-state configuration can be one to two orders of magnitude larger than in the spherically symmetric Proca star, when a central parasitic black hole is present. Our work motivates the need to study extreme mass-ratio inspirals into Proca stars using a fully relativistic setup, where differences between the Proca and scalar boson star ground states are expected to become more significant.

</details>


### [33] [Vacuum Gravity from Entropy: Stability, Spectra, and Exact Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18518)
*David S. Pereira*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从熵导出引力的真空动力学，包括其代数约束的G场形式。通过计算零-、一-、二-形式扇区的曲率迹，证明Minkowski Hessian等于二次引力作用量$A R+B R_{μν}R^{μν}$，系数A和B由β和普朗克长度确定。谱包含无质量引力子、一个标量模式和具有相反留数的自旋-2分支，其中$β>0$会导致快子型自旋-2不稳定性。所有四维Ricci平坦度规在二次曲率阶数上满足局域体方程，而平方为零的Ricci平坦pp-波是该系统精确局域真空解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从熵的角度推导引力的真空动力学，并分析其代数约束的G场形式背后的理论结构。

Method: 计算零-、一-、二-形式扇区的曲率迹，将Minkowski Hessian与二次引力作用量进行比对；对可对角化的曲率块进行求和对数操作；线性化G场方程并结合代数真空约束推导度规方程与协变Hessian。

Result: Minkowski Hessian精确还原为二次引力作用量$A R+B R_{μν}R^{μν}$，系数$A=3β/\ell_{\rm P}^{4}$，$B=5β^{2}/(2\ell_{\rm P}^{4})$。谱包含无质量引力子、质量平方$m_{0}^{2}=3/(5β)$的标量模和具有相反留数、质量平方$m_{2}^{2}=-6/(5β)=-2m_{0}^{2}$的自旋-2分支。$β>0$时出现快子型自旋-2不稳定性。

Conclusion: 该理论在特定条件下与广义相对论一致，但存在快子不稳定性；Ricci平坦度规和pp-波解是该系统的精确局域真空解；在孤立的无质量横迹无迹本征空间上，二次平移流具有标准广义相对论归一化。

Abstract: We analyze the vacuum dynamics of Gravity from Entropy, including its algebraically constrained $G$-field formulation. Evaluating the curvature traces over zero-, one-, and two-form sectors, we show that the complete Minkowski Hessian is exactly that of the quadratic-gravity action $A R+B R_{μν}R^{μν}$, with $A=3β/\ell_{\rm P}^{4}$ and $B=5β^{2}/(2\ell_{\rm P}^{4})$. For diagonalizable curvature blocks, the same action reduces to a sum over eigenvalue logarithms and reproduces these coefficients exactly. A strict diagonal-curvature restriction on the perturbations is instead only a reduced subsector and excludes non-diagonalizable type-N wave curvatures. Linearizing the $G$-field equations and subsequently imposing the algebraic vacuum constraint reproduces the same reduced metric equation and covariant Minkowski Hessian. The spectrum contains the massless graviton, a scalar with $m_{0}^{2}=3/(5β)$, and an opposite-residue spin-2 branch with $m_{2}^{2}=-6/(5β)=-2m_{0}^{2}$. For the foundational choice $β>0$, conventional Einstein normalization therefore implies a tachyonic spin-2 instability. We also show that every four-dimensional Ricci-flat metric solves the local bulk equations through quadratic curvature order, while square-zero Ricci-flat pp-waves are exact local vacuum solutions of the analytic metric-only logarithmic branch. On the isolated massless transverse-traceless eigenspace, the quadratic translation current has the standard general-relativistic normalization.

</details>


### [34] [Modified Cosmology from Mass-to-Horizon Relation: Observational Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18521)
*Pranav Prasanthan,Hussain Gohar,Vincenzo Salzano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于广义质量-视界关系（MHR）约束了一类修正宇宙学模型，利用多种观测数据通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）进行参数约束。熵指数被严格限制在标准值附近，自由参数虽能部分缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension），但贝叶斯对数证据（Bayesian log-evidence）明确否定所有扩展模型优于标准ΛCDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从广义质量-视界关系（mass-to-horizon relation, MHR）出发，推导满足热力学一致性的修正宇宙学模型，并利用多组宇宙学观测数据对其进行严格约束，检验视界热力学（horizon thermodynamics）的修正是否能够解释当前的宇宙学疑难，尤其是哈勃张力（Hubble tension）。

Method: 基于Cai-Kim视界温度（Cai-Kim horizon temperature）与广义视界熵（generalized horizon entropies）之间的热力学一致性，推导修正的弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equations）。引入熵指数m、MHR耦合参数γ和纠缠修正振幅f_B三个自由参数。使用Pantheon+/SH0ES Ia型超新星、宇宙时钟（cosmic chronometers）、DESI DR2重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations）以及Planck 2018 CMB距离先验（CMB distance priors）等多组观测数据，通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）进行参数约束，并利用贝叶斯对数证据（Bayesian log-evidence）进行模型比较。

Result: 熵指数被严格约束：在固定MHR耦合（γ=1）时|m-1|≲O(10⁻⁴)，沿m-γ简并方向放宽至O(10⁻³)，排除任何宏观显著的视界热力学偏离。释放MHR耦合参数或纠缠振幅可使哈勃常数提升至h≃0.70-0.71，将CMB-SH0ES张力从约4σ降低至约1.2-2.6σ，但没有任何场景能在平坦宇宙中完全解决该张力。贝叶斯对数证据在所有数据集组合中均否定所有扩展模型优于ΛCDM（-16≲Δln Z ≲-1）。

Conclusion: 修正视界熵的宇宙学模型在观测约束下面临严重困难：熵指数被严格限制在ΛCDM值附近，无法实现宏观偏离；虽然自由参数可在统计上部分吸收哈勃张力，但这并非真正的热力学修正证据，而是参数吸收效应。贝叶斯模型比较明确排除所有扩展场景，标准ΛCDM模型在当前数据组合下仍是最优选择。

Abstract: We constrain the class of modified cosmologies derived in Paper I [1] from a generalized mass-to-horizon relation (MHR) that enforces thermodynamic consistency between the Cai-Kim horizon temperature and generalized horizon entropies. The modified Friedmann equations depend on an entropy exponent $m$, an MHR coupling parameter $γ$, and an entanglement-correction amplitude $f_B$, with standard $Λ$CDM recovered in the appropriate limit. Using Pantheon$+$/SH0ES Type~Ia supernovae, cosmic chronometers, DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillations, and Planck 2018 CMB distance priors, we constrain eight physically motivated sub-cases via Markov chain Monte Carlo and compare models through the Bayesian log-evidence. The entropy exponent is tightly bounded, $|m-1|\lesssim O(10^{-4})$ when the MHR coupling is fixed ($γ=1$), relaxing to $O(10^{-3})$ along the $m$-$γ$ degeneracy, excluding any macroscopically significant departure from standard horizon thermodynamics. Freeing the MHR coupling parameter or the entanglement amplitude raises the inferred Hubble constant to $h\simeq0.70$-$0.71$, reducing the CMB-SH0ES tension from ${\sim}4σ$ to ${\sim}1.2$-$2.6σ$, but no scenario fully resolves it within a flat universe. The Bayesian log-evidence nevertheless disfavors every extension relative to $Λ$CDM in all dataset combinations ($-16\lesssimΔ\ln Z \lesssim-1$): the improved fits obtained when the SH0ES calibration is included reflect an absorption of the Hubble tension by the additional parameters rather than genuine evidence for modified horizon entropy.

</details>


### [35] [Periodic Orbits and Gravitational Wave Signatures around the Bonanno--Reuter Regular Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18627)
*Mohammad Reza Alipour,Mohammad Ali S. Afshar,Saeed Noori Gashti,Behnam Pourhassan,Jafar Sadeghi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了 Bonanno–Reuter 规则黑洞（regular black hole）时空中类时测地线（timelike geodesics）、周期轨道（periodic orbits）及其引力波信号特征。该黑洞源于渐近安全引力（Asymptotically Safe Gravity），其中运行牛顿耦合将中心奇点替换为 de Sitter 核心。无量纲参数 α/M² 完全决定了强场动力学：增大该参数使边缘束缚轨道与最内稳定圆轨道向内收缩，缩小允许束缚运动的相空间；周期轨道发生轻度内向收缩，降低维持特定拓扑所需的能量。在数值 kludge 框架下计算极端质量比旋近（extreme mass-ratio inspirals）的引力波极化，发现渐近安全修正导致左移相位与峰值振幅增强。波形对轨道拓扑高度敏感，高涡旋轨道（high-whirl orbits）的偏差最为显著。这种内在量子引力修正产生可观测特征，有望被 LISA、Taiji 和 TianQin 等未来空间探测器识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索渐近安全引力框架下规则黑洞的强场动力学行为及其引力波可观测特征，旨在区分量子引力修正与经典环境效应，为未来空间引力波探测器提供判别依据。

Method: 通过解析参数 α/M² 对类时测地线与周期轨道进行分类，利用有理频率比 q = w + v/z 对轨迹进行拓扑分类；采用数值 kludge 框架计算极端质量比旋近的引力波极化波形。

Result: 增大 α/M² 使边缘束缚轨道和最内稳定圆轨道的半径、角动量和能量系统性减小，束缚运动相空间收缩；周期轨道发生内向收缩，所需能量降低。引力波波形呈现左移相位和增强的峰值振幅，高涡旋轨道显示出最显著的偏差。

Conclusion: 渐近安全引力修正产生与经典环境效应（如轨道膨胀）截然不同的可观测特征，这些特征具有拓扑依赖性，为 LISA、Taiji 和 TianQin 等未来空间探测器探测量子引力信号提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Timelike geodesics, periodic orbits, and their associated gravitational-wave signatures are examined in the spacetime of a Bonanno--Reuter regular black hole, a geometry arising from Asymptotically Safe Gravity in which a running Newton coupling replaces the central singularity with a de Sitter core. The dimensionless parameter $α/M^2$ completely determines the strong-field dynamics. Increasing $α/M^2$ shifts the marginally bound and innermost stable circular orbits inward, systematically reducing their characteristic radii, angular momenta, and energies; the allowed phase space for bound motion contracts accordingly. Classifying trajectories via the rational frequency ratio $q = w + v/z$ reveals that periodic orbits experience a mild inward contraction, which reduces the energy necessary to sustain a specific topology. Within the numerical kludge framework, we calculate the gravitational-wave polarizations for extreme mass-ratio inspirals. The asymptotically safe correction induces a leftward phase shift that reflects shorter orbital periods, while mildly enhancing peak amplitudes owing to the smaller periastron distances reached in the deep strong-field regime. Waveform sensitivity displays a strong dependence on topology, with high-whirl orbits, which persist longer in the strong-field region near the horizon, showing markedly more pronounced deviations. Unlike environmental effects that inflate orbital scales, intrinsic quantum-gravity modifications generate distinct, observationally detectable signatures for future space-based detectors such as LISA, Taiji, and TianQin.
