### [36] [Stochastic template banks for GW searches using low-discrepancy sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18633)
*Tarun Kumar,Anand S. Sengupta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出使用低差异序列（low-discrepancy sequences）替代均匀随机采样来构建随机模板库（stochastic template banks），在引力波搜索中只需更少的提议点（proposal points）即可达到相当的恢复率（recovery fractions），从而降低内存使用和记账开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统几何、随机和混合模板放置方法在高维参数空间中可能导致覆盖不均和冗余模板；均匀随机采样需要大量提议点才能实现充分覆盖，亟需更高效的采样策略。

Method: 采用低差异序列（low-discrepancy sequences）构建随机模板库，与传统的均匀随机采样方法进行对比；在二维和三维参数空间中评估提议点数量和最终模板库恢复率。

Result: 低差异序列方法在二维参数空间中减少27.5%的提议点，在三维空间中减少12%的提议点，同时保持相当的恢复率；最终模板数量仅有约1%的微小变化，与度量体积（metric-volume）约束一致；端到端加速比相对适度。

Conclusion: 低差异采样（low-discrepancy sampling）为随机模板库生成提供了一种简单且可扩展的改进方案，适用于当前及未来的引力波搜索任务。

Abstract: Matched filtering remains the most sensitive method for detecting gravitational waves from compact binary coalescences. The efficiency of such searches depends on how well a discrete template bank covers the underlying parameter space. Conventional geometric, stochastic, and hybrid placement methods can lead to uneven coverage and redundant templates in higher dimensions. Hybrid methods are generally the most efficient among these, while stochastic methods are simpler to implement, particularly when the parameter-space metric is difficult to compute. In practice, both approaches rely on uniform random sampling, which often requires a large number of proposal points to achieve adequate coverage. We find that stochastic template banks constructed using low-discrepancy sequences achieve comparable recovery fractions while requiring 27.5\% fewer proposal points in two dimensions and 12\% fewer in three dimensions. The final template count changes only marginally ($\sim 1\%$), consistent with the metric-volume constraints of the covering problem. The primary benefit of low-discrepancy sampling is therefore a reduction in the size of the initial proposal set, leading to lower memory usage and reduced bookkeeping during bank generation. Since the final template count is governed mainly by the metric volume of the target parameter space, the wall-clock speed-up is more modest than the reduction in proposal count. Nevertheless, low-discrepancy sampling provides a simple and scalable improvement to stochastic template-bank generation for current and future gravitational-wave searches.

Abstract: We construct a locally scale-invariant formulation of Schrödinger geometry in symmetric teleparallel gravity. The unique scale transformation preserving autoparallelism, torsionlessness and the Schrödinger affine structure is first identified, from which a quadratic scale-invariant action is obtained. Using the Palatini formalism, we show that the conditions required for scale invariance are exactly those ensuring that the affine connection is dynamically reduced to the Schrödinger form. Our results establish a direct correspondence between local scale symmetry and length-preserving affine geometry, providing a new geometric framework for scale-invariant metric-affine gravity.

Abstract: The Johannsen-Psaltis (JP) metric is constructed by introducing deviation parameters into the Kerr metric. Since black hole imaging provides one of the most direct means of probing the properties of astrophysical black holes, a detailed investigation of the imaging characteristics of JP black holes constitutes a natural first step toward employing the JP metric to explore potential deviations from the Kerr geometry in astrophysical black hole systems. Accordingly, numerical backward ray-tracing simulations are employed to conduct a comprehensive investigation of the image structures, intensity distributions, and redshift-blueshift signatures of JP black holes with both closed and non-closed event horizons. The dependence of these imaging characteristics on the deviation parameter is also investigated systematically. *Ayan Banerjee,sherzod Sayfiyev,Muhtarama Radjapbaeva,Javlon Rayimbaev,Shokhzod Jumaniyozov,Aseel Smerat*

TL;DR: 本文在bumblebee引力（bumblebee gravity）的Neves–Gardim分支中，通过一种有效的度规变形（effective metric-deformation）方法研究静态中子星的潮汐性质，计算了四极潮汐Love数$k_2$和 dimensionless潮汐形变参数$\Lambda$，并与GW170817事件给出的潮汐形变上限进行比较，得到了依赖于物态方程（equation of state）的bumblebee耦合参数$\ell$的约束上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 静态星体背景由完整的修正Tolman–Oppenheimer–Volkoff（TOV）方程组确定，包含$m''(r)$项；对于可微的 barotropic 物态方程，系统被重新表述为代数等价的一阶形式，未丢弃任何依赖于bumblebee场的贡献。潮汐部分采用显式的有效度规变形预设：在修正的bumblebee背景上评估Hinderer流体扰动方程，标准表面匹配关系作为同一预设的一部分予以保留。

Result: 对BSk20、BSk21、DD2和MS1四种物态方程，在bumblebee耦合参数$\ell\in[-0.4,+1.0]$范围内计算了$k_2$和$\Lambda$。广义相对论极限（$\ell=0$）的恢复精度在基准计算中优于$0.2\%$。与GW170817的潮汐形变上限$\widetilde\Lambda\leq720$对比，得到依赖于物态方程的$\ell_{\max}$限值：BSk20为$+0.25$，BSk21为$+0.06$，DD2为$-0.09$，MS1为$-0.25$。

Conclusion: 所得潮汐约束是条件性的，仅在当前采用的扰动预设下有效；当未来完整的线性化矢量–张量问题求解方案可用时，应重新评估这些限值。

Abstract: We investigate the tidal properties of static neutron stars in the Neves--Gardim branch of bumblebee gravity, a vector--tensor theory in which a nonzero vacuum expectation value of the bumblebee field spontaneously breaks local Lorentz symmetry. The stellar background is determined from the full modified Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff system, including the term containing $m''(r)$. For a differentiable barotropic equation of state, this system is recast into an algebraically equivalent first-order form without discarding any bumblebee-dependent contribution. Because a complete coupled derivation of static even-parity metric and bumblebee-field perturbations is not presently available for this stellar branch, the tidal sector is treated through an explicit effective metric-deformation prescription: the Hinderer fluid perturbation equation is evaluated on the modified bumblebee background, and the standard surface matching relation is retained as part of the same prescription. We compute the quadrupolar tidal Love number $k_2$ and the dimensionless tidal deformability $Λ=(2/3)k_2\mathcal{C}^{-5}$ for the BSk20, BSk21, DD2, and MS1 equations of state over $\ell\in[-0.4,+1.0]$. The general-relativistic limit is recovered at $\ell=0$ to within $0.2\%$ in the benchmark calculations. Within the adopted effective prescription, comparison with the GW170817 binary tidal-deformability bound $\widetildeΛ\leq720$ yields the EOS-dependent limiting values $\ell_{\max}=+0.25$ (BSk20), $+0.06$ (BSk21), $-0.09$ (DD2), and $-0.25$ (MS1). These tidal limits are conditional on the stated perturbative prescription and should be reassessed when the complete linearised vector--tensor problem becomes available.

### [41] [Defrosting the Born-Infeld dyonic frozen star with tachyon matter: spectrum of oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18851)
*Ram Brustein,A. J. M. Medved,Tamar Simhon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出“冻结星（frozen star）”作为无奇点、无俘获面的黑洞内部模型，并基于Born-Infeld作用量推导其微扰动力学，验证了冻结星在退冻结（defrosted）状态下声速与寿命的标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构造一个外部与Schwarzschild黑洞不可区分的无奇点常规黑洞模型，并实现其微扰稳定性与内部脉动行为的理论描述。

Method: 将冻结星视为Born-Infeld作用量与Einstein引力耦合下的宏观BIon解，引入微扰性磁单极荷与tachyon动能实现退冻结，转化为DIon；从Born-Infeld拉格朗日量推导非径向振荡方程，替代先前的流体近似方法。

Result: 通过拉格朗日量方法验证了声速按退冻结参数γ标度（scaling as γ），参数长寿命按1/γ²标度；由于方程源自拉格朗日量，其对任意偏离球对称的形变保持一致性。

Conclusion: 该拉格朗日推导方法保证了微扰方程在非球对称情形下的自洽性，为冻结星远离平衡态的数值研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The frozen star is a model for the interior of an astrophysical black hole that is externally indistinguishable from the singular geometry of a Schwarzschild black hole, even though it contains no singularities nor trapped surfaces. The frozen star corresponds to a macroscopic ``BIon'', a solution of a certain type of Born-Infeld Lagrangian coupled to Einstein gravity, which consists of rigid flux tubes sourced by an electric charge localized at its center and a uniform distribution of opposite charge along its outer surface. This configuration is a solution of the effective action that describes the end point of tachyon condensation in string. The rigidity of the flux tubes implies that the star is ultrastable under linear perturbations of the geometry and matter. The star can be effectively deformed, or ``defrosted'', allowing internal pulsations, as expected from regular, horizonless astrophysical black holes. To describe the defrosted star, we need to include a perturbative amount of magnetic-monopole charge and tachyon kinetic energy. This recasts the star as a macroscopic ``DIon'', whose flux tubes can stretch and contract, having both electric and magnetic charges localized at its center and distributed uniformly along its outer surface. Previously, the non-radial oscillations of the defrosted star were analyzed to leading order in a perturbative ``defrosting'' parameter $γ$, by describing the energy-momentum tensor as that of a fluid. Here, we derive the same spectrum in a much simpler way, using the Born-Infeld Lagrangian. Thus, we verify that the sound velocities scale as $γ$ and the parametrically long lifetimes scale as $1/γ^2$. Because the perturbation equations are derived from a Lagrangian, their consistency is guaranteed for arbitrary deviations away from spherical symmetry, facilitating numerical studies on frozen stars away from equilibrium.

</details>


### [42] [On Generalized (Conformal) Killing Tensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18871)

Result: 发现具有混合对称性的高阶广义Killing张量在高维旋转黑洞时空中自然存在，并展现出有趣的代数与微分性质；所提出的推广张量也在该类时空中得以实现。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了Killing张量理论在高维时空中的应用范围，揭示了其与黑洞几何的深层联系，为后续研究提供了新的张量结构与构造方法。

### [43] [Quasinormal Ringdown and Echoes in Accreting Exotic Compact Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18919)
*Chanchal Sharma,Kabir Chakravarti,Sudipta Sarkar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过数值演化动力学背景上的标量微扰，研究奇异致密天体（ECO）在吸积过程中从产生引力波回波到最终形成事件视界、回波信号消失并过渡到标准黑洞振铃的完整动力学过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异致密天体（exotic compact objects, ECOs）可能在晚期产生引力波回波（gravitational-wave echoes），但经历现实吸积的足够致密的ECO最终可能形成事件视界（event horizon），因此需要理解该过渡过程中回波信号的演化行为。

Method: 利用内行Vaidya解（ingoing Vaidya solution）对外部时空进行建模，在由此产生的动力学背景（dynamical background）上数值演化标量微扰（scalar perturbations）。

Result: 回波信号在吸积过程中逐渐被压缩并抑制，当不断生长的事件视界吞没反射表面（reflecting surface）时回波完全消失，此后波形平滑地过渡到标准黑洞振铃（black hole ringdown）。

Conclusion: 引力波回波的消失可被视为事件视界形成的特征信号（characteristic signature），该研究为未来引力波观测中研究动力学致密天体提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Exotic compact objects (ECOs) may produce late-time gravitational-wave (GW) echoes, but sufficiently compact ECOs undergoing realistic accretion may eventually form an event horizon. We investigate the evolution of quasinormal modes and GW echoes during this transition. Modeling the exterior spacetime with the ingoing Vaidya solution, we numerically evolve scalar perturbations on the resulting dynamical background. We show that the echo signal is progressively compressed and suppressed during accretion and disappears once the growing event horizon engulfs the reflecting surface, after which the waveform smoothly approaches the standard black hole ringdown. Our results identify the disappearance of GW echoes as a characteristic signature of horizon formation and provide a framework for studying dynamical compact objects with future GW observations.

</details>


### [44] [Accretion of multipolar massive complex scalar field packets by a Schwarzschild black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18920)
*Flavio Rosales-Infante,Ivan Alvarez-Rios,Francisco S. Guzman*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过时域数值演化研究Schwarzschild黑洞对复合有质量标量波包的有限时标吸积过程，构建了基于Noether流守恒的吸积效率图谱，揭示了吸积效率由Schwarzschild半径与约化Compton波长之比控制的过渡行为，并识别了角动量势垒主导与部分吸积平台等不同吸积区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于确定局域标量波包在与黑洞相互作用后其标量含量如何重新分布，以及哪些谱分量和多极分量（multipolar components）更有效地被黑洞吸收。参数设定受超大质量黑洞周围超轻模糊暗物质（ultralight fuzzy dark matter）的启发。

Method: 将Klein–Gordon场分解为独立的多极扇区，逐模式演化近单色高斯波包（nearly monochromatic Gaussian packets），将问题约化为一系列1+1维演化。吸积通过守恒Noether流（Noether current）在视界面上的通量量化，直接测量黑洞吸收的标量荷。

Result: 构造了载波径向波数$k_0$与多极指数$\ell$平面上的吸积效率图谱，展示出从低效、部分到高效吸积区间的过渡。吸积过程由Schwarzschild半径$R_s$与约化Compton波长$\lambdabar_C$之比控制：$R_s \lesssim \lambdabar_C$时过渡宽广且受角动量势垒主导；$R_s > \lambdabar_C$时过渡在更窄$k_0$范围内锐化，并在低$k_0$出现部分吸积平台。

Conclusion: 提供了基于时域Noether荷的黑洞吸积分类方案，适用于有质量标量波包的吸积过程。

Abstract: We study the finite-time accretion of complex massive scalar wave packets by a Schwarzschild black hole in the test-field regime, with parameters motivated by ultralight fuzzy dark matter around supermassive black holes. Our goal is to determine how the scalar content of a localized configuration is redistributed after interacting with the black hole, and which spectral and multipolar components are more efficiently absorbed. We decompose the Klein--Gordon field into independent multipolar sectors and evolve nearly monochromatic Gaussian packets mode by mode, reducing the problem to a set of 1+1 dimensional evolutions. Accretion is quantified with the flux of the conserved Noether current through the horizon surface, providing a direct measure of the scalar charge absorbed by the black hole. For a carrier radial wavenumber $k_0$ and multipole index $\ell$, we construct accretion-efficiency maps in the $(k_0,\ell)$ plane that contain the fraction of accreted modal charge. These maps exhibit a transition between inefficient, partial, and efficient accretion regimes, which we relate to the structure of an effective potential. We show that the process is controlled by the ratio between the Schwarzschild radius $R_s$ and the reduced Compton wavelength $\lambdabar_C$. For $R_s \lesssim \lambdabar_C$, the transition is broad and dominated by the angular momentum barrier, while for $R_s > \lambdabar_C$ it sharpens across a narrower range of $k_0$ and a partial-accretion floor emerges at low $k_0$. These results provide a time-domain, Noether-charge-based classification of black hole accretion for massive scalar wave packets.

</details>


### [45] [Gravity-Induced Entanglement of Quantum Clocks as a Signature of Genuinely Quantum Local Position Invariance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19141)
*Eyuri Wakakuwa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出利用量子时钟的引力诱导纠缠（GIE）来检验广义相对论中的等效原理在量子引力机制下是否依然成立，重点关注局域位置不变性（LPI）的量子化版本，并设计了两种实验方案来区分量子性和经典性的LPI违背。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论（general relativity）的基本原理——等效原理（equivalence principle）是否适用于量子引力（quantum gravity）机制，是现代物理学的未解问题。本文旨在探索该原理在引力源可能为量子时是否依然有效。

Method: 将已有的量子局域位置不变性（quantum LPI）表述适配到引力诱导纠缠（gravity-induced entanglement, GIE）框架中，分析两种仅初始时钟状态不同的实验方案：一种在量子性LPI违背时产生纠缠，另一种通过纠缠振荡频率表现经典性LPI违背。

Result: 两种方案分别对应LPI的互补方面：方案一在存在量子性的LPI违背时产生纠缠；方案二则在经典性的LPI违背下通过纠缠振荡频率表现出差异。

Conclusion: 量子时钟的引力诱导纠缠为在量子机制下检验广义相对论的基本原理提供了可行途径，为理解量子力学与引力理论之间的相互作用提供了新视角。

Abstract: Whether the principles of general relativity extend to a quantum regime remains one of the open questions in modern physics. In classical general relativity, Einstein's equivalence principle underpins the interpretation of gravity as spacetime geometry. However, it is not known whether the principle remains valid when the source of gravity could be quantum. Here we show that gravity-induced entanglement (GIE) of quantum clocks provides a framework to characterize local position invariance (LPI) in such a regime, which constitutes one of the subprinciples of the equivalence principle. By adapting the existing formulation of quantum LPI to the context of GIE, we analyze two schemes that address complementary aspects of LPI and differ only in the choice of the initial clock state: one in which entanglement will be generated if and only if there is a genuinely quantum violation of LPI, and the other where classical-like LPI violation manifests in the frequency of entanglement oscillation. Our results suggest that GIE of quantum clocks offers an approach to investigating fundamental principles of general relativity in the quantum regime, shedding new light on the interplay between quantum mechanics and the theory of gravity.

### [46] [A wormhole with two black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19145)
*Gérard Clément*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文报告了四维真空爱因斯坦方程（vacuum Einstein equations）的一个稳态解，该解描述了一个洛伦兹虫洞（Lorentzian wormhole），其中包含两个对跖点共转黑洞（antipodal co-rotating black holes），并通过两根半无限宇宙弦（cosmic strings）悬挂在“另一侧”的类空无穷远（spacelike infinity）处。该度规在几乎全部参数范围内还存在一个裸环奇点（naked ring singularity）。

Method: 通过求解四维真空爱因斯坦方程，获得一个描述洛伦兹虫洞的稳态解析解；该解中的两个黑洞共转（co-rotating），并通过两根半无限宇宙弦连接到另一个类空无穷远区域。

Result: 得到了一个稳态解，其中虫洞两侧各有一个共转黑洞，由正张力或负张力的半无限宇宙弦从“另一侧”类空无穷远处“悬挂”下来。此外，除部分特殊参数取值外，该度规包含一个裸环奇点。

Conclusion: 该解展示了真空爱因斯坦方程在虫洞-黑洞复合系统中存在稳态解的可能性，并揭示了裸环奇点的普遍出现，对理解虫洞稳定性与奇点性质具有重要意义。

Abstract: We report on a stationary solution of the four-dimensional vacuum Einstein equations, which describes a Lorentzian wormhole harboring two antipodal co-rotating black holes. These are hung from the ``other'' spacelike infinity by two semi-infinite cosmic strings with positive or negative tension. The metric also admits a naked ring singularity for almost all values of the parameters.

### [47] [Plasma-Induced Modifications of the Shadows of Rotating Bardeen Black Holes with Perfect Fluid Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19152)
*Gowtham Sidharth M,Sanjit Das*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 通过三种等离子体（plasma）模型研究完美流体暗物质（PFDM）环境中的旋转正则Bardeen黑洞的光学外观，利用事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）的阴影观测数据对等离子体及暗物质参数进行约束，结果表明环境效应会对黑洞阴影产生可测量的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在真实天体物理环境中，黑洞周围往往存在等离子体介质与暗物质，而以往对旋转正则Bardeen黑洞阴影的研究较少同时考虑这些环境因素。本文旨在填补这一空白，探讨等离子体与完美流体暗物质（PFDM）对黑洞阴影形态的联合影响。

Method: 研究在PFDM背景下的旋转正则Bardeen黑洞中，光子通过等离子体介质传播时的光学外观。采用三种等离子体模型：均匀分布（homogeneous distribution）、径向变化分布（radially varying distribution）以及同时依赖径向和角度的普适分布。利用阴影可观测量的方法分析等离子体对光子运动及阴影形态的影响，并使用EHT对阴影圆度（circularity）和分数直径偏差（fractional diameter deviation）的观测限对等离子体与PFDM参数进行约束。

Result: PFDM和等离子体产生的环境效应会对黑洞阴影造成可测量的修正。阴影的形态与大小同时受到暗物质参数和等离子体分布特征的影响。

Conclusion: 黑洞成像观测不仅可用于约束黑洞自身的内禀性质，还能有效限制其周围介质（如等离子体和暗物质）的物理特性，从而为研究旋转正则黑洞周边的天体物理环境提供新的手段。

Abstract: We study the optical appearance of a rotating regular Bardeen black hole embedded in perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM) when photon propagation occurs through a plasma medium. Three plasma models are examined: a homogeneous distribution, a radially varying distribution, and a general distribution with both radial and angular dependence. The influence of plasma on photon motion and the resulting shadow morphology is analysed using shadow observables. To assess astrophysical viability, the plasma and PFDM parameters are constrained using the Event Horizon Telescope bounds on shadow circularity and fractional diameter deviation. The results demonstrate that environmental effects arising from both PFDM and plasma produce measurable modifications to the shadow, indicating that black-hole imaging can provide useful constraints on the surrounding medium as well as the intrinsic properties of regular rotating black holes.

### [48] [Calibration of the AdvancedVirgo+ Gravitational Wave Detector and Reconstruction of the Detector Strain h(t) during the Observing Run O4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19273)
*Virgo Collaboration*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文描述了AdvancedVirgo+引力波探测器在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA O4观测运行期间（O4b和O4c阶段）的校准、应变数据h(t)的重建及其频率相关不确定性的估计，并指出该探测器尽管灵敏度有限（约55 Mpc），但其加入网络有效提升了源参数估计精度，尤其是天区定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为支持LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组的O4观测运行（于2023年5月24日启动），AdvancedVirgo+探测器需在O4b和O4c阶段参与网络观测，因此需要对其探测器应变数据h(t)进行在线与离线的校准与重构，并量化相应的频率相关不确定性，以便用于引力波（gravitational wave, GW）源参数的精确估计。

Method: 探测器校准基于辅助执行器、牛顿校准器（Newtonian Calibrators）和光子校准器（Photon Calibrators）。应变数据h(t)的重建采用线性噪声扣除（linear noise subtraction）方法，在线处理延迟约10秒。离线版本（AnalysisReady strain data）大多与在线数据相同，但更新了频率相关的不确定度信息。

Result: 在线探测到约173个瞬态引力波（transient gravitational wave）源，均为涉及黑洞和中子星的致密双星并合（coalescences of binary compact objects）。Virgo的灵敏度限制在约55 Mpc，但其加入网络改善了源参数估计，尤其是天区定位（sky localisation）。在10–2000 Hz频段内，振幅不确定度约为2–3%，相位不确定度低于30 mrad，但在50 Hz和150 Hz附近不确定度较大。

Conclusion: AdvancedVirgo+探测器在O4运行期间成功完成了应变数据的在线与离线校准和重构。生成的AnalysisReady应变数据及关联不确定性已被用于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA离线数据分析，并通过引力波开放科学中心（Gravitational Wave Open Science Center, GWOSC）公开发布。

Abstract: From 10 April 2024 15:00 UTC to 18 November 2025 16:00 UTC, the AdvancedVirgo+ gravitational wave detector participated in the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA O4 observing run, started on 24 May 2023 15:00 UTC. Around 173 transient gravitational wave (GW) sources, all corresponding to coalescences of binary compact objects involving black holes and neutron stars, were detected online during the two run periods O4b and O4c when Virgo was taking data in the detector network. Despite its sensitivity being limited around 55 Mpc, the inclusion of Virgo into the network allowed to improve the accuracy of the source parameter estimation, in particular the sky localisation of the detected events. This article describes the AdvancedVirgo+ detector calibration and the reconstruction of the detector strain h(t) during O4, as well as the estimation of the associated frequency-dependent uncertainties. The detector calibration is based on auxiliary actuators, Newtonian Calibrators and Photon Calibrators, described in other publications. The h(t) reconstruction, including linear noise subtraction, was processed online with a latency of about 10 s. The so-called AnalysisReady strain data were then produced offline. Most of the time, the strain time series was a copy of the online time series, but with updated frequency-dependent uncertainties, around 2-3% in amplitude and below 30 mrad in phase in the 10-2000 Hz frequency band, with the exception of larger uncertainties around 50 Hz and 150 Hz. The AnalysisReady strain data and associated uncertainties have been used for the offline LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA data analysis and are also the data made publicly available through the Gravitational Wave Open Science Center (GWOSC).

</details>

Xu,Y. Xu,N. Yadav,H. Yamamoto,K. Yamamoto,T. S. Yamamoto,T. Yamamoto,R. Yamazaki,T. Yan,H. Yang,K. Z. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yarbrough,J. Yébana Carrilero,A. B. Yelikar,X. Yin,J. Yokoyama,T. Yokozawa,M. Yoshihara,S. Yuan,H. Yuzurihara,M. Zanatta,M. Zanolin,M. Zeeshan,T. Zelenova,J. -P. Zendri,M. Zeoli,M. Zerrad,M. Zevin,H. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,N. Zhang,R. Zhang,T. Zhang,C. Zhao,J. Zhao,Yue Zhao,Yuhang Zhao,L. -M. Zheng,Y. Zheng,L. Zhizhong,H. Zhong,H. Zhou,H. O. Zhu,X. -J. Zhu,Z. -H. Zhu,Z. Zhu,D. Z. Zieba,A. B. Zimmerman,L. Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 基于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA引力波探测器网络的第五次引力波瞬变目录（GWTC-5.0），对168个高置信度双星引力波事件进行了七项广义相对论（general relativity, GR）检验，未发现任何超出GR的新物理证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA探测器网络的引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）信号，在引力场的动力学和强场区域对广义相对论（general relativity, GR）进行高精度检验。

Method: 从GWTC-5.0目录中选取至少被两台探测器观测到且误报率≤10⁻³ yr⁻¹的168个高置信度事件（含第四轮观测期O4b的72个事件和O4a更新后的5个事件），开展七项GR检验，包括残差分析、额外极化检验、后牛顿（post-Newtonian）系数偏差约束以及时域和频域铃宕（ringdown）分析。

Result: 所有事件的残差与探测器噪声一致；未发现GR预测之外的额外极化证据；对GR后牛顿系数的偏离约束提升了1.2–2.6倍。铃宕分析中，GW240621_195059的合并后数据与主导四极（ℓ=|m|=2）模及其第一泛音一致。综合结果显示与GR的偏离较GWTC-4.0有所改善，尤其得益于信噪比76.9的GW250114事件。

Conclusion: 在所有检验中均未发现超出GR的新物理证据，但频域铃宕分析中GR预测值位于联合结果的尾部，这可能受限于当前目录的大小。

Abstract: The signals from the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA network of gravitational-wave (GW) detectors allow us to perform sensitive tests of general relativity (GR) in the dynamical and strong-field regime of gravity. We present the results of seven tests of GR using the observed binary signals in the fifth GW Transient Catalog (GWTC-5.0), i.e., up to and including the second part of the fourth observing run (O4b). We restrict our analysis to the confident signals, henceforth called events, observed by at least two detectors that have estimated false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \ \rm{yr}^{-1}$. These include 72 events from O4b and five events from the first part of the fourth observing run that are now analyzed due to their increased significance from updated search results, bringing the total number of events for tests of GR in the cumulative GWTC to 168. After subtracting the best-fit waveforms, we find the residuals are consistent with detector noise for all events considered. We also find no strong evidence for additional polarizations beyond those predicted by GR. We perform tests of GW generation, improving the constraints on deviations from the GR post-Newtonian coefficients by factors of 1.2-2.6. Finally, we find overall consistency of the remnants with GR using both time- and frequency-domain methods. For GW240621_195059, postmerger data are consistent with the dominant quadrupolar ($\ell=|m|=2$) mode of a Kerr black hole and its first overtone, with spurious high-frequency content preventing a spectroscopic constraint of GR. In the frequency-domain ringdown analysis, the GR prediction lies in the tails of the combined results, possibly due to the limited catalog size. However, the combined results indicate improved consistency with GR over GWTC-4.0, owing to the contribution of GW250114 with a network matched-filter signal-to-noise ratio of 76.9. Overall, we find no evidence for physics beyond GR.

</details>


### [50] [Gravitational wave echoes as probes of the maximum mass of strange stars in quadratic curvature-matter coupled gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19298)
*Debadri Bhattacharjee,Pradip Kumar Chattopadhyay,Kazuharu Bamba*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在含非最小物质耦合的二次曲率引力（quadratic curvature gravity）框架下，研究MIT袋模型（MIT bag model）描述的奇异星（strange stars）能否形成光子球（photon sphere）并产生引力波回波（gravitational wave echoes）。通过求解修正的Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff方程，发现该理论允许更致密的恒星结构，且回波约束给出了比流体静力学平衡更严格的最大质量-半径上限，表明后并合奇异星可作为引力波回波源，并为修正引力与高频引力波提供探测途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波天文学为精确研究奇异致密星提供了重要途径。GW170817事件后并合阶段可能观测到的引力波回波（significance $4.2σ$，主导频率~72 Hz）可能来源于具有光子球的超致密遗迹。然而，在广义相对论中，光子球形成要求恒星致密性（compactness）在1/3到4/9之间，即使是合理的物态方程也难以满足。因此，本文旨在探索在含非最小物质耦合的二次曲率引力下，MIT袋模型奇异星能否实现这一可能性。

Method: 采用MIT袋模型物态方程描述奇异星，在含非最小物质耦合的二次曲率引力框架下，求解修正的Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV)方程，得到质量-半径关系，并识别能够支持光子球和引力波回波的构型。

Result: 在该框架中，修正的Buchdahl极限允许更致密的恒星解，光子球约束则限制了可行的参数空间。增大袋常数（bag constant）会降低最大质量和回波时间（echo time），使回波频率向kHz频段移动。回波约束给出的最大质量-半径限制比流体静力学平衡更为严格，从而提出了奇异星修正的最大质量上限。

Conclusion: 后并合奇异星具有作为引力波回波源的潜力，引力波回波可作为探测修正引力和高频引力波的有效探针。

Abstract: Gravitational wave astronomy provides an exemplary avenue to study exotic compact stars with utmost precision. Recent analyses of GW170817 have reported possible post-merger gravitational wave echoes with a significance of $4.2σ$ and a dominant frequency near $72$ Hz. Such echoes may originate from ultracompact remnants possessing photon spheres that partially trap gravitational perturbations. In general relativity, photon-sphere formation requires the stellar compactness to lie within one-third and four-ninths, which is challenging even for a realistic equations of state. Here, we explore this possibility in quadratic curvature gravity with non-minimal matter coupling, considering strange stars described by the MIT bag model equation of state. By solving the modified Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations, we obtain the mass-radius relations and identify configurations capable of supporting photon spheres and GW echoes. In the proposed framework, the modified Buchdahl limit allows more compact stellar solutions, while photon-sphere constraints restrict the viable parameter space. We find that increasing the bag constant, decreases the maximum mass and echo time, shifting the echo frequency toward the kHz regime. The echo constraints yield more stringent maximum mass-radius limits than hydrostatic equilibrium, suggesting a revised maximum mass bounds for strange stars. These results highlight the potential of post-merger strange stars as GW echo sources and demonstrate the role of echoes as probes of modified gravity and high-frequency gravitational waves.

</details>


### [51] [Optomechanical transfer factors for scattered light noise estimations in the beamtubes of ground-based gravitational wave detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19299)
*M. Andrés-Carcasona*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过改进的分析传递因子（analytical transfer factors），将法布里-珀罗臂腔（Fabry-Pérot arm cavities）中的散射光（scattered light）场扰动完整转换为等效应变噪声（equivalent strain noise），在辐射压耦合（radiation-pressure coupling）、信号提取动力学（signal-extraction dynamics）、微观失谐（microscopic detunings）及零差读出角（homodyne readout angle）等效应下，为当前及未来引力波探测器提供了更完整的散射光噪声估计框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前地基引力波探测器中散射光是一个相关的噪声源，而波束管散射光（beamtube scattered light）估计通常依赖光学传播模拟与未完全传播干涉仪频域光机响应（optomechanical response）的分析耦合，缺乏对完整频率依赖效应的处理。

Method: 使用改进的分析传递因子，将法布里-珀罗臂腔中散射光场扰动转换为等效应变噪声，一致地引入辐射压耦合、信号提取动力学、微观失谐及零差读出角效应；完整保留散射场的振幅和相位正交分量（amplitude and phase quadrature content），包括衍射（diffraction）和反向散射噪声（backscattering noise）中的交叉项（cross terms），并识别了衍射中线性化耦合到挡板运动（baffle motion）的有效区间。

Result: 基于LIGO、Cosmic Explorer (CE) 和 Einstein Telescope - Low Frequency (ET-LF) 配置的分析表明，在相位主导（phase dominated）区域中该形式恢复传统估计，但在辐射压耦合、正交相关性（quadrature correlations）或失谐信号提取起作用时存在差异；特别是由于失谐信号提取腔（detuned signal extraction cavity），修正后的ET-LF估计相对于之前的波束管噪声预算（beamtube noise budgets）发生了显著变化。

Conclusion: 该工作为当前及未来引力波探测器的散射光噪声估计提供了一个更完整的框架。

Abstract: Scattered light is a relevant noise source in current ground-based gravitational-wave detectors and a critical design concern for next-generation observatories. Beamtube scattered light estimates usually combine optical propagation simulations with analytical couplings that do not fully propagate the frequency-dependent optomechanical response of the interferometer to the strain readout. In this work, we use improved analytical transfer factors to convert scattered-light field perturbations in the Fabry--Pérot arm cavities into equivalent strain noise, consistently including radiation-pressure coupling, signal-extraction dynamics, microscopic detunings, and the homodyne readout angle. The formalism keeps the full amplitude and phase quadrature content of the scattered field, including the cross terms that arise in both diffraction and backscattering noise. For diffraction, we also identify the regime in which the linearized coupling to baffle motion is valid, avoiding unnecessary phase wrapping. Using representative LIGO, Cosmic Explorer (CE), and Einstein Telescope - Low Frequency (ET-LF) configurations, we show that legacy estimates are recovered in phase dominated regimes, but can differ when radiation-pressure coupling, quadrature correlations, or detuned signal extraction become important. In particular, the revised ET-LF estimate changes substantially with respect to previous beamtube noise budgets due to the detuned signal extraction cavity. These results provide a more complete framework for scattered light noise estimations for present and future gravitational-wave detectors.

</details>

### [52] [Laplace operators on quantum graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18473)
*Arkadiusz Bochniak,Dawid Jasiński,Paweł Kasprzak*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 本文在算子系统（operator-system）框架下引入了一类与量子图（quantum graph）相关联的拉普拉斯算子（Laplace operator），通过识别特定内积（inner product）使得投影算子正交，从而定义了量子版本的关联算子（incidence operator）和拉普拉斯算子，并将谱图论（spectral graph theory）的基本构造推广到了算子代数（operator-algebraic）框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的量子图研究缺乏统一的算子代数框架来定义类似经典谱图论中的拉普拉斯算子，本文旨在填补这一空白，在算子系统框架下建立量子图的谱理论（spectral theory），从而为量子信息论（quantum information theory）和非交换几何（noncommutative geometry）提供新联系。

Method: 首先研究量子图在舒尔积（Schur product）和转置（transposition）下的结构性质；然后在矩阵空间上识别出一种特定的内积，使得量子图底层算子系统上的投影算子是正交的；基于此定义量子版本的关联算子和相应的拉普拉斯算子，并与近期提出的替代定义进行比较。

Result: 成功定义了一类与量子图相关联的拉普拉斯算子集合，并通过若干量子图家族对该构造进行了验证和比较。

Conclusion: 该工作将经典谱图论的基本构造扩展到了算子代数框架中，朝着建立量子图谱理论迈出了一步，同时揭示了量子信息论和非交换几何之间的新关联。

Abstract: We introduce a class of Laplace operators associated with quantum graphs in the operator-system framework. To this end, we investigate structural properties of quantum graphs related to the Schur product and transposition. Our main innovation is the identification of a specific inner product on the space of matrices with respect to which the projection onto the operator system underlying a quantum graph is orthogonal. This enables us to define a quantum analogue of the classical incidence operator and the associated Laplace operator. We compare this construction with a recently proposed alternative definition and examine the resulting Laplace operators for several families of quantum graphs. These results extend fundamental constructions from spectral graph theory to the operator-algebraic setting, providing a step toward a spectral theory of quantum graphs that generalizes classical graph-theoretic concepts while revealing new connections with quantum information theory and noncommutative geometry.

</details>

### [53] [Variational formulation for the dynamics of soft matter including inertia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18457)
*Andrew J Archer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文展示了如何扩展昂萨格变分原理（Onsager's variational principle），使其在阻尼/耗散与惯性同等重要的情形下仍然有效，从而统一描述过阻尼（over-damped）和欠阻尼（under-damped）运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 昂萨格变分原理在黏性主导的过阻尼体系（如胶体流体、液滴表面运动）中已被广泛应用，但其忽略了惯性（inertia）。然而，惯性在某些系统中不可忽视，会表现为振动和欠阻尼运动。因此，需要将该变分框架推广至阻尼与惯性均重要的情形。

Method: 作者通过扩展昂萨格变分原理，使其不再忽略惯性项，从而在等温条件下同时适用于过阻尼和欠阻尼（惯性主导）的流体及软物质运动方程推导。

Result: 该扩展后的变分框架在阻尼/耗散与惯性同等重要的系统中依然有效，能够统一生成包含惯性效应的运动方程。

Conclusion: 该工作将昂萨格变分原理的适用性从纯黏性（过阻尼）情形推广至惯性与耗散共存的一般情形，为软物质和流体动力学提供了一种统一的变分方法。

Abstract: The motion of liquids and soft matter is over-damped and `slow' when viscosity dominates. In this (low Reynolds-number) limit and when the system is isothermal, the equations of motion may be generated via Onsager's variational principle, which neglects inertia. This variational approach is immensely powerful, being used to obtain equations of motion for colloidal fluids, droplets on surfaces and much more. However, inertia can play a role, manifesting as vibrations and under-damped motion. Here we show how to extend this variational framework so that it remains valid for when damping/dissipation and inertia are both equally important.

</details>


### [54] [Isosbestic points in time resolved SAXS: from spectroscopic analogy to model free structural markers during colloidal gelation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18954)
*Alain Gibaud,Wilbert J. Smit,Safa Jamali,Thomas Gibaud*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了Ludox胶体在盐诱导凝胶化过程中出现的两个等吸收点（isosbestic points）的物理意义：高波矢等吸收点q₂是粒子接触距离决定的通用几何标记，低波矢等吸收点q₁来自Porod不变量的守恒，并定义了无量纲参数Φ(t/t_g)作为无模型、尺度分辨的凝胶化指纹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 凝胶化（gelation）是从流体态转变为非平衡软固体网络的过程，该过程中时间分辨小角X射线散射（SAXS）会出现等吸收点，但其物理意义此前尚不明确。本文旨在阐明这些等吸收点的物理本质及其在软物质转变中的角色。

Method: 通过时间分辨小角X射线散射（time-resolved SAXS）实验观测盐诱导Ludox胶体凝胶化过程中的散射信号，结合Porod不变量（Porod invariant）的分解以及倒易空间（reciprocal-space）区域划分，定义无量纲参数Φ(t/t_g)来描述凝胶化进程。

Result: 发现两个等吸收点q₁和q₂分别反映不同的结构约束：q₂是粒子接触距离决定的通用几何标记（geometric marker），q₁源于Porod不变量的守恒，用于分隔快速形成的局域团簇（local clusters）与生长的介观网络（mesoscopic network）。Φ(t/t_g)的S形演化提供了无模型、尺度分辨的凝胶化指纹。S(q_min,t)与S(q→0,t)的联合演化建立了联系局域结构、全局连通性与散射特征的定量框架。

Conclusion: 等吸收点并非源自简单的二组分互变，而是反映了凝胶化过程中的基本结构约束。所提出的定量框架为理解软物质转变中等吸收点的作用提供了清晰的理论基础。

Abstract: Gelation is the transition from a fluid state into a system-spanning, out of equilibrim soft-solid network through a hierarchical process that couples local particle interactions to mesoscopic clustering and global connectivity. In time-resolved small-angle X-ray scattering (SAXS), isosbestic points -- scattering wavevectors where scattering intensity remains invariant -- emerge during this transformation, yet their physical meaning has remained unclear. Here, we show that two isosbestic points, $q_1$ and $q_2$, observed during salt-induced gelation of Ludox colloids, reflect fundamental structural constraints rather than a two-species interconversion. The high-$q$ point $q_2$ is a universal geometric marker, determined by particle contact distances, while the low-$q$ point $q_1$ arises from Porod invariant conservation and separates rapidly arrested local clusters from the growing mesoscopic network. By decomposing the Porod invariant across the reciprocal-space regions defined by these points, we define a dimensionless parameter, $Φ(t/t_g)$, whose sigmoidal evolution provides a simple, model-free, scale-resolved fingerprint of gelation. Together with the combined evolution of $S(q_{\min},t)$ and $S(q \rightarrow 0,t)$, these results establish a quantitative model free framework linking local structuring, global connectivity, and scattering signatures, clarifying the role of isosbestic points in soft-matter transformations.

</details>


### [55] [Activity and Competing Length Scales in an Anomalous Core-Softened Fluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19024)
*Davi Felipe Kray Silva,Thiago Puccinelli,Walas Silva-Oliveira,Leandro B. Krott,José Rafael Bordin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究活性布朗粒子（Active Brownian Particles）通过类斜坡核软化势（ramp-like core-softened potential）相互作用时的结构与动力学。发现活性（activity）会抑制被动流体中的水样反常（water-like anomalies），其机制在于活性促进了两种局域环境（local environments）之间的粒子转移，减弱了导致反常响应的结构竞争（structural competition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性与竞争性相互作用长度尺度（competing interaction length scales）之间的相互作用在软物质和生物系统中具有重要意义，但目前尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 研究采用活性布朗粒子模型，粒子间通过呈现水样反常平衡行为的类斜坡核软化势相互作用。通过沿两条代表性等温线（一条在反常区域内，另一条在其上方）在较宽密度范围内改变活性，考察自推进（self-propulsion）对流体结构和动力学的修正。利用迭代玻尔兹曼反演（iterative Boltzmann inversion）从稳态对关联（steady-state pair correlations）构建有效相互作用（effective interactions），以获取微观尺度的理解。

Result: 活性逐步抑制了被动流体的反常现象，但在归一化量中仍可观察到潜在结构交叉（structural crossover）的特征。有效相互作用表明，自推进降低了局域环境之间的区分度，促进了两种特征长度尺度之间的粒子转移。

Conclusion: 活性主要通过促进两种局域环境之间的粒子转移来发挥作用，从而削弱导致反常响应的结构竞争。

Abstract: The interplay between activity and competing interaction length scales remains largely unexplored, despite its relevance to many soft and biological systems. Here, we study Active Brownian Particles interacting through a ramp-like core-softened potential that exhibits water-like anomalies in equilibrium. By varying the activity over a broad range of densities along two representative isotherms, one within the anomalous region and the other above it, we examine how self-propulsion modifies the structure and dynamics of the fluid. To gain microscopic insight into these changes, we construct effective interactions from the steady-state pair correlations using iterative Boltzmann inversion. We find that activity progressively suppresses the anomalies of the passive fluid, although signatures of the underlying structural crossover remain visible in normalized quantities. The effective interactions reveal that self-propulsion lowers the distinction between the local environments and facilitates population transfer between the two characteristic length scales. These results indicate that activity primarily acts by facilitating population transfer between the two local environments, thereby reducing the structural competition responsible for the anomalous response.

</details>


### [56] [Auxetic behaviour in crystals of hard polyhedra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19130)
*Rinske M. Alkemade,Silvana A. Caipa Cure,Alptuğ Ulugöl,Andrea Plati,Vera Belde,Haadi Naqvi,Felix Verbiest,Giuseppe Foffi,Daniela Kraft,Frank Smallenburg,Laura Filion*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和模拟研究了由空间填充硬多边形/多面体构成的晶体，发现其中部分系统仅凭熵和几何的相互作用即可展现出部分拉胀（auxetic）行为，并在胶体与颗粒两种实验体系中验证了这一现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拉胀材料（auxetic materials）具有反直觉的力学性质，即在某一方向受压时垂直方向也收缩；已知的大多数拉胀材料依赖刚性各向异性单元铰链连接，在微观尺度上实验实现困难。本文旨在探索是否能在更简单、仅由几何和熵驱动的体系中实现拉胀行为。

Method: 研究了六种由离散的空间填充硬多边形或硬多面体（space-filling hard polygons/polyhedra）构成的晶体，分析其弹性行为；并构建了两种实验体系：由布朗运动（Brownian motion）驱动的胶体粒子（colloidal particles）和由外部振动驱动的颗粒粒子（granular particles），均采用方形粒子实现。

Result: 部分所研究的硬粒子晶体展现出部分拉胀行为（partial auxetic behaviour），该行为仅源于熵（entropy）与几何结构（geometry）的相互作用；两种实验体系（胶体与颗粒）均证实了拉胀性的出现。

Conclusion: 仅依靠熵与几何的相互作用即可在简单硬粒子体系中实现拉胀行为，无需复杂的铰链连接结构，且该现象在微观（胶体）与宏观（颗粒）尺度均具有可行性与鲁棒性（robustness）。

Abstract: Auxetic materials - systems that, when subjected to a compression in one direction, also compress in one or more perpendicular directions - have intrigued researchers for decades due to their counterintuitive mechanical properties. Their unique behaviour gives auxetic materials potential for a wide range of applications such as shock absorbers, and electrodes in piezoelectric sensors. Most known auxetic materials are realized by connecting rigid, anisotropic units in a hinging manner, which are systems that often are hard to realize experimentally on the microscopic scale. Here, we explore the elastic behaviour of six crystals composed of discrete space-filling hard polygons or polyhedra. We show that some of these systems show partial auxetic behaviour, emerging from the interplay of entropy and geometry alone. To demonstrate the feasibility and robustness of this phenomenon, we create two experimental realizations of square-shaped particles, spanning both colloidal particles driven by Brownian motion and granular particles driven by external vibrations, and confirm the emergence of auxeticity in both cases.

</details>


### [57] [One geometric barrier unifies melting, vitrification and jamming of hard spheres in all dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19185)
*Sujin B Babu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文从三个精确几何要素推导出林德曼判据（Lindemann criterion），建立了无参数主方程，在d=3–12维度上准确定位了动力学玻璃转变、随机密堆积、Kauzmann点、玻璃密堆积和平衡晶体熔化五个关键相变点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 林德曼判据（Lindemann criterion）作为固体失稳的经验规则已沿用超过一个世纪，其数值虽被模式耦合理论（mode-coupling theory）和副本理论（replica theory）复现，但从未被一个简单可验证的论证所孤立解释。

Method: 方法基于三个精确几何要素：接触定理（contact theorem）从状态方程固定配位数；各向同性恒等式（isotropy identity）确定非接触邻居向逃逸方向的投影；以及首次通过论证（first-passage argument）推导出基本跳跃跨越一个粒子间距而非一个粒子直径。

Result: 无参数主方程在d=3–12维上定位了五个关键点（动力学玻璃转变、随机密堆积、Kauzmann点、玻璃密堆积、平衡晶体熔化），精度在独立模拟和副本理论值的百分之几以内，并将所有五个点置于单一势垒面上。理论预测了林德曼常数在三维中为0.13倍邻居间距，并随维度增加系统性地下降。在二维中预测了体积分数η_g=0.781处的阻滞、η=0.832处的堵塞以及两步熔化过程，均已获独立模拟和实验验证。

Conclusion: 该理论不仅为林德曼判据提供了基于几何的严格推导，还统一描述了多个相变现象，并做出了可验证的定量预测，表明该几何框架具有跨维度的普适性。

Abstract: The Lindemann criterion that a solid loses stability once atomic vibrations reach roughly a tenth of the interparticle spacing, has remained an empirical rule for over a century. The numerical value was reproduced by mode-coupling and replica theories but never isolated as the consequence of a simple, verifiable argument. Here we show that for hard spheres in $d$ dimensions the rule follows from three exact geometric ingredients. The contact theorem fixing the coordination number from the equation of state, an isotropy identity fixing how non touching neighbors project onto an escape direction, and a first-passage argument which is derived, in which the elementary hop spans one interparticle spacing rather than one particle diameter. The resulting parameter-free master equation locates the kinetic glass transition, random close packing, the Kauzmann point, glass close packing, and equilibrium crystal melting in $d=3$--$12$, each to within a few per cent of reported independent simulation and replica-theory values, and places all five on a single barrier surface. The theory makes two predictions that are verifiable, the Lindemann constant, $\c_L(3)=0.13$ per neighbor spacing in $3$ dimensions derived from the theory, which must fall systematically with increasing dimensions. The other being in two dimensions, the current theory predicts the arrest in the volume fraction $η_g=0.781$, the jamming at $η=0.832$, and both steps of the two-stage melting scenario, all of which are already corroborated by independent simulations and experiments.

</details>


### [58] [Entropy power functional theory for Brownian many-body dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19255)
*Matthias Schmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种形式精确的变分方案（variational scheme），用于描述一般时空非平衡条件下过阻尼布朗动力学（overdamped Brownian dynamics）中具有成对相互作用的多体系统。该方案基于自由功率最小化原理（free power minimization principle），瞬时确定单体流（one-body current）和全局粒子间距通量（global interparticle distance flux），并引入内禀自由功率泛函（intrinsic free power functional）分解为熵速率（entropic rate）与能量速率（energetic rate），后者被显式处理。熵速率的绝热贡献（adiabatic contribution）源自平衡熵元密度泛函（equilibrium entropy metadensity functional）的时间导数，而真实的非平衡效应（nonequilibrium effects）则源于一个普适的超功率泛函（superpower functional）。两个连续性方程（continuity equations）构成该动力学描述的闭合框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多体非平衡统计力学方法在处理过阻尼布朗动力学时缺乏形式精确的变分框架，尤其在描述瞬时流和粒子间距通量方面存在局限。该工作旨在建立一个严格且普适的变分原理，以统一处理熵与能量速率的贡献，并明确非平衡效应的来源。

Method: 通过构建一个联合自由功率最小化原则（joint free power minimization principle），在瞬时层面上同时优化单体流和全局粒子间距通量。将内禀自由功率泛函分解为熵速率部分与能量速率部分，其中能量速率被显式处理；熵速率的绝热部分由平衡熵元密度泛函的时间导数给出，而非平衡部分由普适的熵超功率泛函（entropy superpower functional）描述。最后利用两个连续性方程闭合整个动力学方程组。

Result: 得到了一个形式精确的变分方案，能瞬时确定过阻尼布朗多体系统中的单体流与全局粒子间距通量，并区分了熵速率中的绝热贡献与真正的非平衡贡献。非平衡效应的核心来源被归结为一个普适的熵超功率泛函，两个连续性方程保证了动力学描述的闭合性。

Conclusion: 该工作为一般非平衡条件下过阻尼布朗多体系统的动力学提供了严格且系统的变分框架，阐明了非平衡效应的本质来源，为后续研究奠定了形式基础。

Abstract: We present a formally exact variational scheme for the overdamped Brownian dynamics of pairwise interacting many-body systems in general spatiotemporal nonequilibrium. A joint free power minimization principle determines instantaneously the one-body current and the global interparticle distance flux. The intrinsic free power functional splits into entropic and energetic rates, where the latter are treated explicitly. The adiabatic contribution to the entropy rate is the time derivative of the equilibrium entropy metadensity functional. Genuine nonequilibrium effects originate from a universal entropy superpower functional. Two continuity equations close the dynamical description.

</details>

### [59] [Search for new scalars via $X \rightarrow SH \rightarrow b\bar{b}b\bar{b}$ in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18484)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用ATLAS实验在大型强子对撞机（LHC）Run 2期间采集的质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量√s = 13 TeV，积分亮度126–136 fb⁻¹），寻找通过X → HS → (b\bar{b})(b\bar{b})级联衰变产生的标量共振X。研究覆盖X质量300 GeV–6 TeV、S质量70 GeV–5 TeV范围，未发现超出标准模型（Standard Model）背景的显著信号，在95%置信水平上设定产生截面乘以分支比的上限为0.7 fb至2.6 pb。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理信号，特别是涉及额外标量粒子的级联衰变过程，以探索高能物理中可能存在的扩展希格斯（Higgs）扇区。

Method: 采用两种事件拓扑结构：希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）由单个大半径喷注（large-radius jet）重建，或由一对小半径喷注（small-radius jets）重建。主要多喷注（multijet）和t\bar{t}本底通过基于高斯过程（Gaussian processes）和归一化流（normalizing flows）的层次模型（hierarchical model）进行估计。

Result: 未观察到超出标准模型背景预期的显著信号；在95%置信水平上设定产生截面乘以分支比的上限，范围为0.7 fb至2.6 pb。

Conclusion: 在质量区间300 GeV–6 TeV（X）和70 GeV–5 TeV（S）内，未发现支持新标量共振存在的证据，给出的排除限对相应参数空间中的新物理搜索具有约束意义。

Abstract: A search is performed for a scalar resonance X decaying into a Standard Model Higgs boson H and an additional scalar S, each decaying into a bottom-antibottom-quark pair, giving a $b\bar{b}b\bar{b}$ final state. Two event topologies are considered, depending on whether the Higgs boson is reconstructed from a single large-radius jet or from a pair of small-radius jets. The analysis uses proton-proton collision data at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV, collected by the ATLAS experiment at the Large Hadron Collider during Run 2, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 126-136 fb$^{-1}$ depending on the topology and the associated triggers. The search covers masses of 300 GeV-6 TeV for X and 70 GeV-5 TeV for S. The dominant multijet and $t\bar{t}$ backgrounds are estimated with a hierarchical model using Gaussian processes and normalizing flows. No significant excess over the Standard Model background expectation is observed. Upper limits at 95% confidence level are set on the production cross-section times branching ratio, ranging from 0.7 fb to 2.6 pb.

Method: 作为一篇综述文章，通过整理和分析超外围碰撞中光子的产生机制及相关实验与理论研究，系统呈现其物理应用。

Result: 识别出三个主要应用方向：低Bjorken-x下的核结构研究、最高能量光子对超越标准模型物理的探测、以及无共同起源的双光子源干涉测量对量子力学新机制的探索。

Abstract: Photons in ultra-peripheral collisions of heavy ions (and protons) can be used for a variety of physics purposes - for studies of nuclear structure at low Bjorken$-x$, as probes of beyond-standard-model physics at the highest possible photon energies, and to explore new regimes of quantum mechanics via interferometry between two photon sources that share no common origin. This review will present the origins of photons in ultra-peripheral collisions and discuss the important physics that is being done with these photons, with particular emphasis on those on the energy frontier for photon physics.

### [61] [Analysis Preservation and Reproducibility in Collider Physics: An ADL/CutLang Implementation of ATLAS Open Data Analyses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19034)
*Aytül Adıgüzel,Ahmetcan Sansar,Kağan Şahan,Kürşat Karaca*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出并验证了分析描述语言（Analysis Description Language, ADL）及其实时解释器CutLang，作为一种用于高能物理中对撞数据物理分析描述、执行与保存的可持续解决方案。通过在ATLAS开放数据框架中重新实现多项基准分析，证明了ADL/CutLang工作流能够可靠地替代传统分析框架，并推动分析保存与可重复性问题的解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理中长期存在分析保存（analysis preservation）与分析可重复性（analysis reproducibility）的挑战，主要原因在于物理逻辑与实验特定软件基础设施之间的紧密耦合。摘要旨在通过ADL/CutLang解耦物理逻辑与传统框架，探索一种可持续的分析保存方案。

Method: 使用ADL（一种专为对撞物理设计的领域特定语言，domain-specific language）以人类可读形式描述物理对象和事件选择标准；通过CutLang运行时直接解释执行ADL描述，无需翻译为通用编程语言，将生成的事件选择结果直接输入统计工具。

Result: 基于ATLAS开放数据（质心能量13 TeV，积分亮度10 fb⁻¹）的C++框架重新实现了多项基准分析，结果与原发表文献高度一致，验证了ADL/CutLang工作流的可靠性。

Conclusion: ADL/CutLang可作为传统分析框架的可靠替代方案；研究同时评估了CutLang现有能力并指出待开发方向，为LHC（Large Hadron Collider）社区更广泛采用基于ADL的分析保存提供了路线图。

Abstract: Analysis Description Language (ADL) and the CutLang runtime interpreter offer an innovative and sustainable solution for describing, executing, and preserving the physics content of collider data analyses. In this solution, all physics objects and event selection criteria are expressed in a human-readable form using ADL, a domain-specific language designed for collider physics. ADL descriptions are interpreted directly at runtime by CutLang without translation into a general-purpose programming language, producing event selections that can be readily fed into statistical analysis tools. This approach addresses the long-standing challenge of analysis preservation and analysis reproducibility in high energy physics by decoupling the physics logic from experiment-specific software infrastructures.
  In this study, several benchmark analyses within ATLAS Open Data C++ Framework are reimplemented in ADL and executed with CutLang using data provided by ATLAS Open Data at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV and corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 10 fb$^{-1}$. The reimplemented analyses yield results in good agreement with the original publications, validating the ADL/CutLang workflow as a reliable alternative to traditional analysis frameworks. The study also provides a detailed assessment of CutLang's current capabilities and identifies areas for further development, offering a roadmap toward broader adoption of ADL-based analysis preservation in the LHC community.

</details>


### [62] [Dark matter searches with a 13 meV threshold superconducting sensor array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19319)
*Christopher Albert,Lanqing Yuan,Jacob Harris,Ritoban Basu Thakur,Andrew Bear,Karl K. Berggren,Christopher Cappiello,Christopher Curwen,Peter Day,Byeong H. Eom,Arjun Ghosh,William Ho,Nikita Klimovich,Henry G. LeDuc,Karthik Ramanathan,Alejandro Simon*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: QUALIPHIDE实验利用41像素的微波动力学电感探测器（microwave kinetic inductance detectors）阵列，以13 meV能量阈值同时搜索太赫兹波段隐藏光子暗物质（hidden photon dark matter）和粒子状轻暗物质（light dark matter）的散射信号。22小时盲分析未发现显著超出，在13–90 meV/c²质量范围内对隐藏光子动力学混合参数χ设定了最强限制（在50 meV/c²处达1.5×10⁻¹²），并在核与电子散射暗物质探测领域给出了最早的地面极限之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多动机良好的暗物质模型预言与地面实验相互作用时会产生meV量级的能量沉积，但该能量区间因缺乏成熟的单量子探测器而难以探测。QUALIPHIDE实验旨在填补这一探测空白。

Method: 采用41像素能量分辨微波动力学电感探测器阵列，能量阈值低至13 meV，同时搜索隐藏光子暗物质产生的转换光子（conversion photons）和轻暗物质散射产生的声子（phonons）。针对隐藏光子搜索，设计了聚焦与非聚焦像素，构建数据驱动的本底模型，实现具有发现潜力的盲分析。

Result: 22小时数据盲分析未发现显著超出，在13–90 meV/c²质量范围内对隐藏光子动力学混合参数χ设定了最强约束，在50 meV/c²处达到1.5×10⁻¹²。该数据还给出了暗物质与核（低至5 MeV/c²）及电子（低至20 keV/c²）散射的最早地面极限之一。

Conclusion: QUALIPHIDE实验证明了低阈值微波动力学电感探测器在meV暗物质搜索中的有效性。低能量阈值不仅为当前探测提供了优势，还为未来研究低温探测器中的低能过量（low-energy excess）以及开展太赫兹标度QCD轴子（QCD axion）搜索奠定了基础。

Abstract: Many well-motivated dark matter models predict meV-scale energy deposits in interactions with terrestrial experiments, but this regime is challenging to probe due to a lack of mature single-quantum detectors. Here we report results from QUALIPHIDE (QUAntum LImited PHotons In the Dark Experiment), a cryogenic dark matter search using a $41$-pixel array of energy-resolving microwave kinetic inductance detectors with a $13$ meV threshold, simultaneously used to look for both conversion photons from THz wavelength hidden photon dark matter and phonons from particle-like light dark matter interactions. The experimental design, with on- and off-focus pixels for the hidden photon search, allows for a data-driven background model, giving the experiment discovery potential. A blind analysis of $22$ hours of data shows no significant excess, setting the strongest constraints on the hidden photon kinetic mixing parameter $χ$ over the mass range of $13$-$90$ meV/$c^2$, reaching $1.5\times10^{-12}$ at $50$ meV/$c^2$. These data also yield among the first terrestrial limits on dark matter scattering off nuclei and electrons, down to $5$ MeV/$c^2$ and $20$ keV/$c^2$, respectively. The low threshold also enables future study of the low-energy excess limiting cryogenic detectors and, as we project, will allow for a terahertz-scale QCD axion search with a magnetic field.

</details>


### [63] [Towards anomaly detection searches for new physics signatures including Higgs bosons with weakly supervised machine learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19323)
*Chi Lung Cheng,Julia Gonski,Runze Li,Qibin Liu,Benjamin Nachman,Dennis Noll,Julie Khalilieh Romman,Liangyu Wu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文在HAXAD（Higgs And X Anomaly Detection）方法的基础上，引入两种新的特征嵌入（feature embedding）策略、新的统计推断框架，并大幅扩展信号模型集，将其推向可用于实际对撞机数据的高度。改进后的方法在信号灵敏度上优于原方法，并在多种信号模型下达到或超过基于截断（cut-based）搜索的最佳限值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）因其与质量的普适耦合，为寻找超出标准模型的新物理提供了一个自然入口，因此成为对撞机实验中异常检测（anomaly detection, AD）的理想锚点。现有HAXAD策略已提出基本原理，但尚需在方法成熟度上提升以达到应用于实际记录数据的水平。

Method: 本研究对HAXAD方法进行了三点关键扩展：第一，引入并比较两种新的嵌入策略（embedding strategy），这些策略进一步塑造了背景估计（background estimation）与弱监督分类（weakly supervised classification）的流程；第二，开发了新的统计推断框架，能够给出信号无关（signal-agnostic）和信号特定（signal-specific）的截面限制（cross section limits）；第三，显著扩展了所研究的信号模型集合，以在更广泛的相空间（phase space）上评估灵敏度。

Result: 改进后的方法相比原方法提升了信号灵敏度。在与基于截断搜索的示例方法在同一末态（final state）进行基准对比时，HAXAD在多种信号模型下达到或超过了最佳的单次截断限值（cut-based limits）。

Conclusion: 这些发展强化了HAXAD作为一种可行的、具有新颖发现潜力的基于AD的搜索策略的地位，为未来对撞机实验中的异常分析提供了完整的统计工具与方法基础。

Abstract: The Higgs boson, with its universal coupling to mass, provides a broadly applicable portal to sectors beyond the Standard Model and is therefore a natural anchor for anomaly detection (AD) at collider experiments. The Higgs And X Anomaly Detection (HAXAD) strategy offers a principled approach to searching for such anomalies occurring in association with a Higgs boson by combining machine-learning-based feature embedding, background estimation, and weakly supervised classification. This work extends the previous HAXAD approach towards the level of maturity required for application to recorded collider data. A major addition is the introduction and comparison of two new embedding strategies, which in turn shape the background estimation and classification. In addition, a new inference framework is developed, yielding signal-agnostic and signal-specific cross section limits and thereby completing the statistical machinery needed for future AD analyses built on HAXAD. The set of investigated signal models is also significantly expanded, allowing for the evaluation of sensitivity on a much broader phase space. Improvements to the method increase signal sensitivity with respect to the original method, and when benchmarked against an example cut-based search on the same final state, HAXAD matches or exceeds the best individual cut-based limits for a wide variety of considered signal models. These developments strengthen the case for HAXAD as a viable and compelling AD-based search strategy with novel discovery potential at colliders.

</details>

### [64] [Exotic Electronic Order in a Parabolic Kagome Semimetal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18389)
*C. Alexander Baum,Jonas Issing,Sarbajit Mazumdar,Matteo Dürrnagel,Michael Klett,Ronny Thomale,Lennart Klebl*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过组合功能重整化群（functional renormalization group）和奴隶玻色子（slave-boson）方法，研究了2/3填充的Kagome晶格二次能带接触半金属（quadratic band-touching semimetal）的相互作用相图，揭示了前沿不稳定性包括环电流序（loop-current order）、自发交变磁性（altermagnetism）和自旋-环电流序（spin-loop-current order），并指出能带运动学、电子相互作用和量子几何（quantum geometry）的竞争决定了相的选取，为非常规对称性破缺提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Kagome晶格二次能带接触半金属在中间到强耦合区域内的非常规电子序（unconventional electronic orders），并理解能带运动学、相互作用与量子几何如何共同决定这些相的涌现。

Method: 采用功能重整化群（functional renormalization group, FRG）与奴隶玻色子（slave-boson）方法相结合，覆盖从中等到强耦合区间的相图映射。

Result: 揭示了领先的不稳定性包括环电流序（loop-current order）、由自旋-波梅兰丘克不稳定性（spin-Pomeranchuk instability）引发的自发交变磁性（spontaneous altermagnetism），以及具有新颖且尚未被充分探索性质的自旋-环电流序（spin-loop-current order）。

Conclusion: 二次能带接触半金属是探索非常规对称性破缺的有前途平台，并预示在其他抛物型半金属（parabolic semimetals）中可能存在类似现象。

Abstract: We study an interacting kagome-lattice realization of a quadratic band-touching semimetal at 2/3 filling with onsite and nearest-neighbor repulsive interactions. Combining functional renormalization group and slave-boson approaches, we map its phase diagram from intermediate to strong coupling and uncover a hierarchy of unconventional electronic orders. The leading instabilities comprise loop-current order, spontaneous altermagnetism arising from a spin-Pomeranchuk instability, and spin-loop-current order with distinctive and largely unexplored properties. We demonstrate how the interplay of band kinematics, electronic interactions, and quantum geometry governs the selection of these phases. Our findings establish quadratic band-touching semimetals as a promising platform for unconventional symmetry breaking and suggest analogous phenomena in other parabolic semimetals.

### [65] [Non-Fermi-Liquid Behaviors in Weakly Interacting Two-Dimensional Quasicrystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18394)
*Junmo Jeon,Shiro Sakai*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过数值计算研究弱相互作用准晶中的非费米液体行为。在Penrose和Ammann–Beenker拼图模型中，利用弱耦合微扰框架分析热力学、磁性和输运性质，发现态密度的奇异能量依赖导致Sommerfeld系数和磁化率的异常温度依赖，Wilson比显示增强的自旋涨落，自能表现出反常标度和有限残余散射率，表明准粒子图像失效。局域残余散射率在高局域态密度区域显著增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非费米液体（non-Fermi-liquid, NFL）行为通常与强电子关联、量子临界性（quantum criticality）或奇异涨落相关。准晶（quasicrystals）因缺乏平移对称性，即使在没有电子-电子相互作用的情况下也能产生临界单粒子态和碎片化能谱，从而为NFL行为提供了一条根本不同的路径。本文旨在弱相互作用条件下数值研究准晶中的NFL行为，探索其微观机制。

Method: 以Penrose拼图和Ammann–Beenker拼图作为代表性的准周期系统（quasiperiodic systems），在弱耦合微扰框架（weak-coupling perturbative framework）内分析热力学、磁性和输运性质。采用位点解析分析（site-resolved analysis）研究残余散射率的局域分布特征。

Result: Sommerfeld系数和磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）表现出由费米能级附近态密度的奇异能量依赖所决定的异常温度依赖关系。Wilson比（Wilson ratio）显示低温NFL行为伴随增强的自旋涨落，其幅度和温度依赖对填充分数敏感。自能（self-energy）呈现反常标度和有限残余散射率，表明准粒子（quasiparticle）图像失效。位点解析分析揭示，高局域态密度区域的残余散射率显著增强。

Conclusion: 研究结果为分析准晶实验数据以及识别NFL行为的微观机制提供了指导。弱相互作用准晶中的NFL行为源于准周期结构导致的态密度奇异性能量依赖，而非传统意义上的强电子关联或量子临界性。

Abstract: Non-Fermi-liquid (NFL) behavior is usually associated with strong electronic correlations, quantum criticality, or singular fluctuations that invalidate the quasiparticle picture. Quasicrystals are known to provide a fundamentally different route to such physics: their lack of translational symmetry gives rise to critical single-particle states and fragmented spectra even in the absence of electron-electron interactions. Here, we numerically study the NFL behaviors in quasicrystals with weak interactions. Using Penrose and Ammann--Beenker tilings as representative quasiperiodic systems, we analyze thermodynamic, magnetic, and transport properties within a weak-coupling perturbative framework. The Sommerfeld coefficient and magnetic susceptibility show anomalous temperature dependences governed by the singular energy dependence of the density of states near the Fermi level. The Wilson ratio reveals that low-temperature NFL behavior in quasicrystals is accompanied by enhanced spin fluctuations over a broad range of filling fractions, while its magnitude and temperature dependence vary sensitively with filling fraction. The self-energy shows anomalous scaling and a finite residual scattering rate, indicating the breakdown of quasiparticles. Our site-resolved analysis reveals a pronounced enhancement of the residual scattering rate in regions with a high local density of states. These results serve as a guide to analyze experimental data for quasicrystals and to identify the microscopic mechanism of the NFL behaviors.

</details>


### [66] [Quantum critical fan and emergent relativistic symmetry of two-dimensional Dirac semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18396)
*Friederike Ihssen,Bilal Hawashin,Mireia Tolosa-Simeón,Michael M. Scherer*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用非微扰场论方法，在零温和有限温度下研究了手征伊辛模型（chiral Ising model）的 Gross–Neveu–Yukawa 相图，确定了量子临界点（quantum critical point）及其临界指数、有限温度下的经典相变、量子临界扇区（quantum critical fan）的标度性质，并建立了该模型在量子临界点附近的统一场论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验在高度可调的范德瓦尔斯异质结（van-der-Waals heterostructures）中观察到从狄拉克半金属（Dirac semimetal）到绝缘体的相变，因此有必要更好地理解有限温度效应。本文旨在填补对 Gross–Neveu–Yukawa 模型在有限温度下行为的理论认识空白。

Method: 采用非微扰场论方法（non-perturbative field-theory approach），在零温和有限温度下分析手征伊辛模型（chiral Ising model）的 Gross–Neveu–Yukawa 相图，涵盖半金属相（semimetallic phase）和具有自发 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 对称性破缺的绝缘相（insulating phase）。

Result: 零温下发现一个量子临界点（quantum critical point），其临界指数（critical exponents）接近手征伊辛普适类（chiral Ising universality class），并证明相对论对称性（relativistic symmetry）在量子临界点附近是涌现的。有限温下，有序相存续至有限临界温度（critical temperature），在该温度处观察到向无序相的经典相变，且该相变属于二维伊辛普适类（two-dimensional Ising universality class）。此外，还确定了量子临界扇区（quantum critical fan）的范围与标度性质，以及其中准粒子权重（quasiparticle weight）的行为。

Conclusion: 本文为手征伊辛模型在其量子临界点附近的相图提供了一个统一的场论框架（unified field-theoretical framework）。

Abstract: Two-dimensional Dirac semimetals near a quantum critical point can be described by Gross--Neveu--Yukawa models. In view of recent experimental advances exhibiting a transition from Dirac semimetal to insulator in highly-tunable van-der-Waals heterostructures, a better understanding of finite-temperature effects is mandatory. Here, we study the Gross--Neveu--Yukawa phase diagram of the chiral Ising model with a non-perturbative field-theory approach at zero and finite temperature, both in the semimetallic phase and in the insulating phase with spontaneously broken $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. At zero temperature, we find a quantum critical point with critical exponents that are close to the ones of the chiral Ising universality class, and show that relativistic symmetry is emergent close to the quantum critical point. At finite temperature, the ordered phase survives up to a finite critical temperature, at which we observe a classical phase transition into the disordered phase. We confirm that this transition lies in the two-dimensional Ising universality class. Finally, we determine the extent and scaling properties of the quantum critical fan, and the behavior of the quasiparticle weight, therein. In summary, we present a unified field-theoretical framework for the phase diagram of the chiral Ising model in the surroundings of its quantum critical point.

</details>


### [67] [Coherent Magnons Driven by Photomodulated Anisotropy in Altermagnetic MnTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18421)
*Dingbin Huang,Jonathon Kruppe,Resham Babu Regmi,Nirmal J. Ghimire,James Analytis,Joseph Orenstein*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过空间映射技术同时测量了MnTe中奈尔矢量的局域平衡取向、光激发自旋波的振幅与频率，发现其自旋波能隙的上限极低（约60 μeV），表明六方各向异性极弱，使得交变磁序对光调控高度敏感，并实现了相干自旋波的光致驱动与空间调制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MnTe作为典型的g波交变磁体（g-wave altermagnet），是研究交变磁序（altermagnetic order）非平衡激发的理想平台，但目前对其自旋波激发与各向异性的理解尚不充分。

Method: 同时进行了局域奈尔矢量（Néel vector）平衡取向φ_L(𝐫)的空间映射，以及光激发自旋波（spin wave）的振幅Δφ(𝐫,t)与频率Ω(𝐫)的测量。

Result: 自旋波能隙（spin-wave gap）的固有各向异性上限极低，约为60 μeV（0.7 K）；六方各向异性（hexagonal anisotropy）K₆极弱，使交变磁序对光调控高度敏感；光致K₆增强可驱动相干自旋波；在阈值泵浦通量以上，Δφ对φ_L呈六重对称锯齿依赖，Ω呈现摆线状调制。

Conclusion: MnTe中奈尔矢量的近各向同性（near-isotropy）使得可通过光学和力学手段调控电子能带结构中自旋劈裂（spin-splitting）的取向，为交变磁自旋电子学（altermagnetic spintronics）提供新路径。

Abstract: Manganese telluride ($\text{MnTe}$) has recently emerged as a prototypical $g$-wave altermagnet, providing an ideal platform to investigate the non-equilibrium excitations of altermagnetic order. Here, we report simultaneous spatial mapping of the local equilibrium orientation of the Néel vector, $\varphi_L(\mathbf{r})$, alongside the amplitude, $Δ\varphi(\mathbf{r},t)$, and frequency, $Ω(\mathbf{r})$, of photoexcited spin waves. Based on these measurements, we place a remarkably low upper bound of $\approx 60~μ\text{eV}$ (0.7 K) on the spin-wave gap arising from intrinsic anisotropy. This exceptionally weak hexagonal anisotropy ($K_6$) renders the altermagnetic order highly susceptible to optical tuning, allowing coherent spin waves to be driven by a photoinduced enhancement of $K_6$. Above a threshold pump fluence, our spatial maps reveal that this photomodulation manifests as a six-fold symmetric sawtooth dependence of $Δ\varphi$ on $\varphi_L$ and a cycloid-like modulation of $Ω$. Ultimately, the near-isotropy of the Néel vector in $\text{MnTe}$ enables optical and mechanical control over the orientation of spin-splitting in the electronic band structure, offering new pathways for altermagnetic spintronics.

</details>


### [68] [Theory of two-dimensional Wigner crystals with defects: Interactions, melting transitions and collective modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18477)
*Paweł Matus,Tobias Holder*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用对偶技术（duality techniques）构建了一个研究二维带电晶体（包括Wigner固体）中缺陷（空位、间隙原子、位错、向错）对有效作用量贡献的理论框架，系统分析了缺陷对的相互作用能、缺陷增殖导致的熔化相变，以及发现金属性Wigner晶体中声子色散关系随空位密度的非寻常依赖关系，并讨论了空位费米液体（vacancy Fermi liquid）的热力学性质探测途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Wigner固体的物理特性由弹性（elasticity）与长程静电相互作用（long-range electrostatics）的共同作用所决定，使其晶体缺陷具有与电荷中性晶体截然不同的性质。近期二维体系中晶格熔化及Wigner晶体邻近相的实验观测，迫切要求系统地研究缺陷如何影响该类固体的长波长性质。

Method: 采用对偶技术（duality techniques）构建了描述空位与间隙原子（vacancies and interstitials）、位错（dislocations）和向错（disclinations）对二维带电晶体有效作用量贡献的综合理论框架，并系统计算了不同缺陷对组合的相互作用能。

Result: 在具有有限基态空位密度的金属性Wigner晶体（metallic Wigner crystal）相中，发现声子（phonons）的色散关系以非寻常的方式随空位密度变化；探讨了通过测量熔化温度和声速来探测此类空位费米液体（vacancy Fermi liquid）热力学性质的途径。

Conclusion: 所发展的场论框架可作为研究反常霍尔晶体（anomalous Hall crystals）及含缺陷的电荷密度波（charge density waves with defects）的起点。

Abstract: The physics of Wigner solids is characterized by an interplay of elasticity and long-range electrostatics, endowing crystal defects with properties distinct from those in charge-neutral crystals. Recent experiments observing lattice melting and Wigner-crystal-adjacent phases in two dimensions necessitate an examination of how defects affect the long-wavelength properties of such solids. Here, we use duality techniques to construct a comprehensive framework for studying the contribution of vacancies and interstitials, dislocations, and disclinations to the effective action of two-dimensional charged crystals. This allows for a systematic investigation of the interaction energies for the different combinations of defect pairs. We further study melting transitions due to defect proliferation, assessing and justifying some of the assumptions present in the literature. In the metallic Wigner crystal phase, characterized by a finite ground state density of vacancies, we find phonons with a dispersion relation that varies in an unusual way with the vacancy density. Consequently, we discuss how thermodynamic properties of such a vacancy Fermi liquid can be probed in measurements of the melting temperature and speed of sound. The field theory developed here can serve as a starting point in the study of anomalous Hall crystals and charge density waves with defects.

</details>


### [69] [Manifest charge-transfer physics in T$^\prime$-La$_2$NiO$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19217)
*Wiktoria Lewandowski,Steffen Bötzel,Ilya M. Eremin,Frank Lechermann*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理多体理论（first-principles many-body theory）研究了假设的T'结构La₂NiO₄化合物，发现其为显性电荷转移绝缘体（charge-transfer insulator），具有类铜酸盐的电荷能隙（~1.8 eV），掺杂时呈现强载流子不对称性，且与T结构不同，T'结构中不存在近邻反铁磁有序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受铜酸盐（cuprate）体系中La₂CuO₄存在T'结构同质多晶型的启发，本研究旨在探索La₂NiO₄在T'结构（Ni位为平面正方氧配位）下的电子结构与关联物理特性，以揭示层状镍酸盐（layered nickelates）中新的电荷转移物理机制。

Method: 采用第一性原理多体理论（first-principles many-body theory）对假设的T'结构La₂NiO₄进行从头算研究。

Result: T'-La₂NiO₄为显性电荷转移绝缘体（charge-transfer insulator），电荷能隙（charge gap）约为1.8 eV，与铜酸盐类似；掺杂时呈现强载流子不对称性（carrier asymmetry）：空穴主要进入O(2p)衍生态，电子则主要占据有效Ni-d_{x²-y²}态；在化学计量比下，T'结构中不存在近邻反铁磁有序（antiferromagnetic ordering），与T结构的强反铁磁性形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 该理论预测为层状镍酸盐中具有挑战性电荷转移特征的关联物理（correlation physics）开辟了新方向，有待实验验证。

Abstract: The La$_2$NiO$_4$ compound stabilizes in nature in the so-called T structure with octahedral oxygen coordination of the Ni site. Motivated by a similarly existing polymorph for La$_2$CuO$_4$ in the cuprate system, we here study La$_2$NiO$_4$ in the T$^\prime$-structure with square-planar oxygen coordination of Ni by means of first-principles many-body theory. The hypothetical T$^\prime$-La$_2$NiO$_4$ compound turns out to be a manifest charge-transfer insulator with a cuprate-like charge gap of $\sim 1.8$ eV. Upon doping, a strong carrier asymmetry is revealed, i.e. while holes dominantly enter O$(2p)$-derived states, electrons may become itinerant majorly within effective Ni-$d_{x^2-y^2}$ states. Nearest-neighbor antiferromagnetic ordering at stoichiometry appears absent in the T$^\prime$ structure, in stark contrast to the strong antiferromagnetism in the T structure. Our theoretical study opens up new pathways for correlation physics in layered nickelates with challenging charge-transfer signatures, awaiting experimental inquiries.

</details>


### [70] [Magnetic exchange interactions in the molecular orbital spin system NaV2O5 from a distributed moment point of view](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19224)
*Claudio Garcia,Ilteris K. Turan,Swagata Acharya,Mark van Schilfgaarde,Jerome Jackson,Walter R L. Lambrecht*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于第一性原理计算，提出NaV2O5的磁性源于V2O5窄分裂导带掺杂形成的半填充Mott绝缘态，并采用分布式磁矩（distributed moment approach）方法，发现氧原子上的小诱导磁矩间的交换相互作用与钒原子间的交换相互作用量级相当甚至更大，对临界温度至关重要，自旋波谱中出现高能光学型自旋波集体激发。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于准粒子自洽GW（quasiparticle-self-consistent GW）能带结构的线性响应方法（linear response approach），计算各原子磁位点之间的交换相互作用（exchange interactions），并从中提取经典海森堡型哈密顿量（classical Heisenberg type Hamiltonian），进而计算自旋波谱（spin wave spectra）。

Result: 发现氧原子（包括钒氧基氧和桥氧）上的小诱导磁矩之间的交换相互作用与钒原子之间的交换相互作用量级相同甚至更大；这些氧上的交换相互作用对临界温度（critical temperature）起着至关重要的作用；从第一性原理导出的哈密顿量计算得到的自旋波谱中包含不寻常的高能光学型自旋波集体激发（optic spin wave type collective excitations）。

Conclusion: NaV2O5中氧原子上的小诱导磁矩在磁性行为中不可忽略，其交换相互作用与钒原子相当，对体系临界温度起关键作用，并导致高能光学型自旋波激发，这挑战了将NaV2O5仅视为钒基梯子体系的传统图像。

Abstract: The magnetism in NaV2O5 results from doping of the narrow split-off conduction band of V2O5, which becomes half-filled and leads to a Mott-insulating splitting of spin resolved bands with anti-ferromagnetic order of the spins along the zigzag chains. In the Pmmn structure the spin of this S = 1/2 system is equally shared between two vanadium atoms, residing in a molecular orbital type state. While below 34 K a charge disproportionation occurs into V4+ and V5+, the situation above this temperature is less clear and amounts to a fluctuating moment with equal probability of occupancy of each V. While traditionally described as a quarter-filled ladder system with electron spin localized on the rungs of the ladder, we here take a distributed moment approach in terms of the spin density lumped into individual atomic magnetic sites, including the small induced moments on the oxygen atoms. Exchange interactions are calculated between these sites using a linear response approach based on quasiparticle-self-consistent GW band structures. Surprisingly we find the exchange interactions between the small magnetic moments induced on the vanadyl and bridge oxygen sites to be of the same order of magnitude and even larger than the exchange interactions between vanadium atoms. Their role in the critical temperature is found to be crucial. The spin wave spectra obtained from this classical Heisenberg type Hamiltonian extracted from first-principles contains unusual optic spin wave type collective excitations of high energy.

### [71] [Symmetry-protected cubic-touching topological surface bands with tunable singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19265)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于对称性约束分析拓扑表面能带的色散结构，通过调节粒子-空穴不对称性和各向异性实现能带形态的连续调控；使用角动量3/2电子的棱镜晶格格点模型进行实例验证。

Result: 发现了一类在对称性保护下具有三次方级能带接触的拓扑表面能带，且能带色散可在立方色散、环状带和多极小谷结构之间连续变化，对应从幂律到对数发散的多种密度态奇点族。

Conclusion: 该可调谐的密度态奇点族为在拓扑表面态中工程化强关联物质相提供了灵活平台，具有重要的应用潜力。

Abstract: We propose a class of topological surface bands in three-dimensional topological crystalline insulators that have symmetry-protected cubic-order band touching. Within the symmetry constraint, the band dispersion can continuously vary between cubic dispersion, moat band and multi-mini-valley structure with van Hove singularities by adjusting particle-hole asymmetry and anisotropy. Thus, there is a family of tunable density-of-state singularities ranging from power-law to logarithmic divergences. This offrs a versatile platform for engineering strongly correlated phases of matter in topological surface states.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究体系为由两层MoSe₂与单层h-BN间隔层构成的半导体莫尔材料（semiconductor moiré material）。通过测量散射光子的二阶关联函数（second-order correlation function），探测层间电子动力学行为，并观察一层激子共振散射光中的光子聚束（photon bunching）现象。

Result: 在Ising型层赝自旋相变（layer pseudo-spin phase transition）的起始点，大量电子在两层之间发生关联转移，导致一层激子共振散射光中出现显著的光子聚束效应。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，光子关联可以作为获取电子相变动力学指数（dynamical exponents）的有效方法，为研究电子相变的临界行为提供了新的实验途径。

Abstract: Characterizing phase transitions between correlated electronic phases, extracting their critical exponents, and identifying their universality class are of central interest in many-body physics. Here, we propose and demonstrate that photon correlation spectroscopy can be used to gain insight into the nature of critical electronic density fluctuations. We study a semiconductor moiré material consisting of two MoSe2 layers separated by a monolayer h-BN spacer and measure interlayer electron dynamics via the second-order correlation function of the scattered photons. The correlated transfer of large numbers of electrons between the layers at the onset of an Ising-type layer pseudo-spin phase transition leads to photon bunching in light scattered by the exciton resonance of one layer. Our measurements pave the way for using photon correlations as a method to access dynamical exponents associated with electronic phase transitions.

Starting from the dimensionally reduced action, we derive the decoupled second-order wave equations for the electromagnetic field, and for the gauge-potential. In vacuum, we show that the topological CS parameter works as a dynamical mass generator, modifying the strict transversality of plane waves, and introducing a distinct energy \textit{gap} in the dispersion relation. Considering a planar conducting medium that satisfies the Ohm law, the topological mass induces a novel hybridization mechanism between the Transverse Electric (TE), and Transverse Magnetic (TM) modes, a feature entirely absent in the conventional planar plasmonics. We analyze the asymptotic limits of this system, obtaining the exact real solutions in the lossless reactive Drude regime, and deriving the complex refractive index through a quasi-local approximation in the dissipative regime.

### [74] [Direct Spatiotemporal Imaging of Charge Carrier Dynamics in Operative Semiconductor Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19157)
*Adriano Cola,Antonio Valletta,Isabella Farella,Vaclav Dědič,Lorenzo Dominici*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出载流子动力学波克尔斯成像（CDPI）方法，一种灵敏、定量、非侵入式的光学成像技术，通过探测局域电场实现对光生电子云在实空间内的直接可视化，同时将载流子演化与传导电流、位移电流关联，揭示漂移、扩散、载流子间相互作用、俘获与去俘获等基本机制。该方法在碲化镉（CdTe）辐射探测器中展示了微米级空间分辨率和纳秒级时间分辨率，并可推广至有机、钙钛矿及二维光电子材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子器件中的载流子动力学（carrier dynamics）决定了信号的内部演化与外部可测量电流，然而现有方法通常为间接或固有扰动性（perturbative）测量，难以实现对内部电荷动力学的直接成像。因此，需要一种能够非侵入式、定量地直接观测内部载流子行为的实验方法。

Method: 该方法通过波克尔斯成像（Pockels Imaging）探测局域电场（local electric field），在实空间中直接可视化光生电子云（photogenerated electron clouds），同时将其演化与传导电流（conduction current）和位移电流（displacement current）相关联，建立载流子输运（carrier transport）的统一图像。

Result: 在碲化镉（CdTe）辐射探测器中，CDPI实现了微米级（micrometre-scale）空间分辨率和纳秒级（nanosecond）时间分辨率，能够直接观测漂移（drift）、扩散（diffusion）、载流子-载流子相互作用（carrier-carrier interactions）、俘获与去俘获（trapping and detrapping）等基本机制，以及载流子云形态的时空演化。

Conclusion: CDPI作为一种新范式，适用于具有显著电光响应（electro-optic responses）的系统，并可推广至有机半导体、钙钛矿和二维光电子材料，直接建立内部载流子动力学与器件层面功能之间的关联。

Abstract: Understanding charge carrier dynamics within electronic devices is crucial, as it governs both the internal evolution of signals and the externally measurable current. Yet, direct imaging of these dynamics remains elusive: existing approaches are often indirect or inherently perturbative. Here, we introduce Carrier Dynamics by Pockels Imaging (CDPI), a sensitive, quantitative, and non-invasive method that enables direct access to internal charge dynamics. By probing the local electric field, CDPI visualizes photogenerated electron clouds in real space while simultaneously correlating their evolution with both conduction and displacement currents, thereby establishing a unified picture of carrier transport. The technique provides direct insight into fundamental mechanisms \textemdash including drift, diffusion, carrier-carrier interactions, trapping and detrapping \textemdash as well as the spatiotemporal evolution of carrier cloud morphology. Demonstrated in CdTe radiation detectors with micrometre-scale spatial resolution and nanosecond temporal resolution, CDPI is broadly applicable to systems exhibiting appreciable electro-optic responses. Beyond conventional semiconductors, the approach extends to organic, perovskite, and two-dimensional optoelectronic materials, offering a new paradigm for directly linking internal carrier dynamics to device-level functionality.

### [75] [A First Bound on the Moffat Energy and Thorium--229 Clock as a Probe of the Nonlocal Time-Energy Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18333)
