<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 新型钍-229核钟（Thorium-229 nuclear clock）为检验时间-能量不确定原理（Time-Energy uncertainty principle）的修正提供了新的实验平台。本文旨在推导非局域时间-能量不确定关系，并首次利用公布的²²⁹Th核钟数据对非局域尺度（nonlocality scale）\(E_M\)进行实验探测。

Method: 作者首先推导了非局域时间-能量不确定关系（nonlocal Time-Energy uncertainty principle），然后将其应用于已发表的²²⁹Th核钟数据。通过直接时钟-能量通道（direct clock-energy channel）以及考虑核灵敏度增强（nuclear sensitivity enhancement）效应，分别给出了不同模型依赖程度下的约束估计。

Result: 直接时钟-能量通道给出了保守的下限在数十MeV量级，乐观的当前数据估计可达百MeV量级。考虑²²⁹Th跃迁的核灵敏度增强后，可获得模型依赖的更强约束，达到GeV量级；而核尺度参考能量场景（nuclear-scale reference-energy scenarios）则可达到TeV量级。

Conclusion: 核钟已经为非局域时间-能量不确定关系提供了从理论通向可测量的实验室约束的实验路径，能够对非普朗克尺度非局域性（non-Planckian nonlocality）给出有意义的实验界限。

Abstract: The new Thorium--229 nuclear clocks give us a new laboratory system in which to test if modification of the Time-Energy uncertainty principle is correct. In this paper we derive the nonlocal Time-Energy uncertainty principle and then apply the published $^{229}$Th nuclear clock data as a first probe of the nonlocality scale \(E_M\). We note that since these experiments were not designed to test nonlocal quantum field theory the constraints are interpreted as motivating bounds and not definitive exclusions. By using the direct clock-energy channel, we find conservative lower bounds on \(E_M\) at the tens of MeV scale, with optimistic present-data estimates reaching the hundred MeV scale. Including the known nuclear sensitivity enhancement of the $^{229}$Th transition gives us stronger model dependent bounds in the GeV range, while nuclear-scale reference-energy scenarios can reach the TeV range. The conclusion we draw from this is that nuclear clocks already provide an experimental route from nonlocal time--energy uncertainty to measurable laboratory bounds on non-Planckian nonlocality.

### [76] [How to improve the discrimination power of classically simulable measurements?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19070)
*Yiran Wang,Yongming Li*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究在奇数素维魔幻资源理论中，通过添加魔幻资源、使用量子催化剂和量子存储器三种方法提升经典可模拟测量（CSMs）的区分能力，建立了模拟代价的上下界，并证明有限维量子催化剂和存储器无法提升对具有正Wigner函数态对的CSM最优成功概率（无go定理）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典可模拟测量（classically simulable measurements, CSMs）的区分能力弱于全局测量，因此需要研究如何提升其区分能力，以拓展其在量子信息处理中的应用。

Method: 将具有正离散Wigner函数的测量与完全正Wigner保持测量通道（completely positive Wigner-preserving measurement channels）相关联，将提升CSMs区分能力的问题转化为使用自由操作（free operations）模拟量子通道所需魔幻资源（magic resources）数量的判定问题，并据此推导模拟代价的上下界。

Result: 推导了模拟代价的上下界，并给出一个上下界恰好相等的具体实例，证明可消耗的魔幻资源确实能增强CSMs的区分能力；同时建立了一个无go定理（no-go theorem）：对于区分一对具有正Wigner函数的量子态，有限维量子催化剂（quantum catalysts）和有限维量子存储器（quantum memories）均无法提升CSM的最优成功概率。

Conclusion: 魔幻资源可以提升CSMs的区分能力，但有限维量子催化剂和量子存储器对此任务无效，这为理解CSMs的局限性及资源理论中的区分能力增强机制提供了理论约束。

Abstract: Classically simulable measurements (CSMs) constitute an important class of restricted measurements in the odd-prime-dimensional magic resource theory, referring to those measurements with positive discrete Wigner functions. Since their discrimination power is weaker than that of global measurements, it is necessary to study how to improve the discrimination power of CSMs. In this paper, we consider three methods to improve the discrimination power of CSMs, including adding magic resources, using quantum catalysts, and using quantum memories. Specifically, we relate measurements with positive discrete Wigner functions to completely positive Wigner-preserving measurement channels, thereby transforming the problem of improving the discrimination power of CSMs into the problem of determining how many magic resources are required to simulate quantum channels using free operations. Based on this, we derive the lower and upper bounds of the simulation cost. Moreover, we provide a concrete example for which these bounds coincide and prove that consumable magic resources can enhance the discrimination power of CSMs. Finally, we establish a no-go theorem, which shows that for discriminating a pair of states with positive Wigner functions, neither finite-dimensional quantum catalysts nor finite-dimensional quantum memories can improve the optimal success probability of discrimination using CSMs.

### [77] [The arrow of time, irreversibility, equilibrium and measurement in quantum mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19142)
*Christopher J. N. Coveney,Peter V. Coveney*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证了具有连续谱（continuous spectra）的量子系统（如热力学极限下的大系统）能够自然地容纳量子力学中看似不完整的特性，包括时间反演对称性破缺、热力学平衡、退相干以及测量过程，从而无需引入额外特设假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子力学被广泛认为是不完备的，因为它与热力学第二定律（second law of thermodynamics）不一致，且无法对测量过程提供科学可信的物理解释——即退相干（decoherence）如何发生以及经典可观测量如何被记录。这导致研究者不得不使用大量特设假设（ad hoc assumptions）来解释量子系统的各种性质，例如量子器件的相干时间（coherence time）。

Method: 论文在具有连续谱的量子系统框架下展开分析，重点考察了孤立系统中与幺正时间演化（unitary time evolution）相关联的时间反演对称性。研究表明该对称性会发生自发破缺，产生半群演化（semi-group evolution），最终在长时间下达到热力学平衡。在此基础上，进一步纳入宏观测量仪器，展示了测量结果如何对应冯·诺伊曼投影假设（von Neumann projection postulate），并以符合玻恩规则（Born rule）的概率出现。

Result: 研究发现：第一，非幺正时间不对称性（non-unitary time-asymmetry）的出现导致微正则平衡态（microcanonical equilibrium states），其中所有量子相干性完全丧失；第二，纯态（pure states）转变为混合态（mixtures），熵随之增加；第三，测量结果自然地导出冯·诺伊曼投影假设与玻恩规则。该理论的数学结构与经典遍历理论（classical ergodic theory）高度相似。

Conclusion: 具有连续谱的量子系统能够以自然一致的方式容纳量子力学中看似不完整的诸多特性，无需依赖特设假设。该理论框架将量子统计力学与测量问题统一纳入一个自洽的数学结构之中，其与经典遍历理论的类比进一步加深了对量子系统达到平衡态条件的理解。

Abstract: Quantum mechanics is widely recognised as being incomplete. It is not consistent with the second law of thermodynamics and does not provide a scientifically credible physical account of the measurement process, the means by which coherence is broken and classically observable states are recorded. This had led to many ad hoc assumptions being used to account for various properties of quantum systems, among which is the coherence time of quantum devices that determines their ability to perform computations. Here, we show that all these properties can be accommodated naturally and consistently in the context of quantum systems which exhibit continuous spectra, as arises in the thermodynamic limit of large systems. In particular, for isolated systems we show that the time-reversal symmetry associated with unitary time evolution of the quantum state gives rise to time-symmetry breaking and a semi-group evolution which attains thermodynamic equilibrium at long times. Moreover, the emergence of this non-unitary time-asymmetry leads to microcanonical equilibrium states in which all quantum coherence is lost and is accompanied by the transformation of pure states into mixtures, leading in turn to an increase in entropy. Inclusion of a macroscopic measurement apparatus shows how the outcome of a measurement corresponds to the von Neumann projection postulate, arising with probabilities in conformance with the Born rule. The mathematical structure of the theory which applies to quantum systems with continuous spectra is closely analogous to the classical ergodic theory of dynamical systems and the conditions under which they attain equilibrium states.

</details>


### [78] [Simulating Majorana fermions in black hole with Ising Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18805)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弯曲时空中的量子场论（QFT in curved spacetime）预言了安鲁效应（Unruh effect）和霍金辐射（Hawking radiation），但这些效应的直接观测因信号极其微弱而极为困难，因此需要可操控的量子多体系统来构建桌面实验以模拟这些现象。

Method: 利用横场伊辛模型作为量子模拟器，将史瓦西黑洞时空的四种坐标表示（Schwarzschild、tortoise、Kruskal、conformally flat）分别映射到不同的微观伊辛自旋模型，并在连续极限下考察这些模型如何趋同于相同的马约拉纳场理论。

Conclusion: 该工作为利用可控量子多体系统和桌面实验研究弯曲时空中费米子量子场论提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Quantum field theory (QFT) in curved spacetime has led to profound predictions, including the Unruh effect and Hawking radiation, yet their direct observation remains extraordinarily challenging because of their extremely weak signatures. Here, we show that the transverse-field Ising model provides a quantum simulator for Majorana fermions in a Schwarzschild black hole background. Remarkably, different coordinate representations of the same spacetime-Schwarzschild, tortoise, Kruskal, and conformally flat-map onto distinct microscopic Ising spin models. Despite their microscopic differences, these models converge in the continuum limit to the same Majorana field theory, exhibiting an emergent form of general covariance. This provides a rare example of a fundamental symmetry of general relativity arising as an emergent property of a condensed matter system. We further demonstrate how black hole particle production can be simulated and detected through spin correlation measurements, and discuss experimental platforms capable of realizing these models. Our work establishes a practical route for investigating fermionic QFT in curved spacetime using controllable quantum many-body systems and tabletop experiments.

### [80] [Nishimori Threshold Estimation for Bayesian Inference and $\mathbb{Z}_q$ Surface Code Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18374)
*Rohit Mukherjee,Simon Trebst*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过傅里叶-沃尔什投影方案（Fourier–Walsh projection scheme）解析估计Nishimori普适类（Nishimori universality class）中量子纠错码（quantum error correction）错误阈值（error threshold）的方法，无需大规模数值模拟，即可精确复现已知阈值并推广至新的表面码情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠错中的错误阈值是衡量解码能力与容错（fault-tolerance）的关键定量指标，但通常只能通过大规模数值模拟获得。本文旨在提供一种解析估计方法，以绕过数值模拟的高昂成本，快速且准确地获得阈值。

Method: 采用傅里叶-沃尔什投影方案，将无无序的统计力学模型（statistical-mechanics model）的临界点映射到Born无序的Nishimori临界点；结合最小副本理论（minimal replica theory）方法，通过对精确复制单键权重（replicated single-bond weight）的投影，获得闭式解析估计。

Result: 该方法在空间维度d=2–5下，对随机键与随机plaquette伊辛模型（Ising model）/ ℤ₂稳定子码（stabilizer code）的已知数值阈值实现了百分比精度内的再现，并可推广至q≤4的Potts变量。对于ℤ_q表面码（surface code），投影方案给出两个Nishimori温度，它们界定了中间信息临界相（information-critical phase）；所得阈值与近期退相干ℤ_q环面码（toric code）的数值结果高度一致，并满足Gilbert–Varshamov自对偶熵关系（self-dual entropy relation）。

Conclusion: 该方法揭示了清洁模型（clean model）与Born无序模型之间的深层联系，使得多种稳定子码的错误阈值可以瞬时解析估计，无需依赖数值模拟或对偶性条件（duality condition）。

Abstract: In quantum error correction, the error threshold provides essential quantitative guidance for the ability to bring about fault-tolerance through decoding the effects of incoherent noise, weak measurement or inference. However, the numerical value of an error threshold is typically only accessible through large-scale numerical simulations of the underlying noise model. Here we introduce an analytical estimate of error thresholds falling into the Nishimori universality class via a Fourier--Walsh projection scheme that maps the critical point of the underlying disorder-free statistical-mechanics model to the Born-disordered Nishimori critical point. Using a minimal replica theory approach, this closed-form estimate is obtained from a projection of the exact replicated single-bond weight which we find to reproduce (within a percentage point) the known numerical thresholds of random-bond and random-plaquette Ising models / $\mathbb Z_2$ stabilizer codes in spatial dimensions $d=2-5$, and extends to Potts variables with $q\le4$. The main application of our projection scheme is to $\mathbb Z_q$ surface codes, whose decoding problem maps to the disordered $q$-state clock model. For $q\ge5$ the clean clock model has \textit{two} Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless transitions, which the projection maps to two Nishimori temperatures that bound an intermediate information-critical phase. The resulting threshold values not only accurately agree with recent decohered-$\mathbb Z_q$-toric-code numerics, but are found to satisfy the Gilbert--Varshamov self-dual entropy relation $\ln q \simeq H_q(T_1^\ast)+H_q(T_2^\ast),$ although no duality condition is imposed in the construction. Our approach thereby points to a deeper connection between the clean and Born-disordered models, while allowing for instant analytical estimates of error thresholds for a variety of stabilizer codes.

### [81] [Magic-protected entanglement and Clifford-irreducible structure in magic state space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18400)
*Alejandro Borda Kuhlmann,Julian Rincon*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个克利福德轨道（Clifford-orbit）框架来研究由非稳定子性质（nonstabilizerness）保护的纠缠——即“魔法纠缠（magical entanglement）”，定义了其在克利福德化简（Clifford reduction）下的规范表示、谱与秩，并揭示了T-魔法与W-魔法两种纠缠-魔法相互作用的典型行为与交叉特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对非稳定子资源（magic）与量子纠缠之间的相互作用缺乏系统性的定量描述，尤其是纠缠在克利福德操作化简后剩余的受保护部分尚未被明确定义。本文旨在建立一个以轨道（orbit）为基础的组织原则，将魔法纠缠作为一种状态层次的诊断工具。

Method: 方法包括：（1）构建克利福德轨道框架，通过最优稳定子化简（optimal stabilizer simplification）提取残余纠缠；（2）定义规范代表（canonical representatives）、谱（spectra）和秩（ranks）来刻画态的克利福德不可约结构（Clifford-irreducible structure）；（3）通过解析例子和随机电路数值模拟分析T-魔法与W-魔法两种机制的行为差异。

Result: 识别出两种魔法-纠缠作用机制：T-魔法机制中，局部非稳定子资源可与纠缠共存，但受保护部分较弱且依赖具体态；W-魔法机制中，纠缠与魔法呈克利福德不可约的紧密耦合，表现出强烈的自平均（self-averaging）行为和类哈耳（Haar-like）的集中分布。随机电路数值模拟支持从T-魔法的宽涨落到W-魔法的集中行为的交叉。

Conclusion: 魔法纠缠是一种轨道级别的诊断指标，能够揭示非稳定子性如何通过克利福德化简保护量子关联。该框架为理解量子计算中魔法资源与纠缠结构的深层联系提供了新的组织原理。

Abstract: We develop a Clifford-orbit framework for studying magic-protected entanglement, which we refer to as magical entanglement: the part of bipartite entanglement that remains after optimal stabilizer simplification. This construction leverages residual entanglement under Clifford reduction as a state-level organizing principle for magic state space. It defines canonical representatives, spectra, and ranks that characterize the Clifford-irreducible structure of a state. We identify two regimes of the magic-entanglement interplay. In the $T$-magic regime, local nonstabilizer resources can coexist with entanglement, but the protected component remains weak and state-dependent. In the $W$-magic regime, by contrast, entanglement is Clifford-irreducibly tied to nonstabilizerness, producing typical, strongly self-averaging behavior. Analytical examples and random-circuit numerics support a crossover from broad $T$-magic fluctuations to concentrated, Haar-like $W$-magic behavior. These results identify magical entanglement as an orbit-level diagnostic of how nonstabilizerness protects quantum correlations against Clifford reduction.

### [82] [State $k$-designs from Hamiltonian evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18537)

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究固定哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）时间演化下态k-设计（state k-design）的生成机制。建立了初始系综与演化后系综的帧位势（frame potential）在大时间极限下的简洁关系，证明热力学极限下演化系综可形成精确态k-设计；对于不可积混合场伊辛模型（mixed-field Ising Hamiltonian），数值和解析均显示从Pauli基积态出发可获得高精度近似态k-设计。此外提出M步淬火协议将有限时间修正压低至O(1/T^M)，并将分析推广至酉系综（unitary ensemble）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子态k-设计和酉k-设计（unitary k-design）在量子信息、量子混沌和量子热化等领域具有重要应用。理解固定哈密顿量时间演化能否以及如何生成这些设计，有助于揭示量子动力学与随机系综之间的深层联系，并为量子计算中高效生成随机态和酉算子提供理论依据。

Method: 采用解析推导与数值模拟相结合的方法。对高斯酉系综（Gaussian unitary ensemble, GUE）中的哈密顿量，推导了演化系综帧位势与初始系综帧位势在大时间极限下的递归关系。对于具体模型，选取不可积混合场伊辛哈密顿量，以Pauli基积态为初始态，通过时间演化生成系综，并数值验证其近似形成态k-设计。还提出一个M步淬火协议（M-step quench protocol）以抑制有限时间效应。

Result: 大时间极限下演化系综的帧位势与初始系综帧位势满足简单关系；热力学极限下，只要初始系综构成态1-设计，演化系综即形成精确态k-设计。不可积混合场伊辛模型从Pauli基积态出发可高精度生成近似态k-设计。有限时间修正按O(1/T)标度，而M步淬火协议可将其压低至O(1/T^M)。类似递归关系也适用于酉系综的帧位势。

Conclusion: 本文统一阐明了近期通过序列量子淬火（sequential quantum quenches）生成酉k-设计的相关方案背后的机制。研究表明，固定哈密顿量的时间演化能够高效生成态k-设计和酉k-设计，为量子信息处理中随机态和酉算子的制备提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the generation of state $k$-designs from time evolution under a fixed Hamiltonian. Specifically, we consider the ensemble $\mathcal{E}=\left\{e^{-iHt}|ψ_0\rangle | \ t\sim \mathrm{Unif}[0,T],\, |ψ_0\rangle\sim \mathcal{E}'\right\}$, where the initial states are sampled from an ensemble $\mathcal{E}'$. For Hamiltonians drawn from the Gaussian unitary ensemble, we derive a simple relation between the frame potential of the evolved ensemble $\mathcal{E}$ and that of the initial ensemble $\mathcal{E}'$ in the large evolution time limit. This relation shows that $\mathcal{E}$ forms an exact state $k$-design in the thermodynamic limit as long as $\mathcal{E}'$ forms a state 1-design. Remarkably, we further show, both analytically and numerically, that time evolution under a simple nonintegrable mixed-field Ising Hamiltonian can generate approximate state $k$-designs with high precision, starting from product states in an appropriately chosen Pauli basis. We also analyze the finite-$T$ correction and find it scales as $O(1/T)$. To reduce the evolution time, we propose an $M$-step quench protocol that suppresses this correction to $O(1/T^M)$, which is also verified numerically. We then extend our analysis to unitary ensembles, deriving an analogous recursion relation for the unitary frame potential. Our results elucidate the mechanisms underlying recent proposals for generating unitary $k$-designs through sequential quantum quenches in a unified manner.

### [83] [From Canonical to Tunable Phase Diagrams in Open Quantum Long-Range Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18542)
*Anish Acharya,Shamik Gupta*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了广义Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick（LMG）模型与热库耦合时的耗散动力学。通过线性与非线性的Lindblad主方程，推导了磁化演化方程，发现非线性情形下系统可弛豫至真正的非平衡稳态，且量子跳跃保持参数（jump-retention parameters）能够调控相边界与相变性质，为工程化长程相互作用开放量子系统中的非平衡相提供了机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用通常的线性Lindblad主方程（linear Lindblad master equation）结合热平衡跳跃过程推导磁化演化方程；并进一步引入非线性Lindblad方程（nonlinear Lindblad equation），通过跳跃保持参数（jump-retention parameters）描述不完全量子跳跃过程。

Result: 线性情形下系统稳态复现了模型的典型平衡相图；而非线性情形下系统弛豫至一个性质与线性情形截然不同的真实非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium stationary state），且跳跃保持参数可移动相边界甚至改变相变性质。

Conclusion: 耗散弛豫动力学与稳态行为之间存在直接联系；受控的量子跳跃保持是工程化长程相互作用开放量子系统中非平衡相的有效机制。

Abstract: We investigate the dissipative dynamics of a generalized Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick (LMG) model coupled to a thermal environment. In this generalized model, in addition to the conventional quadratic interaction, one considers quartic interactions between spin-$1/2$'s coupled all-to-all and evolving in presence of a transverse field. Employing the usual linear Lindblad master equation with thermally-balanced jump processes, we derive magnetisation evolution equations, and demonstrate that the corresponding stationary solution reproduces the canonical equilibrium phase diagram of the model. We then extend our analysis to a nonlinear Lindblad equation that incorporates imperfect quantum-jump processes in terms of jump-retention parameters. Here, remarkably, the system relaxes to a genuine nonequilibrium stationary state whose properties differ qualitatively from those obtained in the linear case. The jump-retention parameters provide tunable knobs that shift the phase boundaries and even modify the nature of the phase transitions with respect to the linear case. Our exact results establish a direct connection between dissipative relaxation dynamics and stationary-state behavior, while identifying controlled quantum-jump retention as a mechanism for engineering nonequilibrium phases in long-range interacting open quantum systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dicke模型是描述集体光-物质相互作用的基本模型，长期以来作为量子光学和凝聚态物理中探索广泛物理现象的测试平台。本研究旨在开发一个可在近期量子设备上实现该模型的变分框架，以推进对有限尺寸Dicke模型的高效量子模拟。

Method: 本文构建了一个变分框架（variational framework），在基于量子比特的全数字（digital）平台和量子比特-玻色子混合的数字-模拟（digital-analogue）平台上研究有限尺寸Dicke模型。同时引入了一类混合量子比特-玻色子变分拟设（hybrid qubit-bosonic variational ansatz），直接利用玻色子自由度以降低对量子资源的需求。

Result: 所提出的模型在大自旋极限下成功复现了Dicke模型的特征临界行为（critical behavior），并在经典量子计算机模拟器以及实际的离子阱量子计算机（trapped ion quantum computers）上得到实现，尽管后者受限于噪声。混合变分拟设进一步减少了量子资源消耗。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个可扩展且具有对称性意识（symmetry-aware）的变分量子模拟框架，适用于集体光-物质系统，并为在近期量子设备上高效模拟更一般的自旋-玻色子模型（spin-boson models）提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The Dicke model provides a fundamental description of collective light-matter interactions and has long served as a testbed for exploring a wide range of physical phenomena in quantum optics and condensed matter physics. In this work, we develop a variational framework for investigating the finite-size Dicke model on both fully qubit-based (digital) and hybrid qubit boson based (digital-analogue) quantum computing platforms. We show that the resulting model reproduces the characteristic critical behavior of the Dicke model in the appropriate large-spin limit while remaining suitable for implementation on both classical emulators of quantum computers and actual trapped ion quantum computers, albeit in the case of latter somewhat limited by noise. Finally, we introduce a complementary hybrid qubit-bosonic variational ansatz that directly exploits the bosonic degree of freedom to reduce quantum resources and discuss its potential implementation on hybrid quantum hardware. Our results establish a scalable, symmetry-aware framework for variational quantum simulations of collective light-matter systems and provide a pathway toward efficient simulations of more general spin-boson models on near-term quantum devices.

</details>


### [85] [Lower Bounds on Spectral Gaps of Parent Hamiltonians via Tensor Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19078)
*Milán Ádám Rozmán,András Molnár,Norbert Schuch*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文改进了由Fannes、Nachtergaele和Werner提出的鞅方法（martingale method），通过一种新技术能够精确且高效地计算局部基态空间的重叠（overlap），从而更有效地证明矩阵乘积态（Matrix Product States, MPS）父哈密顿量（parent Hamiltonian）的谱隙（spectral gap）下界，并在多个模型上进行了基准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 证明量子多体系统中基态空间以上的谱隙是一个核心难题，而现有的谱隙下界估计方法通常难以操作。该研究旨在改进经典鞅方法，使其能够更高效、更精确地计算关键量，从而克服现有技术的局限。

Method: 作者重新审视并改进了鞅方法的各个步骤，核心创新是提出了一种新技术，能够精确且高效地计算鞅方法中的关键量——局部基态空间的重叠，并由此简化了MPS父哈密顿量总是有能隙的证明过程。

Result: 通过多个模型的基准测试，改进后的鞅方法在谱隙下界估计上优于现有其他技术。此外，该数值导向的方法同步给出了一个显著简化的证明，表明任何（性质良好的）MPS的父哈密顿量总是有能隙的。

Conclusion: 这项工作为证明量子多体系统的谱隙提供了一种更强大且更简洁的工具，同时从理论上深化了对矩阵乘积态父哈密顿量能隙性质的理解。

Abstract: Proving spectral gaps above the ground space is a central problem in quantum many-body physics. Yet, finding lower bounds on the gap is notoriously difficult. We revisit the martingale method, originally developed by Fannes, Nachtergaele, and Werner [Fannes '92, Nachtergaele '96] to prove the existence of spectral gaps of parent Hamiltonians of Matrix Product States (MPS), and provide improvements to the different steps of the method. Most importantly, we devise a new technique which allows to compute the key quantity in the martingale method -- the overlap of local ground spaces -- exactly and efficiently. This enables a clear improvement of the method, allowing it to outperform other existing techniques to lower bound gaps, which we demonstrate by benchmarking on several models. Remarkably, our -- numerically motivated -- approach at the same time also yields a significantly simplified proof of the fact that parent Hamiltonians of any (well-behaved) MPS are always gapped.

### [86] [Dimension Reduction for Quantum Adaptive Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19156)
*Rishi Sundar,Thomas J. Elliott*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“路径-截断-修复”（route-truncate-repair）方法，将量子自适应智能体（quantum adaptive agents）在熵记忆（entropic memory）方面的优势转化为物理记忆维度（memory dimension）的实际降低，在保持高保真度的前提下显著压缩了量子智能体的记忆维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子自适应智能体能够比经典最优智能体存储更少的信息，但这一熵记忆优势并不必然转化为物理实现时记忆维度的降低。因此，需要一种方法将理论上的熵优势转化为可实际操作的维度缩减。

Method: 通过将参考输入过程（reference input process）路由经过智能体，得到时间矩阵乘积态（temporal matrix product state）表示，其规范键（canonical bond）被视为智能体的记忆。对该键进行截断（truncating），再局部修复（locally repairing）产生的动力学过程，从而得到一个维度更小且物理上有效的智能体，能够继续响应任意输入序列。同时，用一个保真度-散度证书（fidelity-divergence certificate）量化记忆维度与精度之间的权衡。

Result: 在基准自适应过程（benchmark adaptive processes）上，该方法在保持底层行为高保真度（high fidelity）的同时，实现了显著的记忆维度缩减（substantial dimension reduction）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了从熵记忆优势到实用化、低维自适应量子智能体的可行路径，表明量子记忆优势可转化为实际物理系统的维度压缩。

Abstract: Adaptive agents realise complex reactive behaviours by using a memory of past input stimuli and output actions to guide structured future responses. Quantum adaptive agents can operate while storing less information in memory than optimal classical counterparts; yet, this does not necessarily translate into a reduced dimension of the memory that must be physically realised. We introduce a route-truncate-repair procedure that converts entropic quantum memory advantages into reductions in memory dimension. Routing a reference input process through an agent yields a temporal matrix product state representation whose canonical bond is identified with the agent's memory. Truncating this bond and locally repairing the resulting dynamics produces a smaller, physically-valid agent that remains capable of responding to arbitrary input sequences. A fidelity-divergence certificate quantifies the resulting trade-off between accuracy and memory dimension. Benchmark adaptive processes exhibit substantial dimension reduction whilst preserving the underlying behaviour with high fidelity. These results establish a route from entropic memory advantages to practical, dimension-reduced adaptive quantum agents.

</details>

*Hlér Kristjánsson,Jonathan Brugger,Gabriel Dufour,Christian Scheppach,Andreas Buchleitner*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种基于网络节点间耦合与外部振动驱动协同作用的机制。通过构建弗洛凯-希尔伯特空间（Floquet-Hilbert space）中的反射对称性，并识别出占主导地位的弗洛凯态（Floquet states）双峰或三峰结构，推导出两种设计原则以抵抗无序性的干扰。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了一种通过耦合与驱动协同作用实现无序网络中高效量子传输的普适机制，其设计原则为构建人工量子传输系统提供了明确的理论指导。

Abstract: We propose a mechanism for fast and efficient quantum transport through disordered networks with variable on-site energies, inspired by photosynthetic complexes. The mechanism relies on an interplay between inter-site couplings of the network and driving by external vibrations. Two design principles are shown to ensure close-to-perfect transport despite the disorder, namely a reflection symmetry in Floquet-Hilbert space and the existence of a dominant doublet or triplet of Floquet states.

### [89] [Quantum Dynamics of $H_2^+$ in Orthogonal Two-Color Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18854)
*Jinzhen Zhu*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过全维度量子模拟研究了强正交激光场驱动下H₂⁺的解离电离过程，发现正交场能诱导出约4-5 eV的高能质子峰，并可通过载波包络相位实现相干调控，同时改变碎片角分布与电子-质子能量共享模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究强正交激光场的空间与时间几何构型如何影响H₂⁺的解离电离动力学，特别是揭示正交场中出现的、单色线偏振场中不存在的现象及其量子机制。

Method: 采用全维度量子模拟（full-dimensional quantum simulations），考虑等频正交分量（产生椭圆或圆偏振）以及正交800 nm和400 nm双色场，并结合时间相关态投影（time-dependent state projections）与从独立激发态出发的计算进行分析。

Result: 正交场诱导出质子动能释放（kinetic-energy-release, KER）谱中约4-5 eV的高能峰，该峰可通过垂直场分量的相对载波包络相位（carrier-envelope phase）进行相干调控；垂直场还破坏了主解离通道（3-3.5 eV）中清晰的电子-质子能量共享模式，并导致碎片角分布显著偏离主z轴。

Conclusion: 正交激光场的空间与时间几何构型为控制超快电子-核动力学（ultrafast electron-nuclear dynamics）提供了额外的自由度。

Abstract: We present full-dimensional quantum simulations of $H_2^+$ dissociative ionization driven by strong orthogonal laser fields. We consider equal-frequency orthogonal components, which generate elliptical or circular polarization depending on their relative phase and amplitude, as well as orthogonal $800$- and $400$-nm two-color fields. These two-dimensional fields strongly modify the fragmentation dynamics. Most notably, we identify a high-energy peak in the proton kinetic-energy-release (KER) spectrum at approximately $4-5$ eV that is absent from the corresponding single-color, linearly polarized calculations. The yield of this peak can be coherently controlled by varying the relative carrier-envelope phase of the perpendicular field component. The perpendicular field also disrupts the clear electron-proton energy-sharing pattern observed in the main $3-3.5$ eV dissociation channel, indicating more complex multichannel dynamics. Time-dependent state projections and calculations initiated from individual excited states attribute the additional peak to laser-induced vibrational excitation of $H_2^+$. Furthermore, the perpendicular field rotates the fragment angular distributions, causing the most probable proton and electron emission directions to deviate substantially from the principal $z$ axis. These findings demonstrate that the spatial and temporal geometry of orthogonal laser fields provides an additional degree of freedom for controlling ultrafast electron-nuclear dynamics.

### [90] [Fate of Metastable Vacua in the Type-II Two-Higgs Doublet Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18380)
*Debtosh Chowdhury,Kirtimaan A. Mohan,Poulami Mondal,Subrata Samanta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Type-II双希格斯二重态模型（Two-Higgs-Doublet Model, 2HDM）中，通过贝叶斯全局拟合（Bayesian global fit），在树图（tree level）和单圈（one-loop level）层次上采用规范无关（gauge-independent）方法分析电弱真空（electroweak vacuum）的稳定性，发现导致亚稳态电弱真空的参数空间区域在两种层次下均被排除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model, SM）中仅有一个希格斯二重态，而2HDM由于存在两个希格斯二重态，其标量势（scalar potential）可允许多个非简并真空（non-degenerate vacua）。为确保物理可行性，其中一个真空必须对应物理的电弱对称性破缺（electroweak symmetry breaking）真空，但该真空可能并非全局最小（global minimum），而是处于亚稳态（metastable）。因此，需要系统分析该物理真空的稳定性。

Method: 采用规范无关的方法，在树图和单圈层次上分析Type-II 2HDM中标量势的多极值（multiple extrema）结构以及电弱真空的稳定性。同时，结合下一阶领头阶幺正性约束（next-to-leading-order unitarity constraints）和最新实验测量结果，对Type-II 2HDM进行贝叶斯全局拟合。

Result: 贝叶斯全局拟合结果表明，在树图和单圈两个层次上，那些导致电弱真空处于亚稳态的参数空间区域均被排除。

Conclusion: 在Type-II 2HDM中，考虑高阶修正和实验约束后，物理电弱真空的亚稳态参数区域不再可行，这为模型参数空间的进一步限制提供了重要依据。

Abstract: The scalar potential of the Two-Higgs-Doublet Model (2HDM) can admit multiple non-degenerate vacua due to the presence of the two Higgs doublets unlike the Standard Model (SM). For a physically viable parameter point, one of these vacua must correspond to the physical electroweak (EW) symmetry breaking vacuum with the vacuum expectation value of about $246$ GeV. Given the complex structure of the scalar potential, the physical EW vacuum may be metastable in nature rather than the global minimum of the potential. In this work, we delineate regions of the parameter space in the Type-II 2HDM accommodating multiple extrema of the scalar potential and analyze, in a gauge-independent manner, the stability of the EW vacuum there at the tree level and beyond. A Bayesian global fit of the Type-II 2HDM, including next-to-leading-order unitarity constraints and the latest experimental measurements, indicates that parameter space regions leading to metastable EW vacua are excluded at both the tree and one-loop levels.

### [92] [D$e^+e^-$ffusion: Capturing the Beam-Beam Physics of $e^+e^-$ Collisions with Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18512)
*Antonio Chahine,Mariarosaria D'Alfonso,Jan Eysermans,Emmett Forrestel,Loukas Gouskos,Lindsey Gray,Katie Kudela,Haoyun Liu,Benedikt Maier,Dimitrios Ntounis,Christoph Paus,Umar Sohail Qureshi,Caterina Vernieri*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出 D$e^+e^-$ffusion，一种基于去噪扩散概率模型（denoising diffusion probabilistic model）的快速模拟替代方法，用于高亮度正负电子对撞机（如 FCC-ee）中束流诱导本底（beam-induced backgrounds）的非相干正负电子对产生（IPC）模拟。该模型在保持排列等变性（permutation-equivariant）的前提下，能以近四个数量级的速度提升生成事件样本，并忠实再现 IPC 的动力学与几何分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高亮度正负电子对撞机（如 FCC-ee）中，束流诱导本底主要由非相干正负电子对产生（incoherent pair creation, IPC）主导。现有蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo, MC）事件生成器计算开销极大，无法产生探测器与机器-探测器界面研究所需要的足够大样本量，形成了显著的模拟瓶颈。

Method: 采用去噪扩散概率模型（denoising diffusion probabilistic model, DDPM）作为快速模拟替代，构建了一个排列等变（permutation-equivariant）的集值（set-valued）代理模型 D$e^+e^-$ffusion。模型在小型 GuineaPig++ 样本上进行训练，并经过 Geant4 探测器模拟及基于 Transformer 的二分类器进行保真度评估。

Result: D$e^+e^-$ffusion 忠实再现了所有三种 IPC 产生过程的边缘与联合运动学、角度及位置分布。在探测器层面，二分类器在 ROC 曲线下面积（AUC）达到 0.553 ± 0.016。模型生成事件的速度比 Geant4 快近四个数量级。

Conclusion: D$e^+e^-$ffusion 提供了一种高效的快速模拟替代方案，可大幅缓解现有蒙特卡洛模拟的计算瓶颈，为 FCC-ee 设计研究提供了可行的快速模拟代理工具。

Abstract: Beam-induced backgrounds at high-luminosity $e^+e^-$ colliders, such as the FCC-ee, are dominated by incoherent pair creation (IPC), and require computationally expensive simulations with dedicated Monte Carlo (MC) event generators. Reliable detector and machine-detector interface studies necessitate event samples that are several orders of magnitude larger than what is practically attainable with existing MC. To alleviate this bottleneck, we present D$e^+e^-$ffusion, a denoising diffusion probabilistic model that operates as a permutation-equivariant, set-valued surrogate for fast IPC simulation. Trained on a small GuineaPig++ sample, D$e^+e^-$ffusion faithfully reproduces the marginal and joint kinematic, angular, and positional distributions of all three IPC production processes. In addition, we assess the fidelity at the detector level by propagating both Geant4 and D$e^+e^-$ffusion events through a Geant4 simulation of the CLD vertex detector and by training a transformer-based two-sample classifier; the classifier achieves an area under the ROC curve of $0.553 \pm 0.016$. The trained model generates events nearly four orders of magnitude faster than Geant4, paving the way for a fast-simulation surrogate for FCC-ee design studies.

</details>


### [93] [Prospects for $K_{L}\toπ^{0}ν\barν$, $K_S\toμ^+μ^-$, $K_L\toπ^0 \ell^+\ell^-$ and $\varepsilon^{\prime}/\varepsilon$ after the new $K^{+}\toπ^{+}ν\barν$ result from NA62](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19055)
*Monika Blanke,Andrzej J. Buras,Cristina Lazzeroni,Joel C. Swallow*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于NA62对K⁺→π⁺νν̄分支比的精确测量结果，探讨了在引入适当大的新复相位和小量右-handed耦合的条件下，K_L→π⁰νν̄分支比可在保持K⁺→π⁺νν̄和ε_K与标准模型一致的同時，增强一个数量级，并同时影响K_S→μ⁺μ⁻、K_L→π⁰ℓ⁺ℓ⁻及ε′/ε反常。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NA62最新测量显示K⁺→π⁺νν̄分支比与标准模型（Standard Model, SM）预言高度一致，引发了对K_L→π⁰νν̄衰变是否也会遭遇类似命运的疑问。当前KOTO实验对该衰变的上限仍比SM预言高出约两个数量级，而拟议中的KOTO II实验旨在首次发现该衰变并测量其分支比。

Method: 基于先前多篇论文的发现，在左-handed耦合之外引入适当大的新复相位（new complex phases）和少量右-handed s̄d耦合（right-handed couplings），构建一个具体的Z′粒子（Z′ scenario）模型进行理论分析。

Result: 在所选条件下，K_L→π⁰νν̄分支比可相较于SM预言增强一个数量级，同时保持K⁺→π⁺νν̄和ε_K与SM一致；K_S→μ⁺μ⁻（由LHCb研究）和K_L→π⁰ℓ⁺ℓ⁻（由KOTO II搜寻）可被大幅增强；Dual QCD所声称的ε′/ε比率反常可被消除。

Conclusion: 通过引入合适的新复相位和右-handed耦合，在保持某些关键衰变与SM一致的前提下，K_L→π⁰νν̄等稀有衰变可被显著增强，这为KOTO II等实验提供了明确的理论动机和可检验的预言。

Abstract: The recently announced NA62 measurement of the $K^{+}\toπ^{+}ν\barν$ branching ratio, based on 2016--2024 data, is fully consistent with its very accurate Standard Model (SM) prediction. While it is not excluded that the final result based on 2016--2026 data will deviate from the SM prediction, the question arises whether a similar fate awaits the $K_{L}\toπ^{0}ν\barν$ decay. This decay is currently being searched for by the KOTO experiment, with the present upper bound roughly two orders of magnitude above its very precise SM prediction. The proposed KOTO II experiment aims to provide the first discovery of the $K_{L}\toπ^{0}ν\barν$ decay and measure its branching ratio. Building on the findings of several previous papers we demonstrate that in the presence of suitably chosen large new complex phases and of a small amount of new right-handed $\bar s d$ couplings, in addition to the left-handed ones, the $K_{L}\toπ^{0}ν\barν$ branching ratio can still be enhanced by one order of magnitude with respect to the SM prediction while keeping both $K^{+}\toπ^{+}ν\barν$ and $\varepsilon_K$ SM-like. Simultaneously the decays $K_S\toμ^+μ^-$, studied by LHCb, and $K_L\toπ^0\ell^+\ell^-$, searched for by KOTO II, can be strongly enhanced and the anomaly in the ratio $\varepsilon^{\prime}/\varepsilon$, as claimed by Dual QCD, removed. We illustrate this with an example of a specific $Z^\prime$ scenario.

</details>


### [94] [Impact of Z-boson transverse-momentum resummation on PDF determination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19183)
*Juan M. Cruz-Martinez,Emanuele R. Nocera,Luca Rottoli,Paolo Torrielli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了小横动量重求和（small-transverse-momentum resummation）对中性流Drell-Yan过程轻子对产生中胶子部分子分布函数（PDF）确定的影响。基于NNPDF方法，纳入LHC上ATLAS和CMS在8和13 TeV的Z玻色子横动量谱数据，在NNLO QCD加上NNLL精度的小横动量重求和修正下进行PDF拟合，发现重求和改善了数据描述并稳定了胶子PDF，但对扩展拟合运动学区域的结论不具决定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小横动量重求和修正对精确PDF确定的影响尚未被系统研究，尤其是在纳入高精度LHC测量数据后。本文旨在定量评估该修正对PDF拟合、数据描述一致性以及拟合运动学区域选择的影响。

Method: 基于NNPDF方法的PDF拟合框架，理论计算采用NNLO微扰QCD加上来自RadISH的NNLL精度的小横动量重求和修正。通过重正化尺度（renormalisation scale）和因子化尺度（factorisation scale）变化构建理论协方差矩阵（theory covariance matrix）以量化缺失的高阶不确定度。重新处理了8 TeV数据，用数值稳定的NNLO计算替代过去分析中使用的固定阶预言，并移除了额外数值不确定度。

Result: 重求和修正改善了Z玻色子横动量数据的描述，对确保PDF拟合的整体一致性至关重要。但它并不支持将拟合运动学区域扩展到横动量低于几十GeV以下的区间。重求和对PDF的影响适中，主要表现为在LHC现象学相关的运动学区域中稳定了胶子PDF。理论不确定度之间的相关性处理在亚百分比精度测量中可能起核心作用。

Conclusion: 小横动量重求和是保证高精度PDF拟合一致性的关键修正，但其对扩展拟合范围的作用有限。理论不确定度之间的关联性处理将在未来更高精度测量中变得愈发重要。

Abstract: We study the impact of small-transverse-momentum resummation for neutral-current Drell-Yan lepton-pair production on the determination of collinear parton distribution functions (PDFs). We focus on measurements of the Z-boson transverse-momentum spectrum performed by ATLAS and CMS at the LHC at centre-of-mass energies of 8 and 13 TeV, and include them in PDF fits based on the NNPDF methodology. Theoretical predictions are computed at next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) in perturbative QCD and are supplemented with small-transverse-momentum resummation corrections at next-to-next-to-next-to-leading logarithmic accuracy obtained with RadISH. Missing higher-order uncertainties are accounted for through a theory covariance matrix constructed from renormalisation- and factorisation-scale variations. We first revisit the treatment of the 8 TeV data, replacing the fixed-order predictions used in previous analyses with numerically stable NNLO calculations, and removing the additional numerical uncertainties introduced in earlier fits. We then assess the impact of the 13 TeV measurements, of resummation corrections, and of progressively lowering the minimum cut on the dilepton transverse momentum. We find that resummation improves the description of the Z boson transverse-momentum data and is essential for ensuring the overall consistency of the PDF fits. Nevertheless, it does not conclusively support extending the fitted kinematic region to transverse momenta below a few tens of GeV. The impact of resummation on PDFs is moderate, leading primarily to a stabilisation of the gluon PDF in a kinematic region of relevance for LHC phenomenology. Finally, we comment on the fact that the treatment of correlations among theoretical uncertainties may play a central role in PDF fits to measurements with percent- and sub-percent-level precision.

</details>

*Ramkumar Radhakrishnan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用光锥规范（light cone gauge），对快价模（fast valence）与软模（soft mode）进行玻恩-奥本海默（Born-Oppenheimer）分离，并实施程函近似（eikonal approximation）。利用幺正性条件及光锥微扰论（light-cone perturbation theory, LCPT）的显式费曼图计算，确定展开系数，这些系数是非对易价色荷密度算符 ρ 的泛函。

Result: 获得了完全正规序（fully normal ordered）的软胶子产生与湮灭算符级数形式的演化算符 Ω；通过对纯杨-米尔斯软哈密顿量在 g 和 g² 阶的对角化，发现不同福克扇区（Fock sectors）之间的非对角混合矩阵元相互抵消，最终相干背景场能量正比于 ρ²。

Abstract: We construct the soft gluon light cone wave function of a fast moving hadron and the associated unitary evolution operator $Ω$ up to $\mathcal{O}(g^{2})$ in pure Yang Mills theory $(N_{f} = 0)$, within the Color Glass Condensate (CGC) framework. Working in light cone gauge, we perform a Born Oppenheimer separation between fast valence and soft modes and implement the eikonal approximation, which allows $Ω$ to be written as a fully normal ordered series in soft gluon creation and annihilation operators. The expansion coefficients are functionals of the non-commuting valence color charge density operators $ρ$. We fix the coefficients by using the unitarity and explicit diagrammatic calculations within light-cone perturbation theory (LCPT). As an application, we diagonalize the pure Yang Mills soft Hamiltonian through orders $g$ and $g^{2}$ and show that the off diagonal mixing elements between Fock sectors cancel leading to the coherent background field energy proportional to $ρ^{2}$.

### [96] [Astrophysical Neutrino Sources as Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19254)
*Carlos A. Argüelles,P. S. Bhupal Dev,Bhaskar Dutta,Gonzalo Herrera,Nicholas Kamp,Jason Kumar,Stephan A. Meighen-Berger,Mudit Rai,Ian M. Shoemaker*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种从高能中微子点源数据中提取非弹性 pp 和 pγ 截面的双边约束方法，通过电磁观测约束天体物理参数，使得截面成为唯一自由参数。将该方法应用于 IceCube、KM3NeT 等观测数据，得到的约束覆盖质心系能量从约 1 GeV 至约 10^5 GeV，部分约束远超 LHC 和 HERA 可及范围，且严于幺正性（unitarity）极限。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过电磁观测或理论论证独立约束所有天体物理输入参数（宇宙线光度和靶密度），使非弹性 pp 和 pγ 截面成为唯一自由参数，从而从中微子点源数据提取截面的双边界限（two-sided bounds）。

Result: 将框架应用于 IceCube 与 TXS 0506+056、NGC 1068、银道面（Galactic Plane）的关联事件、11个X射线亮塞弗特星系（Seyfert galaxies）的叠加样本、KM3NeT 的极高能事件 KM3-230213A 以及未来极高能中微子观测，获得的截面约束覆盖质心系能量从约 1 GeV 到约 10^5 GeV。部分约束远超 LHC 可及范围，pγ 截面约束则超越 HERA，且多项约束严于幺正性极限。

Conclusion: 该框架可有效利用中微子天文数据对超出对撞机能标的非弹性强子截面进行独立约束，某些能区获得了比理论极限更严格的上限，展示了中微子天文学作为高能物理探针的潜力。

Abstract: High-energy neutrinos arise from processes at large center-of-mass energies, offering a window to test physics at comparable scales or beyond those accessible in collider experiments on Earth. Here, we present a recipe for extracting two-sided bounds on the inelastic $pp$ and $pγ$ cross sections from neutrino point-source data, by independently constraining every astrophysical input (cosmic-ray luminosities and target densities) through electromagnetic observations or theoretical arguments. The cross section is then the only remaining free parameter. Applying this framework to the IceCube associations with TXS~0506+056, NGC~1068, and the Galactic Plane, to a stacked population of eleven X-ray bright Seyfert galaxies, to the ultra-high-energy KM3NeT event KM3-230213A, and to projected observations of ultra-high-energy neutrinos, we obtain constraints that span center-of-mass energies from $\sqrt{s}\sim 1$ GeV to $\sim 10^{5}$ GeV, some of which are well beyond the reach of the LHC and, for the $pγ$ channel, beyond HERA. Several of these bounds are more stringent than unitarity limits.

### [97] [Gravitational waves from self-resonance during reheating with a quantum-corrected inflaton potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18381)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以α-吸引子T模型为基础，引入由重标量粒子（heavy scalar）诱导的单圈科尔曼-温伯格修正作为局域量子修正的具体实现，并利用格点模拟（lattice simulations）计算由此产生的引力波谱。

Result: 当量子修正充分抑制势能极小值附近的二次项时，暴涨子自共振（inflaton self-resonance）会产生尖峰型（peaked）GW谱；若二次项系数变为负值，则产生平滑增强型（smooth and enhanced）GW谱。所有引力波信号均位于超高频波段（频率>kHz）。

Conclusion: 预加热阶段产生的引力波信号有望成为探测暴涨子势能量子修正的探针，从而间接提供关于底层紫外物理的信息。

Abstract: We investigate how localized quantum corrections to the inflaton potential affect preheating dynamics and the resulting stochastic gravitational wave (GW) spectrum. When these corrections sufficiently suppress the quadratic term of the potential near its minimum, inflaton self-resonance can produce a peaked GW spectrum. On the other hand, we find that a smooth and enhanced spectrum can appear if the quadratic term acquires a negative coefficient. As a concrete realization, we analyze the $α$-attractor T-model with a one-loop Coleman--Weinberg correction induced by a heavy scalar and compute the resulting GW spectra using lattice simulations. The GW signals lie in the ultra-high-frequency regime at frequencies above the kHz range. These results suggest that GW signals from preheating may probe quantum corrections to the inflaton potential, thereby providing indirect information about the underlying UV physics.

### [98] [Integral representation of the neutrino mass-squared differences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19340)
*I. Alikhanov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种关于中微子质量平方差Δm²_ij的积分表示（integral representation），用于建立中微子质量间的解析关系，并结合宇宙学边界和JUNO实验数据给出了最轻中微子质量的上限（m₁<0.0023 eV, 95% C.L.），同时推导出其他中微子质量及有效质量的约束，并揭示了Gatto-Sartori-Tonin型质量关系的来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定绝对中微子质量标度（absolute neutrino mass scale）是粒子物理学中最重要的挑战之一；为约束理论模型，需要建立中微子质量之间的精确关系。

Method: 提出一种中微子质量平方差Δm²_ij的简单积分表示（integral representation），作为传统振荡参数视角的补充；在此基础上，结合宇宙学求和边界（cosmological bound）与JUNO实验数据，推导最轻中微子质量m₁的解析条件m₁＜√(61Δm²_21)/30，并进一步导出m₂、m₃及有效电子中微子质量m_{ν_e}和Majorana中微子质量m_{ββ}的解析约束。

Result: 基于JUNO实验数据，得到m₁的竞争性上限为m₁<0.0023 eV（95% C.L.）；同时获得了m₂和m₃的实用解析界限，以及有效电子中微子质量（effective electron neutrino mass）m_{ν_e}和Majorana中微子质量（Majorana neutrino mass）m_{ββ}的允许范围。

Conclusion: 所提出的积分表示能够直接导出中微子质量间的Gatto-Sartori-Tonin型关系（Gatto-Sartori-Tonin type relations），表明该方法不仅为当前实验数据提供约束，也为未来数据中的中微子质量分析提供了可推广的解析框架。

Abstract: Determining the absolute neutrino mass scale remains one of the most compelling challenges in particle physics. To constrain theoretical models, establishing precise relations among neutrino masses is essential. We propose a simple integral representation of the neutrino mass-squared differences $Δm_{ij}^2$ that provides a complementary perspective on these oscillation parameters. We then demonstrate its utility through several examples. Specifically, assuming stringent cosmological bounds that confine the sum of neutrino masses near the normal ordering floor, we derive an analytical condition for the lightest neutrino mass, $m_1 < \sqrt{61Δm^2_{21}}/30$. Using recent data from the JUNO experiment, this yields a competitive upper limit of $m_1<0.0023$ eV (95\% C.L.). We also formulate practical analytical bounds for $m_{2}$ and $m_{3}$ adaptable to future data, and translate the results into allowed ranges for the effective electron and Majorana neutrino masses $m_{ν_e}$ and $m_{ββ}$. Finally, we show that neutrino mass relations of the Gatto-Sartori-Tonin type emerge directly from the proposed integral representation.

### [99] [Feynman Integrals Meet Second-Order Partial Differential Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18406)
*Xiang Chen,Hantian Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于二阶偏微分方程（PDE）的方法，将多圈费曼积分（Feynman integrals）视为平衡问题（equilibrium problem）进行求解。通过伽辽金离散化（Galerkin discretization）和有限元法（finite element method）验证了该方法的可行性，实现了对二维圈四点多维相空间（phase space）的全局一次性求解，建立了微扰量子场论（perturbative quantum field theory）与现代偏微分方程方法之间的新联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多圈费曼积分是微扰量子场论中计算散射振幅的核心工具，但其在多维相空间中的高效求解一直是难点。现有方法往往需要逐点或逐区域分别计算，缺乏全局一次性求解的手段，限制了高精度理论计算在唯象学（phenomenology）中的应用。

Method: 将多圈费曼积分重新表述为一个平衡问题，导出对应的二阶偏微分方程（partial differential equation）；然后对相应的变分形式（variational form）进行伽辽金离散化（Galerkin discretization），并采用有限元法（finite element method）进行数值求解。

Result: 成功通过有限元法计算了双圈四点费曼积分（two-loop four-point Feynman integrals），证明该方法能够在多维相空间的广阔区域上一次性完成积分求解。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了微扰量子场论与现代偏微分方程方法之间的新联系，为简化广泛的唯象学应用（phenomenological applications）提供了潜在的技术路径。

Abstract: We propose a second-order partial differential equation method to solve multi-loop Feynman integrals as an equilibrium problem. As a proof-of-concept demonstration, we perform a Galerkin discretization of the corresponding variational form and employ the finite element method to compute two-loop four-point Feynman integrals. This method can solve the integral over a broad region of multi-dimensional phase space once and for all. This work establishes a new connection between perturbative quantum field theory and modern partial differential equation methods, with the potential to streamline a wide range of phenomenological applications.

</details>


### [100] [Standard Model Symmetries and the Nested Embeddings of $\mathbb{R}\subset\mathbb{C}\subset\mathbb{H}\subset\mathbb{O}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18450)
*N. Furey*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将 $\mathbb{O}\oplus\mathbb{H}\oplus\mathbb{C}\oplus\mathbb{R}$ 视为其乘法代数（multiplication algebra）上的模（module），为规范场论（gauge field theory）中标准模型（Standard Model）的内部对称性（internal symmetries）——包括电弱对称性破缺前后的 $\mathfrak{g}_{SM}$ 和 $\mathfrak{g}_{LE}$——提供了一种起源解释。通过引入 $\mathbb{Z}_2^n$ 分次代数（graded algebra）、湮灭最高阶体积元（volume element）及等迹条件（equal-trace condition），推导出对称性代数结构；弱超荷（weak hypercharge）$Y$ 和电荷（electric charge）$Q$ 算符呈现简洁的 $\sum \frac{1}{n}\mathbb{I}_{n\times n}$ 形式。该向量空间可嵌入到16维实代数 $\mathbb{V}$ 中，对称性源于 $\mathbb{R}\subset\mathbb{C}\subset\mathbb{H}\subset\mathbb{O}\subset\mathbb{V}$ 的嵌套包含序列；在 $\mathbb{V}=\mathbb{S}$（sedenions）情形下，该序列构成Cayley-Dickson塔（Cayley-Dickson tower）。本文定义了粒子物理的自同态模型（endomorphic model），并将 $End_\mathbb{R}(\mathbb{V})\simeq Cl(0,8)$ 与Bott周期性粒子物理（Bott Periodic Particle Physics）联系起来，同时评论了多重复结构（complex structure）与重子不对称问题（baryon asymmetry problem）的可能关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型内部对称性（internal symmetries）的起源至今尚未被充分解释；该论文尝试从代数结构的视角，特别是使用 $\mathbb{O}\oplus\mathbb{H}\oplus\mathbb{C}\oplus\mathbb{R}$ 作为其乘法代数上的模，为 $\mathfrak{su}(3)_C\oplus\mathfrak{su}(2)_L\oplus\mathfrak{u}(1)_Y$（电弱对称性破缺前）和 $\mathfrak{su}(3)_C\oplus\mathfrak{u}(1)_Q$（电弱对称性破缺后）这两种对称性提供具体的起源故事。

Method: 论文将 $\mathbb{O}\oplus\mathbb{H}\oplus\mathbb{C}\oplus\mathbb{R}$ 视为 $\mathbb{Z}_2^n$ 分次代数（graded algebra），通过湮灭特定最高阶体积元（volume element）并对反厄米算符（anti-hermitian operator）施加等迹条件（equal-trace condition），精确导出 $\mathfrak{g}_{SM}$ 和 $\mathfrak{g}_{LE}$。此外，借助辅助虚数单位（auxiliary imaginary unit），将该15维实向量空间嵌入到16维实代数 $\mathbb{V}$ 中，并利用嵌套包含序列 $\mathbb{R}\subset\mathbb{C}\subset\mathbb{H}\subset\mathbb{O}\subset\mathbb{V}$ 分析对称性的结构。

Result: 弱超荷算符（weak hypercharge）$Y$ 和电荷算符（electric charge）$Q$ 获得了 $\sum \frac{1}{n}\mathbb{I}_{n\times n}$ 这一极为简洁的形式；建立了 $End_\mathbb{R}(\mathbb{V})\simeq Cl(0,8)$ 与Bott周期性粒子物理（Bott Periodic Particle Physics）的联系；发现多重复结构（complex structure）的存在可能与重子不对称问题（baryon asymmetry problem）存在潜在关联。

Conclusion: 标准模型的内部对称性可以从 $\mathbb{O}\oplus\mathbb{H}\oplus\mathbb{C}\oplus\mathbb{R}$ 的代数结构及其嵌入到16维代数 $\mathbb{V}$ 的过程中自然导出；论文提出的自同态模型（endomorphic model）为粒子物理的对称性分类提供了新的代数框架，并暗示了多重复结构与宇宙学中重子不对称现象的深层联系。

Abstract: Where do the Standard Model's internal symmetries come from? Treating $\mathbb{O}\oplus\mathbb{H}\oplus\mathbb{C}\oplus\mathbb{R}$ as a module for its own multiplication algebra enables a particular origin story for the Standard Model's pre-Higgs, $\mathfrak{g}_{SM}:=\mathfrak{su}(3)_{C} \oplus \mathfrak{su}(2)_{L} \oplus \mathfrak{u}(1)_{Y},$ and post-Higgs, $\mathfrak{g}_{LE}:=\mathfrak{su}(3)_{C} \oplus \mathfrak{u}(1)_{Q},$ symmetries. We recognize both these endomorphisms and their modules alike as $\mathbb{Z}_2^n$-graded algebras. Then, annihilating certain highest grade (volume) elements, and imposing an equal-trace condition on anti-hermitian operators leads precisely to $\mathfrak{g}_{SM}$ and $\mathfrak{g}_{LE}$. Weak hypercharge and electric charge operators, $Y$ and $Q,$ take on a remarkably simple form: $\sum \frac{1}{n}\mathbb{I}_{n\times n}$.
  With the help of auxiliary imaginary units, this 15 $\mathbb{R}$ dimensional $\mathbb{O}\oplus\mathbb{H}\oplus\mathbb{C}\oplus\mathbb{R}$ embeds naturally as a vector space into several well-studied 16 $\mathbb{R}$ dimensional algebras, which we generically refer to as $\mathbb{V}.$ With this embedding, the Standard Model's internal symmetries may then be seen to arise in part from the sequence of nested inclusions: $\mathbb{R}\subset\mathbb{C}\subset\mathbb{H}\subset \mathbb{O}\subset\mathbb{V}.$ In the sedenionic case of $\mathbb{V} = \mathbb{S},$ the full sequence becomes a Cayley-Dickson tower. We define the notion of endomorphic models of particle physics, and connect $End_\mathbb{R}(\mathbb{V})\simeq Cl(0,8)$ to the earlier ideas of Bott Periodic Particle Physics. We comment on a possible connection between the existence of multiple complex structures and the baryon asymmetry problem.

</details>


### [101] [Transport phenomena and observables associated with viscous properties of an anisotropic hot QCD medium at finite baryon asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18581)
*Shubhalaxmi Rath,Nicolás A. Neill*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过求解相对论玻尔兹曼输运方程（relativistic Boltzmann transport equation），在松弛时间近似（relaxation time approximation）方法下，计算了存在重子不对称（baryon asymmetry）和膨胀诱导的弱动量各向异性（weak-momentum anisotropy）的热QCD介质的剪切粘度和体粘度，并分析了这些粘性性质对普朗特数、雷诺数、比剪切粘度和比体粘度等可观测量（observables）的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解重子不对称热QCD介质在超相对论性重离子碰撞（ultrarelativistic heavy-ion collisions）初期的膨胀诱导动量各向异性下，其粘性输运现象及相关可观测量，以揭示介质中的声衰减、流动性质、流体行为及共形对称性（conformal symmetry）特征。

Method: 采用松弛时间近似方法求解相对论玻尔兹曼输运方程，计算剪切粘度和体粘度；通过准粒子模型（quasiparticle model）在有限温度、各向异性和重子不对称条件下引入部分子间的相互作用。

Result: 膨胀诱导的各向异性降低了剪切粘度和体粘度，无论是否存在重子不对称；重子不对称介质中的粘性系数高于无重子介质；各向异性对重子不对称介质的影响与对无重子介质的影响同样显著；上述结果归因于动量各向异性对分布函数的压缩以及部分子的色散关系（dispersion relations）。

Conclusion: 膨胀诱导的各向异性显著调制了重子不对称介质中的粘性相关可观测量，为介质的声衰减、流动特性、流体行为及共形对称性提供了新的理论预测。

Abstract: We have studied the transport phenomena and observables associated with viscous properties of a baryon asymmetric hot QCD medium in the presence of a weak-momentum anisotropy arising due to the asymptotic expansion of the matter in the initial stages of ultrarelativistic heavy-ion collisions. This study facilitates the understanding of the sound attenuation in the medium through the Prandtl number, the nature of flow through the Reynolds number, fluid behavior through the specific shear viscosity, and conformal symmetry through the specific bulk viscosity for an anisotropic hot QCD medium at finite baryon asymmetry. We have determined the shear and bulk viscosities by solving the relativistic Boltzmann transport equation in the relaxation time approximation method. The interactions among partons are incorporated through their distribution functions within the quasiparticle model of hot QCD medium at finite temperature, anisotropy and baryon asymmetry. We have observed a decrease in the shear and bulk viscosities in the presence of expansion-induced anisotropy for baryonless scenario as well as for baryon asymmetric scenario. Conversely, these viscosities are larger in baryon asymmetric matter compared to their counterparts in baryonless matter. The impact of anisotropy on baryon asymmetric matter is observed to be as conspicuous as on baryonless matter. The above results are broadly attributed to the squeezing of the distribution function due to the momentum anisotropy generated by the asymptotic expansion of baryon asymmetric matter and the dispersion relations of partons in the presence of anisotropy. Additionally, the aforesaid observables are also significantly modulated by the expansion-induced anisotropy in the baryon asymmetric medium, indicating new predictions for the sound attenuation, flow characteristics, fluid behavior and conformal symmetry of the said medium.

</details>


### [102] [Domain Walls From Confining Bubbles: $SU(N_{c})$ Yang Mills at Finite $θ$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18800)
*Bruno Missoni,Enrico Morgante,Nicklas Ramberg*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用改进的全息QCD（Improved Holographic QCD, IHQCD）模型研究有限θ角下SU(N_c)纯杨-米尔斯理论（pure Yang-Mills theory）中的禁闭相变（confinement phase transition），发现临界温度随θ增大而降低，减少了过冷程度。禁闭相变完成后，由于有限θ下杨-米尔斯理论的多分支真空结构（multi-branched vacuum structure），可能产生畴壁（domain walls）网络，并探讨了畴壁与禁闭相变动力学的相互作用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究有限θ角（θ ≠ 0）下SU(N_c)纯杨-米尔斯理论中禁闭相变的特征，特别是θ对临界温度和过冷（supercooling）行为的影响；同时关注禁闭相变完成后畴壁网络的形成及其与相变动力学的潜在相互作用。

Method: 采用改进的全息QCD模型（Improved Holographic QCD, IHQCD），在大N_c近似下分析有限θ角对禁闭相变临界温度的影响，并基于多分支真空结构讨论畴壁的产生机制。

Result: 对于大且固定的N_c，临界温度随θ增大而降低，从而减少了禁闭相变中的过冷程度。禁闭相变完成后，畴壁网络可能由多分支真空结构产生。畴壁的产生涉及强耦合非共形一级相变（strongly coupled non-conformal FOPTs）中气泡合并（bubble coalescence）过程的真空分配、流体动力学（hydrodynamics）和局部再加热（local reheating）等动力学因素。

Conclusion: 强调畴壁与禁闭相变的相互作用是一种包含真空分配、流体动力学和局部再加热效应的动力学过程，可能影响标度律（scaling regime）的趋近行为；还需调节相关参数，方有可能通过畴壁湮灭（domain wall annihilation）与禁闭相变的相互作用产生引力波（gravitational waves）的可观测信号。

Abstract: We study the confinement phase transition in SU($N_{c}$) pure Yang-Mills theory at finite $θ\neq 0$ using the Improved Holographic QCD (IHQCD) model. We show that the critical temperature, as a function of $θ$ for large but fixed $N_{c}$, is reduced, thus decreasing the amount of supercooling in the confinement phase transition. Upon completion of the confinement phase transition, a network of domain walls can be produced, owing to the multi-branched vacuum structure of Yang-Mills theory at finite $θ$. We highlight the potential interplay between the produced domain walls and the confinement phase transition dynamics. We emphasize that DW production from bubble coalescence in strongly coupled non-conformal FOPTs is a dynamical process of vacuum assignment, hydrodynamics, and local reheating effects, all potentially affecting the approach towards the scaling regime. Lastly, we demonstrate the level of tuning necessary for potentially interesting imprints from gravitational waves through domain wall annihilation and its interplay with the confinement PT.

### [103] [Chromoelectric and chromomagnetic matching to scalar and spin-two nucleon structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18831)
*Arkadiy I. Syamtomov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了重夸克偶素（heavy quarkonium）与标量（scalar）和自旋-2（spin-two）胶子算符之间多极相互作用（multipole interaction）的重整化群（renormalization group, RG）一致实现，推导了匹配系数关系、演化方程及运动学投影，并实现了标量与引力结构中色磁极化率（chromomagnetic polarizability）效应的因子化分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 紧凑重夸克偶素通过多极相互作用与标量及自旋-2胶子算符耦合，但领先阶色电（chromoelectric）序下匹配系数满足的约束关系（C₂^Φ = -C_S^Φ）会被独立的色磁极化率（chromomagnetic polarizability）打破，因此需要构建RG一致的框架来处理这一修正并澄清其与核子结构的关联。

Method: 在固定MS（modified minimal subtraction）方案下构建RG一致实现；利用QCD迹恒等式（trace identity）将纯胶子标量匹配条件转化为不变基（invariant basis），并固定重表达于尺度依赖基（scale-dependent basis）时所需的夸克质量系数；通过阈对齐对称运动学（threshold-aligned symmetric kinematics）得到正则自旋非翻转投影；使用Breit框架（Breit frame）计算将该投影与类时间隔（spacelike t）下的非对角螺旋度表示（off-diagonal helicity representation）关联。

Result: 标量和自旋-2演化方程的线性性使得色磁依赖在纯胶子维度四匹配框架内因子化为R_{2/0}^Φ(t;ρ_Φ)=[(1+ρ_Φ)/(1-ρ_Φ)]R_{2/0}^Φ(t;0)；非对角螺旋度形式是运动学效应而非额外的动力学自旋翻转；阈对齐对称运动学中正则自旋非翻转投影包含A_i(t)及组合3B_i(t)-D_i(t)。

Conclusion: 该结果将依赖于态的重夸克偶素匹配与标量及引力核子结构（gravitational nucleon structure）分离开来，并明确陈述了该因子化成立所需的前提假设。

Abstract: Compact heavy quarkonium couples through the multipole interaction to scalar and spin-two gluonic operators. At leading chromoelectric order the corresponding matching coefficients satisfy $C_2^Φ=-C_S^Φ$; an independent chromomagnetic polarizability lifts this relation within the general CP-even, spin-independent, local two-gluon interaction at dimension four and zero derivative order. We construct an RG-consistent realization in a fixed $MS$ convention. The QCD trace identity converts the gluon-only scalar matching condition into an invariant basis and fixes the correlated quark-mass coefficient required when the interaction is re-expressed in the scale-dependent basis away from the matching scale, whereas leading-logarithmic singlet evolution induces a quark spin-two coefficient. In threshold-aligned symmetric kinematics, the canonical-spin non-flip projection contains $A_i(t)$ and the combination $3B_i(t)-D_i(t)$. An explicit Breit-frame calculation relates this projection to an off-diagonal helicity representation for nonzero spacelike $t$; the off-diagonal form is kinematic rather than an additional dynamical spin flip. Linearity of the scalar and spin-two evolution factorizes the chromomagnetic dependence of their ratio as $R_{2/0}^Φ(t;ρ_Φ)=[(1+ρ_Φ)/(1-ρ_Φ)]R_{2/0}^Φ(t;0)$ within the gluon-only dimension-four matching setup. The result separates state-dependent quarkonium matching from scalar and gravitational nucleon structure and states explicitly the assumptions under which this factorization holds.

</details>


### [104] [Holographic Soliton Crystals for Dense Nuclear Matter and Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19125)
*Lorenzo Bartolini,Sven Bjarke Gudnason,Jonas Mager,Anton Rebhan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于Witten-Sakai-Sugimoto（WSS）全息QCD模型，超越均匀近似，通过孤子描述直接构建致密重子物质的核物质状态方程（EOS）。利用双重子相互作用势构建面心立方（FCC）晶体近似量子液体，计算能量密度、化学势和压强。通过固定't Hooft耦合和WSS标度校准对称物质EOS，并加入夸克质量项重现物理π介子质量。扩展至β平衡物质后，获得的混合EOS和中子星可观测量与NICER约束兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有核物质状态方程在全息QCD框架下多基于均匀近似（homogeneous ansatz），未能充分利用全息重子的孤子（solitonic）描述来构建致密重子物质。本文旨在通过更直接的孤子方法构建致密重子物质的核物质EOS，并检验其与中子星观测的兼容性。

Method: 采用WSS模型中的全息重子孤子描述，利用弯曲背景中由点状（芯）瞬子（instantons）产生的线性化孤子尾所导出的两重子相互作用势，构建最近邻处于最强吸引通道的无限面心立方（FCC）晶体，作为重子量子液体的近似。由此计算能量密度$\mathcal{E}(n_B)$、化学势$\mu_B$和压力$P$。通过固定't Hooft耦合$\lambda$和WSS标度$M_{\rm KK}$并加入夸克质量项校准对称物质EOS，使其复现饱和密度与起始化学势特性及物理π介子质量$m_\pi=135\,\mathrm{MeV}$。

Result: 校准后的参数与真空介子扇区所需参数保持合理接近，其修正与稠密介质中的Brown-Rho标度（Brown-Rho scaling）一致，饱和点不可压缩性量级正确，与均匀近似形成鲜明对比。扩展至β平衡物质后，得到的混合EOS和中子星可观测量与NICER约束兼容。

Conclusion: 基于全息QCD孤子描述构建核物质EOS的方法优于均匀近似，能够自洽地描述从饱和核物质到致密中子星物质的转变，且与现有中子星观测（NICER）相符。

Abstract: We construct a nuclear-matter equation of state (EOS) from holographic QCD in the Witten-Sakai-Sugimoto (WSS) model, going beyond the homogeneous ansatz by building dense baryonic matter more directly from the solitonic description of holographic baryons. Employing the two-baryon interaction potential obtained from the linearized soliton tails sourced in the curved background by point-like (core) instantons, we assemble an infinite face-centered cubic (FCC) crystal with nearest neighbors in the most attractive channel as an approximation to the quantum liquid of baryons and compute the energy density $\mathcal{E}(n_B)$, the chemical potential $μ_B$, and the pressure $P$. We calibrate the symmetric-matter EOS by fixing the 't Hooft coupling $λ$ and the WSS scale $M_{\rm KK}$ to saturation-density and onset-chemical-potential properties, and by including a quark-mass term to reproduce the physical pion mass $m_π=135\,\mathrm{MeV}$. This fit turns out to remain reasonably close to the parameters required by the vacuum meson sector, while their modification is consistent with Brown-Rho scaling in a dense medium, and the incompressibility at saturation is of the correct order of magnitude, both in clear contrast to the homogeneous approximation. We then extend to beta-equilibrated matter, using phenomenological input for the symmetry energy, and obtain hybrid EOS and neutron-star observables that are compatible with the NICER constraints.

</details>


### [105] [Detecting Cosmological Stasis with Future Gravitational Wave Observatories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18449)
*Gabriela Barenboim,Anne-Katherine Burns*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统地将宇宙学静态期（cosmological stasis）在暴胀引力波背景（IGWB）中的观测预言映射到当前和未来引力波探测器的灵敏度频段上，分析了四种静态期情景的可探测性，并刻画了标准模型相变精细结构以及静态期终结过渡的有限宽度效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨宇宙学静态期在暴胀引力波背景中的可观测特征，并将其与多个引力波探测器的灵敏度区间进行定量比较，从而评估这些情景能否被实际探测到。

Method: 利用伴随论文中导出的闭式分段频谱模板（closed-form piecewise spectral template），生成针对NANOGrav、SKA、LISA、DECIGO、BBO、爱因斯坦望远镜和宇宙探索者等探测器频段的可探测性图谱；并解析建模标准模型相变引起的g*精细结构（fine structure）以及静态期终结过渡的有限宽度（finite-width）效应。

Result: 在谱抑制（ws<1/3）情景中，BBO在ws≳0.2且张标比r接近普朗克上限（r=0.036）的区域可探测静态期特征；在谱增强（ws>1/3）情景中，BBO可在张标比为O(0.01)时覆盖整个(ws,ΔN)参数空间。标准模型电弱相变和QCD相变分别在~2.6×10⁻⁶ Hz和~3.6×10⁻⁹ Hz处引入约20%和约53%的频谱台阶（spectral steps）。当静态期终结温度低于QCD能标时，这些台阶落入静态期频段内，作为辅助特征。静态期终结过渡使得f_end处的频谱断裂在log频率窗口ΔN_trans×3(1+ws)/4内被平滑，只要ΔN_stasis≫ΔN_trans，一致性关系C²=C²(α)仍可检验。

Conclusion: BBO是探测宇宙学静态期特征的最有前景的探测器之一；标准模型相变在IGWB中留下的精细结构可作为静态期情景的补充签名；静态期终结过渡的有限宽度效应对可探测性影响有限，条件容易满足。

Abstract: We map the observational predictions of cosmological stasis in the inflationary gravitational wave background onto the sensitivity bands of current and planned gravitational wave detectors. Using the closed-form piecewise spectral template derived in the companion paper, we generate detectability maps for four stasis scenarios: canonical, dynamical scalar, vacuum-energy/matter, and vacuum-energy/radiation across the frequency bands probed by NANOGrav, SKA, LISA, DECIGO, BBO, the Einstein Telescope, and Cosmic Explorer. For scenarios in which the spectrum is suppressed, $w_s < 1/3$, the stasis feature is detectable by BBO in the region of $(w_s,ΔN)$ parameter space in which $w_s\gtrsim 0.2$ for tensor-to-scalar ratios close to the Planck upper limit, r = 0.036. For scenarios in which the spectrum is enhanced, $w_s > 1/3$, the stasis feature is detectable by BBO across the entire $(w_s,ΔN)$ parameter space for tensor-to-scalar ratios of $O(0.01)$. We characterize the Standard Model (SM) $g_*$ fine structure of the IGWB, showing that SM phase transitions introduce spectral steps of $\approx 20\%$ (electroweak, at $\sim 2.6\times10^{-6}$~Hz) and $\approx 53\%$ (QCD, at $\sim 3.6\times 10^{-9}$~Hz). For stasis scenarios with end-of-stasis temperatures below the QCD scale these steps fall inside the stasis band and constitute additional spectral features that complement the primary signature. Finally, we model the finite-width end-of-stasis transition phenomenologically, demonstrating that the spectral break at $f_{end}$ is smoothed over a log-frequency window $ΔN_\mathrm{trans}\times 3(1+w_s)/4$, and that the consistency relation $C^2=C^2(α)$ remains testable provided $ΔN_\mathrm{stasis}\gg ΔN_\mathrm{trans}$, a condition easily satisfied for all scenarios of phenomenological interest.

</details>

### [106] [Sound Induced Hall Currents in Weyl Exciton Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18335)
*Xinhong Zhou,Varsha Subramanyan,Qing-Dong Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现外尔激子绝缘体（Weyl excitonic insulator）在有质量相（massive phase）中存在一种由轴向场（axial field）驱动的耗散横向电流，该响应区别于普通矢量势输运和无质量外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal）的轴向响应，来源于质量诱导的贝里结构（Berry structure）重构，并预言声波可产生所需动态轴向场从而实现可探测的声致霍尔输运（sound-induced Hall transport）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal）的无能手性节点（gapless chiral node）可产生反常输运，而有质量（gapped）外尔系统通常被认为会丧失此类特征；本文旨在探索有质量外尔系统中是否可能存在全新的输运响应，并寻找实验探测手段。

Method: 基于有质量外尔系统的低能 Breit 型哈密顿量（Breit-type Hamiltonian），引入应变诱导的轴向势（axial potential），发展半经典波包理论（semiclassical wave-packet theory），分析动态轴向势驱动的耗散横向电流的微观起源。

Result: 识别出一种由动态轴向势（dynamical axial potential）产生的耗散横向电流，该响应在定性上既不同于有质量系统中的普通矢量势输运，也不同于无质量外尔半金属中的轴向响应；物理上源于质量诱导的贝里结构重构，在系统因手性化学势不平衡（chiral chemical-potential imbalance）而偏离平衡时被激活。横声波（transverse sound wave）可产生所需的动态轴向场，使用真实材料参数可估算出可探测的电流幅度。

Conclusion: 声致霍尔输运可直接用于探测外尔激子序（Weyl excitonic order），并为外尔材料中相互作用诱导质量（interaction-generated mass）提供输运特征信号。

Abstract: Weyl semimetals exhibit anomalous transport controlled by their gapless chiral nodes, while gapped Weyl systems are often expected to lose such distinctive responses. Here we show that Weyl excitonic insulators instead host a new form of axial-field-driven transport that exists only in the massive phase. Starting from the low-energy Breit-type Hamiltonian for a gapped Weyl system coupled to strain-induced axial potentials, we develop a semiclassical wave-packet theory and identify a dissipative transverse current generated by a dynamical axial potential. This response is qualitatively distinct from both ordinary vector-potential transport in gapped systems and axial responses in gapless Weyl semimetals. Physically, it originates from a mass-induced Berry structure of the reconstructed Weyl bands, which becomes active when the system is driven out of equilibrium by a chiral chemical-potential imbalance. We show that transverse sound waves provide a natural route to generate the required dynamical axial field and estimate the resulting current for realistic material parameters. Our results reveal sound-induced Hall transport as a direct probe of Weyl excitonic order and provide a transport signature of interaction-generated mass in Weyl materials.

</details>

*Carlos Payá,Ángel Ibabe,Mario Gómez,Thomas Kanne,Jesper Nygård,Ramón Aguado,Pablo San-Jose,Eduardo J. H. Lee,Elsa Prada*

TL;DR: 本文通过实验证明了全壳纳米线（full-shell nanowires）中存在的Caroli-de Gennes-Matricon（CdGM）类 analogs，其特征表现为超阻尼约瑟夫森结（overdamped Josephson junctions）临界电流和零偏电阻中独特的偏斜（skewness）指纹。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于全壳纳米线制备超阻尼约瑟夫森结，测量其临界电流（critical current）和零偏电阻（zero-bias resistance）随轴向磁场的变化，从中提取CdGM类比态的特征偏斜（skewness）指纹。

Result: 实验观察到了CdGM类比态导致的特征偏斜模式，该效应叠加在由磁通量子化（fluxoid quantization）引起的壳层超导能隙的Little-Parks振荡上。

Abstract: Full-shell hybrid nanowires consisting of a semiconductor core fully enveloped by a superconducting shell have emerged as a platform to study Caroli-de Gennes-Matricon (CdGM) analogs. These subgap states can be considered a synthetic version of CdGM states in Abrikosov vortices. Unlike conventional CdGM states, these analogs exhibit a level spacing comparable to the superconducting gap, making them readily observable via tunneling spectroscopy techniques. The spectral density of CdGM analogs follows a characteristic skewed pattern as a function of applied axial magnetic field, an effect that is superimposed on the Little-Parks oscillations of the shell's gap induced by fluxoid quantization. Here, we provide experimental evidence for CdGM analogs through a distinctive skewness fingerprint in the critical current and zero-bias resistance of overdamped Josephson junctions based on full-shell nanowires.

### [108] [Fragile Topology is Unstable Under Translation Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18386)
*Yoonseok Hwang,Saavanth Velury,Taylor L. Hughes*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个系统性的框架，用于判断在扩大原胞（unit-cell enlargement）操作下，脆弱拓扑相（fragile topological phases）能否被平庸化。研究发现，所有由对称性指标指示的二维脆弱拓扑相都可以在足够大的超胞（supercell）中被平滑地连接到原子绝缘体（atomic insulator），表明脆弱拓扑在平移对称性精化下仅有有限稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有多种响应现象和材料实现被提出用于脆弱拓扑相（fragile topological phases），但其中许多现象也可能出现于原子绝缘体（atomic insulator）中，因此脆弱相究竟拥有哪些特有性质尚不明确。扩大原胞为回答这一问题提供了自然视角，但此前缺乏系统性的稳定性判别框架。

Method: 基于物理中的电子-正电子图像（electron-positron picture），并通过对动量空间对称性数据（momentum-space symmetry data）进行希尔伯特基（Hilbert basis）分析，建立了在满足空间群对称性（space-group symmetry）的原胞扩大下判断平庸化的系统性判据。随后对所有二维壁纸群（wallpaper groups），无论是否包含自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和/或时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry），进行了系统分类。

Result: 所有由对称性指标指示的脆弱拓扑相（fragile phase）在合适的有限超胞中都与原子绝缘体（atomic insulator）绝热相连，因此可以被任意小的、保持对称性的微扰平庸化。这意味着脆弱拓扑在平移对称性精化（translation-symmetry refinement）下仅有有限稳定性。

Conclusion: 脆弱拓扑相的命运可能依赖于平移对称性破缺的微扰（如电荷密度波有序（charge-density-wave ordering）），并且那些对平移精化不敏感的物理特征不太可能唯一地刻画脆弱拓扑。

Abstract: Fragile topological phases become trivial upon the addition of suitable trivial bands, distinguishing them from stable topological phases. Nevertheless, various response phenomena and material realizations have been proposed for fragile phases. At the same time, many of these phenomena can also occur in atomic insulators, leaving open the question of what properties are specific to fragile phases. Enlarging the unit cell offers a natural perspective on this question. Band folding increases the number of bands in a manner analogous to adding trivial bands. In this work, we establish a systematic framework for determining the stability of fragile topology under unit-cell enlargement. We first establish a systematic criterion for trivialization under enlargements compatible with space-group symmetry, grounded in a physical electron-positron picture and formulated through a Hilbert-basis analysis of momentum-space symmetry data. We then show that, for all two-dimensional wallpaper groups, with or without spin-orbit coupling and/or time-reversal symmetry, every symmetry-indicated fragile phase is adiabatically connected to an atomic insulator in a suitable finite supercell and can therefore be trivialized by an arbitrarily small symmetry-preserving perturbation. Our results reveal that fragile topology has only finite stability under translation-symmetry refinement. This highlights that the fate of a fragile phase can depend on translation-symmetry-breaking perturbations, such as charge-density-wave ordering, and suggests that physical signatures insensitive to translation refinement are unlikely to uniquely characterize fragile topology.

### [109] [Quantum-Enabled Spintronic "Small" Antennas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18469)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 新型天线的运作基于非经典原理（non-classical principles），而非传统的经典电磁学框架，从而突破了尺寸与性能之间的固有折衷。

Result: 新型天线实现了微型化并保持了高辐射效率，使此前无法实现的嵌入式应用成为可能；此外，单个远小于波长的元件即可实现波束操控，而传统方法需要多个远大于波长的天线单元组成大型相控阵（phased array）；部分天线还具备隐身（stealth）特性，适用于安全与隐蔽通信（covert communication）。

Conclusion: 基于非经典原理的新一代天线克服了传统微型化瓶颈，兼具小型化、波束操控与隐身能力，有望成为一种颠覆性技术。

Abstract: Antennas transmit information wirelessly from one location to another via electromagnetic waves. Miniaturizing them, however, is challenging since the radiation efficiencies of all traditional antennas, based on the principles of classical electromagnetics, plummet when their dimensions are shrunk to tiny fractions of the radiated wavelength. Lately, a new generation of antennas whose operations are underpinned by non-classical principles have been demonstrated and they can overcome this limitation. This enables embedded applications that were hitherto inaccessible. In addition, beam steering, which normally requires a large phased array (multiple antenna elements each much larger than the wavelength), can now be accomplished with a single element much smaller than the wavelength. Some of these antennas also have stealth attributes for secure and covert communication, which makes this new genre a disruptive new technology.

### [110] [Conductivity of the Landau levels of two-dimensional Dirac cones and gapped nodal-rings in the quantum limit under impurity-potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18769)
*Ipsita Mandal,Sanskar Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在超量子极限下，利用Kubo-Bastin形式体系，计算了二维狄拉克锥（Dirac cones）和有隙节点环（gapped nodal rings, GNRs）在垂直磁场中的直流磁导率，揭示了二者截然不同的输运特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 区分二维狄拉克锥与有隙节点环（GNRs）在极端量子极限下的磁输运行为，建立GNRs体系可分辨的输运指纹，为相关实验提供理论框架。

Method: 采用Kubo-Bastin形式体系（Kubo–Bastin formalism），在超量子极限（ultraquantum limit，仅最低朗道能级部分占据）下，针对点状、高斯和汤川三种杂质势（impurity potentials）计算输运系数。

Result: 狄拉克锥：点状杂质下纵向电导率与磁场无关，高斯和汤川势下为磁场的单调函数；霍尔电导率因相邻朗道能级的粒子-空穴对称性而恒为零。GNRs：非单调的拉伸对勾型朗道能级谱导致有效最低朗道能级（LLL）随磁场增大向更低指标迁移，两种电导率均出现显著振荡结构，纵向响应在LLL简并处产生共振峰，霍尔电导率呈现锯齿状并伴随尖锐零交叉。

Conclusion: 两种体系在极端量子极限下具有截然不同的输运指纹，为GNRs的磁输运实验提供了理论解释框架。

Abstract: We investigate the dc magnetoconductivity of two-dimensional Dirac cones and gapped nodal rings (GNRs) subjected to a perpendicular magnetic field, which quantises the electronic spectrum into Landau levels (LLs). Working in the ultraquantum limit, where only the lowest LL (LLL) is partially occupied, we employ the Kubo--Bastin formalism to compute the transport coefficients for pointlike, Gaussian, and Yukawa impurity-potentials. For the Dirac case, the longitudinal conductivity is field-independent for pointlike impurities and a monotonic function of $B$ for the Gaussian and Yukawa potentials, while the Hall conductivity vanishes identically owing to the particle-hole symmetry of the two neighbouring LLs. The GNR case is qualitatively different: its non-monotonic stretched-checkmark LL spectrum causes the effective LLL to migrate to successively lower indices as the field increases, producing a pronounced oscillatory structure in both conductivities. The longitudinal response develops resonant peaks at LLL degeneracies, while the Hall conductivity traces out a sawtooth pattern with sharp zero-crossings at these same points. These results establish distinct transport fingerprints for the two systems in the extreme quantum limit, and provide a theoretical framework for interpreting magnetotransport experiments on GNRs.

### [111] [Charge transfer mediated anomalous photoluminescence enhancement in monolayer MoS2 graphene heterostructure via polystyrene assisted wet transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18733)
*Anagha Gopinath,Arpan De,Dipak Maity,Jyoti Mohanty*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种通过聚苯乙烯辅助湿法转移工艺在n型单层MoS₂与单层石墨烯的异质结中实现反常光致发光增强的现象。研究表明，该增强源于三子（trion）向激子（exciton）的转换，以及界面电荷转移和石墨烯表面官能化（羟基与环氧基团）的协同作用。该工作提出了一种实用的界面工程策略，可提升MoS₂/石墨烯异质结构的激子发射性能，推动其在可规模化光电器件中的应用。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用聚苯乙烯辅助湿法转移工艺将n型单层MoS₂与单层石墨烯集成形成异质结构；利用光致发光光谱（photoluminescence spectroscopy）分析激子与三子的转变；使用开尔文探针力显微镜测量功函数变化；通过拉曼光谱检测石墨烯G峰与2D峰的位移；采用X射线光电子能谱分析石墨烯表面的官能化；结合基于密度泛函理论（DFT）的Bader电荷分析量化官能团对电荷转移的贡献。

Result: 异质结构形成后，光致发光出现反常增强，主要源于三子向激子的转换；开尔文探针力显微镜显示MoS₂的功函数增加了600毫电子伏特（meV），结合石墨烯更高的功函数，表明电子从MoS₂转移至石墨烯；拉曼光谱中石墨烯G峰与2D峰的位移进一步证实了层间电荷转移；X射线光电子能谱检测到石墨烯表面存在羟基与环氧基官能化；DFT Bader电荷分析量化了这些官能团在促进层间电荷转移中的作用。

Conclusion: 聚苯乙烯辅助湿法转移是一种实用的界面工程策略，可有效增强MoS₂/石墨烯异质结构中的激子发射，克服了传统异质结构中光致发光猝灭的局限，为该类异质结构在可规模化光电器件中的应用奠定了重要基础。

Abstract: Van der Waals MoS2 graphene heterostructures are compelling candidates for high performance electronic and optoelectronic device applications. However, the interlayer charge transfer typically quenches the photoluminescence of monolayer MoS2, limiting the use of these heterostructures in light emitting applications. In this work, we report an anomalous photoluminescence enhancement in n-type monolayer MoS2 by integrating it with monolayer graphene via polystyrene assisted wet transfer process. Photoluminescence spectroscopy reveals a dominant trion to exciton conversion in the heterostructure. Kelvin probe force microscopy shows a 600 meV increase in the work function of MoS2 upon heterostructure formation. This work function shift, together with the higher work function of graphene, signifies electron transfer from MoS2 to graphene. Shifts in the graphene G and 2D Raman modes further corroborate the interlayer charge transfer. Hydroxyl and epoxy functionalization of graphene following heterostructure formation is evidenced by X ray photoelectron spectroscopy. DFT based Bader charge analysis quantifies the role of these functional groups in facilitating interlayer charge transfer. Collectively, our findings establish polystyrene assisted wet transfer as a practical interface engineering strategy for enhancing excitonic emission in MoS2 graphene heterostructures, thereby advancing their potential for scalable optoelectronic devices.

### [112] [Double anticrossings induced by nonlinear magnon interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18807)
*Geil Emdi,Tomosato Hioki,Koujiro Hoshi,Takahiko Makiuchi,Aoi Yamauchi,Eiji Saitoh*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示非线性磁子相互作用（magnon interaction）如何在一个单一系统中动态生成多个耦合通道，理解三重磁子散射在其中的作用机制。

Method: 通过测量泵浦功率对双重反交叉的间隙大小和中心频率偏移的影响，并结合高磁场下能量守恒对三磁子劈裂的抑制效应，识别出三磁子散射为底层非线性过程。

Result: 观察到泵浦诱导的双重反交叉现象，其间隙和频率偏移强烈依赖泵浦功率；高磁场下反交叉消失；确定三磁子散射为底层机制；非简并三磁子劈裂产生两个不同频率的磁子布居，各自形成驻波模式并与Kittel模式独立耦合。

Conclusion: 非线性磁子相互作用可以在单一系统中动态生成多个有效耦合通道，这一发现为基于磁子（magnon）的非线性物理和器件设计提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: We observe pump-induced double anticrossings whose gap sizes and center-frequency shifts depend strongly on pump power, indicating a nonlinear mechanism. The anticrossings vanish at high magnetic fields, where energy conservation suppresses three-magnon splitting, thereby identifying the underlying process as three-magnon scattering. We attribute the double anticrossings to nondegenerate three-magnon splitting, which generates two magnon populations at distinct frequencies. Each population forms a standing-wave mode and couples independently to the Kittel mode, giving rise to two effective coupling channels. These results demonstrate that nonlinear magnon interactions can dynamically generate multiple coupling channels within a single system.
