### [113] [Multiscale ensemble Monte Carlo of transport and gas sensing in monolayer MoS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18895)
*Lado Filipovic*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个基于维也纳EMC求解器的自洽系综蒙特卡洛（EMC）框架，用于单层MoS₂的输运模拟。该框架内置完整的玻尔兹曼输运散射机制（包括声子、极化光学、压电耦合、衬底声子、带电杂质和表面粗糙度散射），通过第一性原理DFPT验证了七个关键输运参数，并实现了从微观电子-声子耦合到宏观器件端电流与传感器响应的多尺度耦合。模型成功复现了CVD单层器件在空气和真空中的转移特性，以及氧气、NO₂和NH₃传感的浓度响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维半导体（如单层MoS₂）兼具技术上有用的带隙和全表面几何结构，在场效应晶体管（FET）通道和化学敏感器件中具有应用潜力。预测性器件设计需要一种输运模型，该模型须满足三个条件：（i）基于物理而非经验，（ii）经实验验证，（iii）能够跨越从电子-声子耦合到端电流和传感器响应的多尺度范围。

Method: 采用自洽系综蒙特卡洛（ensemble Monte Carlo, EMC）框架，基于维也纳EMC求解器构建，包含玻尔兹曼输运（Boltzmann transport）核心和完整的本征与非本征散射堆栈（变形势声子与谷间声子、极化光学Fröhlich与压电耦合、远程衬底声子、屏蔽带电杂质与表面粗糙度散射），考虑简并自由载流子统计和自洽泊松耦合。本征输运参数通过第一性原理密度泛函微扰理论（DFPT）验证，七个关键参数与参考参数化一致。通过多尺度耦合，将EMC速度-场特性输入一维速度饱和沟道模型，并扩展到气体吸附传感响应。

Result: 七个本征输运参数（晶格常数、导带有效质量、带隙、波恩有效电荷、纵向光学声子能量以及两个面内声速）与第一性原理DFPT参考参数化一致。在空气和真空条件下，模型复现了CVD单层器件的测量转移特性。在传感扩展中，模型复现了氧气分压下的电导响应以及多个独立器件中NO₂和NH₃传感的浓度依赖性。

Conclusion: 该自洽EMC框架为单层MoS₂提供了一个从第一性原理出发、经实验验证的多尺度输运模型，能够可靠预测场效应器件特性和气体传感响应，为二维半导体的预测性器件设计奠定了基础。

Abstract: Two-dimensional semiconductors, such as monolayer MoS$_2$, combine a technologically useful band gap with an all-surface geometry, making them attractive both as field-effect-transistor channels and as chemically sensitive devices. Predictive device design requires a transport model that is (i) physically grounded rather than empirical, (ii) validated against experiments, and (iii) able to span the scales from electron-phonon coupling to terminal current and sensor response. We present a self-consistent ensemble Monte Carlo (EMC) framework for monolayer MoS$_2$ built on the ViennaEMC solver, comprising a Boltzmann-transport kernel with a full intrinsic and extrinsic scattering stack (deformation-potential acoustic and intervalley phonons, polar-optical Fröhlich and piezoelectric coupling, remote substrate phonons, screened charged-impurity and surface-roughness scattering), degenerate free-carrier statistics, and a self-consistent Poisson coupling. The intrinsic transport parameters are verified against first-principles density-functional perturbation theory (DFPT), and seven quantities (lattice constant, conduction-band effective mass, band gap, Born effective charges, the longitudinal-optical phonon energy, and both in-plane sound velocities) agree with the reference parametrization. In a multiscale coupling, the EMC velocity-field characteristic feeds a one-dimensional velocity-saturation channel model, which captures the velocity-saturated field dependence and reproduces the measured transfer characteristics of a CVD monolayer device in air and vacuum. Finally, an ambient/adsorbate extension reproduces the measured conductivity response to oxygen partial pressure and the concentration dependence of NO$_2$ and NH$_3$ sensing measured in several independent devices.

</details>


### [114] [Bridging distributed quantum materials via multi-hotspot vacuum: remote Cooper pairing and Andreev teleportation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18916)
*Zuzhang Lin,Zhijian Song,Chengxin Xiao,Wang Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于多间隙裂环谐振器（multi-gap split-ring resonator, SRR）的架构，利用腔体真空涨落在毫米级分离的空间节点间诱导平衡态的多体相互作用，将分布式的介观量子物质耦合为单一关联系统。以太赫兹SRR耦合两个金属莫尔超晶格为例，通过密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）和精确对角化（exact diagonalization）计算证明了远程库珀配对（remote Cooper pairing）及安德森隐形传态（Andreev teleportation）等非局域现象，纠缠熵随介观晶格面积线性增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多体量子系统通常局限于空间局域的物质，难以在平衡态下实现毫米级分离的介观量子节点间的长程量子关联。本文旨在设计一种平衡态量子网络架构，使分布式介观物质能通过腔量子电动力学（cavity quantum electrodynamics）机制产生稳定的非局域多体关联，进而实现远程配对和量子资源分发。

Method: 核心设计是多间隙裂环谐振腔（SRR），其腔模光子具有多个热点（hot spots），每个热点位于分裂间隙（split gap）处，具有深度亚波长体积且间隙间相距毫米级。腔的真空涨落（vacuum fluctuations）在嵌入多个间隙的量子材料之间介导多体相互作用，使其在平衡态下耦合为单一关联系统。作为实例，考虑一个太赫兹SRR的两个分裂间隙分别邻近金属莫尔超晶格（metallic moiré superlattice），腔真空中的虚光子交换在间隙间介导流-流相互作用（current-current interaction）。理论计算采用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）和精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法。

Result: 吸引性相互作用通道导致远程库珀配对，表现为介观超导（mesoscopic superconductivity）。一个孔（hole）在一个间隙入射可转化为远程间隙处的出射电子（outgoing electron），即安德森隐形传态（Andreev teleportation）。两个介观超晶格间的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）随介观晶格面积（总格点数）线性增长。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种平衡态下介观物质的量子网络新范式，能够实现非局域功能（emergent nonlocal functionalities）和分布式量子资源（distributed quantum resources）。远程库珀对和安德森隐形传态等非局域现象为构建长程量子关联的介观量子系统提供了原理性基础。

Abstract: We introduce an architecture where mesoscopic quantum matter distributed over spatially separated nodes can be correlated in equilibrium, creating an unprecedented form of many-body quantum system. Central to the design is a multi-gap split-ring resonator (SRR) where the cavity photon has multiple hot spots -- each with deep-subwavelength volume at a split gap and separated by millimeter-scale distances. The cavity's vacuum fluctuations can then mediate a many-body interaction that bridges the distributed quantum materials embedded in the multiple gaps, coupling them into a single correlated mesoscopic system in equilibrium. As an example, we consider a THz SRR with two split gaps, each proximitized to a metallic moiré superlattice, where virtual exchange of a photon in the cavity vacuum mediates a current-current interaction across the gaps. The inherent attractive interaction channels lead to remote Cooper pairing reminiscent of mesoscopic superconductivity, demonstrated with density matrix renormalization group and exact diagonalization calculations. With the two constituents of a Cooper pair now paired across a millimeter-scale separation, a hole incident at one split gap can be converted into an outgoing electron at the remote gap, a process we term Andreev teleportation. The entanglement entropy between the two mesoscopic superlattices is shown to scale linearly with the area (total number of sites) of the mesoscopic lattice. Our results suggest an intriguing paradigm for equilibrium quantum networks of mesoscopic matter that enable emergent nonlocal functionalities and distributed quantum resources.

</details>


### [115] [Pure Spin Bulk Photovoltaic Effect in an Altermagnetic Higher-Order Topological Insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19018)
*Sibgat Ulah,Ankan Bhattacharyya,Manisha Thakurathi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究PT对称拓扑绝缘体与d波交变磁体构成的二维异质结中的体光伏效应（BPVE），建立了适用于PT简并能带的自旋BPVE非阿贝尔理论，发现通过调控Néel矢量方向可实现纯自旋光电流与拓扑相变，揭示了非线性自旋输运对拓扑和磁对称性的敏感响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有BPVE理论局限于孤立非简并能带，无法处理PT对称性导致的简并能带系统。本文旨在发展适用于PT简并流形（PT-degenerate manifolds）的非阿贝尔（non-Abelian）自旋BPVE理论，并探索拓扑绝缘体-交变磁体（altermagnet）异质结中自旋光电流的产生与控制机制。

Method: 构建由拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）与d波交变磁体耦合而成的PT对称二维异质结模型，发展非阿贝尔自旋BPVE理论以描述PT对称性约束下的简并能带；通过分析Néel矢量方向变化对体系对称性和拓扑相的影响，系统研究非线性光响应的特征。

Result: Néel矢量位于xy面内时，异质结实现C_{4z}T对称性保护的二阶拓扑绝缘体（second-order topological insulator, SOTI）相；C_{2z}对称性完全抑制二阶电荷光电流，但允许自旋光电流存在，从而产生纯自旋光伏效应（pure spin photovoltaic effect）。线偏振光驱动自旋移位电流（spin shift current），圆偏振光驱动自旋注入电流（spin injection current），两者均随局域狄拉克质量（local Dirac mass）变号而反转。Néel矢量转向z轴时，SOTI相转变为一阶拓扑绝缘相，电荷与自旋光电流共存。

Conclusion: PT对称交变磁体-拓扑绝缘体异质结可作为产生和调控纯自旋光电流的通用平台（versatile platform），同时揭示了非线性自旋输运（nonlinear spin transport）可作为探测拓扑相和磁对称性的灵敏探针。

Abstract: We investigate the bulk photovoltaic effect (BPVE) in a $PT$-symmetric two-dimensional heterostructure consisting of a topological insulator coupled to a $d$-wave altermagnet. To describe the symmetry-enforced degenerate bands of this system, we develop a non-Abelian formulation of the spin BPVE, extending the conventional theory from isolated nondegenerate bands to $PT$-degenerate manifolds. We show that the orientation of the Néel vector controls both the topological phase and the character of the nonlinear optical response. When the Néel vector lies in the $xy$-plane, the heterostructure realizes a second-order topological insulator (SOTI) protected by $C_{4z}T$ symmetry. The system also retains $C_{2z}$ symmetry, which completely suppresses second-order charge photocurrents while allowing finite spin photocurrents. As a result, the BPVE becomes an intrinsically pure spin photovoltaic effect, generating a dc spin current without an accompanying charge current. We find that linearly polarized light drives a spin shift current, whereas circularly polarized light generates a spin injection current. Both responses undergo a sign reversal whenever the local Dirac mass changes sign. As the Néel vector is rotated toward the $z$-axis, the SOTI phase transforms into a first-order topological insulating phase, leading to the coexistence of charge and spin photocurrents. Our results establish $PT$-symmetric altermagnetic topological-insulator heterostructures as a versatile platform for generating and controlling pure spin photocurrents and reveal nonlinear spin transport as a sensitive probe of topology and magnetic symmetry.

### [116] [Electrostatic Control Enables Robust Helical Edge Channel Transport in III-V Quantum Spin Hall Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19051)
*Manuel Meyer,Tobias Fähndrich,Sebastian Schmid,Justus Walter,Martin Kamp,Adriana Wolf,Sergey Krishtopenko,Guillaume Sigu,Jean-Baptiste Rodriguez,Eric Tournie,Gerald Bastard,Frederic Teppe,Fabian Hartmann,Sven Höfling,Benoit Jouault*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子自旋霍尔输运受寄生体态（bulk）和边缘态（edge）贡献限制，亟需一种可靠策略来抑制这些寄生导电通道。

Method: 在AlSb准衬底上生长双栅InAs/GaInSb/InAs三量子阱，通过静电调控实现宏观与微观霍尔条（Hall bar）器件中的多探针输运分析。

Result: 宏观器件中（尺寸超过相位相干长度（phase coherence length））呈现绝缘体态和恒定边缘电阻；微观器件中（边缘长度小于相位相干长度）边缘电阻在宽电场范围内保持鲁棒且量子化，仅超过阈值后出现寄生边缘贡献。

Conclusion: 双栅调控是抑制寄生导电、稳定螺旋边缘输运的可靠策略，为III-V族量子自旋霍尔系统提供了可重现的可调谐拓扑输运平台。

Abstract: Quantum spin Hall transport in InAs/GaInSb-based two-dimensional topological insulators can be limited by parasitic bulk and edge contributions. We demonstrate that these limitations are effectively mitigated through electrostatic control in dual-gated InAs/GaInSb/InAs trilayer quantum wells grown on AlSb quasi-substrates. In macroscopic Hall bars exceeding the phase coherence length, a multi-probe analysis reveals an insulating bulk and a constant edge resistance over a wide electric-field range. In microscopic devices with edge lengths below the phase coherence lengths, the edge resistance remains robust and quantized accross a broad field range, revealing the intrinsic resilience of helical edge channels to electric-field perturbations. Only beyond a threshold value, parasitic edge contributions emerge. These results establish dual gating as a reliable strategy to suppress parasitic conduction while stabilizing helical edge transport, providing a versatile and reproducible platform for tunable topological transport in III-V quantum spin Hall systems.

### [117] [Magnonic crystalline properties of stripe textures in thin ferromagnetic films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19165)
*Joo-Von Kim,Victor Leroy,Titiksha Srivastava*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过微磁学模拟（micromagnetic simulations）研究铁石榴石薄膜中条形磁畴结构（ordered stripe domains）的自旋波（spin wave）能带，发现布里渊区中心和边界的能隙随外场响应不同，外场和立方各向异性（cubic anisotropy）还会在简约布里渊区中点诱导出额外能隙，其行为被解释为畴壁晶格的Peierls型畸变（Peierls-type distortion）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可调谐的磁畴周期结构为研究磁振子能带结构（magnon band structure）随晶格常数的演化提供了理想平台，这种调控在物理刻蚀材料中难以实现。

Method: 采用微磁学模拟计算模型铁石榴石薄膜的自旋波谱，重点分析外磁场和立方各向异性的影响。

Result: 布里渊区中心（Brillouin-zone center, k = 0）和边界（zone boundary, k = ±π/a）的能带隙（band gaps）对外加磁场的响应不同，且在较宽的频率和波矢范围内出现；垂直磁场或立方各向异性会使简约布里渊区中点（k = ±π/2a）产生额外的能隙。

Conclusion: 上述行为被解释为畴壁晶格（domain-wall lattice）的Peierls型畸变，即“上”和“下”磁畴在有效垂直场作用下交替膨胀和收缩。

Abstract: Ordered stripe domains in ferromagnetic thin films form a natural one-dimensional crystal for propagating spin waves. Their spatial periodicity can be tuned readily with an applied magnetic field, making these systems an attractive platform for exploring how magnon band structures evolve as a function of the lattice constant $a$, a tuning that is difficult to achieve in physically patterned materials. In this work we employ micromagnetic simulations to calculate the spin-wave spectra of a model iron-garnet film, focusing on the influence of the external field and of cubic anisotropy. We find that band gaps at the Brillouin-zone center ($k = 0$) and at the zone boundary ($k = \pm π/a$) respond differently to the applied field, appearing over a broad range of frequencies and wave vectors. When a perpendicular magnetic field or cubic anisotropy is present, additional gaps can appear at the middle of the reduced Brillouin zone ($k = \pm π/2a$). This behavior is interpreted as a Peierls-type distortion of the domain-wall lattice, wherein ``up'' and ``down'' domains alternately expand and contract under the influence of the effective perpendicular field.

### [118] [Quantized heat flow in moiré chern bands of bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19205)
*Santanu Samai,Debangan Sarkar,Abhijit Halder,T. Taniguchi,K. Watanabe,Subroto Mukerjee,Saurabh Kumar Srivastav,Anindya Das*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过约翰逊噪声测温法测量了双层石墨烯-六方氮化硼莫尔超晶格中量子霍尔、陈绝缘体及相互作用驱动的对称性破缺陈绝缘体态的热导，发现热导以热导量子（κ₀T）为单位量子化，且仅由陈数（Chern number）决定，与拓扑态的微观起源无关，直接揭示了霍夫施塔特带（Hofstadter bands）中普适的拓扑热输运现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电输运实验已确立了量子霍尔态与陈绝缘体态的拓扑性质，但其热输运（heat transport）是否同样具有普适性（universal）尚未得到探索。

Method: 采用约翰逊噪声测温法（Johnson-noise thermometry），测量了具有约14纳米莫尔波长的双层石墨烯-六方氮化硼（bilayer graphene-hexagonal boron nitride）莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）中量子霍尔、陈绝缘体及相互作用驱动的对称性破缺陈绝缘体态的热导（thermal conductance）。

Result: 热导（G_Q）以热导量子（thermal conductance quantum，κ₀T）为单位呈量子化，其数值仅由陈数（Chern number, t）决定，与拓扑态（topological state）的微观起源无关。

Conclusion: 该工作直接揭示了霍夫施塔特带（Hofstadter bands）中普适的拓扑热输运（topological heat transport），确立了热导作为莫尔拓扑物质（moiré topological matter）严格探针的方法，并为研究包括分数量子陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulators）在内的更多新奇物相提供了途径。

Abstract: When electrons are subjected simultaneously to a magnetic field and a periodic potential, they form the fractal Hofstadter spectrum, whose topological gaps host quantum Hall and Chern insulating states with distinct Chern numbers. While electrical transport has established the topology of these states, whether their heat transport is likewise universal has remained unexplored. Here, we measure the thermal conductance of quantum Hall, Chern insulator, and interaction-driven symmetry-broken Chern insulator states in a bilayer graphene-hexagonal boron nitride moiré superlattice with a moirè wavelength of $\sim$14 nm using Johnson-noise thermometry. We find that the thermal conductance ($G_Q$) is quantized in units of the thermal conductance quantum ($G_Q = tκ_0T$) and is determined solely by the Chern number ($t$), independent of the microscopic origin of the topological state. By directly revealing universal topological heat transport in Hofstadter bands, our work establishes thermal conductance as a stringent probe of moiré topological matter and provides a route to investigating more exotic phases, including fractional Chern insulators.

</details>

### [119] [Non-Abelian multiplicative chaos on the circle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18824)
*Guillaume Baverez*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种非高斯且非阿贝尔的乘法混沌测度推广，该构造基于紧致连通李群的不可约酉表示与Kac-Moody酉化测度，通过重整化过程在圆上生成取值于正定Hermitian内同态空间的随机测度，其有效性限于L²相范围内的κ值，证明依赖于单点函数的精确公式和碰撞点两点函数的界，这些表达式通过一维Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov方程推导得出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有乘法混沌测度（multiplicative chaos measures）主要局限于高斯框架和阿贝尔结构。本文旨在将其推广至非高斯且非阿贝尔的设定，从而在更广泛的李群表示论和共形场论（conformal field theory）背景下构造随机测度。

Method: 构造以紧致连通李群（compact connected Lie group）的不可约酉表示（irreducible unitary representation）和某个水平κ的Kac-Moody酉化测度（Kac-Moody unitarising measure）为输入，通过重整化过程（renormalisation procedure）输出圆上取值于表示空间正定Hermitian内同态（positive definite Hermitian endomorphisms）的随机测度。证明沿用乘法混沌理论的常规路径，依赖单点函数（one-point function）的精确公式和碰撞点两点函数（two-point function at colliding points）的界，这些结果通过建立一维Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov方程（Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov equations）导出。

Result: 该构造在对应于L²相（L²-phase）的κ值范围内有效。推导得到了单点函数的精确表达式以及碰撞点两点函数的有界性估计。

Conclusion: 本文成功将乘法混沌测度推广至非高斯、非阿贝尔的设定，建立了随机几何、表示论与共形场论之间的新联系。构造的有效范围限于L²相，未来可探索更广参数区域的推广。

Abstract: In this note, we introduce a generalisation of multiplicative chaos measures which is both non-Gaussian and non-Abelian. The renormalisation procedure takes as inputs an irreducible unitary representation of a compact connected Lie group, together with a Kac-Moody unitarising measure at some level $κ$, and outputs a random measure on the circle with values in the space of positive definite Hermitian endomorphisms of the representation space.
  So far, our construction is valid for the range of $κ$-values corresponding to the $L^2$-phase. The proof follows the usual route in the theory of multiplicative chaos, relying on an exact formula for the one-point function and a bound on the two-point function at colliding points. These expressions are derived using the rich algebraic structure of the theory: namely, we establish a one-dimensional version of the Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov equations.

</details>


### [120] [Semiclassical analysis for Yang--Mills random connections on compact surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19037)
*Nguyen Viet Dang,Elias Nohra*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文在紧致曲面上引入各向异性Banach空间（anisotropic Banach spaces）中的分布1-形式（distributional 1-forms），以刻画Morse规范固定Yang–Mills随机联络（Morse gauge-fixed Yang–Mills random connections）的精细正则性。利用支撑在Morse梯度流不稳定曲线上的奇异联络，文章给出了平坦联络模空间及其Atiyah–Bott–Goldman辛形式的新描述。对于特殊酉群，证明了在零面积极限下，Yang–Mills随机联络在这些各向异性空间中收敛到一个随机分布1-形式，其分布恰好对应于Morse理论表述的Atiyah–Bott–Goldman测度。该工作将Witten、Forman、Liu和Sengupta的结果从holonomies层次推广到随机分布联络层次，从而回答了Thierry Lévy关于Yang–Mills随机联络半经典极限的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作（Witten、Forman、Liu、Sengupta）仅从holonomies层次建立了Yang–Mills测度的零面积极限，未能从随机分布联络（random distributional connections）层面描述该极限。本文旨在填补这一空白，并回答Thierry Lévy关于Yang–Mills随机联络半经典极限（semiclassical limits）的提问。

Method: 引入定义在紧致曲面上的各向异性Banach空间中的分布1-形式，以捕捉Morse规范固定Yang–Mills随机联络的精细正则性；利用支撑在Morse梯度流不稳定曲线（unstable curves）上的奇异联络（singular connections），对平坦联络模空间（moduli space of flat connections）及其Atiyah–Bott–Goldman辛形式给出新描述。

Result: 对于特殊酉群（special unitary group），证明了在零面积极限（zero-area limit）下，Yang–Mills随机联络在上述各向异性空间中收敛到一个随机分布1-形式，其分布与Morse理论表述的Atiyah–Bott–Goldman测度一致。

Conclusion: 本文将零面积极限的收敛性从holonomies层次提升到随机分布联络层次，拓展了Witten、Forman、Liu和Sengupta的工作，并回应了Thierry Lévy提出的半经典极限问题。

Abstract: We introduce anisotropic Banach spaces of distributional 1-forms on compact surfaces designed to capture the fine regularity properties of Morse gauge-fixed Yang--Mills random connections.
  Using singular connections supported on unstable curves of a Morse gradient flow, we provide a new description of the moduli space of flat connections and of its canonical Atiyah--Bott--Goldman symplectic form. When the group is the special unitary group, we prove that in the zero-area limit, the Yang--Mills random connection converges, within these anisotropic spaces, to a random distributional 1-form whose law coincides with our Morse-theoretic representative of the Atiyah--Bott--Goldman measure.
  Our approach extends the works of Witten, Forman, Liu, and Sengupta by establishing the zero-area limit of the Yang--Mills measure at the level of random distributional connections, rather than only at the level of holonomies.
  This answers a question of Thierry Lévy on the semiclassical limits of Yang--Mills random connections.

</details>

### [121] [A spacetime positive mass theorem with corners via mollification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19320)
*Hyun Chul Jang,Aidan F. Wood*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明了带角点的渐近平直初始数据集的一个严格主导能量形变定理（strict dominant energy deformation theorem），该形变保持跨越超曲面 Σ 的 Bartnik 边界数据的角点条件（corner condition）。若主导能量条件（dominant energy condition）在 Σ 两侧成立且 Bartnik 数据满足该角点条件，则对所有维度 n ≥ 3，外部末端（exterior end）满足能量动量不等式 E ≥ |P|。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论中，主导能量条件与正质量定理（positive mass theorem）是核心问题。现有定理通常假设初始数据集光滑，而实际物理情形（如两个黑洞的拼合）往往涉及超曲面上的角点（corners）。本文旨在扩展正质量定理至带有角点的渐近平直初始数据（asymptotically flat initial data），并确保形变过程保持 Bartnik 边界数据的角点条件。

Method: 采用严格主导能量形变（strict dominant energy deformation）策略，在超曲面 Σ 上保留角点结构。通过构造保持 Bartnik 数据角点条件的形变过程，将问题归约到每个侧面的主导能量条件分析。利用维度 n ≥ 3 下的全局几何分析工具，推导出外部末端的能量动量约束。

Result: 证明了在 n ≥ 3 的所有维度中，若 Σ 两侧均满足主导能量条件且 Bartnik 数据满足指定的角点条件，则外部末端必然满足 E ≥ |P|。该结果在形变过程中严格保持了角点条件，没有牺牲初始数据的几何奇异性。

Conclusion: 该定理将正质量不等式推广到更一般的带角点初始数据集，为含角点的广义相对论初值问题提供了新的能量动量下界保障。未来的研究方向可能包括将角点条件推广到更一般的超曲面配置或探索其在数值相对论（numerical relativity）中的应用。

Abstract: We prove a strict dominant energy deformation theorem for asymptotically flat initial data with corners along a hypersurface $Σ$. The deformation preserves a corner condition on the Bartnik data across $Σ$. We show that if the dominant energy condition holds on each side of $Σ$ and the Bartnik data satisfy this corner condition, then the exterior end satisfies $E \ge |P|$ in every dimension $n \ge 3$.

</details>

### [122] [Single-Snapshot Inference of Network Couplings from Universal Dynamics at Relative Equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18977)
*Moritz Lampert,Dominic Grün,Ingo Scholtes*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从单次快照（single snapshot）观测推断网络化动力系统中隐藏耦合强度的方法，前提是系统接近相对平衡态（relative equilibrium）。该方法将逆问题转化为齐次线性系统，并通过有效类偏置（effective class bias）吸收共同速度，从而仅依赖局部邻域观测与耦合机制即可求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界系统中的节点间隐藏相互作用难以推断，现有方法通常需要受控扰动（controlled perturbations）、时间分辨观测（time-resolved observations）或多个独立快照（multiple independent snapshots），而这些条件在实践中往往无法满足。

Method: 在系统接近相对平衡态时，所有节点共享共同速度，该速度可被吸收为有效类偏置，将逆问题转化为齐次线性系统。该线性系统的系数完全由观测到的局部邻域（local neighbourhoods）及其耦合机制（coupling mechanism）决定，因而适用于任意已知的耦合函数。

Result: 在三种不同的线性和非线性动力学系统上验证了该方法，成功恢复了基于类的相对耦合强度（relative class-based couplings），并在特殊情况下恢复了绝对耦合强度（absolute couplings）。

Conclusion: 结果表明，空间异质性（spatial heterogeneity）可以替代时间采样（temporal sampling），从而实现在网络化动力系统中仅凭单次快照推断隐藏的耦合强度。

Abstract: Many real-world systems can be modelled as complex networks whose collective behaviour is governed by hidden interactions between nodes. Existing methods for inferring these interactions typically require controlled perturbations, time-resolved observations or multiple independent snapshots, all of which are often unavailable in practice. Here we show that class-based coupling strengths can be inferred from a single snapshot of node states when the system is observed close to a relative equilibrium. In this regime, all nodes share a common velocity, which can be absorbed into an effective class bias, transforming the inverse problem into a homogeneous linear system. The coefficients of this linear system are determined entirely by the observed local neighbourhoods and their coupling mechanism, enabling the application to arbitrary known coupling functions. We validate the approach on three different linear and nonlinear dynamical systems, recovering relative class-based couplings and, in special cases, absolute couplings. These results show that spatial heterogeneity can substitute for temporal sampling, enabling single-snapshot inference of hidden coupling strengths in networked dynamical systems.

</details>

### [123] [Countercurrent Multiplier Networks: A Renal-Inspired Iterative Operator with Provably Bounded Fixed-Point Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18829)
*Snigdha Chandan Khilar*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为逆流倍增器（Countercurrent Multiplier, CCM）层的可微分序列算子，将哺乳动物肾脏浓缩尿液的逆流倍增机制形式化，并作为残差迭代精化（residual iterative refinement）的替代方案进行研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前神经架构中缺乏与哺乳动物肾脏尿液浓缩机制（逆流倍增）类似的设计，该机制通过反平行流与发夹式再循环将微弱的有界局部泵放大为大幅轴向梯度，具有独特的计算潜力。

Method: 将逆流倍增机制形式化为一个可微分序列算子——逆流倍增器（Countercurrent Multiplier, CCM）层，该层包含两个反向平行流动，在发夹处汇合并再循环，通过局部弱泵实现轴向梯度的显著放大。

Result: 该机制能够通过一个在任何点不超过200 mOsm的单次效应梯度，实现四倍的浓度提升，证明了局部小幅提升经循环放大后可达全局显著效果。

Conclusion: CCM层可作为残差迭代精化（residual iterative refinement）的一种替代方案，为神经架构设计提供新的生物启发式思路。

Abstract: The mammalian kidney concentrates urine using a mechanism with no analogue in current neural architectures: the countercurrent multiplier. Two anti-parallel flows joined at a hairpin recirculate a weak magnitude-bounded local pump into a large axial gradient achieving a four-fold concentration increase from a single-effect gradient that never exceeds 200 mOsm at any point. We formalize this mechanism as a differentiable sequence operator the Countercurrent Multiplier (CCM) layer and study it as an alternative to residual iterative refinement.

### [124] [Deep learning-based prediction of time-resolved adhesive forces in viscoelastic Hertzian contacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19060)
*Ali Maghami,Merten Stender,Michele Ciavarella,Antonio Papangelo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究针对粘弹性软接触的快速力响应预测问题，提出了一种基于标量条件的状态化序列到序列深度学习模型（scalar-conditioned, stateful, sequence-to-sequence deep learning model），能够在短程和长程黏附（adhesion）场景下，根据预设位移历史（displacement history）预测完整力演化轨迹。通过引入固定测量步长（FMS）表示处理异质时间尺度，并比较多种架构，发现带拼接条件（concatenated conditioning）的长短期记忆网络（LSTM）表现最优，中位推理时间仅0.16秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软黏弹性接触（adhesive soft viscoelastic contacts）的快速力响应预测是软体机器人（soft robotics）及抓取与操作任务中的当前挑战。完整的时变力轨迹需依赖全数值模拟，其计算成本高度依赖于参数，无法满足实时应用或设计优化循环的需求。

Method: 训练一个标量条件化的、有状态的、序列到序列深度学习模型，数据集涵盖四个数量级的加载/卸载速率及不同驻留时间（dwell time），Tabor参数（Tabor parameter）范围为0.2至3.2。引入固定测量步长（fixed-measurement-step, FMS）表示，将变长轨迹转换为定长序列以保留物理时间信息。训练了长短期记忆网络（LSTM）、时序卷积网络（temporal convolutional neural network, TCN）及时间分布稠密层（time-distributed dense layers）三种架构，并采用了三种不同的Tabor条件化机制。

Result: 最优模型为带拼接条件（concatenated conditioning）的LSTM架构，其留出集均方误差（held-out mean-squared error）为5.0×10⁻⁴，中位拉脱力误差（median pull-off-force error）约为2.2%，中位迟滞误差（median hysteresis error）约为1.1%。对于留出协议，模型预测完整力轨迹的中位推理时间（median inference time）为0.16秒。

Conclusion: 该模型在未见过的参数组合及解析极限情形（analytical limiting cases）下均通过测试，可作为重复数值评估的快速替代模型（rapid surrogate），在控制导向应用中具有潜在用途。

Abstract: Fast prediction of the response of adhesive soft viscoelastic contacts represents a current challenge in soft robotics and for gripping and manipulation tasks. Determining the complete time-resolved force trajectory requires full numerical simulations, whose computational cost is strongly parameter-dependent, making them impractical for real-time application or design-optimization loops. In this work, we overcome this limitation by training a scalar-conditioned, stateful, sequence-to-sequence deep learning model to predict the full force evolution from a prescribed displacement history for both short- and long-range adhesion regimes. The data set spans four orders of magnitude in loading and unloading rates and includes varied dwell times, with the Tabor parameter ranging from $0.2$ to $3.2$. To enable learning across these heterogeneous time scales, we introduce a fixed-measurement-step (FMS) representation that converts variable-length trajectories into fixed-length sequences while preserving their physical-time information. Different architectures were trained, including long short-term memory (LSTM) networks, temporal convolutional neural (TCN) networks, and time-distributed dense layers with three different Tabor-conditioning mechanisms. The models were compared using global waveform and error metrics. We found that the best-performing model has an LSTM architecture with concatenated conditioning, which achieves a held-out mean-squared error of $5.0\times10^{-4}$, a median pull-off-force error of $\approx2.2\%$, and a median hysteresis error of $\approx1.1\%$. For the held-out protocols, the model predicts a complete force trajectory with a median inference time of $0.16$ s. The model is tested across unseen parameter combinations and against analytical limiting cases, providing a rapid surrogate for repeated numerical evaluations with potential use in control-oriented applications.

### [125] [Vakonomic Fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18312)
*Ritoban Roy-Chowdhury,Mohammad Sina Nabizadeh,Oliver Gross,Anthony Gruber,Albert Chern*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于体积保持微分同胚群（volume-preserving diffeomorphisms）上测地线方程的新型不可压缩欧拉方程离散化方法。通过采用vakonomic观点而非Lagrange–d’Alembert框架，离散流体轨迹在（次）黎曼流形上保持测地线性质，并利用低秩Clebsch变量的动量映射表示实现机器精度的Casimir不变量保持和离散开尔文环量定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编码微分同胚及其无穷小生成元的离散化Koopman表示会对离散速度施加非完整约束（nonholonomic constraint），而目前对该约束的变分处理尚无共识。为此，需要寻找一种能够正确处理这种约束、同时保持物理一致性的离散变分框架。

Method: 从vakonomic视角（而非通常的Lagrange–d’Alembert视角）出发，将离散流体动力学表述为（次）黎曼流形（sub-Riemannian manifold）上的测地线问题。采用基于低秩Clebsch变量（low-rank Clebsch variables）的高效动量映射表示（momentum map representation）进行数值实现。

Result: Vakonomic动力学是Lie–Poisson的，其解具有离散重标对称性（discrete relabeling symmetry），从而机器精度地满足Casimir不变量（Casimir invariants）以及离散版本的Kelvin环量定理（Kelvin’s Circulation Theorem）。即使在低网格分辨率下，该vakonomic流体方法也表现出稳定且一致的行为，长期模拟的鲁棒性和物理真实性均得到提升。

Conclusion: 采用vakonomic变分框架可以有效克服非完整约束带来的变分处理困难，为不可压缩欧拉方程提供一种保几何结构（geometry-preserving）的离散化方案，在低分辨率下仍能保持长期稳定性和物理一致性。

Abstract: We introduce a novel discretization of the incompressible Euler equations based on their interpretation as geodesic equations on the Lie group of volume-preserving diffeomorphisms. It is well known that encoding diffeomorphisms and their infinitesimal generators through a discretized Koopman representation places a nonholonomic constraint on discrete velocities, for which there is no consensus on a variational treatment. We show that taking the vakonomic perspective, as opposed to the usual perspective of Lagrange--d'Alembert, yields discrete fluid trajectories that remain geodesics on a (sub-)Riemannian manifold. In particular, the resulting vakonomic dynamics are Lie--Poisson and their solutions admit a discrete relabeling symmetry, leading to machine-precision satisfaction of Casimir invariants along with a discrete analogue of Kelvin's Circulation Theorem. Using an efficient momentum map representation based on low-rank Clebsch variables, we show that these vakonomic fluids behave stably and consistently even at low grid resolutions, leading to increased robustness and physical realism in the long term.

</details>


### [126] [Boundary Free Energies in Disordered Ising Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18326)
*Hexiang Wang,Keheng Zhu,Mauris Chueng*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了无序伊辛模型（disordered Ising model）中边界修正对自由能的影响，发现表面自由能密度（surface free-energy density）可能依赖于van Hove序列，且相应的随机修正不一定依概率收敛。在高维Dobrushin唯一性区域给出收敛性结果，并通过一维反例和精确插值恒等式阐明边界效应的极限行为。最后针对缝跳自由能差（seam-flip free-energy difference）给出方差上界，指出低温柔和Edwards–Anderson模型仍是未解决问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序伊辛模型的边界修正与边界条件、规范化和有限体积序列的选择有关。摘要试图澄清表面自由能密度是否独立于van Hove序列，以及随机修正项是否具有收敛性——这在理论上尚未完全解决。

Method: 给出一个一维独立同分布（i.i.d.）反例以说明表面自由能密度对序列的依赖性。在d≥2的立方体盒子上，针对Dobrushin唯一性（Dobrushin uniqueness）区域中的有界耦合，证明归一化的自由–固定边界自由能差（free-to-fixed boundary free-energy difference）在期望、几乎必然（almost surely）以及L^p意义下的收敛性。对高斯边界耦合导出精确的有限体积插值恒等式（finite-volume interpolation identity），并分析其局限性。对于独立对称键上的缝跳自由能差D_L，给出方差上界Var(D_L)≤4v|S_L|。

Result: 一维反例表明表面自由能密度并非总独立于van Hove序列，对应的随机修正也不一定依概率收敛。在d≥2的立方体盒子的Dobrushin唯一性区域内，自由–固定边界自由能差在期望、几乎必然和L^p意义下均收敛。高斯边界耦合的插值恒等式本身不足以推出低温表面极限。缝跳自由能差的方差受限于4v|S_L|，但一维例子显示对称性和有限矩无法唯一确定刚度指数（stiffness exponent），低温柔和Edwards–Anderson模型问题仍未解决。

Conclusion: 边界修正的行为对无序系统（disordered systems）的有限体积效应和极限性质具有重要影响。Dobrushin唯一性区域内的收敛性为高维情况提供了正向结果，但一维反例及高斯耦合问题的未解性表明，在低温或强无序条件下，边界自由能的收敛性问题依然复杂，尤其Edwards–Anderson模型的表面极限问题仍待进一步研究。

Abstract: The boundary correction to the free energy of a disordered Ising model depends on the boundary condition, the normalization, and the finite-volume sequence. We give a one-dimensional i.i.d. counterexample showing that the surface free-energy density need not be independent of the van Hove sequence and that the corresponding random correction need not converge in probability. For bounded couplings in the Dobrushin uniqueness regime on cubic boxes in dimensions $d\geq2$, we prove convergence of the normalized free-to-fixed boundary free-energy difference in expectation, almost surely, and in every $L^p$, $1\leq p<\infty$. For Gaussian boundary couplings, we derive an exact finite-volume interpolation identity and explain why it does not by itself imply a low-temperature surface limit. For a seam-flip free-energy difference $D_L$ across a set $S_L$ of independent symmetric bonds of variance $v$, we prove $\Var(D_L)\leq4v\abs{S_L}$; one-dimensional examples show that symmetry and finite moments alone do not determine a stiffness exponent, and the low-temperature Gaussian Edwards--Anderson problem remains open.

</details>


### [127] [A converse to generalized Runcorn's theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18379)
*Vjekoslav Kovač,Ivica Smolić*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对月球磁学中的一个表观悖论，研究广义Runcorn定理的反问题，刻画了使特定积分恒为零的平方可积复函数空间，并根据半径参数是否可变给出了解空间的显式球谐展开表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究由月球磁学（lunar magnetism）中一个表观悖论（apparent paradox）驱动，旨在解决广义Runcorn定理（generalized Runcorn's theorem）的反问题（inverse problem），以理解特定球壳区域上的函数在调和函数梯度内积下的零化条件。

Method: 数学上，研究刻画了所有使积分式$$\int_{\{ x\in\mathbb{R}^n : a \leq |x| \leq b \}} f(x) \nabla u(x)\cdot\nabla v(x)\,\mathrm{d}\mathrm{V}(x) = 0$$对任意内球（inner ball）$|x|<r_+$中的复调和函数（complex harmonic function）$u$和在无穷远处衰减的外区域（exterior region）$|x|>r_-$中的复调和函数$v$均成立的平方可积复函数$f$。分析区分了半径参数$a$与$b$（满足$r_-<a<b<r_+$）被视为可变或固定两种情况。

Result: 解空间（solution space）依赖于半径$a$和$b$被视作可变参数还是固定参数。解通过将$f$展开为球谐函数（spherical harmonics）来描述，并给出了显式表示（explicit representations）。

Conclusion: 该研究为广义Runcorn定理的反问题提供了完整的数学刻画，通过球谐展开给出了解空间的显式形式，揭示了半径参数可变性对解空间结构的影响。

Abstract: We study an inverse problem for generalized Runcorn's theorem motivated by an apparent paradox of lunar magnetism. In mathematical terms, we characterize square-integrable complex functions $f$ such that $$ \int_{\{ x\in\mathbb{R}^n : a \leq |x| \leq b \}} f(x) \nabla u(x)\cdot\nabla v(x)\,\mathrm{d}\mathrm{V}(x) = 0 $$ for every complex harmonic function $u$ in the inner ball $|x|<r_+$ and every complex harmonic function $v$ in the exterior region $|x|>r_-$ that vanishes at infinity. The solution space depends on whether the radii $a$ and $b$ such that $r_-<a<b<r_+$ are regarded as varying or fixed. The solutions are described through the expansion of $f$ into spherical harmonics, and explicit representations are provided.

</details>


### [128] [Tau functions and correlation functions of the bosonic universal character hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18780)
*Denghui Li,Jinzhou Liu,Zhaowen Yan*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了玻色子普适特征（bosonic universal character, UC）层级结构，其tau函数在带电自由玻色子（charged free bosons）框架下研究。对应的李代数为$\mathfrak{\widehat{gl}}_{2\infty}$，tau函数可由一系列有序指数算子表示。玻色子UC层级的关联函数（correlation functions）可表达为UC的乘积，并且是广义相位模型关联函数的逆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建玻色子UC层级结构，并在带电自由玻色子框架下研究其tau函数与关联函数，以拓展对普适特征层级和广义相位模型之间关系的理解。

Method: 利用带电自由玻色子框架，通过有序指数算子（ordered exponential operators）表示tau函数；基于该表示推导玻色子UC层级的关联函数，并将其表达为UC的乘积形式。

Result: 玻色子UC层级的tau函数可由一系列有序指数算子表示；其关联函数可表达为UC的乘积；玻色子UC层级的关联函数是广义相位模型关联函数的逆。

Conclusion: 玻色子UC层级结构与广义相位模型之间存在逆关联关系，为进一步理解两类可积系统之间的对偶性提供了新的视角。

Abstract: This paper is concerned with the construction of the bosonic universal character (UC) hierarchy, whose tau functions are investigated within the framework of charged free bosons. The Lie algebra corresponding to the bosonic UC hierarchy is $\mathfrak{\widehat{gl}}_{2\infty}$. It is shown that the tau functions of bosonic UC hierarchy can be represented based on a series of ordered exponential operators. Furthermore, we derive correlation functions of the bosonic UC hierarchy, which can be expressed as the product of UCs. It is worth noting that the correlation functions of the bosonic UC hierarchy are the inverse of the correlation functions of the generalized phase model.

### [129] [Towards General Relativity as a generalized Yang-Mills theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18837)
*Hartwig Winterroth,Lorenzo Fatibene*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于广义主丛理论（generalized principal bundle theory）发展广义规范理论（generalized gauge theories）的实例，旨在为杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theories）与广义相对论（General Relativity）提供统一语言；通过分析广义主联络的运动学和动力学，提出广义杨-米尔斯理论，并证明向量丛上的广义主联络等价于由基本焊接形式（basic soldering forms）给出的仿射联络，从而在适当时机下恢复真空广义相对论的Vielbein表述，暗示一种（广义）规范引力理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将广义主丛理论应用于协变拉格朗日场论（covariant Lagrangian field theories），为杨-米尔斯理论与广义相对论寻找统一的描述框架。

Method: 首先回顾李群纤维丛（Lie group fiber bundles）与广义主丛的基本定义，给出李群纤维丛联络与广义主联络的水平提升（horizontal lift）及局部刻画；然后在经典场论框架下分析广义主联络的运动学与动力学，从而提出广义杨-米尔斯理论的概念；最后展示向量丛（vector bundles）是广义主丛的实例，并证明向量丛上的广义主联络即为由基本焊接形式给出的仿射联络（affine connection）。

Result: 在适当假设下，该框架能够恢复真空广义相对论的Vielbein表述，表明广义相对论可被理解为一种（广义）规范理论。

Conclusion: 广义主丛理论为统一描述杨-米尔斯理论与广义相对论提供了一种潜在的语言，并提出了一种（广义）规范引力理论的前景。

Abstract: As an application of the generalized principal bundle theory to covariant Lagrangian field theories, we aim at the development of an instance of generalized gauge theories, with the prospect of a unifying language for Yang-Mills theories and General Relativity. After reviewing the basic definitions of Lie group fiber bundles and generalized principal bundles, we provide horizontal lift and local characterizations of Lie group fiber bundle connections and generalized principal connections. Subsequently, we consider in the framework of classical field theories the kinematics and dynamics sides of generalized principal connections, which lead to a proposed notion of generalized Yang-Mills theories. Finally, we show how vector bundles are examples of generalized principal bundles and that a generalized principal connection on a vector bundle is an affine connection given in terms of basic soldering forms. We are able to recover, under appropriate assumptions, the Vielbein formulation of (vacuum) General Relativity in this setting, hinting at a (generalized) gauge theory of gravity.

Method: 作者采用带扭率的度量兼容联络（torsionful, metric-compatible connection），结合T-对偶的Buscher规则（Buscher rules），推导出适用于任意阶Killing-Yano形式的坐标无关变换法则。证明过程中使用了明确的匹配假设（explicit matching assumptions）。

Abstract: We investigate the transformation of Killing-Yano (KY) $p$-forms under Abelian T-duality in the presence of a non-trivial three-form torsion. Using a torsionful, metric-compatible connection and the Buscher rules of T-duality, we derive compact, coordinate-free transformation laws applicable to KY forms of arbitrary degree under explicit matching assumptions. In particular, we show that a Killing 1-form is preserved by the direct duality map whenever its transverse components are independent of the isometry direction, with the dual circle component determined by a scalar correction equation. *Cristophe Gomez,Knut Sølna*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出将散射层（scattering layer）建模为粗糙界面（rough interface）而非传统随机介质（random medium），以分析“淋浴帘效应”（shower curtain effect）。在该框架下，推导了图像分辨率（image resolution）和信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）的显式表达式，并揭示了这些量如何依赖于粗糙界面的统计特性及其在物体与观察者之间的相对位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The quality of an image observed through a scattering layer, such as a shower curtain, depends strongly on the relative position of the scattering layer between the object and the observer. This well-known phenomenon is commonly referred to as the shower curtain effect. When the scattering layer is placed close to the observer, the image is strongly degraded, whereas if it is located close to the object, the object may still be observed with relatively high resolution. Previous analyses of the shower curtain effect have primarily modeled the scattering layer as a section of a random medium. In this work, we present a new analysis in which the scattering layer is modeled instead as a rough interface, a description that arises naturally in many physical configurations. Within this framework, we derive explicit characterizations of both the image resolution and the signal-to-noise ratio, and determine how these quantities depend on the statistical properties of the rough interface and on its relative location between the object and the observer.

### [132] [Integrable multi-species SSEP with reactive particle species](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18959)
*Mathieu Dabrowski,Loïc Poulain d'Andecy,Eric Ragoucy*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建并研究了基于杨-巴克斯特方程（Yang-Baxter Equation, YBE）集论解的可积排斥马尔可夫过程（integrable exclusion Markov processes），推广了多物种对称简单排斥过程（multi-species Symmetric Simple Exclusion Process, SSEP），引入了具有反应性粒子物种的新变体 $(p,1)$-SSEP 和 $(p,q)$-SSEP，证明了其在周期和开放边界条件下的可积性，并计算了开放情形下非平衡稳态的物理量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 SSEP 模型主要针对非反应性粒子物种，缺乏对具有反应性（reactive）粒子物种的可积排斥过程的系统性研究。本文旨在通过 YBE 集论解构造更一般的可积过程，涵盖粒子蒸发、凝聚与成对转化等反应机制，丰富非平衡统计力学（non-equilibrium statistical mechanics）的可积模型库。

Method: 利用杨-巴克斯特方程的集论解（set-theoretical solutions）构造可积排斥过程；通过反射方程（reflection equation）的 Baxterisation 引入两类可积边界；采用组合学方法对周期情形下的扇区（sectors）进行完整研究；利用非平衡稳态分析计算相关物理量。

Conclusion: 基于 YBE 集论解成功推广了多物种 SSEP，引入反应性粒子物种的可积排斥过程在周期和开放边界下均保持可积性，为非平衡统计力学提供了新的解析可解模型，并为研究具有化学反应或粒子转化的输运过程提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate integrable exclusion Markov processes constructed from set-theoretical solutions of the Yang-Baxter Equation (YBE) that generalise the multi-species Symmetric Simple Exclusion Process (SSEP). We first introduce the process called the $ (p,1) $-SSEP that is analogous to the multi-species SSEP but with an extra particle species qualified as reactive. Reactive species are able to evaporate and condensate by pairs or to transform by pairs depending on the interpretation. We provide a full combinatorial study of the sectors in the periodic case. We prove the integrability of the process in the periodic case and in the open case for two types of boundaries that we introduce using Baxterisations of solutions of the reflection equation. Next we move on to the process called $ (p,q) $-SSEP, i.e. the multi-species SSEP with an arbitrary number of reactive particle species. We prove its integrability in the periodic case and, for the open case, we introduce integrable boundaries generalising the ones considered for the $ (p,1) $-SSEP. Finally, we define physical quantities relevant to the models and we compute them in the non-equilibrium stationary state of the open $ (p,q) $-SSEP for one type of integrable boundaries.

Abstract: This three-part series establishes a parameter-free, topological classification of multi-field instability in granular continua, extending Maxwell's rigidity count to dynamic, non-equilibrium processes.
  Part 1 (Foundations): a discrete Volumetric-Mechanical-Configurational (VMC) contact formulation maps contact-scale topology to macroscopic multiphysics coupling. A Parity Theorem, $\det(\mathsf{L})=(-1)^N\det(\mathsf{L})$, forces a structural null-mode for every odd channel count $N$, creating "Gateway" layers of broken time-reversal symmetry; once the basis-invariant Gateway number $\mathcal{G}_{\rm inv}\geq 1$, gyroscopic pumping drives non-modal transient amplification along the null direction.

In an acyclic chain (first Betti number $β_1=0$) this isolates dilatancy; closed-form solutions give secular drift for $N=3$ and harmonic confinement for $N=4$.
  Part 3 (numerical upscaling): quad-precision integration of tridiagonal skew-symmetric Onsager chains ($N=3$ to $50$) confirms the contrast between odd-$N$ secular drift and even-$N$ confinement on invariant tori, with even-chain frequencies scaling as $|λ_{\min}^{\rm even}|\simγπ/N$. ### [135] [Metric completion of the Bender--Brody--Müller Hamiltonian: dilation spectrum and missing eigenstates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19067)
*Kejun Liu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了由Bender–Brody–Müller（BBM）哈密顿量诱导的希尔伯特空间完备化过程，证明在BBM候选度规下，其候选本征函数不属于完备空间，因此无法在该$L^2$框架下通过边界条件/本征函数机制产生黎曼零点点谱态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BBM哈密顿量被提出作为非厄米（non-Hermitian）的Hilbert–Pólya算子，旨在通过量子力学方法关联黎曼zeta函数零点。本文旨在严格分析该算子在候选度规$\hatη$下诱导的希尔伯特空间完备化的数学结构，检验其能否实现点谱（point spectrum）与黎曼零点的对应。

Method: 研究从半直线$L^2$核心出发，考察BBM候选度规$\hatη=\sin^2(\hat p/2)=Δ^\daggerΔ/4$诱导的$η_0=Δ^\daggerΔ$形式。通过范数$\|ψ\|_{η_0}=\|Δψ\|$对$C_c^\infty(0,\infty)$进行完备化，构造酉等价于$L^2(\mathbb R_+)$的希尔伯特空间，并识别其自由自伴实现为伸缩生成子（dilation generator）。进一步分析传输后的对称算子的亏指数（deficiency indices）和伴随谱性质。

Result: 主要结果包括：（1）有界夹积$Δ^\dagger h(D)Δ$不具有有界逆；（2）传输后的对称算子亏指数为$(\infty,\infty)$，其伴随在每个实点处都有无穷重数的本征值，而自由延拓为纯连续谱；（3）候选本征函数$Δψ_z=x^{-z}$在$\operatorname{Re}z=1/2$时不属于完备空间，因此原始BBM机制无法在$L^2$度规完备化中产生黎曼零点点谱态。

Conclusion: 在BBM候选度规诱导的$L^2$框架下，原假设的点谱（point spectrum）与黎曼零点对应的机制不成立。该结论独立于具体实现，其数学分析本身也给出了关于有界逆和算子谱结构的两个超越BBM问题的谱论结果。

Abstract: The Bender--Brody--Müller (BBM) Hamiltonian was proposed as a non-Hermitian Hilbert--Pólya operator. We analyze the Hilbert completion induced, on the standard half-line $L^2$ core, by BBM's candidate metric $\hatη=\sin^2(\hat p/2)=Δ^\daggerΔ/4$. The form $η_0=Δ^\daggerΔ$ is positive with trivial kernel but is not coercive. Completing $C_c^\infty(0,\infty)$ in the norm $\|ψ\|_{η_0}=\|Δψ\|$ gives a Hilbert space canonically unitarily equivalent to $L^2(\mathbb R_+)$. Its free self-adjoint realization is the dilation generator, with simple, purely absolutely continuous spectrum $\mathbb R$. The analysis yields two spectral statements of interest beyond the BBM problem. First, no bounded sandwich $Δ^\dagger h(D)Δ$ is boundedly invertible. Second, the transported symmetric operator has deficiency indices $(\infty,\infty)$ and an adjoint with every real point as an eigenvalue of infinite multiplicity, while its free extension is purely continuous. The realization-independent BBM conclusion concerns the candidate eigenfunctions: $Δψ_z=x^{-z}$, so for $\operatorname{Re}z=1/2$ they do not belong to the completed space. Thus the original BBM boundary-condition/eigenfunction mechanism cannot produce point-spectrum Riemann-zero states in this $L^2$-based metric completion.

</details>


### [136] [Lagrange points of the restricted three-body problem in spaces of constant curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19148)
*Miguel Ayala,Carlos Barrera-Anzaldo,Luis C. García-Naranjo*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在常曲率二维空间中系统研究了限制性三体问题的相对平衡点（relative equilibria）分类与稳定性，特别是正曲率（κ>0）情形。通过解析方法与计算机辅助证明相结合，严格证实了此前仅由数值证据支持的现象，并揭示了曲率对三角平衡点L4和L5稳定性的拓扑影响：正曲率具有稳定化效应，而负曲率则相反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 延续Kilin (1999)以及Martínez与Simó (2017)关于常曲率二维空间中限制性三体问题（restricted three-body problem）相对平衡点分类与稳定性的研究，旨在将经典平面拉格朗日点（Lagrange points）推广到弯曲空间，特别是对正曲率情形提供严格的解析与计算证明，并解释曲率符号导致的定性差异。

Method: 将问题建模为具有两个自由度的自主拉格朗日系统（autonomous Lagrangian system），参数仅为曲率κ和主天体质量比μ；针对κ>0情形，采用解析方法与计算机辅助证明（computer-assisted proofs）相结合的手段进行分析。

Result: 建立了正曲率情形下相对平衡点的若干分类结果，严格证实了此前仅由数值证据支持的现象；发现正曲率对三角平衡点L4和L5具有稳定化效应（stabilizing effect），而负曲率则表现出相反的不稳定化效应。

Conclusion: 提供了正曲率与平面及负曲率情形下相对平衡点行为定性差异的拓扑解释（topological explanations）；在小子质量比μ的范围内，曲率的符号是决定三角平衡点稳定性的关键因素，正曲率具有稳定化作用。

Abstract: We continue the study initiated by Kilin ({\em Reg. Chaot. Dyn.} 4, (1999)) and by Martínez and Simó ({\em Celest. Mech. Dynam. Astronom.} 128, (2017)) on the classification and stability of the relative equilibria of the restricted three-body problem in two-dimensional spaces of constant curvature, which generalize the classical Lagrange points of the planar problem. After formulating the problem as an autonomous Lagrangian system with two degrees of freedom, whose only parameters are the curvature $κ$ and the mass ratio $μ$ of the primaries, we establish several classification results for the case $κ>0$ by combining analytical methods with computer-assisted proofs. These results provide rigorous confirmation of phenomena for which previously only numerical evidence was available. We also provide topological explanations for the qualitative differences between the behavior of relative equilibria in positive curvature and that observed in the planar and negative-curvature cases. Our analysis focuses on the regime of small $μ$ and indicates that positive curvature has a stabilizing effect on the triangular equilibria $\Ll_4$ and $\Ll_5$, whereas negative curvature appears to have the opposite effect.

</details>


### [137] [Superintegrable systems of two interacting spin-$\frac12$ particles with first-order vector integrals of motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19155)
*O. Ogulcan Tuncer,I. Yurdusen*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在三维欧氏空间中研究了两自旋1/2非相对论性粒子的量子超可积性（quantum superintegrability），在排除自旋-动量相互作用项的条件下，分类了所有具有非平凡一阶矢量运动积分（first-order vector integrals of motion）的系统，并给出了对应的径向确定方程解及对称性代数分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将先前关于两粒子自旋系统中标量和赝标量一阶积分（scalar and pseudo-scalar first-order integrals）的分类工作拓展到矢量积分情形，以更全面地理解含自旋-轨道（spin-orbit）、自旋-自旋（spin-spin）、张量（tensor）及二次自旋-轨道（quadratic spin-orbit）相互作用的量子可积系统。

Method: 构造了由相对位置、动量、轨道角动量及两个自旋矢量构成的最一般厄密一阶矢量算子（Hermitian first-order vector operator）；通过施加该算子与哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的对易条件，导出一组超定的径向确定方程（overdetermined system of radial determining equations），并求解以获取所有允许的势能形式与对应矢量积分。

Result: 完整列出了在该类框架下所有可能的势能函数及对应的一阶矢量运动积分；并在一个代表性案例中，展示了如何通过标量约化（scalar reduction）得到精确的库仑型（Coulomb-type）和振子型（oscillator-type）解。

Conclusion: 该分类结果完善了含自旋相互作用的两体量子系统的一阶可积性理论，并揭示了矢量积分所生成的对称代数结构（symmetry algebras），为后续高维或更高阶可积性研究提供了基础。

Abstract: We study quantum superintegrability for two interacting non-relativistic spin-$\frac12$ particles in three-dimensional Euclidean space. The Hamiltonian contains a central potential together with spin-orbit, spin-spin, tensor, and quadratic spin-orbit interaction terms, all depending only on the relative distance. We restrict the classification to the $V_4=0$ case, so that the spin-momentum interaction term is not included. We determine all such systems admitting non-trivial first-order vector integrals of motion. For this purpose, we construct the most general Hermitian first-order vector operator built from the relative position, momentum, orbital angular momentum, and the two spin vectors. The commutativity condition with the Hamiltonian leads to an overdetermined system of radial determining equations, whose solution gives the complete list of admissible potentials and the corresponding vector integrals within this class. The results extend the previous classifications of scalar and pseudo-scalar first-order integrals for two particles with spin. We also discuss selected symmetry algebras generated by the vector integrals and show, in one representative case, how a scalar reduction leads to exact Coulomb- and oscillator-type solutions.

</details>

### [138] [Unlocking the Wronskian Tower: A Simplification of the Holomorphic Modular Bootstrap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18375)
*Arpit Das,Sunil Mukhi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文引入微分算子，将高Wronskian指标ℓ的有理共形场论（rational conformal field theory, RCFT）特征标解归结为低ℓ解，从而有效分类并简化候选特征标（quasi-characters）的构造，并证明了一个关于ℓ=2特征标符号性质的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有理共形场论特征标满足模线性微分方程（modular linear differential equation, MLDE），但随着Wronskian指标ℓ增大，直接求解MLDE变得困难，因为会出现可动极点（movable poles）和辅参数（accessory parameters）。需要一种更高效的方法来组织和构造高ℓ的特征标解。

Method: 引入一类微分算子（differential operators），能够在保持模协变性（modular covariance）和q级数整性（integrality of the q-series）的前提下，将高ℓ解与低ℓ解联系起来。在秩二（rank two）情形下，该方法从Mathur–Mukhi–Sen方程出发生成所有允许的Wronskian扇区（Wronskian sectors）；在秩三及以上情形中，将高ℓ拟特征标（quasi-characters）的构造简化为低ℓ的简单方程。

Result: 该方法提供了组织RCFT特征标及更一般的拟特征标（quasi-characters）在Wronskian塔（Wronskian tower）中的高效新路径。在秩二情形下，应用该构造证明了先前关于ℓ=2拟特征标符号性质的一个猜想。

Conclusion: 通过微分算子建立不同ℓ层级之间的关联，显著简化了高Wronskian指标下RCFT特征标的分类与构造问题，为系统研究模线性微分方程的解空间提供了新工具。

Abstract: Characters of rational conformal field theories solve modular linear differential equations labelled by their order and the Wronskian index $\ell$. Direct classification of admissible solutions by solving MLDEs becomes increasingly difficult at higher $\ell$ -- where movable poles and accessory parameters appear. In this work we introduce differential operators that relate higher-$\ell$ solutions to lower-$\ell$ ones while preserving modular covariance and integrality of the \(q\)-series. In rank two, this generates all allowed Wronskian sectors from the Mathur--Mukhi--Sen equation. In rank three and higher, it reduces the construction of higher-$\ell$ quasi-characters to simpler equations with lower $\ell$. This gives an efficient new route for organising candidate RCFT characters, and more generally quasi-characters, across the Wronskian tower. As an application, we apply our construction to prove a previously conjectured property on the signs of $\ell=2$ quasi-characters in rank 2.

</details>


### [139] [The black hole S-matrix in gauge/gravity duality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18393)
*Emil J. Martinec*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文利用规范/引力对偶（gauge/gravity duality）中的库仑支（Coulomb branch）构造了一个S矩阵（S-matrix），其中初态为汇聚于库仑支原点的膜壳（shell of branes）。在引力对偶中，膜壳源生出带有帽状喉部（capped throat）的几何结构；当红移达到弦激发不再被抑制的临界点时，形成俘获面（trapped surface），对应规范理论退禁闭（deconfinement）。中间态为长寿黑洞（long-lived black hole），随后通过缓慢发射膜返回库仑支。论文比较了体有效场论（bulk effective field theory）与对偶规范理论对该过程的描述，并讨论了该构造对黑洞信息悖论（black hole information paradox）的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在利用规范/引力对偶中的库仑支特性构建一个包含黑洞形成与衰变全过程的S矩阵，进而探讨该构造对黑洞信息悖论的启示。

Method: 利用规范/引力对偶（gauge/gravity duality）中库仑支（Coulomb branch）的膜动力学，构造一个初态为汇聚膜壳的S矩阵；在引力对偶中分析膜壳源生的帽状喉部几何、俘获面（trapped surface）形成条件及后续黑洞演化，并比较体有效场论（bulk effective field theory）与对偶规范理论两种描述框架。

Result: 膜壳在引力对偶中源生出帽状喉部几何，当喉部红移达到弦激发不再被抑制的临界点时形成俘获面，对应规范理论退禁闭；中间态为长寿黑洞，随后通过慢速发射膜返回库仑支而衰变。

Conclusion: 该S矩阵构造为理解黑洞信息悖论提供了新的视角，通过对体有效场论与对偶规范理论描述的对比，揭示了两种框架中黑洞形成与衰变过程的内在联系。

Abstract: A variety of examples of gauge/gravity duality have a Coulomb branch for the gauge theory dynamics. We exploit this feature to construct an S-matrix, in which the initial state is a shell of branes converging on the origin of the Coulomb branch. In the gravitational dual, the shell of branes sources a geometry with a capped throat; the cap descends from the asymptotic region to larger and larger redshift. A trapped surface forms when the redshift of the cap reaches the point where the excitation of strings stretching between the branes is unsuppressed, and the dual gauge theory deconfines. The intermediate state is a long-lived black hole, which then decays via the slow emission of branes back onto the Coulomb branch. We compare and contrast the descriptions of this process in the bulk effective field theory and the dual gauge theory; and discuss the consequences of this construction for the black hole information paradox.

### [140] [Asymptotic behaviour of the derivative expansion in the ERG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18397)
*Tim R. Morris*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，无论是使用指数截断还是更一般的光滑截断，精确重整化群（exact renormalization group）的导数展开（derivative expansion）在任意维度下都是一个发散级数。通过无质量 λφ⁴ 微扰理论（massless λφ⁴ perturbation theory）的两环阶首先出现的发散，并结合多环贡献的理论分析，作者得出结论：该导数展开是一个渐近级数（asymptotic series），最初会收敛于精确结果，随后发散行为开始主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究精确重整化群（exact renormalization group）的导数展开（derivative expansion）的收敛性质，因为这一展开是计算临界指数等物理量的常用近似方法，但其数学收敛性尚未得到严格澄清。

Method: 采用无质量 λφ⁴ 微扰理论（massless λφ⁴ perturbation theory），在指数截断和更一般光滑截断下，通过两环阶的解析计算证明发散的首次出现，并进一步分析无限类两环和三环贡献来推断整个级数的渐近性质。

Result: 在任意维度下，导数展开都是一个发散级数；其发散首先出现在两环阶；该级数属于渐近级数（asymptotic series），在低阶时趋近精确结果，但在更高阶时发散行为占据主导。

Conclusion: 导数展开是一个渐近级数，其初始收敛后发散的特性意味着该近似方法在有限阶范围内有效，但高阶修正不可直接信赖，需要结合其他求和技巧（如Borel求和）来提取可靠的非微扰信息。

Abstract: We show that the derivative expansion of the exact (functional) renormalization group is a divergent series in any dimension, both for an exponential cutoff and more general smooth cutoffs. We prove this by showing that within massless $λ\varphi^4$ perturbation theory, such divergences arise first at two loops. From several lines of theoretical argument and by analysing infinite classes of two- and three-loop contributions, we conclude that the derivative expansion is an asymptotic series that initially converges towards the exact result before divergent behaviour takes over.

</details>


### [141] [The fermion sector of the SMEFT from asymptotically safe gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18398)
*Astrid Eichhorn,Moritz Gessner,Shouryya Ray*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过重整化群方法分析量子引力对标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）中四费米子算符的流，发现大多数维度-6相互作用是无关的，从而预测了SMEFT系数量纲比值的特定值；同时识别出由对称性决定的一类相关算符子集，并据此将SMEFT相互作用分为两类：一类预测为非零但被普朗克尺度压制，另一类在小引力耦合下为零，在大引力耦合下可能成为自由参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力通过重整化（renormalization）生成的有效相互作用会影响标准模型（Standard Model）场，这些效应以SMEFT算符的形式出现，其高阶系数参数化了新物理的影响。为了从渐进安全（asymptotically safe）的含量子引力标准模型出发预测这些SMEFT系数，有必要研究引力涨落下四费米子算符的流。

Method: 采用重整化群（renormalization group）方法，分析具有代表性的四费米子算符（four-fermion operators）在引力涨落（gravitational fluctuations）下的流动行为。

Result: 发现这些维度-6（dimension-six）相互作用是无关的（irrelevant），从而支持渐进安全性的近微扰性质；同时发现存在一个由对称性（symmetry）决定的算符子集可以通过某种机制变得相关（relevant）。

Conclusion: 将SMEFT相互作用分为两类：第一类预测为非零但受普朗克尺度（Planck-scale）压制；第二类在小引力耦合下预测为零，但在更大引力耦合下可能成为理论的自由参数。

Abstract: Quantum gravity impacts Standard Model fields through effective interactions generated by renormalization. These appear as Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) operators, where the effects of new physics are parametrized by the values of the higher-order SMEFT coefficients. As a step towards predicting these SMEFT coefficients from the asymptotically safe Standard Model with quantum gravity, we investigate the flow of a representative set of four-fermion operators under gravitational fluctuations. We strengthen the evidence for the near-perturbative nature of asymptotic safety by finding that these dimension-six-interactions remain irrelevant, resulting in the prediction of specific values for the dimensionless ratios of SMEFT coefficients in the IR. We also find a mechanism that can make a specific subset of these operators relevant. This subset is determined by symmetry considerations. On this basis, we provide a categorization of dimension-six-SMEFT interactions into two categories. Interactions in the first category are predicted to be non-zero, but Planck-scale suppressed. Interactions in the second category are predicted to be zero at small gravitational coupling, but may become free parameters of the theory at larger gravitational couplings.

### [142] [Warped Numerical Calabi-Yau Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18402)
*Severin Lüst,Fabian Ruehle,Simon Schreyer*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural networks）计算了 GKP 框架下的翘曲 Type IIB 通量背景，包括 Calabi-Yau 三流形上的 Ricci 平坦度量、调和 (2,1)-形式以及翘曲因子，并在 Dwork 五次族上对两个通量真空进行了验证，展示了近锥点（conifold）处的翘曲效应，同时提出了多项数值改进技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现并数值验证 Giddings-Kachru-Polchinski (GKP) 构造中提出的翘曲 Type IIB 通量背景，特别是在 Calabi-Yau 三流形（Calabi-Yau threefold）上具象化三个核心要素：Ricci 平坦度量、自对偶三形式通量以及翘曲因子，以研究近锥点（conifold）附近的奇异体积问题。

Method: 采用物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural networks, PINNs）近似 GKP 构造所需的三个要素：Ricci 平坦 Calabi-Yau 度量、表示虚自对偶三形式通量（imaginary self-dual three-form flux）的调和 (2,1)-形式，以及求解内部流形上有源泊松方程（sourced Poisson equation）的翘曲因子（warp factor）。应用流程于 Dwork 五次族（Dwork family of quintics）的两个不同通量真空（一个靠近锥点，一个远离锥点），后者作为数值交叉验证。此外，引入改进的点采样算法（在 Calabi-Yau 测度下更均匀）、特征工程化谱网络（feature-engineered spectral network）、多步物理信息训练以及针对刚性偏微分方程（stiff PDEs）的加权 Huber 损失函数。

Result: 对于靠近锥点的基准点，约 0.5% 的 Calabi-Yau 总体积位于喉部（throat），且翘曲因子比体区域（bulk）大一个数量级。远离锥点的真空作为数值交叉验证被成功实施。

Conclusion: 该方法可有效计算翘曲通量背景并研究奇异体积问题（singular bulk problem），所提出的数值改进技术（包括点采样、谱网络设计、多步训练和加权损失函数）对独立于本应用的 Calabi-Yau 度量及相关量的数值研究也具有潜在价值。

Abstract: We compute numerical warped Type IIB flux backgrounds on Calabi-Yau threefolds following the construction of Giddings, Kachru, and Polchinski. Using physics-informed neural networks, we approximate all three ingredients required by the GKP setup: the Ricci-flat Calabi-Yau metric, the harmonic (2,1)-forms representing the imaginary self-dual three-form flux, and the warp factor, which solves a sourced Poisson equation on the internal manifold. We apply our pipeline to the Dwork family of quintics for two different flux vacua, one near a conifold point and one away from it, the latter serving as a numerical cross-check. With these tools, we study the singular bulk problem, and find that for our benchmark point close to the conifold, approximately 0.5 percent of the total Calabi-Yau volume sits in the throat, and the warp factor is an order of magnitude larger as compared to the bulk. We also introduce several improvements to techniques used for numerical studies of CY metrics and quantities derived from them that might be of interest independently of our application. These include an improved point sampling algorithm that produces samples that are more uniform under the Calabi-Yau measure, a feature-engineered spectral network for the metric, multi-step physics-informed training, and a weighted Huber loss tailored to stiff PDEs with highly non-uniform sources.

### [143] [(De)Coherence of a quantum system in an anti-de Sitter spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18407)
*Mandas Biswas,Anupam Mazumdar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在反德西特时空（anti-de Sitter spacetime）中，通过量子化具有非平凡边界条件的弯曲背景下的引力子（graviton），研究了量子谐振子的相干/退相干（coherence/decoherence）问题，并计算了主导阶的退相干率和选择定则（selection rules），发现AdS全局曲率可能导致量子系统再相干（recoherence）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弯曲时空量子场论框架下，理解引力效应对量子系统相干性的影响，特别是AdS时空背景下引力的量子涨落如何导致退相干或再相干。

Method: 采用量子场论方法，在具有非平凡边界条件的弯曲背景中量子化引力子，并在G和1/ω^2的主导阶下对引力场进行求迹（tracing away），得到主方程（master equation）；进而通过半马尔可夫分析（semi-Markovian analysis）计算林布拉德方程（Lindbladian equation），估算退相干率和选择定则。

Result: 主导阶的退相干效应分为两类：一类源自物质与引力子的局域相互作用，另一类与AdS全局曲率（global curvature）相关。后者在特定谐振子频率与全局曲率组合下，会导致量子系统的再相干。通过适当近似，可恢复平直时空极限。

Conclusion: AdS时空中的全局曲率对量子系统的相干性具有双重作用：既贡献退相干效应，也可能在特定条件下引发再相干，这为弯曲时空量子信息过程提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the coherence/decoherence of a quantum harmonic oscillator in anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime by quantising the graviton in a curved background with a nontrivial boundary condition. In the quantum-field-theory framework, we obtain a master equation by tracing away the gravitational field at the leading order in G and 1/omega^2, where omega is related to the trapped frequency of the harmonic oscillator. We will proceed with a semi-Markovian analysis to compute the Lindbladian equation and estimate the decoherence rate and selection rules at the leading order, which come in two kinds: one responsible for the local interaction between matter and graviton, and the other related to the AdS global curvature. The latter determines the recoherence of the quantum system for a certain choice of the trapped harmonic oscillator's frequency and the global curvature. We also demonstrate that we recover the flat spacetime limit by taking appropriate approximations.

</details>


### [144] [Refined Vafa-Witten invariants for toric surfaces from supersymmetric localization in 5D gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18410)
*Osama Khlaif,Boris Pioline,Alessandro Tanzini*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了五维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ $U(N)$ 超对称杨-米尔斯理论在环面凯勒曲面乘以一个圆上的配分函数，发现路径积分局域化为各仿射片上 Nekrasov 5D 配分函数的乘积沿 Cartan 环面的积分；对于 $U(2)$ 规范群，贡献极点与半稳定无挠层模空间中的环面不动点一一对应，且对于非偶第一陈类，其贡献与等变参数无关，加总后得到该模空间的 $\chi_{y^2}$-亏格，即精细 Vafa-Witten 不变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展先前在 $\mathcal{N}=2^*$ SYM 理论在曲面 $S$ 上以及纯 $\mathcal{N}=1$ SYM 在 $S\times \mathbb{S}^1_{\boldsymbolβ}$ 上的工作，将配分函数的局域化分析和极点求和结构推广到带有伴随超多重态的五维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ SYM 理论，并建立与模空间不变量之间的关系。

Method: 利用路径积分局域化（path integral localization）将配分函数约化为沿 Cartan 环面的积分，表示为各仿射片上 Nekrasov 5D 配分函数的乘积；针对 $U(2)$ 规范群，分析被积函数中无穷多极点的结构及其与半稳定无挠层模空间（moduli space of semi-stable torsion-free sheaves）中环面不动点（torus-fixed points）的对应关系。

Result: 对于 $U(2)$ 规范群，极点度数不超过 $\chi(S)-2$；采用自然的极点积分方案后，贡献极点与半稳定无挠层模空间中的环面不动点一一对应。当第一陈类非偶时，极点贡献与等变参数 $\varepsilon_1,\varepsilon_2$ 无关，加和得到模空间的 $\chi_{y^2}$-亏格（其中 $y^2=e^{-\boldsymbolβ m_{\rm adj}}$），与精细 Vafa-Witten 不变量（refined Vafa-Witten invariants）一致。当第一陈类为偶时，配分函数依赖于等变参数 $\varepsilon_1,\varepsilon_2$ 及 $y$，与有理精细 Vafa-Witten 不变量的关系尚不明确。

Conclusion: 五维 $\mathcal{N}=1$ $U(2)$ SYM 理论的配分函数在非偶第一陈类情形下可自然地解释为模空间上的 $\chi_{y^2}$-亏格，从而与精细 Vafa-Witten 不变量相联系；偶第一陈类情形则显示出更丰富的参数依赖性，有待进一步研究。

Abstract: We study the partition function of five-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ $U(N)$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills (SYM) theory with an adjoint hypermultiplet of mass $m_{\rm adj}$ on a toric Kähler surface $S$ times a circle of radius $\boldsymbolβ$. Extending earlier work in $\mathcal{N}=2^*$ SYM theory on $S$, and in pure $\mathcal{N}=1$ SYM on $S\times \mathbb{S}^1_{\boldsymbolβ}$, we find that the path integral localizes to an integral along the Cartan torus of the product of Nekrasov 5D partition functions for each affine patch. Restricting to the gauge group $U(2)$ for simplicity, the integrand has an infinite set of poles of degree at most $χ(S)-2$. With a natural prescription for integrating around such poles, we find that the contributing poles are in one-to-one correspondence with the torus-fixed points in the moduli space of semi-stable torsion-free sheaves on $S$. Moreover, for non-even first Chern class, their contributions are independent of the equivariant parameters $ε_1,ε_2$ and add up to the $χ_{y^2}$-genus of that moduli space, where $y^2=e^{-\boldsymbolβ m_{\rm adj}}$, and hence coincide with the refined Vafa-Witten invariants. For even Chern class, the partition function depends on the equivariant parameters $ε_1,ε_2$ as well as $y$, and its relation to rational, refined Vafa-Witten invariants remains unclear.

### [145] [Global Asymptotics, the Swampland Conjectures, and Preheating of String Moduli](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18442)
*Leia Price,Kuver Sinha,Robert Wiley Deal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究沼泽地猜想（Swampland Conjectures）对弦模量（string moduli）自共振预热（self-resonant preheating）过程的影响，指出势能局域曲率与来自距离猜想（Distance Conjecture）的轻态塔（tower of light states）共同主导预热动力学，且轻态主要通过重塑已有共振带而非开辟新加热通道影响预热。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 沼泽地猜想的宇宙学含义通常局限于暴胀模型构建，但该猜想同样对暴胀之后或弦模量位移后的剧烈非绝热动力学有重要影响。本文旨在通过自共振预热的视角，系统研究沼泽地猜想如何制约这一后期演化过程。

Method: 摘要未提供具体推导公式或数值模拟细节，但指出采用两种沼泽地猜想驱动的结构进行分析：(1) 势能的局域曲率（通过 refined de Sitter Conjecture 的 tachyonic 分支识别负曲率驱动的 tachyonic 放大）；(2) 将距离猜想预言的轻态塔建模为有效随机环境（effective stochastic environment），在其中研究弦模量的预热动力学。研究中考察了 LVS 和 KKLT 紧化中的体模量（bulk moduli）、典型 blow-up 模量势以及 α-吸引子模型。

Result: 局域曲率信息不足以完全确定共振效率；势能在大场值区域（large field asymptotics）的渐近行为（如高原、势垒或 runaway）决定模量如何采样不稳定区域，从而导致不同的共振效率。轻态塔建模显示，这些轻态主要通过涂抹（smearing）、平移（shifting）和轻微种子化不稳定性（mildly seeding instabilities）来重塑已有共振带，而非打开一个稳健的新再加热通道。

Conclusion: 沼泽地物理通过两条路径影响预热过程：一是控制势能的确定性曲率结构（deterministic curvature structure），二是通过涌现的轻态引入随机修正（stochastic corrections）。这表明沼泽地猜想不仅约束暴胀，也对暴胀后非绝热动力学具有重要调控作用。

Abstract: While the cosmological implications of the Swampland Conjectures are usually discussed in the context of inflationary model building, they also have implications for the violent, non-adiabatic dynamics that can follow inflation or any displacement of string moduli. We study this question through the lens of self-resonant preheating, where we point out that two Swampland motivated structures play central roles. The first is the local curvature of the potential: the tachyonic branch of the refined de Sitter Conjecture singles out the kind of negative curvature that can drive tachyonic amplification. We show, however, that local curvature data is not enough; the large field asymptotics of the potential determines how the modulus samples the unstable region. Thus, plateaus, barriers, and runaways can lead to different resonance efficiencies; we study tachyonic resonance for bulk moduli in LVS and KKLT compactifications, as well as for typical blow-up moduli potentials and alpha-attractor models. The second Swampland motivated structure pertains to the tower of light states predicted by the Swampland Distance Conjecture. Modeling a finite subset of such states as an effective stochastic environment within which a string modulus preheats, we find that the light states mainly reshape existing resonance bands by smearing, shifting, and mildly seeding instabilities, rather than opening a robust new reheating channel. Our results suggest that Swampland physics affects preheating by controlling both the deterministic curvature structure of the potential as well as stochastic corrections from emergent light states.

</details>

### [147] [Gravitational Memory Beyond Null Infinity through Finite-Distance Carrollian Screens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18675)
*Felipe Diaz,Sercan Hüsnügil,Oriana Labrin,Leonardo Sanhueza*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过研究带有Carroll几何的有限距离零超曲面，将引力记忆（gravitational memory）从无穷远推广至有限距离。利用Robinson–Trautman时空作为精确可解的辐射背景，证明了Bondi位移记忆是更广泛的准局域Carroll耗散系统的普适渐近投影，有限距离修正则保留了聚焦、嵌入依赖、角漂移、库仑数据和近区信息等额外特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力记忆效应多在零无穷远（null infinity）处定义，但其在有限距离处的准局域（quasilocal）表现尚不清晰。作者希望建立有限距离零屏幕（null screen）上的Carroll几何框架，以刻画辐射通过后残留的几何响应，并揭示其与标准渐近记忆效应之间的内在联系。

Method: 采用具有Carroll几何（Carrollian geometry）的有限距离零超曲面描述引力记忆。选取Robinson–Trautman时空作为辐射背景，将其变换至Bondi规范（Bondi gauge）以提取渐近数据。在准局域层面，利用内在退化几何、光学数据（optical data）及零Brown–York张量（null Brown–York tensor）定义Carroll耗散系统，并通过线性化分析比较有限屏幕记忆与Bondi记忆的关系。

Result: 在渐进平直的Robinson–Trautman几何中，Bondi剪切（Bondi shear）为纯电型，产生标准的位移记忆效应（displacement-memory effect）。有限屏幕记忆的领先阶大半径无迹分量退化为Bondi位移记忆，而有限距离修正包含聚焦、嵌入依赖、角漂移、库仑数据及近区信息。晚期屏幕逼近最终Schwarzschild视界时，各向异性Carroll数据指数衰减，仅保留各向同性的零Brown–York应力。此外，在非零宇宙常数下构造了二阶辐射幅度的Robinson–Trautman解，发现对应的荷不满足普适单调性。

Conclusion: Bondi记忆可视为更广泛的准局域Carroll响应的普适渐近投影；有限距离屏幕系统包含了比渐近记忆更丰富的几何信息。这一框架为理解引力记忆在有限距离处的表现与视界演化之间的联系提供了基础，同时也揭示了非零宇宙常数下辐射电荷行为的新特征。

Abstract: We investigate gravitational memory beyond null infinity by studying finite-distance null hypersurfaces endowed with Carrollian geometry. We show that the intrinsic degenerate geometry, optical data, and null Brown--York tensor of a finite null screen define a quasilocal Carrollian dissipative system, providing a natural framework to characterize the residual geometric response after the passage of radiation. To make this construction explicit and compare it with the standard asymptotic description, we use Robinson--Trautman spacetimes as an exactly solvable radiative setting. For asymptotically flat Robinson--Trautman geometries, we transform the solution to Bondi gauge and extract the asymptotic data directly in terms of the Robinson--Trautman field. In the linearized sector, the Bondi shear is purely electric and produces the standard displacement-memory effect associated with the relaxation toward the final Schwarzschild geometry. We show that the leading large-radius tracefree component of the finite-screen memory reduces to the Bondi displacement memory, while finite-distance corrections retain additional focusing, embedding dependence, angular drift, Coulombic data, and near-zone information. Thus, Bondi memory emerges as the universal asymptotic projection of a broader quasilocal Carrollian response. Late-time screens approaching the final Schwarzschild horizon exhibit exponentially decaying non-isotropic Carrollian data, leaving only the isotropic null Brown--York stress. As a by-product, we construct the Robinson--Trautman solution with nonzero cosmological constant to second order in the radiative amplitude and use the holographic dictionary to study the associated energy fluxes and find that the resulting charge does not obey a universal monotonicity property.

Abstract: In this paper, we present a unified computational framework to analyze the microscopic vacuum structure of 4-charge extremal black holes in Type IIA string theory, applying techniques from computational algebraic geometry and numerical topology to their pure D-brane effective quantum mechanics. Second, we apply complementary techniques to a configuration where supersymmetry is explicitly broken at the level of the effective action. The corresponding 4-charge non-BPS extremal pure D-brane system is obtained by replacing the D6-brane with an anti-D6-brane and assigning incompatible R-symmetry rotations to different brane triplets. Analyzing the associated scalar potential using analytical Gröbner bases, we demonstrate the absence of zero-energy classical ground states. To handle the continuous flat directions populating the non-BPS landscape, we implement specific topological regularizations, namely Morse-Bott deformations and gated soft-trapping. These methods allow us to systematically characterize the classical energy landscape, identifying a non-compact Coulomb branch, marginally bound stabilizer submanifolds, and an isolated collection of doubly degenerate low-energy stable states.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 态Krylov复杂度（spread complexity）依赖于循环对 $(H,|K_0\rangle)$，初始态变化时Lanczos链会在固定哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的参考循环子空间内重组。现有研究缺乏对这种重组机制的数学刻画，以及从谱系角度理解复杂度结构变化的统一理论。

Method: 采用正交多项式理论特别是Christoffel加权变换（Christoffel reweighting）与Christoffel-Darboux核的有限秩投影，将参考测度的Fourier正交多项式矩映射为转移振幅；通过无根剩余递推（root-free remainder recurrences）处理Heisenberg-Weyl/Charlier振子中的数态跳跃；利用乘积恒等式与乘积Gram分解处理有限SU(2)/Krawtchouk链和紧束缚/Chebyshev链；通过Weyl反射（Weyl reflection）配对自旋权重，并引入矩阵值母测度（matrix-valued parent measure）处理有限种子族。

Result: 在Heisenberg-Weyl/Charlier振子中，无根剩余递推的大指标行为区分了普通平移和Poisson原子的共振删除，决定了Jacobi渐近行为，并证明了任意固定跳跃下有限时间复杂度的有界性。在有限SU(2)/Krawtchouk和紧束缚/Chebyshev链中，终端商的乘积恒等式与Gram分解确定了所有权重态和局域位点连接器，Weyl反射配对相反自旋权重。首次跳跃的Charlier-Hermite标度将结构推广至连续谱支撑。

Conclusion: 一个已求解的循环问题可以确定一族固定哈密顿量动力学，并将制备依赖性（preparation dependence）与生成器变化或希尔伯特空间维度（Hilbert-space dimension）变化分离开来。该框架还表明，在Liouvillian具有自伴实现（self-adjoint realization）时，相对演算可自然推广至多项式算符后代。

Abstract: State Krylov, or spread, complexity belongs to the cyclic pair $(H,|K_0\rangle)$, so changing the initial state at fixed-$H$ reorganizes the Lanczos chain within the reference cyclic subspace. For normalized polynomial descendants $|ψ_Q\rangle \propto Q(H)|K_0\rangle$, this reorganization is the positive Christoffel reweighting of the reference measure by $|Q|^2$. Orthogonality gives a finite-band transfer from reference Fourier-orthogonal-polynomial moments to shifted amplitudes, while a finite-rank projection of its Christoffel-Darboux kernel yields cumulative probabilities and spread complexity. Complex superpositions, confluent roots, deletion of spectral atoms and terminal closure enter the same construction. In the Heisenberg-Weyl/Charlier oscillator, root-free remainder recurrences govern arbitrary number-state jumps. Their large-index behavior distinguishes generic shifts from resonant deletion of Poisson atoms, determines the Jacobi asymptotics, and proves the finiteness of the complexity at finite time for every fixed jump. In finite $SU(2)$/Krawtchouk and tight-binding/Chebyshev chains, product identities and product-Gram factorizations in the terminal quotient determine all weight-state and localized-site connectors through the terminal edge, while Weyl reflection pairs opposite spin weights. The first-jump Charlier-Hermite scaling carries it to continuous spectral support. Finite seed families admit a matrix-valued parent measure, and the relative calculus extends to polynomial operator descendants whenever the Liouvillian has a self-adjoint realization for the chosen inner product. A solved cyclic problem determines a family of fixed-$H$ dynamics and separates preparation dependence from changes of the generator or Hilbert-space dimension.

</details>


### [151] [The complete massless singlet spectrum in the free-field construction of heterotic strings on Calabi--Yau orbifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19289)
*Vladimir Belavin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用自由场构造和 Shapovalov 矩阵秩方法，计算了杂化弦在 Berglund–Hübsch Calabi–Yau 轨形上紧致化后的无质量 E6 单态谱，纠正了五次轨形单态数之前被引用的 326 为 330，并给出了另外两个五次轨形的新谱系，所有例子均通过精确镜像对称检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确计算杂化弦（heterotic string）在 Berglund–Hübsch Calabi–Yau 轨形上紧致化后的无质量 E6 单态（massless E6 singlet）全谱，以验证和修正此前几何描述中引用的单态数（如五次轨形的 326）。

Method: 采用自由场构造（free-field construction），将不可约 N=2 极小模型（irreducible N=2 minimal model）表示的精确内容（编码于 Shapovalov 矩阵的秩）与轨形的扭转扇区结构（twisted sector structure）相结合，从而得到后代顶点（descendant vertices）的贡献，并显式构造一般顶点。

Result: 重现了具有 Hodge 数 (17,21) 的五次轨形谱（17 代、21 反代、234 单态）；对于五次族本身得到 330 个单态，而非几何描述中常引用的 326；给出了另外两个五次轨形 $Z_5[0,1,2,3,4]$ 的谱 (21,1,210) 和 $Z_5[0,0,0,1,4]$ 的谱 (49,5,258)，其中后者异常 Hodge 数 $h^{2,1}=49$ 来自扭转扇区。

Conclusion: 在 Gepner 点处，五次轨形的正确单态数为 330，与 Kachru–Witten 的 Landau–Ginzburg 计算一致；所有四个例子均通过了精确镜像对称（mirror symmetry）检验。

Abstract: We apply the free-field construction of the heterotic string compactified on Berglund--Hübsch Calabi--Yau orbifolds by computing the full spectrum of massless $E_6$ singlets. The contribution of the descendant vertices is obtained by combining the exact content of the irreducible $N=2$ minimal model representations, encoded in the ranks of the Shapovalov matrices, with the twisted sector structure of the orbifold. The method reproduces the known spectrum of the quintic orbifold with Hodge numbers $(17,21)$, namely $17$ generations, $21$ antigenerations and $234$ singlets. For the quintic itself we obtain $330$ singlets. We show that this number, rather than the frequently quoted value $326$, obtained from the geometric description, is the correct one at the Gepner point, in agreement with the Landau--Ginzburg computation of Kachru and Witten. We also provide an explicit construction of the general vertices. We then compute the new spectra of the two remaining quintic orbifolds, $Z_5[0,1,2,3,4]$ with $(21,1,210)$ and $Z_5[0,0,0,1,4]$ with $(49,5,258)$, where the exceptional Hodge number $h^{2,1}=49$ arises from the twisted sectors. All four examples satisfy exact mirror-symmetry checks.

### [152] [Ecological networks of viable species with degree-dependent interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18809)
*Hae Seong Lee,Deok-Sun Lee,Sang Hoon Lee,Samir Suweis,Hye Jin Park*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本研究在广义Lotka-Volterra（GLV）框架中引入度依赖的相互作用强度，发现两种截然不同的相——枢纽有利相（hub-favored phase）和枢纽抑制相（hub-suppressed phase），分别使高度连接的物种更易存活或面临更高灭绝风险；这些相通过选择性移除特定物种间的相互作用，系统地改变存活物种网络的度-度相关性（assortativity），从而解释了真实生态网络中观察到的广泛同配性变化范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生态网络模型通常假设所有连接对的相互作用强度服从相同的分布，但真实生态群落中相互作用强度与物种度（degree）之间存在相关性；为了弥补这一被忽视的特征，本研究引入度依赖的相互作用强度。

Method: 在广义随机Lotka-Volterra（GLV）模型中引入度依赖的相互作用强度，结合动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）进行系统性分析，并解析推导相边界条件。

Result: 识别出两种相：枢纽有利相（hub-favored phase）和枢纽抑制相（hub-suppressed phase），分别导致高度连接物种优先存活或面临更高灭绝风险；解析推导了度依赖作用力与连通性效应精确平衡的相边界；枢纽有利相通过选择性移除低度物种之间的相互作用增强网络的异配性（disassortativity），而枢纽抑制相通过消除涉及枢纽物种的相互作用降低异配性。

Conclusion: 度依赖的相互作用不仅是塑造物种存活的基本机制，而且能够自然地再现真实生态网络中观察到的广泛度-度相关性（assortativity）值范围。

Abstract: The generalized Lotka-Volterra (GLV) framework, recently advanced by dynamical mean-field theory, enables the systematic analysis of large ecological networks. When combined with structured interaction topologies, previous studies have shown that the viability of species, defined by having a positive stationary abundance, depends on the number of their interacting neighbors or the "degree." While such model studies usually assume that interaction strengths follow an identical distribution across all connected pairs, real ecological communities often exhibit correlations between interaction strength and a species' degree. To capture this overlooked feature, we introduce degree-dependent interaction strengths into a generalized random LV model. We identify two distinct regimes: a hub-favored phase, where highly connected species survive preferentially, and a hub-suppressed phase, where they face higher extinction risks. We analytically derive the phase boundary where these degree-dependent strengths precisely balance the connectivity effect, leaving all species equally susceptible. Crucially, these phases induce opposing shifts in the degree-degree correlation or "assortativity" of the network of viable species: the hub-favored phase enhances disassortativity by selectively removing the interactions between low-degree species, whereas the hub-suppressed phase reduces it as the interactions involving hub species tend to disappear. Ultimately, our findings demonstrate that degree-dependent interactions are a fundamental mechanism not only for shaping species survival, but for naturally reproducing the wide range of assortativity values observed in real ecological networks.

</details>
