### [153] [Free energy landscape of Dense Associative Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19195)
*Sumedha,Abhishek Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文基于大偏差理论（large deviations theory），求解并得到了包括密集联想记忆（dense associative memories）在内的广泛联想记忆（associative memories）的自由能泛函（free energy functional）的通用表达式，并系统分析了高阶网络中的记忆检索机制与精确检索阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为广泛类别的联想记忆模型（包括密集联想记忆）建立解析通用的自由能泛函表达式，并发展一种能够系统分析复杂联想记忆架构的方法。

Method: 采用大偏差理论（large deviations theory）作为核心分析工具，求解自由能泛函；通过重现Hopfield模型（Hopfield model）的经典结果验证方法有效性；针对有限模式数（finite number of patterns），推导了含多项式相互作用（polynomial interactions）和对数-求和-指数（Log-Sum-Exponential, LSE）激活函数（activation）的密集联想记忆的温度依赖性自由能泛函（temperature-dependent free energy functional）。

Result: 在广泛极限（extensive limit）下，计算了上述系统的无序平均基态能量（disorder-averaged ground-state energy）；揭示了高阶密集网络中记忆检索（memory retrieval）对初始状态（initial state）的依赖性；给出了LSE模型的精确全检索阈值（exact full-retrieval threshold）。

Conclusion: 该方法为分析联想记忆中多样化的复杂架构提供了一种系统化流程（systematic procedure），可推广至更一般的联想记忆结构。

Abstract: Using large deviations theory, we solve and obtain a general expression for the free energy functional for a broad class of associative memories, including dense associative memories. We illustrate the method by reproducing classical results for the Hopfield model. For a finite number of patterns, we derive the temperature-dependent free energy functional for dense associative memories featuring polynomial interactions and Log-Sum-Exponential (LSE) activation. We also evaluate the disorder-averaged ground-state energy of these systems in the extensive limit. Our analytical framework reveals how memory retrieval depends on the initial state in higher-order dense networks, and gives the exact full-retrieval threshold for the LSE model. This method provides a systematic procedure for analyzing diverse, complex architectures in associative memory.

Result: 在通用参数值下观察到无限多个QSD，每个QSD具有不同的逃逸率（escape rate）；数值模拟表明这些QSD对摄动随机噪声具有稳定性；在部分参数值下还建立了唯一QSD的存在性。

Conclusion: 可数状态空间上的次随机马尔可夫链可以支持无限多个拟平稳分布，且每个分布对应不同的逃逸率，这丰富了对拟平稳分布谱的理解。

Abstract: In this paper we present a concrete example of a substochastic discrete-time Markov chain on a countable state space producing a spectrum of infinitely many quasi-stationary distributions (QSDs) for generic parameter values, with each QSD supporting a distinct escape rate. Our system is motivated by an open variant of the Pelikan dynamical system, a random map introduced in the 1980s. These QSDs, and their stability to perturbative random noise, are tested in numerical simulations. The existence of unique QEDs is also established for some parameter values.

### [155] [Finite Group Reduction of the DR/DZ Hierarchies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16607)
*Si-Qi Liu,Youjin Zhang,Tianwen Zhong*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文证明了与半单CohFT相关的Dubrovin-Zhang/Double Ramification层次结构的有限群约化保持其双哈密顿结构和tau结构。将此结果应用于以ℙ¹₂,₂,₂,₂为靶空间的orbifold Gromov-Witten理论，发现Hurwitz空间M₁;₁上的Frobenius流形结构可关联两个不同的可积层次结构，其中之一等价于亏格1拓扑递归。

Method: 采用有限群约化（finite group reduction）方法处理与半单CohFT关联的Dubrovin-Zhang/Double Ramification层次结构，分析其约化后的双哈密顿性质；通过具体实例——以ℙ¹₂,₂,₂,₂为靶空间的orbifold Gromov-Witten理论（orbifold Gromov-Witten theory）——验证该约化结论，并对比所得的两种可积层次结构。

Result: 有限群约化保持Dubrovin-Zhang/Double Ramification层次结构的双哈密顿结构和tau结构。在ℙ¹₂,₂,₂,₂的orbifold Gromov-Witten理论中，Hurwitz空间M₁;₁上的Frobenius流形结构可导出两种不同的可积层次结构（integrable hierarchies），其中一种等价于亏格1拓扑递归（genus 1 topological recursion）。

Conclusion: 半单CohFT的有限群约化在层次结构层面保持双哈密顿性和tau对称性，这一性质为连接orbifold Gromov-Witten理论与Hurwitz空间上的可积系统提供了桥梁，并揭示了亏格1拓扑递归与Frobenius流形结构之间的等价关系。

Abstract: We show that the finite group reduction of the Dubrovin-Zhang/Double Ramification hierarchy associated to a semisimple CohFT preserves its bihamiltonian structure and its tau structure. By applying this result to the orbifold Gromov-Witten theory with the target $\mathbb{P}^1_{2,2,2,2}$, we see that there are two different and interesting integrable hierarchies that can be associated to the Frobenius manifold structure on the Hurwitz space $M_{1;1}$. One of them is equivalent to the genus $1$ topological recursion.

### [156] [The Research and Development of New Electronics Systems and Testing on the JNE-1ton Prototype Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19066)
*Haoyan Yang,Yuzi Yang,Yapeng Wang,Changxu Wei,Haoyang Fu,Haozhe Sun,Juntao Liu,Zhiyi Liu,Tao Xue,Jianmin Li,Yinong Liu,Zhe Wang,Shaomin Chen*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文介绍了为锦屏中微子实验（JNE）开发的高性能读出电子学系统（PDS1500），该系统具有1 GSa/s实时采样、14位物理分辨率（有效位数10.6）、64 Gbps总数据吞吐量和确定性零延迟时钟分发架构。通过台架测试和JNE-1ton原型探测器验证，系统在1000 ns采集窗口内实现零数据丢失、基线噪声降至参考水平三分之一、时序漂移限制在0.3 ns、能量阈值低至0.1 MeV，满足探测低能太阳中微子的要求，并具备全规模3000通道探测器的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锦屏中微子实验（JNE）作为下一代中微子观测站，需要基于波形的（waveform-based）高精度事件重建，这对读出电子学系统提出了极高的性能要求。因此，需要开发一套满足高采样率、高分辨率、大吞吐量和低噪声等关键指标的读出系统。

Method: 研制了一套单机箱64通道读出系统（PDS1500），采用1 GSa/s实时采样、14位物理分辨率（有效位数ENOB为10.6）、64 Gbps总数据吞吐量以及确定性零延迟时钟分发（deterministic zero-delay clock distribution）架构。通过台架测试以及在升级后的JNE-1ton原型探测器上的部署进行验证，并与商用参考系统进行性能对比评估。

Result: 实验结果表明：在1000 ns采集窗口内实现零数据丢失；基线噪声降至参考水平的三分之一；跨电源周期的时序漂移（timing drift）限制在0.3 ns；能量阈值低至0.1 MeV，可探测低能太阳中微子。14位物理分辨率提供了更高的波形保真度（waveform fidelity），但整体能量分辨率仍受限于JNE-1ton探测器本身。模块化架构可支持全规模3000通道JNE探测器。

Conclusion: 新开发的读出电子学系统完全满足未来锦屏中微子实验（JNE）的技术要求，为高精度波形重建和低能中微子探测提供了可靠保障。

Abstract: The Jinping Neutrino Experiment (JNE), a next-generation neutrino observatory under construction at the China Jinping Underground Laboratory II (CJPL-II), requires high-precision waveform-based event reconstruction, imposing stringent demands on its readout electronics. To meet these requirements, we have developed a high-performance readout system featuring 1 GSa/s real-time sampling, 14-bit physical resolution with an effective number of bits (ENOB) of 10.6, a total data throughput of 64 Gbps, and a deterministic zero-delay clock distribution architecture. The new single-crate 64-channel system (PDS1500) was validated through bench tests and deployment on the upgraded JNE-1ton prototype detector. Its performance was further evaluated against a commercial reference system. The results demonstrate that all key metrics meet the JNE experimental requirements: zero data loss within a 1000 ns acquisition window, baseline noise reduced to one-third of the reference level, timing drift limited to 0.3 ns across power cycles, and an energy threshold as low as 0.1 MeV, enabling the detection of low-energy solar neutrinos. While the 14-bit physical resolution provides significantly higher waveform fidelity, the overall energy resolution in this test remains dominated by the intrinsic limitations of the JNE-1ton detector, as expected. Furthermore, the modular architecture provides the throughput and scalability required to support the full-scale 3000-channel JNE detector. These results collectively demonstrate that the newly developed electronics system fully satisfies the technical requirements of the future JNE experiment.

### [157] [Search for Planetary-mass Black Holes with an Improved Viterbi Algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18352)
*Raul Rodriguez,George Alestas,Sachiko Kuroyanagi,Juan Garcia-Bellido*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出并验证了一个基于维特比算法（Viterbi algorithm）与隐马尔可夫模型（Hidden Markov Model）的全新搜索管道，用于探测行星质量级原初黑洞双星（primordial black hole binaries）在旋近阶段（inspiral phase）发射的引力波信号，并在LIGO O3数据上以固定虚警率3%成功恢复大部分注入信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 行星质量级原初黑洞（planetary-mass primordial black holes）近期重新引起关注，但由于该类双星信号持续时间长，现有引力波搜索方法难以有效探测，亟需开发专用的全自动搜索管道。

Method: 采用维特比算法（Viterbi algorithm）结合隐马尔可夫模型（Hidden Markov Model）恢复最可能的信号轨迹；引入一种新型时频表示（time-frequency representation）以及候选信号隔离程序（candidate isolation procedure）以区分信号与背景噪声；候选评估使用两个检测统计量：功率显著性nσ和与预期双星演化的一致性指标NMSE。

Result: 在LIGO Hanford O3数据上以固定虚警率（false-alarm ratio）3%进行注入验证，管道能恢复大部分信号；在大多数参数空间内覆盖银河系尺度，在最灵敏区域可达到约100 kpc的亮度距离；对每个候选信号还提供啁啾质量（chirp mass）估计，在整个可探测范围内精度保持较高。

Conclusion: 该搜索管道在行星质量级原初黑洞双星探测任务中具备完整可操作性，能够实现信号的快速识别与系统参数（如啁啾质量）的初步表征，为后续引力波天文学研究提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Primordial black holes in the planetary-mass range have attracted renewed interest; however, the search for gravitational waves from such binaries remains challenging due to their long-lived nature. In this work, we present, define, and validate a fully operational search pipeline developed to detect planetary-mass binaries during their inspiral phase. We use the Viterbi algorithm, a dynamic programming technique that recovers the most likely track based on a Hidden Markov Model. To enhance its performance, we introduce a novel time-frequency representation of the data and a candidate isolation procedure that separates signals from background noise. The evaluation of candidates is carried out using the two detection statistics, $n_σ$ and NMSE, which quantify the power significance and the consistency with the expected binary evolution. We then validate the search method using O3 LIGO Hanford data with a population of injected signals. The pipeline is able to recover most of the signals with a fixed false-alarm ratio of $3\%$, covering Galactic scales across most of the parameter space and reaching luminosity distances $ \gtrsim 100$ kpc in the most sensitive region. For each candidate, we also obtain an estimate of the system's chirp mass, whose accuracy remains high throughout the detectable range, enabling a rapid characterization of the system upon detection.

</details>

### [158] [Acoustic Phonon Dynamics in Co-Doped BaFe$_2$As$_2$ Thin Film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18583)
*Alexander Bartenev,Roman Kolodka,Larry Theran,Ki-Tae Eom,Jong-Hoon Kang,Jason Kawasaki,Chang-Beom Eom,Sergiy Lysenko*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Ba(Fe$_{0.92}$Co$_{0.08}$)$_2$As$_2$薄膜中相干声学振荡的动力学行为，特别是高频与低频声学模式之间可能的能量转移机制。

Method: 采用泵浦-探测反射率技术测量相干声学振荡，并利用修正逻辑函数模型对声学响应进行定量分析。

Result: 在Ba(Fe$_{0.92}$Co$_{0.08}$)$_2$As$_2$薄膜中观测到33 GHz和8.2 GHz两个离散频率的相干声学振荡；分析表明存在相干声学能量的时间重分布。

Conclusion: 观测到的声学行为与高频模式（33 GHz）通过非谐衰减转变为低频模式（8.2 GHz）的物理图像一致，揭示了该材料中声子-声子耦合（phonon-phonon coupling）的非谐机制。

Abstract: Pump-probe reflectivity reveals coherent acoustic oscillations at 33 and 8.2 GHz in a Ba(Fe$_{0.92}$Co$_{0.08}$)$_2$As$_2$ thin film. The acoustic response was analyzed using a modified logistic-function model, suggesting a temporal redistribution of coherent acoustic energy consistent with anharmonic decay of the higher-frequency mode into the lower-frequency mode.

### [159] [Domain wall motion in a polycrystalline vortex lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18592)
*Malcolm Durkin,Emily Waite,Taylor L. Hughes,Nadya Mason*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过调控超导岛阵列中的磁场偏离公度（commensurate）涡旋填充，在非公度填充下观察到一种两步脱钉（two-step depinning）转变。实验结合分子涡旋模型模拟证实，这一中间态对应着多晶涡旋晶格（polycrystalline vortex lattice）中的畴壁运动（domain wall motion）。结果表明，在强周期性钉扎（strong periodic pinning）条件下，无序相互作用涡旋系统更倾向于界面物理（interface physics）而非均匀玻璃态动力学（homogeneous glassy dynamics）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序如何重塑晶体系统对外力的响应尚不明确：它究竟驱动相互作用的晶格（interacting lattices）走向玻璃态（glassy states），还是将其碎裂成由可移动界面分隔的畴（domains）。

Method: 在超导岛阵列（superconducting island arrays）中，通过将磁场调至非公度涡旋填充（incommensurate vortex fillings）来可控引入无序，并施加电流驱动涡旋运动，从而观察脱钉转变（depinning transition）行为。实验结果与分子涡旋模型（molecular vortex model）模拟进行对比验证。

Result: 在非公度填充下观察到两步脱钉转变，中间态对应多晶涡旋晶格中畴壁运动的行为特征。两步脱钉在理论上已有探讨，但此前缺乏将其与界面主导的涡旋运动直接联系的实验证据。

Conclusion: 无序且相互作用的涡旋系统在强周期性钉扎条件下，会偏好畴壁运动所代表的界面物理，而非均匀的玻璃态动力学，这为理解无序驱动下晶格系统的响应机制提供了实验依据。

Abstract: Disorder fundamentally reshapes how crystalline systems respond to external forces, yet it remains unclear whether disorder drives interacting lattices toward glassy states or instead fragments them into domains separated by mobile interfaces. Here, we investigate vortex motion in superconducting island arrays, where disorder is introduced in a controlled manner by tuning the magnetic field away from commensurate vortex fillings. By driving vortices with an applied current, we observe a two-step depinning transition at incommensurate fillings. Comparison with molecular vortex model simulations shows that this intermediate regime is consistent with domain wall motion in a polycrystalline vortex lattice. While two-step depinning has been explored theoretically in driven periodic systems, direct experimental evidence linking this behavior to interface-dominated vortex motion has been lacking. Our results demonstrate that disordered, interacting vortex systems with strong periodic pinning can favor interface physics over homogeneous glassy dynamics.

### [160] [Quadrature magnetoresistance scaling reflects linear field dependence rather than strange metallicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18685)
*D. B. Zhou,Y. Yang,L. F. Feng,M. F. Zhao,Z. Y. Jia,K. H. Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过系统研究NiTe₂纳米片和SrTiO₃基异质结构的磁输运性质，证明磁阻的平方标度（quadrature scaling）并不是奇异金属态（strange metal state）的独有特征；只要线性磁阻（linear magnetoresistance）占据主导，该标度就可能出现，因此不应将其作为诊断奇异金属态的可靠工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁阻的平方标度（quadrature scaling）被广泛视为奇异金属态（strange metal state）的标志性特征，但其究竟反映量子临界性（quantum criticality）还是常规输运行为，学界仍存在争议。本文旨在厘清这一标度的真实物理起源。

Method: 系统测量了NiTe₂纳米片（nanosheets）的磁输运（magnetotransport）性质，并通过受控模拟（controlled simulations）分析平方标度的出现条件；另在SrTiO₃基异质结构（heterostructures）中进行验证性观测。

Result: 平方标度仅在交叉场（crossover field）——即从二次磁阻（quadratic magnetoresistance）向线性磁阻（linear magnetoresistance）转变的特征场——相对于外加磁场范围足够小时成立；当线性磁阻区域无法到达时，该标度失效。在缺乏奇异金属行为的SrTiO₃基异质结构中同样观察到平方标度。

Conclusion: 磁阻的平方标度仅仅反映了线性磁阻（linear magnetoresistance）的存在，而非奇异金属态的独特标志。因此，在利用该标度作为探索奇异金属态的诊断工具（diagnostic tool）时需保持谨慎。

Abstract: The quadrature scaling of magnetoresistance has been widely adopted as a hallmark of the strange metal state. However, whether this scaling signals quantum criticality or reflects conventional transport behavior remains controversial. Here, by systematically investigating the magnetotransport properties of NiTe2 nanosheets, we demonstrate that the quadrature scaling is not a unique signature of strange metallicity. We find that the scaling holds only when the crossover field , marking the transition from quadratic to linear magnetoresistance, is sufficiently small relative to the applied field range. Through controlled simulations, we show that the scaling emerges whenever linear magnetoresistance dominates, irrespective of its origin, and fails when the linear regime is inaccessible. This conclusion is supported by observations in SrTiO3 based heterostructures, where quadrature scaling appears despite the absence of strange metal behavior. Our results establish that the quadrature scaling merely reflects the presence of linear magneto resistance, urging caution in using this scaling as a diagnostic tool for exploring the strange metal state.

</details>


### [161] [Incommensurate modulation with $Q=0$ A-type Antiferromagnetic Order in CeRh$_2$As$_2$ revealed by NQR studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18686)
*Shiki Ogata,Shunsaku Kitagawa,Kenji Ishida,Manuel Brando,Elena Hassinger,Christoph Geibel,Seunghyun Khim*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本论文通过对高质量单晶 CeRh₂As₂（一种重费米子超导体）进行 ⁷⁵As 核四极共振（NQR）与核磁共振（NMR）测量，揭示了在更高品质样品中反铁磁（AFM）序的增强及其与超导（SC）相的关联，并发现磁结构具有二维非公度调制叠加在 Q=0 A 型反铁磁分量上的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CeRh₂As₂ 在沿 c 轴方向施加磁场下表现出多超导相（multiple SC phases）现象，被认为源于与局域破缺反演对称性相关的交错 Rashba 自旋-轨道耦合（staggered Rashba spin-orbit coupling）。早期样品中还观察到相 I（T₀ ~ 0.5 K）和反铁磁态（AFM state, T_N ~ 0.25 K）。为了深入理解这些有序相之间的相互作用，特别是磁序与超导的关系，需要对高质量样品中磁有序的特性进行细致表征。

Method: 对高质量 CeRh₂As₂ 单晶样品进行了 ⁷⁵As 核四极共振（nuclear quadrupole resonance, NQR）和核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance, NMR）测量，通过分析 As(1) 位点的 NQR 谱和内场变化来表征磁序特征。

Result: 在高质量样品中，反铁磁（AFM）转变更为显著，T_N 升高至几乎与超导转变温度 T_SC 一致。As(1) 位点的 NQR 谱表明存在具有非公度分布的内场（internal field with an incommensurate distribution），指示磁结构为在 Q=0 A 型反铁磁分量上叠加了二维非公度调制（two-dimensional incommensurate modulation）。此外，在远高于 T_N 的 T₀ 处观察到 NQR 强度的显著下降，并在 T_N 处观察到内场的急剧增加。

Conclusion: 上述结果表明，CeRh₂As₂ 中在 T₀ 处出现了缓慢涨落的反铁磁序（slowly fluctuating AFM order），该磁序在 T_N 处转变为静态有序（static order）。这一发现揭示了磁有序的演化过程及其与超导相之间可能存在的紧密关联。

Abstract: We performed $^{75}$As nuclear quadrupole resonance (NQR) and nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) measurements on a higher-quality single-crystalline CeRh$_2$As$_2$, a heavy-fermion superconductor exhibiting multiple superconducting (SC) phases under magnetic fields along the $c$ axis. This SC multiphase is believed to originate from staggered Rashba spin-orbit coupling associated with locally broken inversion symmetry. In addition to superconductivity, CeRh$_2$As$_2$ exhibits phase I below $T_0\sim0.5$ K and an antiferromagnetic (AFM) state below $T_{N}\sim 0.25$ K in the early-stage samples. In the higher-quality sample, the AFM transition becomes more pronounced, and $T_{N}$ increases to nearly coincide with $T_{SC}$. The NQR spectra at the As(1) site imply an internal field with an incommensurate distribution, indicating a two-dimensional incommensurate modulation of the magnetic structure superimposed on a $Q=0$ A-type AFM component. Moreover, a pronounced decrease in the NQR intensity at $T_0$ well-above $T_{N}$ and an abrupt increase in the internal field at $T_{N}$ suggest the emergence of a slowly fluctuating AFM order at $T_0$ which becomes static at $T_{N}$.

### [162] [Self-consistent GW theory for superconductivity in SrTiO3 models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18757)
*Zhi-Hao Cui,John Sous,Andrew J. Millis,David R. Reichman*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过全动量-频率依赖的有限温度GW方程（无截断和库仑赝势）求解掺杂SrTiO₃的超导问题，发现单次G₀W₀方法会高估配对起始温度1-2个数量级，而自洽GW计算表明配对通道为被初期铁电性屏蔽的Fröhlich声子相互作用，且配对尺度在密度趋于零时仍非零，强调了自洽性、初期铁电性和全动量-频率处理的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 掺杂SrTiO₃在载流子密度极低（费米能低于极性纵向光学声子能标）时仍表现出超导性，但传统Migdal-Eliashberg理论（含声子能标截断和库仑赝势μ*）在此区域的假设不成立。因此需要一种无需这些假设的方法来准确描述该体系的超导机制。

Method: 采用有限温度GW方程，保留完整动量（momentum）和频率（frequency）依赖，不使用截断或库仑赝势μ*。针对极性单带SrTiO₃模型，基于从头算参数化的有效质量和三声子介电函数，比较了三种自洽层次：单次G₀W₀、GW₀和完全自洽GW。

Result: 单次G₀W₀方法高估配对起始温度（pairing-onset temperature）1-2个数量级；主要抑制来自用G替代G₀（引入电子格林函数中的声子重整化因子）；自洽计算W进一步降低并收窄配对起始穹顶。在稀极限下配对通道为被初期铁电性（incipient ferroelectricity）屏蔽的Fröhlich声子相互作用，等离子体与电子屏蔽效应可忽略。全方程数值解显示配对起始尺度在密度趋零时非零，但费米面投影或费米能频率截断会消除这一性质。

Conclusion: 该工作强调了初期铁电性在掺杂极性半导体超导中的关键作用，指出自洽性以及全动量-频率依赖处理对于准确建模SrTiO₃类体系超导性的必要性，并揭示了传统截断方法可能遗漏的物理行为。

Abstract: Superconductivity in doped SrTiO$_3$ occurs over a wide range of carrier densities, including those for which the Fermi energy is below the polar longitudinal optical phonon scale. In this regime, the assumptions underpinning conventional implementations of Migdal-Eliashberg theory, including frequency cutoffs at the phonon scale and a Coulomb pseudopotential $μ^\ast$, are not valid. We solve the finite-temperature $GW$ equations with full momentum and frequency dependence, without cutoffs or $μ^\ast$, for polar one-band models of SrTiO$_3$, using effective masses and three-phonon dielectric functions parameterized from ab initio calculations. Comparing different self-consistency levels, namely $G_0W_0$, $GW_0$, and fully self-consistent $GW$, we find that the one-shot ($G_0W_0$) kernel overestimates the pairing-onset temperature by one to two orders of magnitude. The dominant suppression comes from replacing $G_0$ by $G$, thereby incorporating the phonon renormalization factor in the electron Green function. Using the self-consistently computed interaction $W$ further lowers and narrows the pairing-onset dome. In the dilute limit, our calculations identify the pairing channel as the Fröhlich phonon interaction screened by the incipient ferroelectricity of the material, with plasmonic and electronic screening effects negligible. The numerical solution of the full equations reveals a pairing-onset scale that remains non-zero as the density tends to zero, whereas Fermi-surface projection or Fermi-energy frequency truncation removes it. This work highlights the relevance of incipient ferroelectricity, the importance of self-consistency, and the need for a full momentum- and frequency-dependent treatment in modeling superconductivity in SrTiO$_3$-like doped polar semiconductors.

</details>


### [163] [Collective modes in non-Hermitian fermionic superfluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18814)
*Gabriel Angelo V. Vila,Kristian Hauser Villegas*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文基于度规化非厄米量子力学，为具有复数值配对相互作用的非厄米BCS型超流体系构建了自洽的赝自旋框架，发现了一种在厄米超流中不存在的、具有有限共振响应且对初始相位敏感的新型有隙相位模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希格斯（Higgs）和南部-戈德斯通（Nambu-Goldstone）模式是超导体和超流体中的典范集体激发，通常在BCS理论的赝自旋（pseudospin）框架中分析。然而，当直接将此构造推广到非厄米（non-Hermitian）系统时会出现不一致性，因此需要发展一种适用于非厄米费米子超流体的自洽赝自旋框架。

Method: 基于度规化非厄米量子力学（metricized formulation of non-Hermitian quantum mechanics），为具有复数值配对相互作用的驱动非厄米BCS型哈密顿量（driven non-Hermitian BCS-type Hamiltonian）构建了自洽的赝自旋框架，并分析了其集体激发谱（collective excitation spectrum）。

Result: 在传统的希格斯振幅模式（Higgs (amplitude) mode）之外，系统存在一种在厄米超流中没有对应物的新型相位模式（phase mode）。该模式即使在缺乏安德森-希格斯机制（Anderson-Higgs mechanism）的中性超流中也是有隙的（gapped）。共振谱显式地依赖于复数序参量的初始非规范相位（initial nongauge phase），且动力学的共振响应是有限的，这与厄米系统中的发散行为形成对比。这些共振在出现例外点（exceptional points）时消失。

Conclusion: 非厄米性为超流/超导集体激发谱引入了全新的物理特征——包括有隙相位模式、对初始相位的依赖以及有限共振响应——这些现象在厄米系统中无法出现，为非厄米量子多体系统的研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: The Higgs and Nambu-Goldstone modes are paradigmatic collective excitations in superconductors and superfluids. These modes are commonly analyzed within the pseudospin formulation of BCS theory, where the dynamics are obtained from the Heisenberg equations of motion for pseudospins. However, this construction becomes inconsistent when directly extended to non-Hermitian systems. In this work, we develop a consistent pseudospin framework for non-Hermitian fermionic superfluids based on the metricized formulation of non-Hermitian quantum mechanics. We apply this formalism to a driven non-Hermitian BCS-type Hamiltonian with complex pairing interaction and analyze its collective excitation spectrum. We find that, in addition to the conventional Higgs (amplitude) mode, the system hosts a novel phase mode that has no counterpart in Hermitian superfluids. Remarkably, this mode is gapped even in the absence of the Anderson-Higgs mechanism, as is the case in neutral superfluids. Furthermore, the resonance spectrum depends explicitly on the initial nongauge phase of the complex order parameter and the dynamical response remains finite at resonance, in contrast to the divergence characteristic of Hermitian systems. These resonances disappear upon the emergence of exceptional points.

</details>


### [164] [Optical Properties of Iron-Selenide Na$_{0.27}$K$_{0.27}$Rb$_{0.27}$Fe$_{1.7}$Se$_2$ Single Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18876)
*Andrei Muratov,Yevgeny Rakhmanov,Andrei Shilov,Igor Morozov,Yurii Aleshchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过红外傅里叶变换光谱和光谱椭圆偏振术，研究了超导Na0.27K0.27Rb0.27Fe1.7Se2单晶在4–300 K、宽频率范围内的面内反射率，并利用Drude-Lorentz模型分析了正常态响应。研究发现了1430 cm⁻¹处的Fano形状模式及低频宽带，这些特征在正常态和超导态都持续存在，表明超导性与磁性在该材料中呈介观共存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Na0.27K0.27Rb0.27Fe1.7Se2单晶在正常态和超导态下的光学响应特性，揭示其电子结构、散射机制以及超导与磁性之间的共存关系。

Method: 采用红外傅里叶变换光谱（infrared Fourier-transform spectroscopy）和光谱椭圆偏振术（spectroscopic ellipsometry），在4–300 K温度范围内测量样品面内反射率，并通过Drude-Lorentz模型（包含一个Drude分量）分析正常态光学响应。

Result: 给出了正常态Drude分量的等离子频率（plasma frequency）、光学电导率（optical conductivity）、散射率（scattering rate）和直流电阻率（dc resistivity）的温度依赖性。观测到1430 cm⁻¹处的Fano形状模式（Fano-shaped mode），该模式表明离散模式可能与某个电子跃迁耦合到双磁子连续态（two-magnon continuum）；同时发现一个低频宽带，归属于反铁磁超结构（antiferromagnetic superstructure）的声学磁子支（acoustic magnon branch）。上述特征在正常态和超导态反射谱中均持续存在。

Conclusion: Na0.27K0.27Rb0.27Fe1.7Se2中超导性与磁性在介观尺度上共存（mesoscopic coexistence），光学测量揭示的磁相关模式在两个电子态中均未被压制，为理解铁基超导体中磁性与超导电性的相互作用提供了实验依据。

Abstract: With infrared Fourier-transform spectroscopy and spectroscopic ellipsometry we investigated the in-plane reflectance of the superconducting Na$_{0.27}$K$_{0.27}$Rb$_{0.27}$Fe$_{1.7}$Se$_2$ single crystals with a critical temperature $T_c\approx 34.3$ K over a broad frequency range at temperatures of 4--300 K. The normal-state response of Na$_{0.27}$K$_{0.27}$Rb$_{0.27}$Fe$_{1.7}$Se$_2$ is analyzed by a Drude-Lorentz model with one Drude component. The temperature dependences of the plasma frequency, optical conductivity, scattering rate, and dc resistivity of the Drude component in the normal state are presented. We report a Fano-shaped mode at 1430~cm$^{-1}$ indicating a coupling of the discrete mode presumably related to some electronic transition to a two-magnon continuum as well as a low-frequency broad band assigned to the acoustic magnon branch of the antiferromagnetic superstructure. These features persist in the reflectance in both the normal and superconducting states suggesting a mesoscopic coexistence of superconductivity and magnetism in Na$_{0.27}$K$_{0.27}$Rb$_{0.27}$Fe$_{1.7}$Se$_2$.

</details>


### [165] [Annealing-enhanced spin-orbit effects in non-centrosymmetric superconducting NbRe films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18994)
*Zahra Makhdoumi Kakhaki,Yuriy Yerin,Francesco Avitabile,Abhishek Kumar,Francesco Colangelo,Carla Cirillo,Oleksandr V. Dobrovolskiy,Carmine Attanasio*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过热退火处理研究了非中心对称超导体Nb₀.₁₈Re₀.₈₂薄膜的超导与正常态磁输运性质变化，发现退火显著增强了自旋-轨道散射强度，使上临界场超越传统的轨道极限场和泡利顺磁极限，证明微结构热修饰可有效增强自旋-轨道介导的量子输运，从而保护非中心对称超导态免受顺磁对破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 块材和单晶NbRe展现出多能隙超导（multigap superconductivity）特征，但薄膜由于结构无序和晶粒尺寸减小通常表现为单能隙超导态。本研究旨在探究热退火对NbRe薄膜超导和正常态磁输运性质的影响，以验证能否通过微结构调控增强自旋-轨道耦合效应。

Method: 采用微观Werthamer–Helfand–Hohenberg (WHH) 框架分析上临界场Bc₂(T)的温度依赖性；利用三维Kawabata弱局域化/弱反局域化（weak-localization/weak-anti-localization）模型描述正常态磁导率。

Result: 退火后薄膜正常态表现出强烈的弱反局域化（weak anti-localization）行为；上临界场同时超越传统轨道极限场（orbital-limiting field）和泡利顺磁极限（Pauli paramagnetic limit）；微观分析显示相对自旋-轨道散射强度显著增强，自旋-轨道场与退相场的比值大幅提高。

Conclusion: 热退火对NbRe微结构的热修饰成功放大了自旋-轨道介导的量子输运，这是保护非中心对称超导态（non-centrosymmetric superconducting state）免受顺磁对破坏、使其超越常规理论边界的关键机制。

Abstract: $\text{Nb}_{0.18}\text{Re}_{0.82}$ (NbRe) is a non-centrosymmetric superconductor with a transition temperature $T_\mathrm{c}$ reaching $9\text{ K}$ in bulk form. While bulk and single-crystalline NbRe exhibit signatures of multigap superconductivity, thin films generally display a single-gap superconducting state due to structural disorder and reduced crystallite dimensions. Here, we investigate the impact of thermal annealing on the superconducting and normal-state magnetotransport properties of NbRe films. The temperature dependence of the upper critical field, $B_{\mathrm{c2}}(T)$, is analyzed within the microscopic Werthamer--Helfand--Hohenberg (WHH) framework, while the normal-state magnetoconductivity is described using the three-dimensional Kawabata weak-localization/weak-anti-localization model. Annealing drives a pronounced change in the electronic response, manifested by a strong weak anti-localization behavior in the normal state and an upper critical field that surpasses both the conventional orbital-limiting field and the Pauli paramagnetic limit. The microscopic analysis reveals a strong intrinsic increase in the relative spin--orbit scattering strength, with the annealed film showing a significantly enhanced spin--orbit-to-dephasing field ratio. These findings provide direct, independent evidence that thermal modification of the NbRe microstructure successfully amplifies spin--orbit-mediated quantum transport, which acts as the key mechanism protecting the non-centrosymmetric superconducting state against paramagnetic pair-breaking well beyond conventional theoretical boundaries.

</details>


### [166] [A unified tight-binding description of the electronic structure and Ising protection of superconductivity in misfit layered compounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19308)
*G. A. Bobkov,I. A. Shvets,I. V. Bobkova*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文针对错配层状化合物（MLCs）开发了一个统一的紧束缚模型，基于密度泛函理论（DFT）计算进行参数化，揭示了中间四方层在层间自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）中的主动作用，并阐明了这一耦合对伊辛超导（Ising superconductivity）保护的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 错配层状化合物（MLCs）是实现与二维过渡金属二硫属化物（TMDs）相关的奇异量子态（尤其是伊辛超导）的独特体材料平台，但长期以来缺乏能超越“TMD层电子孤立”这一简化图像的理论描述。

Method: 基于对多种结构构型和化学组分进行的大规模密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，开发了一个统一的紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），并通过将模型纳入Bogoliubov–de Gennes（BdG）计算来检验其对超导特性的影响。

Result: 中间四方层不仅扮演电荷库（charge reservoir）角色，还介导了显著的层间自旋-轨道耦合（interlayer spin-orbit coupling），这一耦合在标准刚带图像（rigid-band picture）中完全缺失，且对重现体材料MLCs的DFT能带结构至关重要。该耦合通过显著增强面内临界场（in-plane critical field），为伊辛超导保护提供了微观机制。

Conclusion: 该框架将MLCs确立为一类具有内在层间耦合和涌现自旋-轨道现象的三维材料，突破了传统二维孤立层图像的局限。

Abstract: Misfit layered compounds (MLCs) offer a unique bulk platform for realizing exotic quantum states typically associated with two-dimensional transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDs), most notably Ising-protected superconductivity. Yet a theoretical description capturing their electronic structure beyond the simplistic picture of electronically isolated TMD layers has been lacking. Here, we develop a unified tight-binding model for metal dichalcogenide-based MLCs, parameterized by extensive density-functional theory (DFT) calculations across multiple structural configurations and chemical compositions. We show that the intervening tetragonal layers play an active role beyond charge reservoirs: they mediate a significant interlayer spin-orbit coupling entirely absent in the standard rigid-band picture. This emergent interlayer spin-orbit coupling is essential for reproducing the DFT band structure of bulk MLCs and, when incorporated into Bogoliubov--de Gennes calculations, provides a microscopic mechanism for the Ising protection of superconductivity by strongly enhancing the in-plane critical field. Our framework establishes MLCs as a distinct class of three-dimensional materials with intrinsically coupled layers and emergent spin-orbit phenomena.

</details>

### [167] [Information Compression at Criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18388)
*Simon Jiricek,Miroslav Hopjan,Boris Altshuler,Vladimir Kravtsov,Lev Vidmar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过能量空间中的内在信息压缩，揭示了处于遍历性临界边界的高激发量子态的动力学复杂性，展示了哈密顿谱的截断可以保留动力学核心特征，并发现截断谱具有分形结构，其能级间距分布呈幂律尾巴，谱型因子与存活概率表现出相同的渐近幂律衰减行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高度激发的量子态在遍历性临界边界（critical boundary of ergodicity）处偏离热力学行为，但其动力学性质尚不清晰，亟需新的理论视角来理解这一临界区域的量子动力学复杂性。

Method: 通过在能量空间中引入内在信息压缩（intrinsic information compression）框架，系统性地截断哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）谱，以简化动力学描述同时保留其核心特征；并针对相互作用（interacting）与非相互作用（noninteracting）系统，检验截断谱对存活概率（survival probability）幂律衰减行为的复现能力。

Result: 对于相互作用和非相互作用系统，仅需一个消失比例的哈密顿量本征能级（eigenlevels）即可复现存活概率的幂律衰减；截断后的谱呈现分形结构（fractal structure），其能级间距分布（level-spacing distribution）具有幂律尾巴（power-law tail），且谱型因子（spectral form factor）与存活概率展示出相同的渐近幂律衰减行为。

Conclusion: 能量空间中的谱截断方法能够有效揭示临界量子动力学中的分形特征，表明系统内在的信息压缩机制是理解遍历性破缺临界行为的关键。

Abstract: Highly excited quantum states at the critical boundary of ergodicity are known to deviate from thermal behavior, yet their dynamical properties remain poorly understood. Here, we uncover the complexity of quantum dynamics at criticality through the lens of intrinsic information compression in energy space. We show that the Hamiltonian spectrum can be systematically truncated, yielding a simplified description of the dynamics while preserving its essential features. Specifically, for both interacting and noninteracting systems, we demonstrate that a vanishing fraction of Hamiltonian eigenlevels suffices to reproduce the power-law decay of the survival probability. The resulting truncated spectrum exhibits a fractal structure characterized by a level-spacing distribution with a power-law tail, while its spectral form factor displays the same asymptotic power-law decay as the survival probability.

</details>


### [168] [Absence of hidden analytic conserved quantities in harmonically confined rods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18872)
*Sahil Kumar Singh,Abhishek Dhar,Sanjay Moudgalya*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过系统分析一维谐振陷阱中等长硬杆（hard rods）系统的守恒量结构，严格排除了除总能量和质心能量之外存在任何额外解析（analytic）隐藏守恒量的可能性。证明过程依赖自由运动时的U(1)旋转不变性以及碰撞时的S_N动量置换不变性；而当杆长度为零（点粒子）时，碰撞条件仅要求更弱的置换对称性，从而允许存在大量额外的解析守恒量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一维谐振陷阱中硬杆系统表现出奇异的非遍历（non-ergodic）行为，暗示可能存在超出已知总能量和质心能量的新隐藏守恒量。本文旨在系统性地检验这一可能性。

Method: 通过系统约束守恒量的可能形式，利用自由运动要求每个杆的位置和动量在U(1)旋转下守恒量不变，以及碰撞要求在一个杆长度非零时守恒量在动量置换群S_N下不变，推导出任何解析守恒量必然函数依赖于两个已知守恒量。对零长度（点粒子）情形，则仅需较小的标签置换群S_N不变性。

Result: 严格证明了一维等长硬杆系统中不存在任何额外的解析隐藏守恒量；同时指出，当杆长度为零（点粒子）时，由于碰撞条件仅要求标签置换下的S_N不变性，存在大量额外的解析守恒量，并明确给出了这些守恒量的形式。

Conclusion: 本文澄清了硬杆问题中守恒量的完整结构，为解释非遍历行为提供了理论依据，并激励将此类系统化方法推广至其他经典系统。

Abstract: Systems of hard rods of equal length in a one-dimensional harmonic trap have been observed to exhibit peculiar non-ergodic behavior that might suggest the existence of a novel hidden conserved quantity beyond the two well known ones, i.e., the total energy and the center-of-mass energy. In this work, we investigate this possibility by systematically constraining the forms of the conserved quantities, and we rigorously rule out the existence of any extra hidden conserved quantity that is analytic in the positions and momenta of the rods involved. We do so by showing two key results: conservation during free motion demands the $U(1)$ invariance of these quantities under rotations of the position and momenta of each rod, and conservation during collisions demand an $S_N$ invariance under the permutation of the momenta of the rods as long as one of the rods have non-zero length. We then show that these conditions imply that any conserved quantity is functionally dependent on the two known conserved quantities. In addition, we show that in the special case where all rods have zero length (i.e., when they are point particles), conservation under collisions only requires invariance under a smaller $S_N$ group of permutations of the labels of the rods, which leads to a much larger set of analytic conserved quantities that we explicitly write down. In all, this rigorously clarifies the structure of conserved quantities in the hard rod problem, and motivates the application of such systematic methods to other classical systems.

</details>


### [169] [Boundary quenches in (1+1)-dimensional conformal field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19166)
*Michele Fossati,Colin Rylands,Eytan Grosfeld,Eran Sela,Pasquale Calabrese*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类局域量子淬火（local quantum quenches），其中(1+1)维共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）中的共形边界条件（conformal boundary condition）发生突变。推导出半直线上单点函数时间演化的简洁普适表达式，揭示了淬火引发扰动的传播机制，并发现与边界相邻子系统的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）在完全因果连接后会发生尖锐的有限跳变，其大小由初始与最终边界条件的g-因子（g-factors）之比的对数普适给出。通过在临界伊辛自旋链（Ising spin chain）上进行矩阵乘积态（Matrix Product State, MPS）模拟，验证了理论预测，并进一步分析了自旋翻转纠缠不对称性（spin-flip entanglement asymmetry）的时间演化，揭示了边界处对称性破缺扰动的传播过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子多体系统中非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium dynamics）的普适行为是当前理论物理的重要课题。边界淬火（boundary quenches）作为一类典型的局域扰动，其引发的纠缠演化与临界现象（critical phenomena）之间的联系尚待系统阐明。本文旨在建立边界淬火动力学与边界临界现象之间直接的解析联系，并寻找可实验检验的普适动力学特征。

Method: 理论方面，作者利用(1+1)维共形场论的边界共形场论（boundary conformal field theory, BCFT）框架，推导了边界条件突变后半直线上单点函数（one-point functions）的精确时间演化表达式，并基于此计算了与边界相邻子系统的纠缠熵时间演化。数值方面，对临界伊辛自旋链进行矩阵乘积态模拟，验证了理论预测的普适纠缠跳变，并进一步研究了自旋翻转纠缠不对称性的动力学行为。

Result: 推导出单点函数时间演化的简洁普适表达式，揭示了边界淬火后扰动的传播规律。纠缠熵在子系统完全因果连接到淬火事件后，发生尖锐的有限跳变（finite jump），其幅度由边界g-因子比值的对数普适给出。临界伊辛链的MPS模拟与理论预测吻合极好，并展示了对称性破缺扰动从边界向体系统传播的动力学过程。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了边界淬火中非平衡纠缠动力学（nonequilibrium entanglement dynamics）与边界临界现象（boundary critical phenomena）之间的直接普适联系，为理解局域量子淬火的普适动力学特征提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate a class of local quantum quenches in which the conformal boundary condition of a (1+1)-dimensional conformal field theory is abruptly changed. We derive a remarkably simple and universal expression for the time evolution of one-point functions on the half-line. This result provides a direct description of the propagation of the disturbance generated by the quench and, in turn, allows us to determine the dynamics of bipartite entanglement for subsystems adjacent to the boundary. We show that, once the subsystem becomes fully causally connected to the quench event, the entanglement entropy undergoes a sharp finite jump whose magnitude is universally given by the logarithm of the ratio of the boundary g-factors associated with the initial and final boundary conditions. We benchmark these analytical predictions against Matrix Product State simulations of the critical Ising spin chain, finding excellent agreement. The numerical analysis further allows us to investigate the time evolution of the spin-flip entanglement asymmetry, revealing how the symmetry-breaking perturbation emitted from the boundary propagates through the system. Our results uncover universal dynamical signatures of boundary quenches and establish a direct connection between nonequilibrium entanglement dynamics and boundary critical phenomena.

</details>


### [170] [Statistical properties of quadrangular surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19221)
*Hrant Topchyan,Rudik Badalyan,Ara Sedrakyan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了三种随机四边形曲面（GKNS、DQ、GQ）的统计性质，建立统一图论框架，揭示其度分布、几何维度和临界行为，发现DQ与动力学三角剖分（DT）属同一普适类，而GKNS和GQ构成不同随机几何类，可能对应新型非临界弦理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解不同随机化过程生成的随机四边形曲面（random quadrangular surfaces）的统计与几何性质，并探究它们与已知随机曲面类型（如动力学三角剖分 DT）之间的关系。

Method: 建立统一的图论框架（graph-theoretic framework）描述三种随机曲面；利用逾渗（percolation）过程分析GKNS构造；通过马尔可夫链（Markov chain）分析DQ和GQ的混合与弛豫时间；比较度分布（degree distribution）、度关联、距离统计和豪斯多夫维数（Hausdorff dimension）。

Result: GKNS等价于两个相互约束的逾渗过程，临界指数偏离普通逾渗；DQ和GQ的马尔可夫链混合与弛豫时间具有不同标度行为；DQ的度分布呈指数衰减，几何性质与DT类似，而GKNS和GQ呈无标度（scale-free）度分布；GKNS的渐近豪斯多夫维数约为2，DQ和GQ约为4。

Conclusion: DQ与DT属于同一普适类（universality class），而GKNS和GQ定义了不同的随机几何类，可能对应随机曲面空间中不同的底层测度，并为新型非临界弦理论（noncritical string theory）提供几何框架。

Abstract: We investigate the statistical properties of random quadrangular surfaces generated by different randomization procedures: the Gruzberg-Klümper-Nuding-Sedrakyan (GKNS) construction, and two newly introduced generalizations of dynamical triangulations (DT), dynamical (DQ) and general quadrangulations (GQ). We formulate these surfaces within a unified graph-theoretic framework and establish the relationships between the elementary operations defining the different ensembles. For GKNS surfaces, we demonstrate that the construction is equivalent to two mutually constrained percolation processes and determine the associated critical point and critical exponents, revealing deviations from ordinary percolation. For DQ and GQ, we analyze the underlying Markov chains and determine the scaling of mixing and relaxation times. We further analyze all three ensembles through their degree distributions, degree correlations, distance statistics, and Hausdorff dimensions. While DQ exhibits exponentially decaying degree distributions and geometric properties similar to DT, GKNS and GQ display broad, scale-free degree distributions. Moreover, GKNS surfaces possess an asymptotic Hausdorff dimension $Δ_H\approx 2$, whereas DQ and GQ approach $Δ_H\approx 4$, similarly to DT. This indicates that DQ is compatible with the universal behavior of DT, while GKNS and GQ define distinct classes of random geometry, implying a different underlying measure in the space of random surfaces and a possible geometric framework for a new class of noncritical string theories.

</details>


### [171] [Deterministic cascade coarsening in a Bistable Gene Toggle model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18891)
*Priyanka D. Bhoyar,Prashant M. Gade*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 研究了一个具有扩散耦合的双稳基因开关模型（bistable gene toggle model）中的确定性粗化动力学（deterministic coarsening dynamics），发现该系统中畴壁（domain walls）通过间歇性级联崩塌而非连续曲率驱动方式消失，粗化过程呈现对数周期振荡（log-periodic oscillations）及偏离经典 Allen–Cahn 指数（δ=1/2）的标度行为，并表明振荡由级联中消失的畴而非畴壁密度控制，符合离散标度不变性（discrete scale invariance）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究空间扩展的双稳基因开关模型中粗化动力学的具体机制，特别是其是否遵循经典曲率驱动粗化的标准行为（如 Allen–Cahn 预言）。

Method: 在具有扩散耦合的空间扩展双稳基因开关模型中，通过数值模拟研究畴壁的动力学演化，测量畴壁密度随时间的衰减 $ρ(t)\sim t^{-δ}$，分析log-periodic振荡行为，并考察级联事件中消失畴的尺寸随级联指数的变化。

Result: 畴壁在长时间内保持钉扎（pinned），并通过集体级联事件（collective cascade events）突然消失；畴壁密度衰减满足幂律 $ρ(t)\sim t^{-δ}$ 但叠加明显log-periodic振荡；在所有考虑的启动子强度α下，指数 δ<0.5，偏离经典 Allen–Cahn 预测的 1/2；log-periodic振荡不由畴壁密度控制，而由每次级联中消失的畴控制；消失畴的平均尺寸随级联指数大致线性增长，产生恒定几何间隔的级联时间，与离散标度不变性一致。

Conclusion: 该系统的粗化动力学与经典曲率驱动粗化存在质的差异，表现出钉扎-级联机制、对数周期振荡和偏离 1/2 的标度指数，同时级联行为揭示了离散标度不变性的存在，提示基因调控网络中可能出现非经典动力学标度行为。

Abstract: We investigate deterministic coarsening dynamics in a spatially extended bistable gene toggle model with diffusive coupling. Unlike classical curvature-driven coarsening, where domain walls move continuously and annihilate gradually, the present system exhibits a qualitatively different mechanism. The domain walls remain pinned for long intervals and disappear abruptly through collective cascade events. The density of domain walls decays approximately as $ρ(t)\sim t^{-δ}$, but the coarsening exhibits clear log-periodic oscillations superimposed on the power-law behavior. For all values of the promoter strength $α$ considered, the measured exponent satisfies $δ<0.5$, indicating a systematic deviation from the classical Allen--Cahn prediction $δ=1/2$ for curvature-driven coarsening. We show that log-periodic oscillations are not controlled by the density of domain walls, but by the \emph{domains that disappear} in each cascade. The average size of disappearing domains grows roughly linearly with cascade index, producing a constant geometric spacing of cascade times, consistent with discrete scale invariance.

</details>


### [172] [Energy Conversion, Fluctuation Suppression, and Information Transfer in the Thermodynamic Performance of Kinesin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18905)
*Riku Kato,Takayuki Ariga,Tomohiro Tanogami*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在一个统一的驱动蛋白-货物（kinesin-cargo）模型中系统比较了多种热力学效率，发现这些效率普遍较低，表明驱动蛋白并非以最大化这些热力学效率为目标，热力学效率本身可能不足以全面表征分子马达的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究利用随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）框架中的多种效率指标量化驱动蛋白（kinesin）的性能，但由于不同模型和假设的存在，定量比较困难，因此不清楚驱动蛋白在热力学上是否被优化，以及哪个方面被优化。

Method: 构建了一个热力学一致的两态驱动蛋白-货物模型（two-state kinesin-cargo model），保留了驱动蛋白的离散步进及其与货物的耦合。在马达与货物之间存在时间尺度分离（separation of time scales）的假设下，推导了热力学效率、信息-热力学效率（information-thermodynamic efficiency）、热力学不确定关系效率（TUR efficiency）以及二分热力学不确定关系效率（bipartite TUR efficiency）的解析表达式，并与数值模拟结果进行比较。

Result: 多种热力学效率普遍较低，表明驱动蛋白并非以最大化所考虑的这些热力学效率为优化目标。

Conclusion: 仅靠热力学效率可能无法全面表征驱动蛋白的性能，需要进一步从互补的动力学（kinetic）视角来评估分子马达的功能。

Abstract: Kinesin is a molecular motor that transports intracellular cargoes along microtubules. Recent studies have quantified kinesin performance using various efficiencies within the framework of stochastic thermodynamics; however, quantitative comparisons remain difficult because different models and assumptions have been employed. As a result, it remains unclear which aspect of kinesin performance, if any, is thermodynamically optimized. Here, we systematically compare multiple thermodynamic efficiencies within a single kinesin-cargo model. To this end, we construct a thermodynamically consistent two-state kinesin-cargo model that retains both the discrete stepping of kinesin and its coupling to the cargo. Assuming a separation of time scales between the motor and the cargo, we derive analytical expressions for the thermodynamic efficiency, the information-thermodynamic efficiency, the thermodynamic uncertainty relation (TUR) efficiency, and the bipartite TUR efficiency, and compare them with numerical simulation results. We find that these efficiencies generally remain low, suggesting that kinesin is not optimized for maximizing the thermodynamic efficiencies considered here. Our results suggest that thermodynamic efficiencies alone may not fully characterize kinesin performance and motivate further investigation of complementary kinetic perspectives for assessing molecular motor function.

</details>


### [173] [Discrete distributions and statistical mechanics of small systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18968)
*Lev B. Klebanov,Michal Šumbera*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过概率生成函数（probability generating function）研究离散概率分布与统计力学（statistical mechanics）小系统之间的联系，引入马尔可夫分布（Markovian distribution）等新类别，并将其应用于巨正则系综描述、位力展开（virial expansion）以及气液相变动力学模型，同时探讨了Tsallis非广延热力学中的分布可扩展性（scalability）与q-变形分布（q-deformation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索离散概率分布与统计力学小系统之间的深层联系，试图建立从概率论到统计系综描述的桥梁，并揭示由无穷可分性（infinite divisibility）与可扩展性（scalability）等概念导出的物理图像，如準粒子图像（quasiparticle picture）与重整化（renormalization）临界行为。

Method: 利用概率生成函数（probability generating functions）发展幂级数（power series）、无穷可分（infinitely divisible）与可扩展（scalable）分布理论；引入由生灭过程（birth-death processes）稳态解自然产生的马尔可夫分布（Markovian distribution）类别；采用巨正则系综框架与重整化半群变换（renormalization semi-group transformation）进行分析。

Result: 无穷可分性导致相互作用气体的準粒子图像；位力展开与分布的组合数（combinants）建立联系。气液相变临界点处的粒子数分布收敛到离散稳定分布（Discrete Stable distribution），即重整化半群变换的不动点。Tsallis非广延热力学中分布的可扩展性保持但无穷可分性失效。负二项分布（negative binomial）作为Poisson分布的q-变形自然出现。

Conclusion: 离散概率分布理论为统计力学小系统提供了统一的数学框架，从气体準粒子描述到临界现象及非广延热力学均能自然衔接，揭示了无穷可分性与可扩展性在统计物理中的核心地位。

Abstract: We study connections between discrete probability distributions and the statistical mechanics of small systems. Using probability generating functions, we develop the theory of power series, infinitely divisible, and scalable distributions of non-negative integer-valued random variables, and introduce the class of Markovian distributions that arise naturally in stationary solutions of birth-death processes and in scalable infinitely divisible distributions.
  These results are applied to the grand canonical ensemble description in statistical mechanics: the infinite divisibility leads to a quasiparticle picture of an interacting gas, and the virial expansion is linked to the combinants of the distribution. A kinetic model of the liquid-vapor phase transition is presented, in which the particle-number distribution at the critical point converges to the Discrete Stable distribution - the fixed point of a renormalization semi-group transformation. We also show that the scalability of the particle-number distribution is preserved in Tsallis non-extensive thermodynamics, even though infinite divisibility fails. Moreover, deformed discrete distributions, including the negative binomial as a q-deformation of the Poisson, arise naturally in this setting.

</details>


### [174] [Dynamical correlation functions of extensive charges after global quantum quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19208)
*Riccardo Travaglino,Katja Klobas,Bruno Bertini,Pasquale Calabrese*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究量子淬火（quantum quench）后广延 U(1) 电荷的 n-时间累积量母函数（n-time cumulant generating function），利用时空对偶性（space-time duality）证明在传输为弹道输运（ballistic transport）等弱时间关联条件下，该函数可分解为时间壳层（time-shell）结构下单时间 FCS 的和，从而极大简化动力学关联函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子淬火后广延 U(1) 电荷的 n-时间全计数统计量（n-Full Counting Statistics, n-FCS），旨在理解多体量子系统中长时间尺度的电荷涨落行为及其结构。

Method: 利用时空对偶性（space-time duality）分析从电荷对称初始态演化后的 n-时间累积量母函数；在弱时间关联（如弹道输运）条件下，将 n-FCS 分解为时间壳层结构的单时间 FCS 之和；在自由与相互作用模型中进行解析与数值验证。

Result: n-FCS 在弱时间关联条件下可分解为时间壳层结构中单时间 FCS 的和；该结构导致动力学关联函数大幅简化：存在时间排序（time ordering）时，关联函数仅依赖于其中最小的时间参数。

Conclusion: 这项工作揭示了一类可分解的 n-时间统计结构，为理解和计算量子淬火后 U(1) 对称系统中的多时间电荷涨落与动力学关联函数提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the $n$-time cumulant generating function (or $n$-Full Counting Statistics, $n$-FCS) of extensive $U(1)$ charges following a quantum quench. Exploiting space-time duality we characterise this function when evolving from initial states that are symmetric under the action of the charge. In particular, we show that if the correlations in time are sufficiently weak, e.g.\ the transport is ballistic, the $n$-FCS factorises into a sum of single-time FCS arranged in a time-shell structure. A direct implication of this structure is a drastic simplification of dynamical correlation functions: in the presence of time ordering they only depend on the smallest time entering the correlator. We support these findings with several analytical and numerical tests performed in free and interacting models.

</details>
